sa tayā śraddhayā pūto vimuktaḥ sarvapātakaiḥ
snātvā yaḥ pūrvasaṃdhyāyāṃ sadā mām upagacchati
sa mitraṃ yakṣarājasya yakṣo bhavati vīryavān
saṃmārjanaṃ pañcaśataṃ sahasram upalepanam
gandhāśca daśasāhasrā ānantyaṃ cārcanaṃ smṛtam
abhyaṅgo 'aṣṭaśataṃ caiva snapanaṃ triśataṃ bhavet
kṣamāmi devi cāsyeha aparādhān bahūnapi
agaruṃ daśasāhasraṃ ṣaṭsahasraṃ tu candanam
caturdaśasahasrāṇi dhūpaḥ kālāgaruḥ smṛtaḥ
akṣatāstaṇḍulayavāḥ śālayo dviśatāḥ smṛtāḥ
dve sahasre palānāṃ tu mahiṣākṣasya yo dahet
ubhe pakṣe trayodaśyām aṣṭamyāṃ copavāsikaḥ
upatiṣṭheta māṃ bhaktyā sopahāram anindite
dadānyasya svakaṃ lokaṃ tuṣṭo 'ahaṃ devi śāśvatam
ekarātraṃ ca yo martyo dīpaṃ dhārayati sthitaḥ
mayaiva mohitāḥ sarve lokāḥ sajaḍapaṇḍitāḥ
na māṃ paśyanti rāgāndhāstamasā bahulīkṛtāḥ
dhyānino nityayuktā ye satyadharmaparāyaṇāḥ
ekāgramanaso dāntāste māṃ paśyanti nityadā
ye me bhaktāḥ sadā caiva sāṃkhyayogaviśāradāḥ
dhyānino nityayuktāśca devi paśyanti māṃ budhāḥ
yāni lokeṣu tīrthāni devatāyatanāni ca
pādayostāni suśroṇi sadā saṃnihitāni me
sarvāvastho 'api pāpātmā jñānaniṣṭhena cetasā
praviśeta sa māṃ kṣipram atra nāsti vicāraṇā
iti skandapurāṇe saptaviṃśatitamo 'adhyāyaḥ
aṣṭāviṃśo adhyāyaḥ
tato vyāsa punardevī patiṃ vratapatiṃ śubhā
vratānāṃ phalam alpaṃ vā mahadvā yat trilokapa
vrataṃ bhavati yādṛgvā tat prabrūhi maheśvara
vrataṃ yādṛk ca yat proktaṃ tacchṛṇuṣvamanindite
caturdaśyāṃ tathāṣṭamyām ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ śuciḥ
saṃvatsaram abhuñjānaḥ śānto dānto jitendriyaḥ
sattrayājiphalaṃ yacca satyavāgṛtugāminām
sa tapyati ā nakhāgrebhyo nityaṃ yo māṃ samāśritaḥ
lokāstasyākṣayā devi yadyapi syāt supāpakṛt
navamī aṣṭamī caiva paurṇamāsī trayodaśī
bhūtānāṃ dayitaścaiva divyaṃ rūpaṃ bibharti ca
śrīvatsaṃ yaśca piṣṭena dadyāddhemaphalaṃ śubham
kiret kṛṣṇatilāṃścātra taṇḍulākṣatam eva ca
sa vai varṣasahasrāṇi dviṣaṣṭiṃ divi modate
divyarūpadharaḥ śrīmān devataiḥ saha nityaśaḥ
hariberamayīṃ yo me dadyāt pratikṛtiṃ svakām
sarvagandharasairyuktāṃ niryāsaiśca susaṃskṛtām
pārśveṣu haritālaṃ ca kṛṣṇāgarumanaḥśilām
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ devi śṛṇu yanmattakāśini
varṣakoṭiśatānyaṣṭau divi bhuktvā mahat sukham
ratnāvaliṃ tu yo dadyādbrāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo 'atha viṭ
śūdraḥ strī vā sa me loke matsaukhyaṃ prāpnute param
ṛṣīṃśca sarvadevāṃśca rūpaṃ cāpnoti puṣkalam
sarve devāstathā viṣṇurbrahmā ṛṣaya eva ca
prajñārūpaguṇairyuktaḥ saṃvatsaraśatāyutam
kṣīreṇa yo māṃ satataṃ snāpayeta trirudyataḥ
aparādhasahasraṃ tu kṣame tasyāham antaśaḥ
saṃvatsaraṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt kṣīreṇa snapanaṃ śuciḥ
sarpiṣā yo mamābhyaṅgaṃ karotyavimanā naraḥ
niṣkāṇāṃ ca suvarṇasya sahasrasya phalaṃ labhet
saṃmārjanaṃ ca yaḥ kuryāt saṃvatsaram anuvrataḥ
vitarāmi śubhaṃ lokaṃ nityaṃ tasya dhruvaṃ śivam
liṅgapūjāṃ tu yaḥ kuryānmama devi dṛḍhavrataḥ
śataṃ varṣasahasrāṇi divyāni divi modate
caturṇāṃ puṣpajātīnāṃ gandham āghrāti śaṃkaraḥ
nirmālyaṃ yo hi me nityaṃ śirasā dhārayiṣyati
brahmacārī śucirbhūtvā nirmālyaṃ yastu dhārayet
tasya pāpam ahaṃ śīghraṃ nāśayāmi mahāvrate
dīpamālāṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt kārttike māsi vai mama
avasāne ca dīpānāṃ brāhmaṇāṃstarpayecchuciḥ
dadyāt kṛṣṇatilāṃścaiva saha siddhārthakāṃśca ha
ye hi siddhārthakāḥ proktāstathā kṛṣṇatilāśca ye
tyaktvā sarvāṇi duḥkhāni mām eva pratipadyate
na tuṣyāmyarcito 'arcāyāṃ tathā devi nagātmaje
tyaktvā sarvāṇi pāpāni nirdvandvo dagdhakilbiṣaḥ
apṛcchat puṣpyamāṇāsyā kena tvaṃ deva tuṣyasi
tataḥ prahasamānāsyaḥ sarvalokeśvareśvaraḥ
vacaḥ provāca bhagavāllokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
śṛṇu devi yathātattvaṃ yena yānti śubhāṃ gatim
na ca prakāśayedguhyaṃ nāma te kīrtayennaraḥ
sadā sarvasahetyevaṃ prātaḥ prāñjalirutthitaḥ
yaśaḥ kīrtiṃ ca samprāpya rudraloke mahīyate
sarvamālyāni yo dadyāt sarvamūrtiṣu nityaśaḥ
somāya bhūtanāthāya bhāvanāya bhavāya ca
kaṭaṃkaṭāyaiva svāhā svāhā devāya śuṣmiṇe
athāñjalim amāvāsyāṃ susampūrṇāṃ samāhitaḥ
tilānāṃ caiva kṛṣṇānāṃ sarṣapāṇāṃ ca pārvati
arcayitvā yathānyāyaṃ yathālābhaṃ prayacchati
arcayitvā ca māṃ devi brāhmaṇān na ca tarpayet
arcayitvā dvijān māṃ ca yo me nāmāni kīrtayet
caturdaśyām athāṣṭamyāṃ pakṣayorubhayorapi
umāpate nīlakaṇṭha śānta śrīkaṇṭha gopate
eteṣām ekam api yaḥ kathayedvā paṭheta vā
amāvāsyāṃ tu yo nityaṃ saghṛtaṃ guggulaṃ dahet
kṣīreṇa caiva saṃmiśraṃ guhyam etanmama priye
so 'acyutaṃ sthānam āpnoti matprasādānna saṃśayaḥ
arkaparṇapuṭaṃ pūrṇaṃ ghṛtasya madhunā saha
imāni ca mahābhāge yo me nāmāni kīrtayet
śmaśānanilayo nagno bhasmaśāyī yatavrataḥ
vāmadevaḥ praśāntaśca stabdhaśephastrilocanaḥ
purāṇaḥ puruhūtaśca mṛtyormṛtyurjitendriyaḥ
saṃsāracakrī yogātmā kāpālī diṇḍireva ca
japedetanniyamavān śṛṇuyādvāpi nityaśaḥ
nāśubhāya na pāpāya nānṛtāya kadācana
śrāvayedbhaktimān puṇyaṃ nāpetāya kadācana
dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ śāntivṛddhikaraṃ śubham
pūtaṃ pavitraṃ paramaṃ maṅgalānāṃ ca maṅgalam
iti skandapurāṇe īśvarapūjā nāmāṣṭāviṃśatitamo 'adhyāyaḥ
ūnatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
vyāsa uvāca
evaṃ kālena samprāpya vārāṇasyāṃ niketanam
tataḥ sa bhagavān devo devīṃ himavataḥ sutām
uvāca devi paśyāma udyānaṃ yadi rocate
evaṃ bhavatu deveśa yathāttha tvaṃ vṛṣadhvaja
saha devyā tato vyāsa vārāṇasyāṃ vṛṣadhvajaḥ
devodyānadidṛkṣārthaṃ vicacāra samantataḥ
pūrvasmin sa diśābhāge devyā devaḥ pinākadhṛk
udyānaṃ darśayāmāsa nānākusumaśobhitam
campakāśokapuṃnāgapriyaṅgūcūtasaṃkulam
ramyaiḥ surabhipuṣpaiśca ṣaṭpadavrātasevitaiḥ
saṃyuktaṃ sarvataḥ śrīmadvanaṃ vaibhrājasaṃnibham
sa tadudyānam āsādya devīm āha jagatpatiḥ
ūrdhvaṃ golokasaṃsthānāṃ gavāṃ vatsaiḥ svayaṃbhuvaiḥ
pīyatīnāṃ payo vegāt phenaṃ mūrdhni samāpatat
tato mayordhvaṃ dṛṣṭāstu gāvastāḥ somapārśvagāḥ
tatastāḥ prekṣitāstatra mayā gāvastadābhavan
tejasā dahyamānāstu naikavarṇā bhṛśārditāḥ
gāvaḥ pūrvam imā devi āsan kapilavarṇajāḥ
naikavarṇāstadābhūvan yadā samprekṣitā mayā
tāsāṃ śaraṇyatāṃ yātvā tābhirmām eva śailaje
goprekṣeśvaram āgatya dṛṣṭvā cārcya ca mānavaḥ
atrāpi svayam evāhaṃ vṛṣadhvaja iti śrutaḥ
sāṃnidhyaṃ kṛtavān devi sa cāyaṃ dṛśyatāṃ sthitaḥ
kapilāhradatīrthe 'asmin snātvā nānyamanā naraḥ
vṛṣadhvajam imaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhet
salokatāṃ mṛtaścāpi arcayitvā tu mām iha
śāntyarthaṃ sarvalokānāṃ sarvā dugdhāḥ payomṛtam
tāsāṃ kṣīreṇa saṃjātaṃ hradam etanmanoharam
gacchopaśamam īśeti upaśāntaśivastataḥ
dṛṣṭvainaṃ prayato martyaḥ svargalokam avāpnuyāt
atrāhaṃ brahmaṇānīya sthāpitaḥ parameṣṭhinā
brahmaṇaścāpi saṃgṛhya viṣṇunā sthāpitaḥ punaḥ
brahmaṇā sa tato viṣṇuḥ proktaḥ saṃvignacetasā
mayānītam idaṃ liṅgaṃ kasmāt sthāpitavānasi
tam uvāca punarviṣṇurbrahmāṇaṃ kupitānanam
dṛṣṭvainam api deveśaṃ mama lokaṃ vrajennaraḥ
punaścāpi tato brahmā mama liṅgam imaṃ śubhe
sthāpayāmāsa vidhivadbhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ
tasmāt svarlīna ityevaṃ guhyaṃ kṣetraṃ mama smṛtam
ānantyā sā gatistasya yogināṃ caiva sā smṛtā
vyāghrarūpaṃ samāsthāya nihato darpito balī
vyāghreśvarastataḥ khyāto nityam atrāham āsthitaḥ
na punardurgatiṃ yāti dṛṣṭvainam amareśvaram
sāvajñaṃ geṇḍukenātra tasyedaṃ cihnam āsthitam
ādāvatrāham āgatya āsthito gaṇapaiḥ saha
jyeṣṭhaṃ sthānam idaṃ tasmādetanme puṇyadarśanam
dṛṣṭvemaṃ mama liṅgaṃ tu jyeṣṭhasthānasamāśritam
kṣetraṃ vārāṇasī puṇyā muktidaṃ sambhaviṣyati
avimukteśvaraṃ māṃ vai yo 'atra drakṣyati mānavaḥ
prāṇāniha tu saṃnyasya yāsyate muktim uttamām
mama priyam idaṃ sthānaṃ jñātvā liṅgaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
śaileśvaram iti khyātaṃ dṛśyatām idam āsthitam
nadī vārāṇasī ceyaṃ puṇyā pāpapramocanī
kṣetram etadalaṃkṛtya jāhnavyā saha saṃgatā
sthāpitaṃ saṃgame cāsmin brahmaṇā liṅgam uttamam
saṃgameśvaram ityevaṃ khyātaṃ jagati dṛśyatām
saṃgame devanadyostu yaḥ snātvā manujaḥ śuciḥ
arcayet saṃgameśānaṃ tasya janmabhayaṃ kutaḥ
idam anyadbṛhat kṣetraṃ nivāsaṃ yogināṃ param
kṣetramadhye ca yatrāhaṃ svayaṃ bhūtvā samāsthitaḥ
siddhānāṃ sthānam etaddhi madīyavratacāriṇām
yogināṃ mokṣalipsūnāṃ janmamṛtyujitātmanām
dṛṣṭvedaṃ madhyameśānaṃ janma prati na śocati
sthāpitaṃ liṅgam etacca śukreṇa tava sūnunā
nāmnā śukreśvaraṃ nāma sarvasiddhāmarārcitam
dṛṣṭvedaṃ mānavaḥ sadyo muktaḥ syāt sarvakilbiṣaiḥ
purā jambukarūpeṇa asurā devakaṇṭakāḥ
brahmaṇo 'atha varaṃ labdhvā gomāyuvadhaśaṅkitāḥ
abhavaṃ jagati khyātaḥ surāsuranamaskṛtaḥ
dṛṣṭvainam api deveśaṃ sarvakāmānavāpnuyāt
grahaiḥ śukrapurogaiśca etāni sthāpitāni hi
paśya liṅgāni puṇyāni sarvakāmapradāni tu
evam etāni puṇyāni mannivāsāni pārvati
kathitāni tava kṣetre guhyaṃ cānyadidaṃ śṛṇu
krośaṃ krośaṃ caturdikṣu kṣetram etat prakīrtitam
gaṇatvaṃ labhate dṛṣṭvā kṣetre 'asmin mokṣamāpyate
gāṇapatyapadāt tasmādyataḥ sā muktiruttamā
tato mahālayāt tasmāt kedārānmadhyamādapi
smṛtaṃ puṇyatamaṃ kṣetram avimuktam idaṃ śubhe
mama puṇyāni bhūrloke tebhyaḥ śreṣṭhatamaṃ tvidam
yataḥ sṛṣṭāni lokāni tataḥ kṣetram idaṃ śubham
avimukteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ mama dṛṣṭveha mānavaḥ
sadyaḥ pāpavinirmuktaḥ paśupāśairvimucyate
śaileśaṃ saṃgameśaṃ ca svarlīnaṃ madhyameśvaram
hiraṇyagarbham īśānaṃ goprekṣaṃ savṛṣadhvajam
upaśāntaśivaṃ caiva jyeṣṭhasthānanivāsinam
śukreśvaraṃ ca vikhyātaṃ vyāghreśaṃ jambukeśvaram
dṛṣṭvā na jāyate martyaḥ saṃsāre duḥkhasāgare
savidyutstanitāghoṣaṃ sūryāyutaśatoditam
tataḥ pāśupatāḥ siddhā bhasmābhyaṅgasitaprabhāḥ
yogīśvarā mahātmānastathā vaitānikavratāḥ
punarnirīkṣya deveśaṃ dhyānayogaṃ ca kṛtsnaśaḥ
tasthurātmānam ādhāya līyamānā iveśvare
sthitānāṃ sa tathā teṣāṃ devadeva umāpatiḥ
saṃcintya paramāṃ mūrtiṃ babhūva puruṣaḥ prabhuḥ
tasya tāṃ paramāṃ mūrtim āsthitasya jagatprabhoḥ
na śaśāka vapurdraṣṭuṃ hṛṣṭaromā girīndrajā
tatastatsṛṣṭam ātmānaṃ buddhvā sā prakṛtisthitam
prakṛtermūrtim āsthāya yogena paramātmikā
taṃ śaśāka vapurdraṣṭuṃ puruṣasya parātmanaḥ
viviśurhṛdayaṃ sarve dagdhasaṃsārabījinaḥ
anugṛhya tataḥ sarvān tān siddhān yatipuṃgavān
taṃ dṛṣṭvā śailajā prāha hṛṣṭasarvatanūruhā
tām uvāca suraśreṣṭhastadā devīṃ girīndrajām
kṣetrasyāsya prabhāveṇa bhaktyā ca mama bhāvataḥ
pratimāsam athāṣṭamyāṃ pratimāsaṃ caturdaśīm
ubhayoḥ pakṣayordevi vārāṇasyāṃ mamāspade
śaśibhānūparāge ca kārttikyāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ
pṛthivyāṃ sarvatīrthāni vārāṇasyāṃ tu jāhnavīm
uttarapravahāṃ puṇyāṃ mama maulivinirgatām
pituste girirājācca srutāṃ himavataḥ śubhām
saṃnihityā kurukṣetraṃ sārdhaṃ tīrthaśataistathā
puṣkaraṃ naimiśaṃ caiva prayāgaṃ sapṛthūdakam
sandhyā saptaṛcaṃ caiva sarvā nadyaḥ sarāṃsi ca
samudrāḥ sapta caivātra devatīrthāni kṛtsnaśaḥ
bhāgīrathīṃ sameṣyanti sarvaparvasu kāśigām
avimukteśvaraṃ māṃ ca kāśīstham acalātmaje
pṛthivyāṃ yāni puṇyāni mahyam āyatanāni ca
kedāre caiva yalliṅgaṃ yacca liṅgaṃ mahālaye
madhyameśvarasaṃsthaṃ ca tathā paśupatīśvaram
śaṅkukarṇeśvaraṃ caiva gokarṇe ca tathā hyubhau
sthāneśvaram athaikāmraṃ kāleśvaram ajeśvaram
bhairaveśvaram īśānaṃ tathā kārohaṇāsthitam
yāni cānyāni puṇyāni sthānāni mama bhūtale
tāni sarvāṇyaśeṣeṇa kāśipuryāṃ viśanti mām
snātasya caiva gaṅgāyāṃ dṛṣṭena ca mayā śubhe
sarvayajñaphalaistulyam iṣṭaiḥ śatasahasraśaḥ
sarvāyatanamukhyānāṃ divi bhūmau giriṣvapi
nātaḥ parataraṃ devi budhyasvāstīti kṛtsnaśaḥ
sthānaṃ mamedaṃ himaśailaputri guhyaṃ sadā kṣetram idaṃ supuṇyam
kṣetre 'asmin nivasanti ye sukṛtino bhaktāḥ sadā māṃ narāḥ
evam etat suvistīrṇaṃ nānādrumalatākulam
jāhnavyālaṃkṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ kṣetraṃ guhyatamaṃ mama
bhāgīrathīm ihāsādya vārāṇasyāṃ mamāspade
nātaḥ puṇyatamaṃ devi nāto guhyatamaṃ kvacit
nātaḥ śubhataraṃ kiṃcinnātaḥ priyataraṃ mama
kṣetraṃ mamedaṃ surasiddhajuṣṭaṃ samprāpya martyaḥ sukṛtaprabhāvāt
khyāto bhavet sarvasurāsurāṇāṃ mṛtaśca yāyāt paramaṃ padaṃ tam
triṃśo adhyāyaḥ
vyāsa uvāca
bhagavan piṅgalaḥ kena gaṇatvaṃ samupāgataḥ
annadatvaṃ ca samprāpto vārāṇasyāṃ mahādyutiḥ
kṣetrapālaḥ kathaṃ jātaḥ priyatvaṃ ca kathaṃ gataḥ
śṛṇu vyāsa yathā lebhe gaṇeśatvaṃ sa piṅgalaḥ
annadatvaṃ ca lokānāṃ sthānaṃ vārāṇasīṃ ca hi
pūrṇabhadrasutaḥ śrīmān āsīdyakṣaḥ pratāpavān
tadāśīstannamaskārastanniṣṭhastatparāyaṇaḥ
āsīnaśca śayānaśca gacchaṃstiṣṭhannanuvrajan
tam evaṃ yuktamanasaṃ pūrṇabhadraḥ pitābravīt
na hi yakṣakulīnānām etadvṛttaṃ bhavatyuta
guhyakā vata yūyaṃ vai svabhāvāt krūracetasaḥ
kravyādāścaiva kiṃbhakṣā hiṃsāśīlāśca putraka
maivaṃ kārṣīrna no vṛttirevaṃ dṛṣṭā mahātmanām
svayambhuvā yathā sṛṣṭā saiva vṛttiḥ praśasyate
harikeśa uvāca
duṣṭā caivāpraśastā ca garhitā sādhubhiḥ sadā
vṛttiḥ svayambhuvā sṛṣṭā tyaktavyā yadi no bhavet
āśramāntarajaṃ karma na kuryurgṛhiṇastataḥ
devatvaṃ no vimārgeyurmānuṣyāṃ jātim eva ca
atha cedvihitaṃ teṣāṃ karma tatprāptisaṃśritam
mamāpi vihitaṃ paśya karmaitannātra saṃśayaḥ
sa evam uktaḥ putreṇa pūrṇabhadraḥ pratāpavān
vārāṇasīṃ samāsādya tapastepe suduścaram
sthāṇubhūto hyanimiṣaḥ śuṣkakāṣṭhopalopamaḥ
saṃniyamyendriyagrāmam avātiṣṭhata niścalaḥ
atha tasyaivam aniśaṃ tatparasya tadāśiṣaḥ
sahasram ekaṃ varṣāṇāṃ divyam abhyativartata
valmīkena samākrānto bhakṣyamāṇaḥ pipīlikaiḥ
udyānaṃ punarevedaṃ draṣṭum icchāmi sarvada
kṣetrasya caiva māhātmyaṃ śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
iti vijñāpito devaḥ pārvatyā bhuvaneśvaraḥ
sarvaṃ pṛṣṭaṃ yathānyāyam ākhyātum upacakrame
nirjagāma ca deveśaḥ pārvatyā saha śaṃkaraḥ
udyānaṃ darśayāmāsa devyā devaḥ pinākadhṛk
virūḍhapuṣpaiḥ paritaḥ priyaṅgubhiḥ supuṣpitaiḥ kaṇṭakitaiśca ketakaiḥ
aśokapuṃnāgavanaiḥ supuṣpitairdvirephamālākulapuṣpasaṃcayaiḥ
kvacit praphullāmbujareṇurūṣitairvihaṃgamaiścārukalapraṇādibhiḥ
vināditaṃ sārasahaṃsanādibhiḥ pramattadātyūharutaiśca valgubhiḥ
kvacicca kāraṇḍavanādanāditaṃ kvacicca mattālikulākulīkṛtam
madākulābhirbhramarāṅganābhirniṣevitaṃ cārusugandhipuṣpam
kvacit supuṣpaiḥ sahakāravṛkṣairlatopagūḍhaistilakaiśca gūḍham
pragītavidyādharasiddhacāraṇaṃ pranṛttanityānugatāpsarogaṇam
prahṛṣṭanānāvidhapakṣisevitaṃ pramattahārītakulopanāditam
niviḍaniculanīlaṃ nīlakaṇṭhābhirāmaṃ
kvacidvilāsālasagāminībhirniṣevitaṃ kiṃpuruṣāṅganābhiḥ
pārāvatadhvaninikūjitacāruśṛṅgairabhraṃkaṣaiḥ sitamanoharacārurūpaiḥ
haṃsānāṃ pakṣapātapracalitakamalasvacchavistīrṇatoyaṃ
sāraṅgaiḥ kvacidupasevitapradeśaṃ
saṃsṛṣṭaiḥ kvacidupaliptakīrṇapuṣpair
puṣpotkarānilavighūrṇitapādapāgram

kvacidañjanacūrṇābhaiḥ kvacidvidrumasaṃnibhaiḥ
kvacit kāñcanasaṃkāśaiḥ puṣpairācitabhūtalam
udyānaṃ darśitaṃ deva śobhayā parayā yutam
idaṃ guhyatamaṃ kṣetraṃ sadā vārāṇasī mama
sarveṣām eva jantūnāṃ heturmokṣasya sarvadā
asmin siddhāḥ sadā devi madīyaṃ vratam āśritāḥ
nānāliṅgadharā nityaṃ mama lokābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ
nānāvṛkṣasamākīrṇe nānāvihagasevite
kamalotpalapuṣpāḍhyaiḥ sarobhiḥ samalaṃkṛte
rocate me sadāvāso yena kāryeṇa tacchṛṇu
vimuktaṃ na mayā yasmānmokṣyate vā kadācana
snānāt saṃsevanādvāpi na mokṣaḥ prāpyate yataḥ
prayāgādapi tīrthāgryādidam eva mahat smṛtam
jaigīṣavyaḥ parāṃ siddhiṃ yo gataḥ sa mahātapāḥ
asya kṣetrasya māhātmyādbhaktyā ca mama bhāvataḥ
jaigīṣavyaguhā śreṣṭhā yogināṃ sthānam iṣyate
dhyāyatastatra māṃ nityaṃ yogāgnirdīpyate bhṛśam
ātmanaścaiva sāyujyam īpsitaṃ sthānam eva ca
kuberaḥ sa mahāyakṣastathā sarvārpitakriyaḥ
kṣetrasaṃsevanāddevi gaṇeśatvam avāpa ha
ihaivārādhya māṃ devi siddhiṃ yāsyatyanuttamām
parāśarasuto yogī ṛṣirvyāso mahātapāḥ
brahmā devarṣibhiḥ sārdhaṃ viṣṇurvāyurdivākaraḥ
anye ca yoginaḥ siddhāśchannarūpā mahāvrate
alarkaśca purīm etāṃ matprasādādavāpsyati
sa caināṃ pūrvavat kṛtvā caturvarṇasamākulām
sphītāṃ janapadākīrṇāṃ bhuktvā ca suciraṃ nṛpaḥ
tataḥ prabhṛti cārvaṅgi ye 'api kṣetranivāsinaḥ
gṛhiṇo liṅgino vāpi madbhaktā matparāyaṇāḥ
iha kṣetre mṛtaḥ so 'api saṃsāraṃ na punarviśet
ye punarnirmamā dhīrāḥ sattvasthā vijitendriyāḥ
vratinaśca nirārambhāḥ sarvato mayi bhāvitāḥ
dehabhedaṃ samāsādya dhīmantaḥ saṅgavarjitāḥ
gatā eva paraṃ mokṣaṃ prasādānmama suvrate
janmāntarasahasreṣu yuñjan yogī yam āpnuyāt
ataḥ parataraṃ nāsti kṣetraṃ guhyam itīśvari
vārāṇasīti bhuvanatrayasārabhūtā
iti skandapurāṇe triṃśattamo adhyāyaḥ
triṃśo adhyāyaḥ
udyānāni tato devaḥ sthānāni ca tathātmanaḥ
ākhyāya himavatputryā vicacāra tadā punaḥ
so 'apaśyata tadā vipraṃ tapyamānaṃ paraṃ tapaḥ
putraṃ śataśalākasya jaigīṣavyaṃ tapodhanam
sa liṅgaṃ devadevasya pratiṣṭhāpyārcayan sadā
japyena vṛṣanādaiśca tapasā bhāvitaḥ śuciḥ
jaigīṣavya mahābuddhe paśya māṃ divyacakṣuṣā
praṇamya śirasā pādāvavadat parayā mudā
jaigīṣavya uvāca
namaḥ pavanavegāya dhyeyāya dhyānibhiḥ sadā
namo gaṇādhipataye namaḥ śāntendriyāya ca
dhāriṇe sarvalokānāṃ sarvalokeśvarāya ca
namo daśārdhavarṇāya saṃsārāpanudāya ca
namaḥ saṃsāraparāya apāraparamāya ca
namaḥ kālakalājñāya sakalāyākalāya ca
namaḥ śramāya śramiṇe śramāpanayanāya ca
namo jñānarasajñāya jñānine 'ajñānahāriṇe
namo jñānānubandhāya ajñānavinivartine
namaḥ sarvānubhāvāya bhāvānugatacetase
namaḥ śamadamādhvāya mṛtyudūtāpahāriṇe
namaḥ śailādināthāya śailādigaṇapāya ca
sa evaṃ stūyamānaśca bhaktyā paramayāpi ca
tuṣṭastutoṣa bhūyo 'asya idaṃ cainam uvāca ha
mahāyogī mahāvīryo yogaiśvaryasamanvitaḥ
prabhāvāccāsya guhyasya kṣetrasya mama śāśvatam
yoge 'aṣṭaguṇam aiśvaryaṃ prāpsyase paramaṃ mahat
bhaviṣyasi dvijaśreṣṭha yogācāryaśca viśrutaḥ
yaścedaṃ tvatkṛtaṃ liṅgaṃ niyamenārcayiṣyati
jaigīṣavya guhāṃ cemāṃ prāpya yo yokṣyate dvijaḥ
māsena pūrvāṃ jātiṃ ca pūrvādhītaṃ ca vetsyati
ekarātraṃ gatiṃ śuddhāṃ dvābhyāṃ tārayate pitRn
trirātreṇa vyatītāṃśca parān sapta ca tārayet
jaigīṣavya uvāca
ato 'ahaṃ nānyadicchāmi yogākṣayyāt paraṃ hi tam
anutsekaṃ tathā kṣāntiṃ śamaṃ damam athāpi ca
tataḥ sa bhagavān devaḥ pārāśaryo mayā saha
tapyato yakṣarājasya kṛtvā hṛdi maheśvaram
atha dṛṣṭvā tripādaṃ ca hrasvabāhūrupādakam
dṛṣṭvovāca tato devaḥ kuberaṃ dīptatejasam
somaṃ paśya mahāsattva māṃ tvaṃ divyena cakṣuṣā
tataḥ sa dṛṣṭvā deveśaṃ sāmbaṃ nandipurassaram
praṇamya karṣitaḥ samyagutthātuṃ na śaśāka ha
abalaṃ taṃ samālakṣya utthāne 'aśaktam īśvaraḥ
uvācottiṣṭha bhadraṃ te balaṃ paurāṇam astu te
tata utthāya jānubhyāṃ kubero hyavatiṣṭhata
pārśvagāṃ caiva netreṇa devīm ālokayan sthitaḥ
mātā lokatrayasyāsya mahāyogabalānvitā
tam evaṃbhūtamanasam īkṣamāṇaṃ ca pārvatīm
viśuṣkaṃ kakṣam ādīptā dadāhāgneḥ śikhā yathā
punaścāsya vināśāya kuberasya śubhānanā
yaśasvī dhārmikaścāyaṃ bhaktastvāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
kautūhalatayā hyeṣa tvāṃ nirīkṣitavān śubhe
eṣo 'asakṛnmāṃ deveśa vīkṣate 'avinayāt prabho
tejasāṃ yo 'aprameyānāṃ kuryānmohena laṅghanam
tām evaṃ krodhatāmrākṣīṃ kruddhāṃ saṃprekṣya śaṃkarīm
uvāca madhuraṃ ślakṣṇaṃ girīndratanayāṃ vacaḥ
bravīmi tvāṃ mahābhāge mā krudho jagato 'araṇi
tvayā sṛṣṭaṃ jagat sarvaṃ prakṛtistvaṃ sureśvari
mātaraṃ caiva putrasya vīkṣamāṇasya śobhane
tuṣṭāsmi mā kṛthāścaivaṃ punastejasvilaṅghanam
yat tvidaṃ te mayā dagdham īkṣamāṇasya locanam
anena cāṅkito loke bhaviṣyasi na saṃśayaḥ
ekākṣipiṅgalo nāmnā khyātaḥ sarvatra pūjitaḥ
evam uktvā tato devī virarāma śubhānanā
tuṣṭāva devaṃ devīṃ ca śirasā prāñjalirnataḥ
namaḥ paṭṭiśahastāya kirīṭavaradhāriṇe
namaḥ sarvāṅgakeśāya dīrghakeśyai namo namaḥ
namaścitraśikhaṇḍinyai namaḥ piṅgajaṭābhṛte
namo jñānāya tanave bhūtādhipataye namaḥ
namastārābhidhāriṇyai siṃhoraskāya vai namaḥ
namaḥ kṛtyai karmaṇe ca ārambhāya samāptaye
namo yajñāya mantrāya dakṣiṇāyai ṛce namaḥ
namaḥ siddhyai tathā puṣṭyai tuṣṭyai kṣāntyai namo namaḥ
mokṣāya muktaye caiva namaḥ kālāya mṛtyave
ya imaṃ paṭhate nityaṃ stavaṃ prātaḥ samutthitaḥ
japaṃśca vipro vaiśyo vā śūdraḥ kṣatriya eva vā
somaśca bhagavāṃstuṣṭo gatim iṣṭāṃ prayacchati
tvattaḥ prasādaṃ satataṃ bhaktiṃ ca tvayi śāśvatīm
ātmanā saha sakhyaṃ ca dadau ātyantikaṃ tadā
gṛhāṇa caitāṃ śibikāṃ narayuktām asaṃginīm
lokān yatheṣṭāllokeśa yām āruhya cariṣyasi
imāṃ caivāśaniṃ divyām apratīghātalakṣaṇām
gṛhāṇāyudham etat te bhaviṣyatyariduḥsaham
tataḥ sa devastuṣṭātmā mālāṃ svīyām aninditām
ābabaddhāsya śirasi bhāskarākāravarcasam
kuśeśayānāṃ phullānāṃ sragdāma ca manoramam
ābabaddhāsya kaṇṭhe vai prīyamāṇa umāpatiḥ
prakāmaṃ darśanaṃ cāsya dattvā caiva dhaneśatām
śṛṇuyācchrāvayedvāpi nityaṃ viprān samāhitaḥ
atha devī mahābhāgā sahitā śambhunā tadā
saṃcintya pañcacūḍāstu tapantyo 'apsarasaḥ śubhāḥ

hariḥ śaraṃ sa sandhāya viśiraskam athākarot
śaraṃ cāparam ādāya vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān
palāyamānaṃ taṃ yajñaṃ sasāra mṛgarūpiṇam
nakṣatrasamatāṃ yātuṃ dvābaddhaṃ vītamabhyagāt
evaṃ te nikṛtā vyāsa gaṇaiḥ kāltyā tathaiva ca

tān prapannāṃstadā sarvān devān samunilokapān

prasādayitum avyagrā duḥkhaśokasamanvitāḥ
tataste nātidūre tu sāmbaṃ sagaṇam īśvaram

devā ūcuḥ

tvayā sṛṣṭam idaṃ viśvaṃ yajño devāśca yajñahan
prasīda mā krudho 'asmākaṃ mā naḥ kṛtvā vināśaya
uvāca prahasan vākyaṃ sarvātmā sarvabhāvanaḥ
kruddhe hi mayi yuṣmākaṃ na syājjīvaṃ kṣaṇāntare
evam uktvā tadā devaḥ surāṇāṃ hitakāmyayā
prāveśayat surān sarvāṃstatastān yogamāyayā
te praviṣṭāstadā deham īśvarasya mahātmanaḥ
te paribhramya tāllokān kṛtsnān sarve bhayānvitāḥ
pañcākṣaṃ gaṇapaṃ vīraṃ tatrāpaśyan samāgatāḥ
tena te suraśārdūlāḥ sarve hi ūrdhvam atandritāḥ
ākṣiptāstanmuhūrtena lokam anyam upāgatāḥ
apaśyaṃste mahābhāgā nagaraṃ sūryasannibham
sphāṭikenātimahatā prākāreṇābhisaṃvṛtam
śṛṅgaiśca vividhiścitrairmaṇihemojjvalaiḥ śubhaiḥ
saptayojanakoṭīkaṃ samantānnagaraṃ śubham
rājatenāvṛtaṃ divyaṃ prākāreṇenduvarcasā
tasya madhye 'aparaṃ cordhvaṃ ṣaṭkoṭyā vistṛtaṃ puram
jāmbūnadamayenaiva prākāreṇa susaṃvṛtam
tasya madhye tataścānyat pañcakoṭīpramāṇataḥ
indranīlopalenaiva prākāreṇa samāvṛtam
caturyojanakoṭīkaṃ vistārāyāmataḥ samam
vaidūryopalayuktena prākāreṇābhisaṃvṛtam
sarvaratnavicitreṇa prākāreṇābhisaṃvṛtam
teṣāṃ madhye janapadāḥ sarvaduḥkhavivarjitāḥ
kṣutpisāvinirmuktā rogaśokavivarjitāḥ
amarā jarayā tyaktā nityaṃ muditamānasāḥ
dīrghikābhirvicitrābhirvāpībhiścāpyalaṃkṛtāḥ
vṛkṣairnānāvidhaiścitraiḥ sadā puṣpaphalopagaiḥ
sarvabhakṣān prasūyante vṛkṣāstatrāpare śubhāḥ
apare cāpyalaṃkārān sarvavāsāṃsi cāpare
sarvabhāvāṃstathā cānye madhu cāmākṣikaṃ śubham
apare kṣīriṇastatra vṛkṣā vyāsa mahāprabhāḥ
kṣīraṃ kṣaranti te nityaṃ sarve gavyaṃ samanvitāḥ
sarvā maṇimayī bhūmiḥ śubhā kāñcanavālukā
tasya madhye puraṃ cānyaddvikoṭīvistṛtaṃ śubham
padmarāgamayenaiva prākāreṇa pariṣkṛtam
īdṛśāni purāṇi sma vyatikramya surāstataḥ
koṭīyojanavistīrṇaṃ samantādvahnināvṛtam
saṃvartakānalākāraṃ durnirīkṣyaṃ puraṃ mahat
advāraṃ dadṛśurdivyam anantaṃ te surottamāḥ
dṛṣṭvā jagmuḥ puraṃ caiva vismayaṃ bhayam eva ca
tān bhītavadanān vyāsa vepamānān sureśvarān
pañcākṣo gaṇapaḥ prāha mā bhīrbhavatu vaḥ surāḥ
idaṃ tat sumahadghoraṃ puraṃ ghorānalāvṛtam
draṣṭvyaṃ vo mahātmano yatkṛte cāgatāstviha
evam uktvā sa pañcākṣaḥ śūlenānalavarcasā
paśyatāṃ surasaṃghānāṃ dvāraṃ cakre mahābalaḥ
te praviṣṭā mahātmānaḥ pañcākṣasahitāḥ surāḥ
divyaṃ dadṛśire pūrṇaṃ siṃhānāṃ tat puraṃ mahat
merumandarakalpānāṃ nakhadaṃṣṭrāvatāṃ tathā
ghorāṇām agnivarṇānāṃ kruddhānām atitejasām
teṣām ekastadā siṃhaśchittvā bandhanam ūrjitaḥ
viṣaṇṇavadanāḥ sarve pañcākṣaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ
pañcākṣa uvāca
na bhetavyaṃ surā devaṃ darśayāmyadhunā hi vaḥ
ityuktā dadṛśuḥ śarvaṃ sahasā te sahomayā
na caiva tat puraṃ vyāsa na siṃhaṃ nāpi kiṃcana
vepamānā bhayeneśaṃ śaraṇaṃ paryupāgatāḥ
tāñcharaṇyaḥ sa bhagavānuvāca prahasaṃstadā
dṛṣṭā hi vo mama krodhāḥ siṃharūpā bhayānakāḥ
ekena teṣāṃ raudreṇa yūyaṃ sarve 'api tarjitāḥ
yadi sarvānahaṃ krodhādvisṛjeyaṃ kadācana
na bhaveta na sandehaḥ sarve yūyaṃ kṣaṇāntare
iyaṃ tu devī yuṣmākaṃ kupitā parvatātmajā
etāṃ prasādayata vai nāhaṃ kupyāmi vaḥ surāḥ
devī devīṃ mukhādghorāṃ sasṛje bhayavardhanīm
daṃṣṭrākarālavadanāṃ bahupādakarāṅgulim
dhanuḥparaśukhaḍgogracakraśūleṣudhāriṇīm
jvalardakasahasrāṃśutejasaṃ viśvarūpiṇīm
daśayojanasāhasrastasyā dehaḥ pramāṇataḥ
tayābhibhūtāste devā vadhyamānāśca sarvaśaḥ
na śekuḥ purataḥ sthātuṃ vyāghrānmṛgagaṇā iva
tato vyathitacittāste kālakarṇībhayāt surāḥ
bhasmarāśiṃ sthitaṃ pārśve devasya viviśurbhayāt
tān dṛṣṭvā bhasmakūṭaṃ tu praviṣṭāñcharaṇārthinaḥ
surān bhasmaviliptāṅgān devī devīṃ nyaṣedhayat
kālakarṇi nivartasva mā vadhīḥ surasattamān
ete pāśupatībhūtā bhasmanā digdhamūrtayaḥ
etat paśupatiproktaṃ vrataṃ pāśupataṃ purā
ete bhagavato vaśyam anugrāhyāḥ surottamāḥ
bhasma yena praviṣṭāstu tasmānmaitān vināśaya
raudrāḥ paśava ete hi praveśādbhasmaso 'adhunā
jātāśca gaṇapāḥ sarve hantavyā na tvayeśvari
naiṣāṃ mṛtyuḥ prabhavati śaṅkarārpitacetasām
mayā hyetadvrataṃ śarvaṃ caritaṃ sārvakāmikam
ityuktā kālakarṇī tu devyā bhairavarūpiṇī
kālakarṇīṃ nivṛttāṃ tu dṛṣṭvā te 'api surāstataḥ
śāntaṃ ca bhayam atyugraṃ tuṣṭuvurhimavatsutām
devā ūcuḥ
haravaramahiṣīṃ mahādevapatnīṃ priyāṃ tryambakasyāmbikāṃ
vācam ekākṣarāṃ lokasaṃhārakartrīmumāṃ devadevasya
pātnīṃ śubhāṃ śaṃkhakundenduhārāmbugaurogradaṃṣṭrāṃ
jayām āhaverdurnirīkṣyām acintyogradṛṣṭiṃ viśālekṣaṇāṃ
pītakośeyavastrāṃ mahāśūlaghaṇṭāpatākādhvajāṃ divyagandhājyadhūpapriyāṃ
kāladaṇḍāsicarmograhastāṃ vapāśoṇitāntravasāpūrṇabhāṇḍāṃ
diśāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ cārucāmīkarābaddhapaṭṭāṃ
yugāntānalābhekṣaṇām aṭṭahāsān sṛjantīṃ
yathākāmakartrīm anaṅgāyudhāvikṣatāṃ śūrasenāṃ nadīṃ viśrutāṃ
mandarāvāsanityāṃ diviṣṭhāṃ prapadyāmahe
kānasīṣṭim
asuramahiṣadaraṇīṃ dāraṇīṃ sundubheḥ sundamārīṃ niśumbhasya
mṛtyuṃ vibhāṃ somamūryāgnibhāsāṃ sṛjatkāntim iṣṭapradāṃ
śokaduḥkhārtihartrīṃ viśekām aghorāṃ ghanām antakasyāntakartrīṃ
rājarājñīṃ manojñāṃ karālāṃ kṣapāṃ daṇḍanītiṃ sthitisiddhim
iṣṭāṃ śubhāṃ kālarātrīm
aparṇāṃ samādhiṃ śaraṇyāṃ nagendrādhivāsapriyāṃ kṣīrodanityāṃ śubhām
mahākiṃkiṇīkāṃ prakīrṇordhvakeśīṃ pradīptāgnisandhyābhrarāgatviṣam
baddhagodhāṅgulitrāṃ trinetrāṃ jaṭākeśaraktāmbujābaddhamālāṃ viśalyām
anaṅgārinetrolkajāṃ hemamālānibaddhasrajāṃ dīrghaveṇīṃ suveṇīm
yaśaḥkīrtiyuktāṃ mayūrāṅgajābaddhacitradhvajāṃ rājasāṃ śāntikartrīm
prapadye 'aham ekāṃ sadā
bhujaṅgaśatakṛtāṅgadāṃ mahādānavaprāṇaśauṇḍām
citābhasmarūkṣāṅgakeśīṃ mahājānulambodarāṃ sarpayajñopavītarddhavaktroddhṛtākṣārdhapādārdrahastāvataṃsām
gītahāsyapralāpapramodapriyāṃ jāpyahomopavāsādavāsāpravāsādhivāsātiriktām
mahāyogavijñātasārānusārograsārāṃ dhṛtim
jyānughaṇṭāvabaddhograśabdāṃ mahāmeghavajraprapātodadhiprakyatīvrograghoṣām
kriyāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ ca
dīkṣāṃ virūpākṣabhāryāṃ harasyārdhadehādhivāsāṃ prapadye mukholykodbhavāṃ devīm
ādyāṃ parāṃ pārvatīṃ sarvavidyādhidevīṃ gatiṃ yamaniyamadamātmabhūtām
pitRṇāṃ ca kanyāṃ śubhāṃ parvatendrātmajāṃ dakṣayajñāntakartrīm
viṣṇukeśāpahartrīṃ mahāsiṃhayuktātivāhāṃ mahābhairavāṃ bhīṣitām
skandacandrāraṇīṃ mātaraṃ hastivaktrasya cāgryāṃ viśākhasya
janmāraṇīṃ nandino naigameṣasya cotpādanīṃ sarvalokasya
cādyāraṇīṃ pūjyāṃ mātaraṃ yogināṃ yoginīṃ dhyāyamānāṃ dhṛtim
devaviprairmahāyogatarkairagamyāṃ viśiṣṭeṣṭaśiṣṭādhivāsāṃ ca
lakṣmīṃ narībhūrbhuvaḥsvarjanassatyavairājamāhātmyalokāraṇīm
kāraṇīm indriyāṇām ahaṅkāratanmātrakartrīṃ tamassatvarāgapravṛttim
parāṃ ca pravṛttiṃ maheśasya śaktiṃ tathā cetanāṃ sarvavijñanacintyām
prapadyāma devīm umāṃ mātaraṃ diśa
tvaṃ sukhaṃ mātarasmāsu tuṣṭā
mahādevapatnīṃ śubhāṃ yāṃ vayaṃ cintyām aikayā saṃvidā dhyāyamānāḥ sadā
dāruṇaṃ cāpi sarvaṃ kṛtaṃ yat tvayā tacca no jātikoṭīsahasreṣu
pūrvaṃ kṛtaṃ yat kariṣyāma yat kurma tat sarvam evaṃ ca dadyāśca
naḥ sarvam arthaṃ sakāmaṃ tathārogyam ūrjāṃ śriyaṃ jñānavijñānanedhāstathā
dhāraṇāṃ tarkam ūhām apohaṃ dhṛtiṃ cārthabhāvaṃ gatiṃ caiva divyāṃ tathā
dharmanityatvam etāṃśca ye cāpyato 'anye guṇāstāṃśca
sarvāñjuṣasvādya devi tubhyaṃ namaḥ
evaṃ sā saṃstutā devī devairhṛṣṭena cetasā
tryambakānugrahāccaiva devāṃstuṣṭābravīdidam
gacchadhvaṃ vijvarāḥ sarve tuṣṭāhaṃ vo na saṃśayaḥ
maivaṃ kārṣṭa punardevā mā vināśo hi vo bhavet
prakṛtisthān surān sarvāṃścakāra suraśatruhā
uvāca caitān deveśo gacchadhvaṃ vigatajvarāḥ
yajñaścaiva yadā kṛtyaṃ tadāyaṃ bhavitā hi vaḥ
saśirasko diteḥ putrā mantreṇānena sandhitaḥ
dadau ātharvaṇaṃ devaḥ provācedaṃ ca susvaram
nakṣatrasamatāṃ yātu yajño 'ayaṃ surasattamāḥ
bhadrakālī hariścaiva gaṇāśceme mahābalāḥ
sarve bhadrā bhaviṣyanti yuṣmākam amarāḥ sadā
evam uktā bhagavatā devāste brahmāṇā saha
śirobhiḥ praṇatāḥ sarve śarvam ūcuridaṃ vacaḥ
bhāgānāṃ sarvayajñeṣu tubhyaṃ sarvaṃ dadāmahe
cakāra rūpaṃ paramaṃ sarvadevamayaṃ śubham
svātmānaṃ te tadā devā hyapaśyanta maheśvare
śirobāhūrupādeṣu vastihastodarādiṣu
avasthitān mahātmāno munīṃścaiva tapodhanān
sa tadrūpaṃ tadā kṛtvā devān provāca śaṃkaraḥ
sarve yūyaṃ mahātmāno maccharīrasamudbhavāḥ
yuṣmākaṃ ca śarīrāṇi manmayāni prapaśyata
ātmānaṃ cāpyapaśyanta vismayāpannacetasaḥ
evaṃ sa teṣāṃ deveśo darśayitvātmano balam
uvāca suraśārdūlān dṛṣṭā hyetā vibhūtayaḥ
yo yāṃ pūjayate mūrtiṃ bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ
tasya tāṃ mūrtim āsthāya pūjāṃ gṛhṇāmyahaṃ surāḥ
na bhāgadheyaiḥ kṛtyaṃ me bhāgadheyāni vaḥ surāḥ
sarvāṇyeva dadāmyadya yāta sarve gatajvarāḥ
devā ūcuḥ
sādhayitvā caruṃ caiva bhojayedbrāhmaṇāñchuciḥ
parityakṣyati yaścātra kaścit prāṇān narottamaḥ
jagāma bhagavāñcharvaḥ somo gaṇaśatirvṛtaḥ
devāpi rājñā sahitāstasmiṃsthāne yathāsukham
tasthurbrahmā ca viṣṇuśca jagmaturdevapṛṣṭhataḥ
sa gatvā stokam adhvānam ubhābhyāṃ sahitaḥ prabhuḥ
nātidūre tataḥ prāha tiṣṭha viṣṇo mahābala
nirīkṣamāṇo deveśaṃ deśastasmādabhūdasau
kubjāmraka iti khyāto viṣṇoḥ kṣetraṃ samṛddhimat
nātidūraṃ tato gatvā bhūvo devaḥ pitāmaham
pradakṣiṇaṃ samāvṛtya praṇamya prayayau tataḥ
āvarttaḥ svaśarīrasya prakṛtaḥ puṇyakarmaṇā
aśvamedhaphalaṃ tatra snātaḥ prāpnoti mānavaḥ
sādhayitvā caruṃ cātra bhojayitvā tathā dvijān
tato 'abhyetya suraiḥ sārrdhaṃ brahmā viṣṇupuraḥsaraiḥ
sa liṅgaṃ tatra saṃsthāpya pūjāṃ kṛtvātibhāsvaraṃ
taṃ prayāntaṃ tadā dakṣo brahmāṇam idam ūcivān
pitāmaha uvāca
prasādaya maheṣvāsaṃ śarvam ugraṃ kapardinam
tato yajñasamāptiṃ ca lokāṃśca prāpsyase 'avyayān
tasya saṃvatsaraśate pūrṇe divye prajāpateḥ
tato dṛṣṭvā mahādevī vāyubhakṣam avasthitam
liṅge paramayā bhaktyā pūjayantaṃ maheśvaram
uvāca hṛṣitā devī devaṃ sarvasurārcitam
kṛtāñjalipuṭā vyāsa sarvadevapatiṃ patim
kṣudro 'ayaṃ duṣṭacetāśca stabdho mānī ca durmatiḥ
diṣṭyā tvayā vinikṛtastvām eva śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
anujñātā mayā subhru tvam evāsya varaṃ diśa
ūcatuḥ paśya dakṣāvāṃ tuṣṭau divyena cakṣuṣā
kāmarūpadharaḥ śrīmān gaṇeśaśca bhavasva me
akṣayaścāmaraścaiva duḥkhaśokavivarjitaḥ
śṛṇuṣva bhūyaḥ kiṃ cānyat prayacchatu maheśvaraḥ
prāñjaliḥ praṇato bhūtvā idam āha mahāmatiḥ
dakṣa uvāca
bhaktānām aśubhaharaṃ pinākapāṇiṃ taṃ devaṃ śaraṇagatā vayaṃ sabhāryam
yo 'ajñānādasuratayātimānamohānnāsmābhiḥ saha khalu pūjito 'adriputryā
yaḥ śāpaṃ mama ruṣito dadau sureśastaṃ devaṃ śaraṇagatā vayaṃ sabhāryam
yaḥ sraṣṭā suragaṇayakṣarākṣasānāṃ siddhānāṃ ditisutadānavendranRṇām
bhūtānāṃ paśumṛgapakṣipattagānāṃ taṃ devaṃ śaraṇagatā vayaṃ sabhāryam
yaḥ kodhānmahadasṛjadgaṇeśvareśaṃ siṃhendraṃ harim amitaprabhāvarūpam
patnīṃ cāpyabhitaguṇaprabhāvayuktāṃ taṃ devaṃ śaraṇagatā vayaṃ sabhāryam
yo devān sahavaruṇān savittagopān sabrahmān saśatamakhān saviṣṇuvāyūn
indrāgryān samunimahāyudhān vijigye taṃ devaṃ śaraṇagatā vayaṃ sabhāryam
yat kiṃcit tvayi kaluṣaṃ kṛtaṃ ca duṣṭaṃ hyajñānādapi ca hi rāgadoṣamohāt
tat sarvaṃ mama saha bhāryayādya śarvo viśvātmā kṣamatu mahānubhāvabhāvāt
tata evaṃ sa deveśaṃ stutvā sāsrāvilekṣaṇaḥ
prasārya bāhū sarveṇa śarīreṇāpatadbhuvi
taṃ prapannaṃ tadā devo dakṣaṃ sāsrāvilekṣaṇam
tasyāśrūṇyapatan bhūmau bindubhūtāni tatra vai
tām uvāca tato devo nadīṃ vai puṇyalakṣaṇām
arjunādaśrubindostvaṃ yasmāddevi viniḥsṛtā
tasmāt khyātā bhavitrī tvam arjunā nāmataḥ śubhā
trirātropoṣito yaśca caruṃ kṛtvā nivedya ca
gavāṃ lokaṃ mahātejā na ca tasmāt patiṣyati
evaṃ sa sṛṣṭvā saritaṃ kṛtvā caivāpyanugraham
tam āśvāsya sureśastu dakṣaṃ prāha nṛpaṃ tadā
brūhi kiṃ te punaḥ sādho dadāni varam īpsitam
atha dakṣastadovāca praṇamya śubhayā girā
bhūya bhūyaḥ samāśvasya nirīkṣya ca punaḥ punaḥ
dakṣa uvāca
sthānaṃ pavitraṃ puṇyaṃ ca vara eṣo 'astu me śiva
kṛtavatyau mahābhāge tvaṃ ca dakṣo yataḥ sthitaḥ
tīrthaṃ caiva mahat puṇyaṃ gaṅgāsāgarasannibham
nātra pāpā na ca śaḥtā nāstikā na ca māninaḥ
atrābhigamya snātvā ca caruṃ kṛtvā tathaiva ca
kālīṃ cāsmai dadau prītyā bhāryāṃ sarvaguṇoditām
varāṃśca vipulān divyān dvīpaṃ cāpi ghṛtodakam
vyāsa uvāca
sā devīmukhajā ghorā divyā devabhayaṃkarī
stutā yadā bhagavatī praṇataiḥ surasattamaiḥ
tadāsya sāmbikā prāha brūhi kiṃ karavāṇyaham
tato brahmā mahādevīṃ praṇamya bahumānataḥ
sarvaprāṇabṛtāṃ devīṃ prāṇāpaharaṇe śubhām
sāpi tatkāryakaraṇe niyuktā brahmaṇā svayam
ūrdhvabāhuḥ sadeveśā sadodyuktā tvayā mayā
bhadreśvarapratiṣṭhāṃ ca dakṣānugraham eva ca
paṭhedvā śṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayīta dvijānapi
suragurumakhakālaṃ saptalokādhipālaṃ śaraṇam upagato 'ahaṃ śaṃkaraṃ śarmahetoḥ
dakṣayajñapramathane dvātriṃśo 'adhyāyaḥ
trayastriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
himavantaṃ giriṃ prāpya vāyvāhārau babhūvatuḥ
varṣāṇāṃ tu sahasrāṇi daśa dvādaśa caiva tau
māṇuṣāni tato bhūyaḥ śākāhārau babhūvatuḥ
tāṃstau maheśvarān dṛṣṭvā bahūn vai sadṛśaprabhān
parasparam amanyetāṃ ko nveṣām īśvaro bhavet
tau tadā vīkṣya saṃmantrya smṛtvā caiva punaḥ punaḥ
madhye maheśvaraṃ teṣāṃ menāte tejasāṃ nidhim
śirasorañjalī kṛtvā tuṣṭuvāte 'amitaujasau
namastrailokyanāthāya digvāsāyāmṛtātmane
caturmukhāya śuddhāya jālāntaravicāriṇe
ūrdhvaliṅgāya devāya madanāyāmadāya ca
namo hiraṇyavarṇāya sūryākṣāya tathaiva ca
namaste naikapādāya ekākṣāya namo namaḥ
namaḥ sahasraghaṇṭāya sahasrākṣāya vai namaḥ
namaḥ sahasraśīrṣāya saṃvartāya namo namaḥ
namo 'astu nārīrūpāya subhagāya namo namaḥ
āvayorīpsitān kāmān vidhatsva bhuvaneśvara
sarvakāmaiḥ sa sampanno yatheṣṭāṃ gatim āpnuyāt
atha devastu tān sarvānanayat prakṛtiṃ gaṇān
nandinaṃ caiva devīṃ ca svayaṃ cātmānam apyuta
uvāca caitau tuṣṭo 'asmi gṛhyatām īpsito varaḥ
devaūcatuḥ
idaṃ ca guhyaṃ sthānaṃ nau tapasātīva bhāvitam
pañceṣukṣepamātraṃ vai mṛgo 'atra gaṇapo bhavet
vāhanatvaṃ mamāsādya lokān sandhārayiṣyathaḥ
tayā varṣasahasreṇa tapasā toṣito bhavaḥ
jagāma darśanaṃ vyāsa varado 'asmīti cābravīt
sā vavre putram atulaṃ sarvaprāṇabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
putrāṃścānyān mahāsattvān yajñiyān surasattamān
tathā duhitRścānyāśca jagaddhartrīḥ suśobhanāḥ
tataḥ sarvaṃ dadau devo hyadṛśyatvaṃ jagāma ca
sarvabhūtāgrajaṃ putraṃ vṛṣabhaṃ samasūyata
ekādaśa tathā rudrān vṛṣabhasyānujāñchubhān
sapta kanyāśca tā gā vai jagaddhātrī prasūyata
vṛṣabhaḥ sa tu saṃgatya nityaṃ prātaḥ kṛtāhnikaḥ
vanaṃ siddhagaṇāvāsaṃ yatra sā hyamṛtodbhavā
dūrvāmṛtarasā divyā chinnadagdhaprasehaṇī
sa kadrācidvane tasmiṃścaraṃstṛptastṛḍarditaḥ
jagāma sāgaraṃ pātuṃ vṛṣarāṭ surabhīsutaḥ
so 'avagāhya mahāgrāsaḥ sāgarasya tadā mahat
madhyaṃ vyādāya vadanaṃ sajhaṣaṃ satimiṃgalam
tasmin pibati daityendrāḥ sannaddhāḥ sāsimārgaṇāḥ
sadhanuṣpāṇayaḥ sarve sahasrāṇi caturdaśa
niṣpetuḥ śakrasaṃkāśā yamakālānalopamāḥ
mayaputrā mahāsatvā vṛṣabhaṃ prati vegitāḥ
tāṃstathā ruṣitān daityān sāsimudgaratomarān
tān pītān pīyamānāṃśca dṛṣṭvā hyarṇavavāsinaḥ
vitresuḥ sahasā sarve vineduścāpi duḥkhitāḥ
tataḥ samudro bhagavān pīyamānaḥ suduḥkhitaḥ
vaḍavāmukham āgatya saṃvartaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayau
sa cānalaḥ susaṃrabdho dattvā tasya mahābalaḥ
abhayaṃ vṛṣam āgatya provācedaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ
sarvabhūtaśaraṇyo 'ayaṃ daityānāṃ cālayaḥ śubhaḥ
nainaṃ hīnaṃ bhavānadbhiḥ kartum arhati vīryavān
vṛṣabha uvāca
tanme darśaya havyeśa pibāmyenaṃ tavāgrataḥ
evam uktvā vṛṣendrastu vaḍavāmukhavāsinam
saṃrambhāt sāgaraṃ pātuṃ niḥśeṣam upacakrame
ahaṃ tvāṃ vārayiṣyāmi surabhīsuta katthana
yat pītaṃ chardayāmāsa tat toyaṃ dānavairvinā
visṛjyovāca gaccheti na tvāṃ hanmi vṛṣeśvara
tathāpyahaṃ na garjāmi garjitaiḥ kiṃ balīyasām
visṛjya vṛṣabhaṃ vahnirāśu yātaḥ svam ālayam
vṛṣabho 'api jagāmaiva duḥkhaśokābhisaṃvṛtaḥ
so 'avamānena tejasvī mahokṣaḥ surabhīsutaḥ
abalo 'ahaṃ balī vahniryenāhaṃ nikṛtastathā
jīviteśena bhūtvā ca nāhaṃ prāṇairviyojitaḥ
adya prāṇānahaṃ tyakṣye niyato vratam āthitaḥ
śatruṇā nigṛhītasya durbalasya durātmanaḥ
jīvitānmaraṇaṃ manye viśiṣṭaṃ jīvitena kim
sa evaṃ cintayannukṣā vācaṃ śuśrāva khāc chubhām
sa sraṣṭā sarvabhūtānāṃ brahmādīnāṃ na saṃśayaḥ
sa te duḥkham idaṃ sarvaṃ vyapaneṣyati bho vṛṣa
etacchrutvā mahātejāḥ sādhyasya sumahātmanaḥ
himavantaṃ giriṃ prāpya tatāpa vipulaṃ tapaḥ
tasya vartṣasahasreṇa tatparasya tadāśiṣaḥ
bhagavān sarvabhūteśaḥ sāmbaḥ sagaṇa ūcivān
iṣṭān brūhi varān vatsa dāsye tān subahūnapi
tataḥ sa devaṃ saṃdṛśya sāmbaṃ sagaṇam īśvaram
praṇamya śirasā pādau prāñjaliḥ susamāhitaḥ
bhūyo bhūyo nirīkṣyainaṃ praṇamya ca punaḥ punaḥ
balaṃ cānuttamaṃ deva yogaiśvaryaṃ tathākṣayam
tvadīyo vāhanaścāham agninaivaṃ vimānitaḥ
saṃvartakānalaṃ caiva vaḍavāmukhavāsinam
draṣṭum icchāmi deveśa nigṛhītaṃ tvayāvyaya
vāmaṃ pārśvaṃ tathā mṛjya rudram ekaṃ sasarja ha
kirīṭamālinaṃ tryakṣaṃ kuṇḍalāṅgadabhūṣaṇam
baddhagodhāṅgulitraṃ ca khaṅgadivyāstradhāriṇam
jagāma sāgaraṃ vegāddadarśa ca hutāśanam
saṃvarttakānalaṃ baddhvā devapārśvam upānayat
vyāsa uvāca
etadicchāmi vijñātuṃ vada tvaṃ vadatāṃ vara
gaṇapa uvāca
svāmī sarvasya jagato devaścandrārdhabūṣaṇaḥ
ājñāpayati vahne tvāṃ vṛṣam enaṃ prasādaya
praṇato 'asmīti taṃ brūhi vṛṣabhaṃ sasuhṛjjanaḥ
uvāca na tisaṃhṛṣṭastvidaṃ vacanam arthavat
yadi māṃ vakṣyati punaḥ kariṣye 'ahaṃ tatastathā
gaṇeśvara uvāca
bāliśā vata ye prājñā balajñānabahiṣkṛtāḥ
ta evam uktā gacchanti yathā māṃ tvaṃ prabhāṣase
sakṛdājñā balavatāṃ sakṛt prabhavatām api
dūtaścāpi sa vai śreṣṭho yo bhavedarthasādhakaḥ
visphurantaṃ mahāpāśairneṣyāmi dyubhṛto 'antikam
sa evam uktastejasvī krodhadīptānalekṣaṇaḥ
gaṇapaṃ prati dudrāva tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
tāḍayāmāsa balavān sa prajajvāla vegavān
jvalantaṃ taṃ tadābhyāsam āgataṃ krodhamūrcchitam
visphurantaṃ mahāvahniṃ gaṇapaḥ krodhamūrcchitaḥ
taṃ baddhaṃ pāśavaryeṇa patitaṃ vīkṣya caiva hi
tasya putrasuhṛdvargā vividhāyudhapāṇayaḥ
dudruvurgaṇapaṃ kruddhāḥ śataśo 'atha sahasraśaḥ
upaninye harāyāśu paśuṃ medhyam ivādhvare
tam ānītaṃ mahādevaḥ samprekṣyārṇavabhojanam
uvāca vṛṣabhaṃ brūhi kim asya kriyatām iti
sa taṃ kṛpaṇam ālakṣya mahokṣā dīnacetasam
praṇamya śirasā pādāvidam āha kṛtāñjaliḥ
dṛṣṭam etat tava vibho māhātmyaṃ sadasatpate
dṛṣṭo 'ayaṃ kṛpaṇaścāpi hyabalaśca mahābala
visṛjyatāṃ suraśreṣṭha hata eṣa na saṃśayaḥ
putrā hyasya hatāḥ sarve suhṛdaścaiva sarvaśaḥ
etadvaco maheśo vai vṛṣabhasyāmibhāṣitam
śrutvā tuṣṭaḥ prahasyainaṃ dahanaṃ vyasṛjat tadā
gaṇeśvarapatiṃ kṛtvā dvīpam asmai dadat prabhuḥ
jāmbūnadamayaiḥ śubhraiḥ sarvakāmasamanvitaiḥ
tasmin kāle tadā devyāḥ sarve brahmapuraḥsarāḥ
tvayā hyadhyāsitaḥ pūrvaṃ nādenāpūrayadbalī
vegena ca diśaḥ sarvā vimānaiḥ saha bhūtapa
bhrāmayaṃstridaśān nādādgagane saṃcacāra ha
tvaṃ no gatiśca deveśa śaraṇaṃ caiva bhūtapa
sadā bhayābhibhūtānāṃ tvaṃ trātā sarvaśaḥ prabho
yathā bhayaṃ na bhavati yathā svasthāśca nityaśaḥ
asṛjadvaradānācca gaṇeśaṃ cārukuṇḍalam
ākarṇāddāritāsyaṃ ca mahākāyaṃ mahābalam
mahāparighabāhuṃ ca vajrasaṃhananaṃ dṛḍham
mahādaṃṣṭraṃ mahoraskaṃ mahākhaḍgadhanurdharam
grahanakṣatracitreṇa taḍitsūryāvabhāsitā
uttarīyeṇa viyatā bhāsvantaṃ merukūṭavat
abravīt sarvadevānāṃ samakṣaṃ taṃ prabhākaram
prabhākara mayājñaptastvaṃ devānāṃ guṇākara
paramaiśvaryasaṃyukto vṛṣavegaṃ nivāraya
jyotsnā bhavitrī patnī te tathā caivājarāmaraḥ
tatastaṃ devatāḥ sarvāḥ praṇamya brahmaṇā saha
jagmuḥ svāni kṣayāni sma devo 'api vṛṣavān babhau
cakṣuṣī candrasūryau ca brahmā mūrdhānam āśritaḥ
jihvāyāṃ tasya varuṇo vāyurantaścaraḥ svayam
pādān viṣṇurbhagaścaiva pūṣā śakraśca saṃsthitāḥ
jaṃghāḥ śeṣāstathā divyā ūrūścaiva samāśritāḥ
rudrāḥ karṇau ca nāsāṃ ca grīvoṣṭhau hanum eva ca
āyudhāni khurāstasya cakravajrau ca śṛṅgayoḥ
apāne ca svayaṃ mitraḥ pucchaṃ dānāni sarvaśaḥ
asthīni parvatāḥ sarve purīṣaṃ śrīrabhūcchubhā
mūtraṃ cāsyābhavaddivyam amṛtaṃ vyāsa pāvanam
romāṇi ṛṣayaḥ sarve nakṣatrāṇi ca sarvaśaḥ
grahāstasyābhavan vyāsa sandhayaḥ śubhadarśanāḥ
iṣṭayo vedayajñāśca mantrāḥ stotrāḥ phalāni ca
abhavaṃstasya māṃsāni rudhiraṃ saridarṇavāḥ
mantrabhūtāśca paśavaḥ sakṛt snāyuśca vīrudhaḥ
ballyo 'atha vṛkṣagulmāśca tathaivānye nagāḥ śubhāḥ
nāgāstasyābhavan nāḍyo vasavaḥ śukrasaṃcayaḥ
āmapakvāśayau tasya tau devāvaśvinau smṛtau
meghāstasyābhavaṃstvak ca taḍinmālā
mānuṣā mātaraścaiva bhūtāni vividhāni ca
romakūpāṇi tasyāsan vṛṣabhasya mahātmanaḥ
evaṃ sa bhagavān devaḥ paramaiśvaryasaṃyutaḥ
mahātyam akhilaṃ caiva śṛṇuyādvā paṭheta vā
nityaṃ śuciradīnātmā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
mṛtaśca kāle kāle vā rudralokam avāpnuyāt
nedaṃ śaṭhāya dātavyaṃ śrāvyaṃ vāpi kathaṃcana
na nāstikāya duṣṭāya tathā vā pāpakarmaṇe
idaṃ putraya śiṣyāya dhārmikāya mahātmane
deyaṃ śrāvyaṃ ca śucaye guhyam etat sanātanam
vṛṣotpattimāhātmyaṃ nāma trayastriṃśo 'adhyāyaḥ
catustriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
vṛṣavāhaḥ samabhavadyathā te kathitaṃ mayā
vyāsa uvāca
kathaṃ bhagavatī devī kṛṣṇā gauratvam āgatā
kāraṇaṃ tatra kiṃ cāpi hyetadicchāmi veditum
āsīnau mandaraprasthe umākāmāṅganāśanau
remāte pramathaiḥ sārdhaṃ nānārūpadharaistadā
atha devena tatrasthā krīḍatā sā kathāntare
kṛṣṇetyuktā bhagavatī sā cukopa manasvinī
kupitāṃ tāṃ mahādevaḥ pariṣvajya mahādyutiḥ
uvācāsakṛdavyagraḥ sāntvayan madhuraṃ vacaḥ
hāsyaṃ prakṛtam etanme kṛṣṇeti samudāhṛtam
adya prabhṛti nānena vacasāhaṃ śubhānane
vakṣyāmi tvāṃ tyaja krodhaṃ tām uvāca pinākadhṛk
pañcatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
tataḥ sa bhagavān devaḥ sukeśaṃ gaṇapaṃ punaḥ
cakāra brāhmaṇaṃ vyāsa tapaḥsatyaparāyaṇam
vyāsa uvāca
kathaṃ sa brāhmaṇaḥ pūrvaṃ gaṇeśatvam upāgataḥ
kenāsya tapasā tuṣṭo gaṇeśatvaṃ dadau prabhuḥ
āsīdvasiṣṭhakulajo brāhmaṇaḥ satyavāk śuciḥ
tīrthayātrāsvabhirata upavāsaparāyaṇaḥ
vyāghraṃ vyāttānanaṃ ghoraṃ nakhadaṃṣṭrāyudhaṃ tadā
dṛṣṭvā taṃ sa tadā viprastyaktvā panthānam āśugaḥ
viveśa mahatīṃ ghorām aṭavīṃ prāṇivarjitām
tatrāpaśyat sa purato vīraṇastambam āśritān
puruṣāllambamānāṃśca krandamānān suduḥkhitān
tānavākśiraso dṛṣṭvā lambamānāṃstadā dvijān
pitara ūcuḥ
narakāditi sa tvaṃ naḥ pātayiṣyasi duḥkhitān
janmaprabhṛti yaccāpi mayā kiṃcit kṛtaṃ śubham
tena yūyam ito garttāduddharadhvaṃ pitāmahāḥ
pitara ūcuḥ
na vayaṃ tapasā śakyā nayajñairnāpyato 'anyathā
na dārān āhariṣyāmi tārayiṣye ca vai pitRn
tataḥ sa tāṃstathotsṛjya duḥkhena mahatā vṛtaḥ
jagāma rudraṃ śaraṇaṃ pitaro 'antarhitāstataḥ
pitṛṣvantarhiteṣvevaṃ vāyubhakṣastadā dvijaḥ
kāṣṭhaloṣṭhopalībhūto nirucchvāso 'avatiṣṭhata
sandhāya mānasaṃ rudre niścalaḥ susamāhitaḥ
hṛdayena japan rudrān ākāśe samatiṣṭhata
tasya pūrṇe tadā māsi vātavarṣam abhūnmahat
duḥkhaṃ vāpi athavā bhaṅgaḥ samyagevāvatasthivān
viṣṇurūpadharo bhūtvā provāca dvijasattamam
sukeśastu tato dṛṣṭvā nārāyaṇam upāgatam
viṣṇuruvāca
devairapi na śakyo 'asau draṣṭuṃ kim uta mānuṣaiḥ
sukeśa uvāca
draṣṭuṃ śakyo na vā śakyaḥ kim ebhirvo vicāritaiḥ
kugrahaḥ sugraho vāhaṃ tathāpīśe mānrmama
śaṃkarādeva cakreśa śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham
varaṃ kāṃkṣe na ca tvatto na cānyasmāt kathaṃcana
tasya taṃ niścayaṃ jñātvā saṃtuṣṭo bhagavān haraḥ
viṣṇurūpaṃ parityajya svaṃ rūpaṃ pratyapadyata
uvāca cainaṃ viprendra gaṇapo me bhavākṣayaḥ
aiśvaryeṇa ca saṃyuktaḥ priyo mama puraḥsaraḥ
imaṃ ca matkṛtaṃ divyaṃ trikūṭaṃ nāma parvatam
bhavanaiḥ kāñcanairyuktaṃ kāmagaṃ te dadāmyaham
yeṣāṃ kṛte ca putra tvaṃ māṃ toṣayitum udyataḥ
tāritā narakādghorādgaṇeśaṃ tvām upasthitāḥ
kiṃkarāste bhaviṣyanti nityaṃ duḥkhavivarjitāḥ
gaṇeśvarāstavaiveme bhaviṣyanti vaśānugāḥ
sadā cāṣṭaguṇaiśvaryasamāyuktaścariṣyasi
tataḥ sa dṛṣṭvātha pitRn narakāt sasuhṛjjanān
tīrṇān gaṇeśvaratvena punaḥ pūjyena saṃyutān
maheśvaraṃ hṛṣṭamanāḥ śirasā prāñjalirnataḥ
uvāca hṛṣyamāṇāsyastadā vacanakovidaḥ
sukeśa uvāca
amaratvaṃ tathākṣayyaṃ tathaivājaratā varā
pitarastāritāśceme gaṇapāścaiva me kṛtāḥ
icchāmi tvāṃ mahādeva somaṃ sapravareśvaram
sadā sumukham atyarthaṃ sudṛśyaṃ caiva kāmada
uvācaivam idaṃ sarvaṃ bhaviṣyati gaṇeśvara
gaccha sveṣṭāṃ gatiṃ vatsa devān viprāṃśca pālaya
visṛjya taṃ tato devaḥ sukeśaṃ gaṇanāyakam
jagāmādarśanaṃ somaḥ sarveṣām eva paśyatām
narakāṇāṃ sa tattvārthaṃ pitRn papraccha yatnataḥ
vyāsa uvāca
etadvistaraśastāta saṃkṣepādvā yathātatham
sūta uvāca
jagāda vākyaṃ suralokavardhanaḥ purā kṛtaṃ suṣkṛtasarvanāśanam
iti skandapurāṇe sukeśavarapradānaṃ nāma
pañcatriṃśo 'adhyāyaḥ
ṣaṭtriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
āsīnaḥ kāñcane divye vimāne strīsamākule
pitRn sarvān samāhūya saṃpūjya vidhivat tadā
sukhopaviṣṭāṃstān dṛṣṭvā idaṃ vacanam abravīt
sukeśa uvāca
yuṣmākaṃ tejasā sarvam idam aiśvaryam īdṛśam
bhavadbhistat kṛtaṃ devā yenāsmni sukhabhāk kṛtaḥ
pitara ūcuḥ
nāsmatprasādādaiśvaryaṃ tava putra kadācana
vayaṃ tu niraye ghore yātyamānāḥ sudāruṇe
tvayā vayaṃ suputreṇa tāritā nirayādyathā
tathā nānyaṃ prapaśyāmo dhanyo hi tvaṃ suto hi naḥ
bahavaḥ prāṇinaḥ putra yātyante tātra saṃyatāḥ
sukeśa uvāca
pitaro noktapūrvaṃ me mṛṣā na ca vadāmi vai
yathā prabhāvādyuṣmākam aiśvaryaṃ mama tat tadā
śṛṇudhvaṃ vadataḥ samyaṅmāvamadhvaṃ vaco mama
nityaṃ cāśāsate caiva prajā naḥ santu puṣkalāḥ
dhārmikāśca kṛtajñāśca satkarmaratayastathā
teṣāṃ tatkāryakaraṇāt svadharmācyavanena ca
sa dharmo 'anuṣṭhitaḥ samyak prajā janayate śubhāḥ
dhārmikāśca vadanyāśca kṛtajñāḥ satpathe sthitāḥ
pitṛbhaktāśca sarvatra pitRṇāṃ tāraṇe ratāḥ
devam ārādhya narakāt pitRṃstāritavān punaḥ
eṣa prabhāvo yuṣmākaṃ tapaḥ sucaritaṃ ca ha
mamātra kiṃ mahāprajñā anṛtaṃ vātra kiṃ vacaḥ
iyaṃ ca vaidikī śubhrā śritirvedavidāṃ varāḥ
pramāṇaṃ yadi manyadhva ātmanā kṛtam ityuta
aṅgādaṅgāt saṃbhavasi hṛdayādadhijāyase
ātmā vai putranāmāsi sa jīva śaradāṃ śatam
aṅgebhyo 'ahaṃ samutpanno yuṣmākaṃ hṛdayācca ha
ātmanāhaṃ tathātmānaṃ yuṣmāṃstāritavāṃstataḥ
tasmāddhi ghorānnarakāt tāritāḥ svena karmaṇā
svakarmaṇā hi jantūnāṃ phalapāko vidhīyate
harṣeṇa sāśrunayanā idam ūcustadā vacaḥ
pitara ūcuḥ
tvadanyaḥ ko vadedevaṃ yo na syādīśasaṃmataḥ
yo na syādīdṛśaḥ putra kathaṃ taṃ sarvadevapaḥ
iṣṭaistu yojayet samyagyathā tvāṃ govṛṣadhvajaḥ
tvaṃ dhātā tvaṃ hi no bandhustvaṃ janetā mahāmate
pitā tvam eva putrā hi vayaṃ tava na saṃśayaḥ
atra te tarpayiṣyāmaḥ purāvṛttaṃ mahāmate
pitara ūcuḥ
putrā hi brahmaṇā sṛṣṭā devā yajata mām iti
te yajanta tadātmānaṃ teṣāṃ brahmā cukopa ha
uvāca cainān saṃrabdho naṣṭasaṃjñā bhaviṣyatha
duḥkhaśokasamāyuktā dīnāstaṃ tuṣṭuvustadā
prasannaṃ taṃ samālakṣya ta ūcuḥ śirasā natāḥ
naṣṭasaṃjñā vayaṃ deva tān no yaccha punaḥ prabho
tat kṣamasva ca deveśa ajñānādyat kṛtaṃ hi naḥ
uvāca praṇatān devān sānukrośam idaṃ vacaḥ
prāyaścittaṃ mahāsattvāścaradhvaṃ niyamena ha
vyabhicārakṛtaṃ sarvaṃ tataḥ pāpaṃ prahāsyatha
devā ūcuḥ
yayā jñāsyāmahe tāni prāyaścittāni lokapa
svān putrān paripṛcchadhvaṃ tataḥ śreyam avāpsyatha
punaḥ saṃjñāṃ ca dharmajñā mā kurudhvam ato 'anyathā
pitara ūcuḥ
tataste suraśārdūlāḥ papracchuḥ svān sutāṃstadā
prāyaścittāni dharmāṃśca vedān sāṅgān savistarān
te ca tebhyastadā putrā ācakhyuḥ prayatāḥ śubhāḥ
yātātahyena tat sarvaṃ parameṇa samādhinā
svān putrānabhyabhāṣanta prīyamāṇā mudā yutāḥ
devā ūcuḥ
putrā na yūyam asmākaṃ vayaṃ putrā hi vaḥ sutāḥ
yairjñānaṃ naṣṭasaṃjñānāṃ kṛtam asmākam avyayam
uvāca cedaṃ tān devān sarvāneva mahāyaśāḥ
vadanti nānṛtaṃ devāḥ satyaṃ deveṣu vartate
sutāścoktā hi vaḥ sarve pitaro nānṛtaṃ hi tat
tasmāt pitṛtvaṃ yuṣmākaṃ putrāṇāṃ nityam avyayam
bhaviṣyati na sandeho yūyaṃ putrāśca sarvaśaḥ
ekārthau putraśiṣyau ca tasmāt putrāḥ stha sarvaśaḥ
taranti putraiḥ pitaraḥ putrāṃstāṃstārayanti ca
tārayitvā pitṛtvaṃ ca karmaṇā tena yānti te
yūyaṃ ca tāritāḥ putrairajñānānnarakāt tathā
tasmādime hi pitaro yūyaṃ putrāśca sarvaśaḥ
pāti yasmāt pitā tasmājjanayatyapi vā pitā
balāḥ
pitarastān varairiṣṭaiśchandayāmāsuravyathāḥ
yathāgataṃ tato jagmurbrahmaṇā saha sarvaśaḥ
pitara ūcuḥ
yathā vayaṃ tvayā putra narakānnaṣṭacetasaḥ
tāritāścetanāvantaḥ punaśca pravarīkṛtāḥ
pitā tato bhavān pūjyo yo 'anuyāsi mahā
praṇataḥ prāñjalirbhūtvā pitRn vacanam abravīt
evam etadyathoktaṃ vo nānṛtaṃ vo vacaḥ śubham
parasparapitṛtvaṃ hi sarveṣāṃ samudāhṛtam
varaṃ bhūya imaṃ mahyaṃ prayacchata gaṇeśvarāḥ
pitara ūcuḥ
bhavānasmatpramāṇārthaṃ vyākhyātattvam ihecchasi
śrutaṃ vāpyanubhūtaṃ va yathāśakti yathātatham
sukeśa uvāca
bhavanto narake ghore parikliṣṭāḥ sudāruṇe
ataḥ śrutijñāḥ sarveṣāṃ narakāṇām asaṃśayaṃ
teṣāṃ satattvaṃ yogaṃ ca kālabhedaṃ tathā kramam
kiyanto narakāste ca kimpramāṇāḥ kimāśrayāḥ
kiṃrūpāḥ ke ca yātyante kathaṃ caiva suduḥkhitāḥ
kathayadhvaṃ mahāprajñāḥ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
iti skandapurāṇe sukeśamahābhāgyaṃ nāma
ṣaṭtriṃśo 'adhyāyaḥ
saptatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
suśarmāṇam iti khyātaṃ kathayāmāsuravyayāḥ
pitara ūcuḥ
ayaṃ te janakaḥ putra suśarmā lokaviśrutaḥ
tataḥ suśarmā viprarṣe tam āmantrya mahāmanāḥ
uvācedaṃ mahāsattvaṃ sukeśaṃ gaṇasattamam
suśarmovāca
sukeśa na vayaṃ sākṣāt patitā narakārṇave
kiṃ tu tadyātanābhītāścintayāmastvaharniśam
kīdṛśāste mahāghorā narakāḥ śrutidāruṇāḥ
tataste kathayiṣyāma yathāprajñaṃ yathāśrutam
gaṇeśvareśa śṛnu me narakā ye prakīrtitāḥ
durāsadā mahādurgāḥ sarvaprāṇibhayaṃkarāḥ
dvitīyaḥ śālmalo nāma tṛtīyaḥ kālasūtrakaḥ
tathā vaitaraṇī ṣaṣṭhaḥ saptamaścāpyayodhanaḥ
aṣṭamaḥ padma ityeva mahāpadmastathāparaḥ
ete mahānto narakā ucchrāyāśca tathāpare
ekaikasyocchrayā hyaṣṭau narakāste 'api kīrtitāḥ
ucchrayeṣu saviśrāmā yātanā bhavatīśvara
itareṣu tvaviśrāmo viśeṣo hyeṣa kīrtitaḥ
teṣāṃ satataduḥkhaṃ tu nRṇāṃ pāpena karmaṇā
bhedaḥ kṣayācca pāpasya kramasteṣāṃ pravakṣyate
pramāṇaṃ tu gaṇeśeha na śakyaṃ vaktum ekaśaḥ
kṣīṇapāpāḥ prapaśyanti yathā tacchṛṇu me 'avyaya
yātyamāno 'atikaruṇaṃ diśam ekāṃ prapadyate
sa gatvā śīghram adhvānaṃ bahuyojanavistṛtam
bahūnanyānanāsādya tasyāntaṃ vinivartate
evaṃ sarvā diśo gatvā hyantam aprāpya duḥkhitaḥ
yātanānte tvakaruṇaṃ pāpasyānte tataḥ punaḥ
evaṃ hi narakāḥ sarve hyanantāścākṣayāvyayāḥ
na teṣāṃ parisaṃkhyānaṃ yojanaiḥ saṃvidhīyate
kṛtvā pāpāni karmāṇi kṣayānte duṣṭacetanaḥ
vyādhyādhiyuktaḥ kleśena tyajati svāṃstanūṃstataḥ
yamadūtairmahāpāśairbaddhvā duḥkhasamīritaḥ
viṣameṇa pathā deva nīyate vikṛtākṛtiḥ
keśamajjāsthipaṅkaiśca dihyamānaḥ samantataḥ
tatra bhinnaśirojānupādabāhūrubandhanaḥ
kṛṣyate yamadūtaiśca punaḥ kaṇṭakibhirdrumaiḥ
nīyamāno vaśaḥ kleśān prāpnoti yamasādanam
sa tato yamam aprāpya dūrādeva yamājñayā
somo 'agnirvaruṇo vāyuḥ sūryaśceti tadā naram
sākṣiṇastatra jantūnāṃ bruvate yat kṛtākṛtam
narake pātyate ārtta ūrdhvapādo hyadhaḥśirāḥ
tomaraiścātitīkṣṇāgraiḥ śaraiścātha paraśvadhaiḥ
kīlaiśca muśalaiścaiva kṣārapiṣṭena caiva hi
hanyamāno divārātraṃ vinadan karuṇaṃ bahu
varṣāṇāṃ tu sahasreṇa narakaṃ prāpnute 'aśubham
sa tatra patito bhūyo yātyamānaḥ suduḥkhitaḥ
varṣakoṭim aviśrāntaṃ nirayāntaṃ prapadyate
mahānarakamuktaśca ucchrayāntaram āśritaḥ
śītena vāyunā spṛṣṭaḥ sukhaṃ tatra sa vindati
sa taṃ viśrāmam āsādya vismṛto yātanāṃ tadā
muhūrtam āhṛte svapne rākṣasenāpakṛṣyate
sa tena kṛṣyamāṇaśca bhūyo duḥkhaśucārditaḥ
karuṇaṃ bahudhātīva pravilapyāvatiṣṭhate
tato bhūyaḥ samākṛṣya yātanāyāṃ sa rākṣasaḥ
yātayatyeva taṃ jantuṃ saviśrāmaṃ sacetanam
evaṃ sa ucchrayān prāpya aṣṭau pāpena karmaṇā
saṃsāre kṛmikīṭādijantuḥ sampratipadyate
ye tu gacchanti tān ghorān narakān puruṣādhamāḥ
tānahaṃ sampravakṣyāmi tava putra samāsataḥ
yātyante tatra puruṣā mahānirayagāminaḥ
pakṣibhirvividhākāraiḥ puruṣaiścodyatāyudhaiḥ
vṛkṣairaparṇaiḥ saṃyuktau sucībhirvajrakaṇṭakaiḥ
tayorantaram ekaṃ vai samaṃ sūcībhirāvṛtam
anyataḥ puruṣairghoraiḥ śastrapāṇibhirāvṛtau
ākāśe cāpi lauhena tau jālena samāvṛtau
ākramanti parakyāṃ vai kanyādūṣaka eva ca
nyāsāpahārakaścaiva tathā māṃsāpahārakaḥ
rasāpahārakaścaiva yaścāpi paradūṣakaḥ
indriyagrāmaghātī ca mithyāliṅgī tathaiva ca
mṛgaśvāpadahantā ca pṛṣṭhamāṃsāśinaśca ye
vṛthāmāṃsāśino ye ca hiṃsāṃ ye ca prakurvate
yamaleṣu ca jāteṣu yo na kuryānnarādhamaḥ
tatra vyāghraiśca kupitaiḥ śarabhaiśca tarakṣubhiḥ
sarpairviḍālaiḥ patagairayastuṇḍaiśca bhakṣyate
tairbhakṣyamāṇo yadi ca vṛkṣaṃ samadhirohati
tatra taiḥ kaṇṭakaistīkṣṇairbhidyate pakṣibhiśca ha
atha cet kandarāṃ tasya guhāṃ vā yātum icchati
samāgamamyācalau kṣipraṃ pīḍayetām atīva hi
pīḍyamāno 'acalābhyāṃ sa yantreṇekṣuvadāturaḥ
karuṇaṃ krandamānastu yātanāṃ tāṃ samaśnute
dagdhasya ca navaṃ bhūyaḥ śarīram abhijāyate
evaṃ sa yātyamāno vai bahūnabdān suduḥkhitaḥ
dvāraṃ labdhvā viniryāta ucchrāyeṣu nipātyate
śṛṇuyādyo 'abhīkṣṇaśo 'ativegaṃ sa na yātyeva tam ugrapāpayogam
yamalācalakathanaṃ nāma saptatriṃśo 'adhyāyaḥ
aṣṭatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
suśarmovāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi śālmalīnarakaṃ punaḥ
yātyante tatra puruṣāḥ subhṛśaṃ pāpakarmiṇaḥ
śālmalīnāṃ sahasrāṇi bahūni pravareśvara
uccāḥ sarvāśca tā ghorā bahuyojanavistṛtāḥ
mahāśākhā mahāpatrā mahākaṇṭakasaṃyutāḥ
lauhena mahatā caiva prākārenābhisaṃvṛtāḥ
jālena mahatā sarvā upariṣṭāt samāvṛtāḥ
puruṣāstatra tiṣṭhanti bahavo ruṣitānanāḥ
vajradaṇḍopaladharā asimudgaradhāriṇaḥ
anyaiśca vividhākārairāyudhairvṛtapāṇayaḥ
yātayanti bhṛśaṃ jantūnavaśāste sudāruṇāḥ
chidyamānaśca tatrāpi rākṣasaiḥ krūrakarmabhiḥ
diśaḥ prapadyate sarvā vedanārtaḥ suduḥkhitaḥ
garteṣu partitaṃ caiva rākṣasāḥ prāpta sarvaśaḥ
śastraiśca vividhākārairnikṛntantyatidāruṇāḥ
śrāvayantaḥ purānena kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ durātmanā
tata utthāya bhinnāṅgaḥ so 'anubaddhaśca rākṣasaiḥ
sūcīkaṇṭakasaṃyuktaṃ deśam anyaṃ prapadyate
tatra sūcībhirugrābhiḥ kaṇṭakaiścāyasaiḥ punaḥ
tatrāpyenaṃ samāsādya vividhāyudhapāṇayaḥ
rākṣasābhidravantyeva vairiṇo vairiṇaṃ yathā
patraiśca vividhākārairayastuṇḍaiśca pakṣibhiḥ
hṛtakarṇākṣināsoṣṭhaḥ patito dharaṇītale
evaṃ bahuvidhākārā yātanāstatra duḥkhitāḥ
prāpnivanti durācārā ye tān nigadataḥ śṛṇu
puṃsi yo vocchṛjecchukraṃ viṣado māṃsavikrayī
samudrayāyī duṣṭātmā yaścaiko miṣṭam aśnute
ghaṇṭiko grāmayājī ca śūdrādhyāpaka eva ca
ete gacchanti durvṛttāḥ kūṭaśālmalisaṃjñakam
koṭīdvayena tūttirṇā varṣāṇāṃ vai punaśca te
ucchraye pātitāḥ stokaṃ kālaṃ viśrāmya vai punaḥ
pātyante narake tasmin yāvat kṣīṇaṃ tadenasam
eṣaiva vidhiranyeṣāṃ narakāṇāṃ mune smṛtaḥ
ya imaṃ bṛśaduḥkhitopalambhaṃ sukṛtīnām atidurgamācalam
śṛṇuyāt prayataḥ kutūhalātmā na sa gacchennirayaṃ hi śālmalam
kūṭaśālmalikarthanaṃ nāma aṣṭatriṃśo 'adhyāyaḥ
ūnacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
suśarmovāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi narakaṃ kālasūtrakam
samantānmahatoccena prākāreṇa susaṃvṛtam
lohajālena ca tathā ākāśe 'apyabhisaṃvṛtaḥ
yathaikaśca tathā sarve narakā abhisaṃvṛtāḥ
socchrayāścaiva vijñeyā na vakṣye tānahaṃ punaḥ
lokadruho janāstatra yātyante puruṣādhamāḥ
dharmasya cātmanaścaiva brāhmaṇānāṃ ca nindakaḥ
chadmanā yaśca śāstrāṇi gurubho 'apahnavet punaḥ
guruṃ nindati yaścāpi pitaraṃ mātaraṃ tathā
śvaśuraṃ bhrātaraṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ tathā cānyān garīyasaḥ
āśramāṇāṃ tathā bhettā rahasyānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
tisraḥ koṭīstu saṃpūrṇā varṣāṇāṃ tu narādhamāḥ
yātyante mṛtyuvacanāt krandamānā vicetasaḥ
kālasūtreṇa mahatā mitvā mitvā tu duṣkṛtam
chindantyaṅgāni jantūnāṃ kuṇṭhāgrairāyudhairbhṛśam
kiṃkaraistairaviśrāntaṃ divārātram atandritaiḥ
viśrāmya sa tadā jantuḥ pātyate narake punaḥ
yāvadasya kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ kṣīṇaṃ sarvam aśeṣataḥ
ya imaṃ bahupāpakartṛsūtraṃ śṛṇuyādduṣkaralokakarmasūtram
iti skandapurāṇe narakavarṇane kālasūtraṃ nāma
ūnacatvāriśattamo 'adhyāyaḥ
catvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
suśarmovāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi kumbhīpākaṃ mahābhayam
śrotRṇām api tatkālaṃ bhayadaṃ hyakṛtātmanām
āyasyastatra bahvyaśca añjanācalasannibhāḥ
kumbhyastailena sampūrṇā vahnivarṇāḥ suduḥsahāḥ
duṣkṛtīṃstāsu taptāsu baddhvā baddhvā mahābalāḥ
kṣipanti rākṣasā ghorāḥ krandamānāḥ subhairavam
iṣṭakāpākakārīca kumbhapākakarastathā
vane khale 'atha goṣṭhe vā annapānavināśakaḥ
bhojane vighnakārī ca yajñahā yajñadāhakaḥ
kūṭakarmakaro yaśca kūṭasākṣī tathaiva ca
mithyāgnicayanī caiva mithyāgnyāharaṇī tathā
mithyāpākapradātā ca edānāṃ yaśca dūṣakaḥ
hartopakaraṇānāṃ ca śilpināṃ yo narādhamaḥ
evaṃ te yātitāstatra viśrāmaṃ punarucchraye
ya imaṃ bahuduṣkṛtāntapākaṃ śṛṇuyādvā manujo hi karmapākam
catvāriṃśo 'adhyāyaḥ
ekacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
suśarmovāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi asipatravanaṃ punaḥ
asipatra iti khyātā vṛkṣāstatra durāsadāḥ
bahavaḥ sumahāśākhā ghanāścoccāśca te bhṛśam
teṣāṃ patrāṇi ghorāṇi tīkṣṇānyasinibhāni ca
āyasebhyo viśiṣṭāni na ca tāni āyasāni hi
taikṣṇyāt tāni viśiṣṭāni chedane ca mahāmate
taiḥ patrairācitāścaiva tathā kaṇṭakinaśca te
agninā dahyamānāśca vṛkṣāṃstān samprayānti te
tān āgatān samīkṣyaiva parṇāni prapatantyuta
mahāgurūṇi tīkṣṇāni vinikṛntanti tāṃśca ha
te nikṛttaśirogrīvā deśāt tasmāt prayānti vai
te gatā rākṣasairbhūyo bhūyo vṛkṣairdurāsadaiḥ
yātyante varṣakoṭīstu tatra pañca suduḥkhitāḥ
pātyante vivaśā mūḍhā yāvat pāpaṃ kṣayaṃ gatam
ye tu taṃ narakaṃ ghoraṃ narā gacchanti pāpinaḥ
tāṃste 'ahaṃ sampravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvāvahito dvija
vṛkṣaṃ yaḥ putrakṛtakaṃ vināśayati durmatiḥ
ārāme vātha grāme vā vikrīṇāti ca durmatiḥ
niṣpāditaṃ tathā vṛkṣam āśrame pathi vā punaḥ
taḍāge vā tathodyāne devatāyataneṣu vā
gṛhe prapāyām atha vā nadyāstīre catuṣpathe
yatra vā tatra vā jātaṃ yo nāśayati durmatiḥ
pādapān gulmavallīrvā kṣupānatha tṛṇānyapi
chāyāpuṣpaphalārthaṃ hi svakāryakaraṇāya vā
vināśayati yo mūḍhaḥ sa ca taṃ pratipadyate
yaścāpaharate mūlaṃ puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca
ātmārthaṃ kāmasampattau na devapitṛkāraṇāt
nadīṃ yaścāvarudhnīyāt kūpān yaśca prapūrayet
yaśca parṇatvacām arthe vṛkṣaṃ chindyānnarādhamaḥ
vināśayedvā taṃ vṛkṣaṃ sa ca taṃ pratipadyate
yaśca chāyāsamāsannāñjantūn vai samprabādhate
svasthānaṃ ca samāsannāṃstrāsayedvārayedapi
uttīrṇāśca tato bhūyaḥ saṃsāraṃ yānti te śubhāḥ
ya imaṃ śṛṇuyādatandritātmā narakaṃ pāpakṛtām aśarmabhūtam
asipatravanaṃ nāma ekacatvāriṃśo 'adhyāyaḥ
dvicatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
suśarmovāca
ataḥ paraṃ vaitaraṇīṃ nadīṃ pāpapraṇāśanīm
śṛṇuṣvāvahitaḥ putra pāpakarmabhayāvahām
nadī vaitaraṇī putra ṭaṅkacchinnataṭā śubhā
keśāsthirudhirāpūrṇā mahākṣārarasā tathā
śiśumāraiśca nakraiśca tantukai rākṣasairapi
mahādaṃṣṭrairmahākāyaiḥ piśitāśaiḥ samākulā
asipatraiśca tairvṛkṣaistīrajātaiḥ samāvṛtā
śaivalena ca dīrgheṇa vitāneneva saṃvṛtā
tasyāstīre vanaṃ ghoraṃ śarabharkṣasamākulam
vyāghradvīpisamākīrṇaṃ siṃhebhakharasaṃkulam
tatra duṣkṛtakarmāṇastairvyāghrādibhirarditāḥ
tāṃ nadīṃ sumahāghorāṃ pātyante duḥkhitāstataḥ
vitānena ca saṃnaddhā bhakṣyante tairjhaṣādibhiḥ
kṣārodakena dahyanto nādayantaśca duḥkhitāḥ
ṣaḍvarṣakoṭīryātyante yāvat pāpasya saṃkṣayaḥ
pātyante vivaśā mūḍhā yāvat pāpaṃ kṣayaṃ gatam
uttīrṇaḥ socchrayānetān saṃsāraṃ pratipadyate
tīrṇo 'antameṣu ca punarnarakeṣu pṛthak pṛthak
ucchrayāṇāṃ tu sarveṣām ekaikasya pṛthak pṛthak
sahasraṃ vardhate putra varṣāṇāṃ vai samāsataḥ
śṛṇuṣva tānimān samyagucyamānān mayānagha
niṣṭhīvedatha mūtraṃ vā purīṣaṃ vāpyathotsṛjet
apaśca harate yastu kṣetrārāmajanopagāḥ
apāṃ setuharaścaiva taḍāgasya ca bhedakaḥ
tathā puṣkariṇīnāṃ ca dūṣako yaśca mānavaḥ
duṣṭām aduṣṭām atha vā yaśca nārīṃ pradūṣayet
padminīṃ yaśca harati nāśayedvāpi durmatiḥ
ya imām aśubhapraṇāśinīṃ śṛṇuyānnityam aśuddhavādhanīm
prayataḥ sa na yāti bhāvanīṃ saritaṃ vaitaraṇīm asaṅginīm
it skandapurāṇe narakavarṇane vaitaraṇīnāma
dvicatvāriṃśo 'adhyāyaḥ
tricatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
suśarmovāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi narakaṃ pāpanāśanam
yatra te puruṣā ghorā yamābhā yamakiṃkarāḥ
mahābalā mahāsattvāḥ sarve yogeśvarāstathā
ayaskārā yathā piṇḍam ayaso 'agnipratāpitam
saṃdeśenābhisaṃgṛhya sthāpayitvāyase ghane
varṣakoṭīstathā sapta yātitāḥ svena karmaṇā
ucchrayeṣu tathā ghorāṃ yātanāṃ prāpnuvanti te
etadye yānti puruṣāḥ socchrayaṃ narakaṃ mahat
tānahaṃ sampravakṣyāmi anirdeśyān narādhamān
pādena hanyāt pitaraṃ mātaraṃ pūjyam eva vā
anyāṃ kāṃcit striyaṃ vāpi hastenātha kaśādibhiḥ
bālam arthakṛte yaśca mṛtyunā yojayet tathā
striyaṃ vātha pumāṃsaṃ vā klībaṃ vānyaṃ narādhamaḥ
patiryaścaiva bhāryāṃ svāṃ putrāṃścaivābhisaṃdhayet
bhāryā patiṃ vā putrān vā teṣāṃ sā gatirucyate
kīlayedyaśca devārcāstīrthāni ca durātmavān
vidyāḥ śāstrāṇi divyāni teṣāṃ sā gatirucyate
ya imaṃ bahupāpayogakāraṇaṃ śṛṇuyānnityam asaukhyasarvadāraṇam
tricatvāriṃśo 'adhyāyaḥ
catuścatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
suśarmovāca
sukṛtīnām alabhyaṃ ca duṣkṛtīnāṃ bhayāvaham
taṃ te gatvā pragūhanti so 'apyagniratidāruṇaḥ
evaṃ tatrāniśaṃ ghoraṃ yātitāstūcchrayeṣvapi
narāstaṃ yānti niḥsaṅgaṃ ye tān me tvaṃ niśāmaya
devadravyaṃ bhakṣayedyo nāśayedvāpyabhīkṣṇaśaḥ
brāhmaṇasvaṃ haredyaśca balāddhārayate 'api vā
bāladravyāpahārī ca hartā ca strīdhanasya ca
klīvāṃśca tyajate yaśca yo hanyāccharaṇāgatam
sarvabhakṣa yaḥ syādvai yaśca pānīyavikrayī
agnipraharaṇo yaśca viṣapraharaṇaśca yaḥ
aśastraṃ yaśca saṃgrāme hanyācchatreṇa mānavaḥ
yācamānaṃ tathā caiva upaviṣṭam athāpi vā
catuścatvāriṃśo 'adhyāyaḥ
pañcacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
suśarmovāca
mahāpadmastataścānyo nirayo romaharṣaṇaḥ
yatra te kiṃkarā ghorā yamasya yamasaṃnibhāḥ
jantūnām āyudhaiḥ kuṇṭhairnighṛṇāḥ pāpakarmiṇām
te bhakṣayitvā māṃsāni svāni duṣkṛtakāriṇaḥ
mukhe 'apāvṛtya yacchanti dāruṇā yamakiṃkarāḥ
ayomayāstathā nāryo narāścāgnisamaprabhāḥ
samāśliṣyanti saṃgatya dravamāṇāstatastataḥ
vṛkṣāśca bahavastatra supuṣyāḥ phalapatriṇaḥ
tān āśrayanti duḥkhārtā agniṃ varṣanti te 'api ca
śilāśca bahvyastatrānyāstāḥ śliṣyanti yadā ca te
tadā tāścāgnivarṇābhā dahante tān bhṛśaṃ narān
suvarṇahārī yaścaiva mātṛyāyī ca yo naraḥ
mātā putraṃ ca yo 'abhyeti vedadūṣyavakīrṇakaḥ
matsarī yaśca durvṛttaḥ śramaṇānāṃ ca pūjakaḥ
vṛṣalo yaḥ śrutiṃ brūyācchṛṇuyādapi vā punaḥ
gṛhṇīyādvāpi durbuddhirbrāhmaṇān vāvamanyate
brāhmaṇebhyo rahasyāni āśramāntarajāni ca
yasminnadhikṛto na syācchṛṇuyādvā paṭheta vā
duṣṭaśramaṇanirgranthā tathaivājīvakāśca ye
yogeśvarāṃśca durvṛtto yogadharmam athāpi vā
vedavarṇāśramā yajñāstannindābhirataḥ śaṭaḥ
tataḥ śeṣeṇa sambaddhā jāyante kīṭayoniṣu
śṛṇuyādya imaṃ vicintya dhīmān matimān nityam alobhamohaśokaḥ
pañcacatvāriṃśo 'adhyāyaḥ
ṣaṭcatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi rauravaṃ narakaṃ punaḥ
yatra te vivaśā baddhāḥ karmaṇā svena jantavaḥ
yātyante duḥkhaśokārttā mahānirayagāminaḥ
pūrṇastu sarvaḥ kārīṣyājjvalate so 'atidāruṇaḥ
tatra janturbṛśaṃ magnaḥ praviśan dahyate 'avaśaḥ
ārtanādān prakurvāṇo mūrchitaḥ patitaḥ punaḥ
tataḥ kleśena mahatā uddhṛtyātmānam ātmanā
bhūyo 'anyaṃ deśam āsādya tathaiva praviśecca saḥ
evaṃ sa yātyate tatra bahūnabdān suduḥkhitaḥ
tato visṛṣṭo bhūyaśca ucchrayān pratipadyate
taṃ hi gacchanti puruṣāḥ surāpā dharmadeśakāḥ
pitṛhā mātṛhā caiva bhrātṛhā guruhā tathā
vādebhiratāsteṣām eva ca nindakāḥ
goghno 'atha damakaścaiva jantūnāṃ bhṛśadāruṇaḥ
galakartā kūṭamānī karmaṇānukaroti yaḥ
ya imaṃ śṛṇuyācca rauravaṃ narakaṃ pāpakṛtāṃ surauravam
ṣaṭcatvāriṃśo 'adhyāyaḥ
saptacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
suśarmovāca
mahārauravam anyacca śṛṇu me duṣṭayātanam
yatra dhārāśca toyaṃ ca taḍāgāni ca putraka
kārīṣī kanakābhāśca kulyāścāgniprapūritāḥ
āyasā bahavaḥ stambhā vṛkṣāśca bahukaṇṭakāḥ
rākṣasā vividhākārāstīkṣṇaśastrāstradhāriṇaḥ
tatra pāpena bahunā jantuḥ samabhipāśitaḥ
nipatedvikṛtākāraḥ krandamāno muhurmuhuḥ
kārīṣyām agnivarṇāyāṃ pacyate bhṛśadāruṇam
tataḥ sa tena dāhena duḥkhitaḥ paramārtimān
dāhapraśamanārthāya taḍāge vinimajjati
tatra kṣāreṇa taptena dviguṇaṃ vedanārditaḥ
vegenotthāya vṛkṣaṃ vā stambhaṃ vāpyadhirohati
tatra taiḥ kaṇṭakaistīkṣṇairāyasaiścāvatakṣitaḥ
patate hyagnikulyāyāṃ karuṇaṃ bahudhā nadan
evaṃ sa yātyamānastu tṛṣārtto vilapan bahu
dhārām āśrayate pātuṃ sāpi tasyāyasaṃ tadā
sampūrṇayātanaścāpi muktastasmānmahābhayāt
ucchrayeṣu tadā janturyātyate bhṛśadāruṇam
tatra gacchati rājaghno rājabhāryāvamānakaḥ
āśāṃ dattvā na dadyādyo yaśca tīrthāvadūṣakaḥ
moṣakaḥ sūcakaścaiva strībhṛto yaśca pāpakṛt
agnau gavi ca yo dānaṃ brāhmaṇe cāpi vārayet
vikrīṇīyāt svabhāryāṃ yo hyapatyaṃ vā narādhamaḥ
harate cāgnibhaṇḍāni yogināṃ caiva kiṃcana
corān vā yo 'anugṛhṇāti manuṣyāstasya ye ca ha
brāhmaṇādhikṛtaścaiva dharmādhikṛta eva ca
rāṣṭralopaṃ dāralopaṃ dhanalopaṃ ca yo naraḥ
deśavidrarm vaṇaṃ caiva yaḥ kuryāḍḍāmarāṇi vā
ya imaṃ śṛṇuyādabhīkṣṇaśo niyataṃ dharmamatiśca tiṣṭhati
saptacatvāriṃśo 'adhyāyaḥ
aṣṭacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ
suśarmovāca
asimudgaraśaṅkvagrairgadāmuśalapaṭṭiśaiḥ
bhayadaiḥ parighaiḥ ṭaṅkairvajrairṛṣṭiparaśvadhaiḥ
sa dehena vinaṣṭena tamasā mūrcchitākṛtiḥ
suḥkhasantatisaṃnaddho yātanām aśnute bhṛśam
yasmāt sa tamasā grasto 'anāśvasto 'atidāruṇām
sarvā bahuvidhākārā yātanā yāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
samāptayātanaścāpi santīrṇasvena karmaṇā
brahmahā bhrūṇahā caiva surāpo brāhmaṇaśca yaḥ
gavāṃ nipāne yaścaiva pipāsūnāṃ narādhamaḥ
brāhmaṇān dveṣṭi nityaṃ yo 'arthinaṃ yaśca dūṣayet
śāstrāṇi harate yaśca goghno yaśca naraḥ smṛtaḥ
kāpilaśca vṛthādṛṣṭirvedadharmārthadūṣakaḥ
brāhmaṇākrośakaścaiva vedadharmārthadūṣakaḥ
nāstikāśca surātmāna ityete taṃ prayānti vai
ya imaṃ śṛṇuyāt tamomayaṃ tamasā nityam atandritendriyaḥ
na sa yāti tamomayaṃ sadā narakaṃ dāruṇajantuśokadam
tamo nāma aṣṭacatvāriṃśo 'adhyāyaḥ
ūnapañcāśattamo adhyāyaḥ
suśarmovāca
tamastamataraṃ ghoraṃ narakaṃ śṛṇvataḥ param
prakāśo yatra naivāsti naiva dṛṣṭiḥ pravartate
tatrāsau patito mūḍho vahninā dahyate bhṛśam
tato 'api vegādutthāya dṛṣṭihīno vicetanaḥ
tatrāpi nigṛhītastaiḥ paśumāreṇa māryate
tato bhūyaśca kūpeṣu kṣipto durgeṣvacetanaḥ
nimagnaścāgnikārīṣyāṃ niṣkūjan so 'abhijāyate
evaṃ sa yātanā bahvīstvanubhūya suduḥkhitaḥ
garbhapātanakāraśca rājyakāmaśca yo bhavet
anācāryaśca yaḥ karma ācāryāṇāṃ prapadyate
śāstravidyauṣadhīnāṃ ca gadānām agadaiḥ saha
yo vināśayitā kaścidyaḥ praśaṃsati dānavān
upadeśaṃ ca yo dveṣādācāryo na prayacchati
kṛtaghnaṃ tu samāsādhya nārakāḥ sarva eva te
bhagavan na vayaṃ śaktāḥ pāpasyāsya vināśane
upāyam anyaṃ paśyeha prasādaṃ kuru naḥ prabho
niṣkṛtiḥ sumahāghorādbhavet pāpasya karmaṇaḥ
tataste ṛṣayaḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā dīrgheṇa cakṣuṣā
yamaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭham idaṃ vai bruvate vacaḥ
niṣkṛtirvihitā sadbhiḥ kṛtaghne nāsti niṣkṛtiḥ
tataḥ sa bhagavān devo mārtaṇḍatanayo varaḥ
nārakebhyo dadāti ājñāṃ sarve yūyam imaṃ naram
śodhayiṣyatha gacchadhvaṃ naikā hyasya gatiḥ smṛtā
tataste tasya vacanānnārakāḥ pāpakarmiṇam
sarveṣvevānupūrvyeṇa yātayantyatidāruṇāḥ
bhartṛpiṇḍāpahartā ca pitṛpiṇḍāpahārakaḥ
tasmādgṛhītvā vidyāṃ ca dakṣiṇāṃ yo na yacchati
puṣṭaśca yastaṃ nānveti yaśca taṃ ghātayennaraḥ
na smarecca kṛtaṃ yastu āśramān yaśca dūṣayet
na puṣṇāti tathā vāhān āśritāṃścopakāriṇaḥ
bhṛtyāṃśca karmaniratāṃstathaiva hitakāriṇaḥ
bhāryāṃ karmakarāṇāṃ ca narmāṇi vadate ca yaḥ
sarvāṃstānṛṣibhiḥ sārdhaṃ kṛtaghnānabravīnmanuḥ
kṛtaghnaśca śaṭhaścaiva nāstikocchinnasaṃśayaḥ
bhayatrātānnadātā ca pañcaite pitaraḥ smṛtāḥ
yasteṣāṃ doṣavaktā ca abhyasūyaka eva ca
mitradhugyaśca duṣṭātmā tasya randhrāvakīrtitaḥ
kṛtopakāriṇe purrvaṃ na karoti priyaṃ ca yaḥ
ete sarve narā duṣṭāḥ sarva evāśubhe ratāḥ
ya imaṃ tāmasaṃ ghoraṃ śṛṇuyādvā paṭheta vā
ūnapañcāśattamo 'adhyāyaḥ
pañcāśo adhyāyaḥ
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi saṃsāraparivartanam
yathā vai narakāt tīrṇaḥ saṃsaranti samāsataḥ
śeṣeṇa karmaṇā te tu jāyante kṛmiyoniṣu
kṛmiyonau parāvṛttāḥ sahasrāṇāṃ śataṃ samāḥ
tatra tāvat parāvṛttā jāyante goṣu te yadā
tadā tatra śatenaiva janmanāṃ śeṣatastataḥ
mānuṣeṣūpajāyante tāvadeva na saṃśayaḥ
dvitīye tu mayā proktāste muktāḥ śeṣakarmaṇā
kṛmikīṭeṣu jāyante sahasrāṇāṃ śatāni ṣaṭ
tathā śatasahasraṃ ca śatānāṃ te punargatāḥ
tato vyāghrāśca ṛkṣāśca tato gotvam avāpyate
mānuṣeṣūpapadyante kutsitāḥ svena karmaṇā
tṛtīye tvatha ye proktā mayā duṣkṛtakāriṇaḥ
te muktāḥ karmaṇastasmāccheṣeṇa samaveṣṭitāḥ
kṛmikīṭeṣu jāyante sahasrāṇāṃ śatāni ṣaṭ
tathaivadaśa cānyāni pakṣiṇastāvadeva ca
tataḥ siṃhāśca sarpāśca gāvaḥ paścācca mānuṣāḥ
caturthe tvatha ye proktā mayā duṣkṛtakāriṇaḥ
sahasrāṇāṃ śatānyaṣṭau tathā cānyāni ṣoḍaśa
yonīnāṃ hi tathā bhūyo jāyante te tato mṛgāḥ
mṛgabhāvādvinirmuktā jāyante ca punaḥ kharāḥ
tato 'ajā gavayāścāpi gāvo mānuṣatāṃ tataḥ
pañcame ye mayā proktāste 'api śeṣeṇa karmaṇā
kṛmikīṭeṣu jāyante janmanāṃ koṭim eva hi
hastiyonau ca tāvaddhi uṣṭreṣvaśveṣu caiva hi
tato gotvaṃ samāsādya mānuṣyaṃ prāpnuvanti te
ṣaṣṭhāccaiva vinirmuktāstataḥ śeṣeṇa karmaṇā
jāyante kṛmikīṭeṣu janmanāṃ dviguṇena hi
koṭim ekāṃ tato yūkāstato matsyo 'atha sūkaraḥ
mahiṣatvaṃ tataḥ prāpya gotvājjāyeta mānuṣaḥ
mānuṣatve kutsitaśca vyādhitaścaiva jāyate
saptamācca vinirmuktaḥ kṛmikīṭeṣu jāyate
koṭītrayaṃ tāvadeva vṛkṣatvam adhigacchati
gotvaṃ ca samanuprāpya jāyate mānuṣastataḥ
aṣṭamācca vinirmukto baddhaḥ śeṣeṇa karmaṇā
jāyate kṛmikīṭeṣu dve koṭyau dviguṇe ca saḥ
tataścauṣadhibhāvena vīrutsu ca kuśeṣu ca
navamādapi cottīrṇo baddhaḥ śeṣeṇa karmaṇā
jāyate kṛmikīṭeṣu pañcakoṭīstataḥ khagaḥ
tato matsyaśca tāvadvai tāvadeva sarīsṛpaḥ
daśamādapi cottīrṇaḥ ṣaṭ koṭīrjanmanāṃ kṛmiḥ
śeṣeṇa karmaṇā jātastato bhavati vānaraḥ
tāvadeva ca kākastu jīvaṃjīvaka eva ca
vṛkṣadārakamārjārapipilīkāśca jāyate
tato goṣu prajāto 'asau mānuṣeṣūpajāyate
mahārauravanirmuktaḥ saptakoṭīḥ suduḥkhitaḥ
janmanāṃ kṛmikīṭeṣu jāto matsyatvam aśnute
tataḥ śvā gardabhaścaiva bhaināśī śuka eva ca
tato bhavati gauścāpi tataḥ ṣaṇḍhaśca mānuṣe
tamonarakanirmuktastvaṣṭakoṭīḥ suduḥkhitaḥ
janmanāṃ prāpnute janturviṣṭhāyāṃ kṛmiyoniṣu
tataḥ śvā jāyate bhūyaścakrāhvaśca punaḥ punaḥ
tato maṇḍūkatāṃ prāpya jāyate mṛgapakṣiṣu
jāyate kinnaraścāpi dvīpī śarabha eva ca
tato gotvaṃ samāsādya mānuṣatvam avāpnute
tamonarako nirmuktaḥ śeṣeṇaiva hi karmaṇā
jāyate kṛmikīṭeṣu navakoṭiḥ sa janmanām
vāntāśī ca tataḥ pakṣī ulūkaśca tataḥ punaḥ
punarvṛkṣaśca gulmaśca tato bhavati vai mṛgaḥ
punaḥ punarjāyamānaḥ sahasrāṇāṃ śataṃ samāḥ
vyādhitaḥ kutsitaścaiva jāyate ca punaḥ punaḥ
yadi mānuṣatāṃ yāti kadācit kālaparyayāt
tatrāpi kutsitāṃ yoniṃ bhūyo bhūyaḥ prapadyate
aniṣṭaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ duḥkhito vyādhitastathā
vikṛtaṃ rūpam āpnoti karmaṇā svena duḥkhitaḥ
devabrāhmaṇavidveṣṭā sarvavratabahiṣkṛtaḥ
nirnamaskāraduḥśīlaḥ kimbhakṣo brahmanindakaḥ
akīrtanīyo lokānāṃ jāyate svena karmaṇā
suśarmovāca
etat te kathitaṃ sarvaṃ samāsāt putra sarvaśaḥ
narakāṇāṃ satattvaṃ ca kramabhedo yathāmati
ya imaṃ śṛṇuyādyuktaḥ sadā parvasu parvasu
dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ svargyaṃ sarvārthasādhakam
śravyaṃ ca paṭhitavyaṃ ca satataṃ bhūtim icchatā
idaṃ tu sarvārthasukhāvahaṃ dhruvaṃ mahānubhāvaṃ sugatipradaṃ śubham
sadaiva vipreṇa samāhitātmanā adhītya dhāryaṃ śrutisaṃmitaṃ dhruvam
iti skandapurāṇe saṃsāragativarṇanaṃ nāma
pañcāśo 'adhyāyaḥ
ekapañcāśo adhyāyaḥ
sukeśastu tato vyāsa pituḥ śrutvā sudīnavat
duḥkhitaścintayāmāsa jantūnāṃ tāṃ gatiṃ tadā
cintayābhiparītātmā duḥkhena ca samāhataḥ
jantūnāṃ mokṣaṇopāyaṃ mūḍhacetā na jajñivān
cintāpannaḥ sa tu yadā pitRṃstān nābhyabhāṣata
pitara ūcuḥ
sukeśa uvāca
jantūnāṃ karmajaṃ kleśaṃ śrutvā yuṣmābhirīritam
cintayāmi kathaṃ teāṃ mokṣopāyo bhavediti
anādṛtya kṣayaṃ putra mokṣasteṣāṃ na vidyate
karmaṇaḥ svakṛtasyeha sa ca bhogāt kṣayo mataḥ
bhogaśca narake 'avaśyaṃ jantūnāṃ saṃvidhīyate
na ca te nārakāḥ śakyā hartuṃ karmakṣayaṃ vinā
aśakyāḥ khalu ye hyarthā na tān prājñaḥ samārabhet
arṇavasya prataraṇaṃ yathā tvāṃ mṛtyum ṛcchati
evam uktaḥ sa tejasvī pitRṃstān hṛcchayāvṛtaḥ
uvāca praṇato bhūtvā māvamadhvaṃ sutaṃ hi mām
kā śaktirmama tāñjantūn balāt tārayituṃ śubhān
mahādevaprasādastāṃstārayiṣyati durgatīn
yūyaṃ yathaiva tīrṇāḥ stha narakasthā vicetasaḥ
tathā te jantavaḥ sarve tariṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ
tatastān sa tadāmantrya mahātmā gaṇanāyakaḥ
jajāpa rudrāñchuddhātmā niścalaḥ susamāhitaḥ
kasyedaṃ tapaso vīryaṃ kasya yogo 'ayam īdṛśaḥ
ka eṣa suraśārdūla tapastapyati dāruṇam
uvāca mā bhayaṃ vo 'astu nāyaṃ kaścidasaṃmataḥ
sa eṣa devadevasya mahātmā gaṇanāyakaḥ
samudrāntarjalāsīno rudrāñjapati yogavān
na cāsya duṣṭo 'abhiprāyo lokān prati mahābalāḥ
gatā mandaram avyagrā nandinā sampraveśitāḥ
te dṛṣṭvā devam īśānaṃ stutvedam abruvan vibhum
sukeśo bhagavāṃstubhyaṃ vallabho gaṇanāyakaḥ
kāruṇyaṃ prāṇināṃ kṛtvā tapastapyati duścaram
tasya kāmaṃ sakāmaṃ tvaṃ kuruṣva bhuvaneśvara
teṣāṃ vijñaptim ākarṇya devadevastato bhavaḥ
samudrastatra ye cānye munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ
ardhyam ādāya śataśas nemuḥ śaṅkaram āgatam
tam asau gaṇapaśreṣṭhaṃ devadeva idaṃ vacaḥ
tataḥ sukeśa utthāya stutvā ca vṛṣabhadhvajam
narakeṣu narā deva yātyante pāpakāriṇaḥ
teṣām upari ceto me duḥkhenārditam īśvara
teṣāṃ tu pratimokṣārthaṃ yāce 'ahaṃ tvāṃ sureśvara
evaṃ bhavatu te vatsa muktā nārakiṇo narāḥ
tataste nārakāḥ sarve vimānāni samāśritāḥ
tam uvāca punardevaḥ sukeśaṃ gaṇanāyakam
yo hi tārayate jantūn āpadaḥ kāṃścideva tu
teṣāṃ dharmapitā bhūtvā saṃsāraṃ na sa paśyati
manasāpi hi yaḥ prāṇī kleśājjantūn sadecchati
sa tvaṃ pareṇa yogena aiśvaryeṇa ca saṃyutaḥ
jantūnāṃ tāraṇe yuktastvayānyaḥ kaḥ samo bhuvi
sukeśa uvāca
tavāsmi kiṃkaro dāso nāścaryaṃ yan mamedṛśam
abhyagānmandaraṃ vyāsa vṛtaḥ sarvāmaraistadā
devā api vimānasthān nārakān vīkṣya sarvaśaḥ
śāntaṃ ca jagato duḥkhaṃ dṛṣṭvā jagmuryathāgatam
ya imaṃ nārakottāraṃ śṛṇuyādvā paṭheta vā
etadyogavidhānasarvasamayaṃ śrutvā naro nityaśaḥ pāpātmāpi sunirghṛṇaṃ pratibhayaṃ nābhyeti pāpāśrayam
kiṃ tvetadya ihābhyupetya satataṃ śaucānvitaḥ śrāvayeddevabrahmaṇavaidyasaṃsadi dṛḍhaṃ bhaktaḥ sadā śaṅkaram
iti skandapurāṇe nārakīyamokṣaṇe ekapañcāśo 'adhyāyaḥ
dvipañcāśo adhyāyaḥ
vyāsa uvāca
tathā strīṇāṃ ca kā yuktā gatiḥ paramikā śubhā
na gacchanti narā yena narakaṃ taṃ suduḥkhitāḥ
pāpakarmaṇyapi ratāstānimāñchṛṇu mānada
nāgnicinnarakaṃ yāti na trisūtrī na govratī
brāhmaṇāṃstārayedyaśca āpado maraṇāntikāt
brāhmaṇaṃ vyādhitaṃ dīnam anāthaṃ duḥkhapīḍitam
śuśrūṣedyāvadetena yukto dharmeṇa mānavaḥ
brāhmaṇaṃ vāsayedyastu gṛhavāsaparicchadaiḥ
niḥsvaṃ svādhyāyasaṃpannaṃ narakaṃ na sa paśyati
tathā gāṃ caiva saṃmagnāṃ patitāṃ śaktivarjitām
maheśaṃ yaśca bhāvena parameṇa samādhinā
itareṣāṃ tu saṃsāro bhavatyeva na saṃśayaḥ
brāhmaṇāstaṃ na gacchanti vedavedāṅgapāragāḥ
ṣaṭkarmaniratā vyāsa ātmadharmavyavasthitāḥ
tapaḥśaucasamāyuktā dayāvanto dṛḍhavratāḥ
pratigrahanivṛttāśca īśabhaktāśca ye dvijāḥ
kṣatriyā ye ca rakṣārthaṃ prajānāṃ nityam udyatāḥ
vaiśyā vārtāsamāyuktā nyāyadharmavyavasthitāḥ
yeṣāṃ vṛttiravicchinnā devabrāhmaṇapūjakāḥ
bhaktā varṇatrayaṃ ye ca śūdrā darpavivarjitāḥ
brāhmaṇāṃśca viśeṣeṇa nityaṃ ye samupāsate
te na paśyanti narakaṃ sugatiṃ ca mṛtā yayuḥ
caturṣvapi ca varṇeṣu manujā bhāvataḥ śivam
śarvārpitakriyāvasthā bhaktā nityam anuvratāḥ
prāsādaṃ caiva ye kṛtvā devadevam upāsate
khanitāḥ puṣkariṇyo yaistaḍāgāni hradāni ca
ropitā vṛkṣaṣaṇḍāśca te 'api tān na prayānti hi
paritrāṇaṃ dvijātīnām anyeṣāṃ caiva duḥkhinām
akrodhanāśca ye nityaṃ devabrāhmaṇapūjakāḥ
satyābhidhānasaṃyuktā dṛṣṭārambhavivarjitāḥ
svadharmācārasaṃyuktāḥ paśyanti narakaṃ na te
dhyānī ta sarvadā yo vai gaṇāñjapati vā śuciḥ
strīṇāṃ tu paramo devaḥ patirbhavati sarvadā
tasmānnānyaṃ prapaśyanti yāḥ kāściddharmacintikāḥ
karmaṇā manasā vācā yaddadāti juhoti vā
patiśuśrūṣaṇe raktā manovākkāyakarmabhiḥ
sā nārī narakān sarvān manasāpi na gāchati
saṃsāraṃ naiva sā ghoraṃ sarvaṃ saṃpratipadyate
sukeśaṃ tvanugṛhyaivaṃ devo 'api vṛṣavāhanaḥ
kāṣṭhakūṭāśramaṃ gataḥ
anujagrāha taṃ vipraṃ kāṣṭhakūṭaṃ tapodhanam
vyāsa uvāca
gautamasyānvaye vipro nāmnā kṛṣṇa iti prabhuḥ
tasya patnyabhavat sukhrūrātreyī nāmato yaśāḥ
sa kadācit kṛtodvāho bhūmanyurnāma gautamaḥ
nāvindata sutaṃ tasyāṃ jarayā cābhisaṃvṛtaḥ
sa bhāryām āha duḥkhārta idaṃ vacanakovidaḥ
putreṇecchanti lokāṃśca anṛṇāśca bhavantyuta
jarāṃ parigataścāhaṃ na ca me dṛśyate sutaḥ
sā tvaṃ kaṃcit sagotraṃ me anujñātā mayā śubhe
abhipadyasva putrārthaṃ yāce tvāṃ prāñjalirnataḥ
suyaśovāca
atrīṇāṃ tu kule jātā gautamaṃ kulam āgatā
putrān kulaṃ ca kolāṃśca tapaḥ kuru mahāmune
tapasā hi suto labdhaḥ śaktinā sa parāśaraḥ
lapsyase tvaṃ sutaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ mahāyogabalānvitam
māṃ hi dṛṣṭvā purā prāha atrirbrahmasutaḥ svayam
tayaivaṃ samanujñāto rudraṃ śaraṇam īyivān
tvaritaṃ sa samāgamya narmadāṃ harṣasaṃyutaḥ
tasyāstīre samudviśya tasthau vāyvāśanaḥ samāḥ
tataḥ sa duḥkhito bhūyaḥ prāṇāyāmena tasthivān
cintayāmāsa maraṇaṃ na gantuṃ svaṃ gṛhaṃ prati
sa kāṣṭhakūṭaṃ saṃbhṛtya gṛhītvāgniṃ suduḥkhitaḥ
putraste bhavitā gaccha mā caivaṃ sāhasaṃ kṛthāḥ
kāṣṭhakūṭeti nāmnā ca bhaviṣyati sa te sutaḥ
atha hṛṣṭamanā vipro gatvā patnyāṃ mahātapāḥ
utpādayāmāsa sutaṃ kāṣṭhakūṭaṃ mahāmunim
aśakto 'ayaṃ vṛddhabhāvānmām adhyāpayituṃ pitā
tasmādyāsyāmi cāmantrya pitaraṃ vedakāraṇāt
sa gatvā mātaraṃ vipraḥ pitaraṃ ca mahāyaśāḥ
suto yuvābhyāṃ jāto 'ahaṃ dharmahetorna kāmataḥ
āvāṃ tārayitā cāyaṃ tathaiva ca pitāmahān
santatiścāpyavicchinnā bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
iṣṭāṃśca lokān prāpsyāva suputreṇeti sarvathā
pitRṇāṃ cānṛṇau syāva ityabhīṣṭo 'asmi vāṃ sutaḥ
so 'ahaṃ dharmeṣvakuśalaḥ śrutismṛtibahiṣkṛtaḥ
kartājñānena tat karma pitaro yena duḥkhitāḥ
bhavāṃśca niraye magnaściraṃ vatsyati duṣṭavat
ācāryaṃ matisaṃpannaṃ saṃśrayāmīti me matiḥ
kuryādyaḥ pādayornityaṃ śuśrūṣām iti cintayan
na ca nākhyayam etadvāṃ mayā cintā kṛtā śubham
aśubhaṃ vāpi yat kiṃcidyuvāṃ mama gatiḥ parā
aśrupūrṇekṣaṇau sthitvā muhūrtam idam ūcatuḥ
āghrāyāliṅgya saṃmṛjya snehāt priyasutau tadā
śuśrūṣā dvividhā putra pitRṇāṃ dharmasaṃmitā
aihikī cāṅguśuśrūṣā yā paratra ca dharmadā
yayā taranti pitaraḥ kāmāṃścāpnuvate 'akṣayān
tatraihikaṃ na no hīṣṭaṃ yathā hi āmuṣmikaṃ hitam
gacchādhīṣva śrutiṃ caiva smṛtiṃ caiva sukarmaṇām
suyaśovāca
yathā te 'ayaṃ pitā putra bravīti viditātmavān
udareṇa mayā duḥkhaṃ dhāritastvaṃ mahāmate
pitrā ca tapasogreṇa prāṇāṃstyaktvātidustyajān
yathā tuṣṭau tvayā putra jīvau jīvena saṃgatau
āvām ubhāvapi syāva tathā samyak samācara
tatastābhyām anujñāta āghrātaścaiva mūrdhani
pradakṣiṇam upāvṛtya jagāma sa kṛtātmavān
sa jagāma tadā tābhyāṃ visṛṣṭaścyavanaṃ prati
ṛgyajurbhyām ivotsṛṣṭā svāhutirvaruṇaṃ prati
sa tam āsādya tuṣṭena tenāsau saphalaḥ kṛtaḥ
atha putre gate tasmin pitā diṣṭāntam īyivān
kāṣṭhakūṭastato 'abhyetya kṛtavidyaḥ sudhārmikaḥ
apaśyanmātaraṃ dīnāṃ vitoyām iva padminīm
somahīnām iva niśām ājñāhīnām iva śriyam
rudatīm aśrupūrṇākṣīṃ vilapantīṃ suduḥkhitām
kāṣṭhakūṭastu tāṃ dṛṣṭvā duḥkhena samabhiplutām
jayaṃta iva paulomīṃ śakre naṣṭe 'abravīdidam
kāṣṭhakūṭa uvāca
mā śoke mana ādhatsva eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
devānāṃ ca ṛṣīṇāṃ ca yogināṃ ca mahātmanām
martyānāṃ kiṃ puno māto mā śucastaṃ tapodhanam
ahaṃ tenātmanātmā vai sṛṣṭaḥ svenaiva tejasā
paśya māṃ kṛtakṛtyaṃ tvaṃ gāyatrīvātmanaḥ sutam
vedāḥ sarve mayādhītāḥ sāṅgopāṅgāḥ savistarāḥ
tathopavedāḥ sarve ca adhyātmaṃ caiva kṛtsnaśaḥ
yat kiṃit puruṣairjñeyaṃ tat sarvaṃ jñānam eva ca
śrotavyaṃ ca śrutaṃ sarvam upāstāścāpi yoginaḥ
anenāpi prakarṣeṇa hṛṣyamāṇā mudānvitā
māṃ pālaya mahāsattve gāyatrīva sadā kratum
śrutvā tasya vacastadvai mātā tathyaṃ mahātmanaḥ
suyaśovāca
sarveṣāṃ prāṇinām etadvihitaṃ martyadharmiṇām
sa cāpi kṛtakṛtyaśca mahātmā tapasānvitaḥ
ātmānaṃ putra śocāmi yāhaṃ tena vinā kṛtā
tam evānu mṛtā nāsmi tavāgamanakāṃkṣiṇī
nārthā na bhogasvajanā na putrā naiva bāndhavāḥ
yoṣitāṃ tatra tiṣṭhanti patiryatrāvatiṣṭhate
patiryadi tataḥ sarvaṃ nāsti kiṃcit patiṃ vinā
sarvaṃ hi duḥkhadaṃ tāsāṃ yāsāṃ nāsti patiḥ suta
idaṃ ca me puno duḥkhaṃ yat tvāṃ tena sahādya vai
nābhinandāmi saṃhṛṣṭā sutaṃ śrīriva viṣṇunā
bahuśaḥ sa hi mām āha kāṣṭhakūṭa ihaiṣyati
kṛtavidyastatastasya varayiṣye snuṣāṃ śubhām
kāśyapasyodalasyeyaṃ sutā guṇavatī bhṛśam
tām ahaṃ varayiṣyāmi kāṣṭhakūṭasya suvratām
tadā drakṣyāmi taṃ putraṃ sapatnīkaṃ dṛḍhavratam
agnīṃścaivāhariṣyāmi patnīvantaṃ samīkṣya vai
patnyāḥ kadāhaṃ putrasya pāṇigrahaṇatoṣitaḥ
śubhāni manasā vācā vidhāsyāmi bahūnyapi
jīvau yathā tvāṃ paśyāvastacca naivābhavat tathā
yā tvāṃ paśyāmi putreha vinā tenāsatī punaḥ
tataḥ sā kurarī yadvadvinā patyā mahāyaśā
vilapya bahuduḥkhārtā papāta dharaṇītale
tāṃ kāṣṭhakūṭo duḥkhārtāṃ patitāṃ gatajīvitām
visaṃjñām agninā dagdhvā vilalāpa suduḥkhitaḥ
nanu tvayāhaṃ nirdiṣṭo gacchādhīṣveti hṛṣṭavat
so 'aham adyāgato 'adhītya kasmānmāṃ nābhibhāṣase
putro 'ahaṃ devadevādvai rudrāt kiṃ nābhibhāṣase
kiṃ mayāpakṛtaṃ tāta sahabhāryasya te 'anagha
yanmāṃ sahāmbayāgatya dṛḍhaṃ naivābhinandasi
arājakam idaṃ manye pitṛghnaṃ māṃ na hanti yat
saṃsthāpitaḥ samāśvaste nākarodudakakriyām
imāṃ pratijñāṃ cakre ca ṛṣimadhye mahātapāḥ
duṣkarāṃ sarvabhūtānām upaspṛśya kṛtāñjaliḥ
kāṣṭhaloṣṭhopalībhūto bhaviṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ
rudraṃ drakṣyāmi yāvacca yāvacca pitaraṃ tathā
sabhāryaṃ saṃprapaśyāmi tāvaccratam idaṃ mama
tataḥ sa ṛṣibhistaistu dṛśyamāno mahātapāḥ
maheśvaraṃ sadā dhyāyaṃstatraiva samatiṣṭhata
tuṣṭo dine 'aṣṭame vyāsa svayam evāha śaṃkaraḥ
kāṣṭhakūṭa prayacchāmi divyaṃ cakṣustavānagha
paśya māṃ tvaṃ suviśrabdham adṛśyaṃ yoginām api
brūhi putra varaṃ cāpi yaste hṛdi samāhitaḥ
tataḥ sa dṛṣṭvā deveśam udyantam iva bhāskaram
papāta pādayorhṛṣṭa idaṃ covāca susvaram
kāṣṭhakūṭa uvāca
jīvetāṃ tāvubhau deva etadicchāmyahaṃ varam
na tau śakyau puno jīvau kartum anyadvṛṇīṣva me
kāṣṭhakūṭa uvāca
śarīraṃ cenmṛtasyāsti tacchakyaṃ jīvitena hi
yādṛk ca sa pitā tubhyaṃ bhavāṃstādṛk śarīrataḥ
kāṣṭhakūṭa uvāca
śarīraṃ ca vinā dṛṣṭam utthānaṃ vai dhruvasya tu
na cāpi me śarīreṇa vinā tābhyāṃ ratiḥ prabho
tasmādgṛhāṇa deveśa śarīraṃ yadi manyase
tasyaivedaṃ tahādeva aṅgādaṅgaṃ samutthitam
prītātmā pratyuvācedaṃ yuyukṣustaṃ śubhena hi
parīkṣeyaṃ kṛtā putra tava dharmavṛtāṃ vara
pitṛbhaktyānayā samyak tuṣṭo 'asmi śṛṇu me vacaḥ
akṣayaścāvyayaścāpi jarāmṛtyuvivarjitaḥ
aiśvaryeṇa ca saṃyuktaḥ priyo me gaṇapo bhavān
kāṣṭhakūṭa iti khyātaḥ sarvayogabalānvitaḥ
ime ca ṛṣayaḥ sarva āśrame 'asmiṃstapasvinaḥ
tavaivānucarā bhūtvā bhaviṣyanti gaṇeśvarāḥ
akṣayāścāvyayāścaiva mahāyogabalānvitāḥ
aiśvaryeṇa ca tulyāste bhaviṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ
ayaṃ ca te pitā putra bhūmanyuḥ saha bhāryayā
jagāma mandaraṃ bhūyaḥ so 'apīṣṭaṃ deśam āvrajat
yavaddevī tapoyuktā pituḥ śikharam āsthitā
ya idaṃ devadevasya ceṣṭitaṃ śṛṇuyānnaraḥ
śrāvayīta dvijān vāpi na sa durgatim āpnuyāt
nityam etadadhīyānaḥ śuciḥ prayatamānasaḥ
ya imaṃ bahupāpanāśanaṃ paramaṃ rudrasamīpayojanam
paṭhate ca gaṇaprasādhanaṃ sa mṛto yāti na dīnasaṃbhavam
iti skandapurāṇe kāṣṭhakūṭamahābhāgyaṃ nāma
dvipañcāśo 'adhyāyaḥ
tripañcāśattamo adhyāyaḥ
vyāsa uvāca
kathaṃ labdhavatī cāpi varaṃ varaśatāraṇiḥ
śṛṇu kāle vyatīte hi tapo devyāḥ suduścaram
prayatā prāñjalirbhūtvā samādhāya manastathā
tasthau vṛkṣāvabaddheva dārvarcānimiṣekṣaṇā
ekapādordhvabāhuśca nirucchvāsā babhūva ha
vyāghradvitīyā rudrāṇī tapoyuktā śubhavratā
pūrvavacca hi sā devī tapaso vāvatiṣṭatha
tasyāstapaḥprabhāveṇa sarvaṃ sasthāṇujaṅgamam
nātidīpto 'abhavat sūryasścandramā na prakāśate
jyotīṃṣi timirāṇi āsan vyomni siddhā na yānti ca
dhūmāyanti diśaḥ sarvāstrailkoyaṃ caiva kṛtsnaśaḥ
vidyādhṛtāṃ gatirbhagnā prajvalanti āyudhāni ca
mṛgā vyāghrāśca siṃhāśca viḍālolūkamūṣikāḥ
pannagā nakulāścaiva ekasthāḥ saṃcarantyuta
kāraṇaṃ mahadatrāsti nedaṃ niṣkāraṇaṃ bhavet
kiṃ tiṣṭhāmaḥ samudvignā gacchāma brahmaṇo 'antikam
ityuktvā te surāḥ sarve bṛhaspatipurogamāḥ
vairājabhavanaṃ gatvā brahmāṇaṃ saṃpraṇemire
pūjitā brahmaṇā samyagupaviṣṭā yathārhataḥ
pṛṣṭāstenāgame hetum ūcurhṛcchokapīḍitāḥ
teṣāṃ tad vacanaṃ śrutvā bhītānāṃ sarvayogavit
uvāca madhuraṃ ślakṣṇam idaṃ gambhīravadvacaḥ
eṣā haimavatī devī rudrāṇī lokadhāriṇī
tapaścarati yuktātmā yogam āsthāya niścalam
adya varṣasahasraṃ hi divyaṃ tasyāḥ samādhinā
