tānutthitān vīkṣya sahasraśo 'anye kuṭhāravajrāśaniśūlahastāḥ
pradudruvuḥ śaṃkarakiṃkarāṇāṃ balaṃ samuddhūtamahārṇavābham
samāgamastatra punarbabhūva gaṇāsurāṇām atibhīmanādaḥ
yugātyate mārutavejitānāṃ yathā samudyoga ivārṇavānām
ṣaṭcatvāriṃśottaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
saptacatvāriṃśaduttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
utthāpiteṣu daityeṣu bhārgaveṇograkarmaṇā
nedurdevāḥ sagandharvā dānavāśca sahāndhakāḥ
tataḥ śaṅkharavonmiśrā māḍukānakanisvanāḥ
babhūvuḥ siṃhanādāśca rathahastiravaiḥ saha
huṇḍatuhuṇḍau jambhaśca kujambhaśca mahāsuraḥ
śailaśūlaśilāghātairyuyudhurdevatārayaḥ
mamarduḥ pramathānīkaṃ vairaṃ praticikīrṣayā
teṣāṃ vegaṃ saṃnivārya pramathā api darpitāḥ
śilātarukarāḥ sarve dānavānabhidudruvuḥ
gaṇeśvarāḥ surāṇāṃ tu tasmin yuddhe 'atibhairave
śrūyante dhanuṣāṃ śabdā rathaśabdāśca bhairavāḥ
pramathānāṃ jaye saktā dānavānāṃ tathāpare
cakruḥ kolāhalaṃ ghoraṃ pakṣavādāṃstathāmbare
garjatāṃ dhāvatāṃ caiva balānāṃ samabhūt svanaḥ
garjatāṃ dhāvatāṃ caiva samudrāṇām ivātyaye
yuddhātiśayamattāśca siddhagandharvacāraṇāḥ
neduścaivotsasarjuśca nānākusumasaṃcayān
nānāvidhāni puṣpāṇi patamānāni rejire
siddhacāraṇamuktāni nakṣatrāṇi yathātyaye
yuddhasaṃsaktabhāvānāṃ viremuśca punaḥ punaḥ
tam āpatantaṃ dṛṣṭvā tu dānavaṃ jambham āhave
utkṣipya dānavaṃ yuddhe tatāḍa sa vināyakaḥ
śṛṅgayoracalendrasya taḍitvāniva cāmnudaḥ
sa śarāroṣitamanā vidhūya saśiraḥkaram
vināyakaṃ śarairugrairavatastāra roṣitaḥ
śalabhā iva kedāraṃ bhramarā iva pādapam
rudhiraṃ kṣaramāṇāste trivittrairdāritānanās
śarā vināyake rejuḥ sarpā merum ivāśritāḥ
dhunvan karāgraṃ ca śiraśca devo dudrāva jambhaṃ tṛṣito yathāmbhaḥ
sa taṃ karāgreṇa dṛḍhaṃ dṛḍhena muhuḥ samāhatya muhurvinadya
rathaṃ gṛhītvā balavāṃstadājau cikṣepa sāśvadhvajaśastracakram
soddhūtabhagnātipatākaketuścyutāsiśaktyṛṣṭisahasrabāṇaḥ
patīṣyamāṇaṃ tu rathaṃ vihāya prahrādirindrāmbudharaprabhāvaḥ
sa tāṃ saghaṇṭāṃ kanakāvadātāṃ kṛśānulekhām iva dīpyamānām
vināyakāyāsurarājaputraścikṣepa śaktiṃ samudīrṇaśaktiḥ
sā khāt patantī bhujagāṅganeva śastrāṅganā prajvalamānavaktrā
śarāhatā viṭpatinā papāta śaktiryathāgryā puruṣe hatāśe
āścaryabhūte pramathāsurāṇāṃ tasmiṃstathā vartati yuddhayajñe
amarṣito bhārgavakarma dṛṣṭvā śilādaputro 'abhyagamanmaheśam
gaṇeśvarāṇāṃ raṇakarma deva devaiḥ sahendrairapi duṣkaraṃ yat
tadbhārgaveṇādya kṛtaṃ vṛthā naḥ saṃjīvayānena hi dānavendrān
ete hi te dānavayūthapālā yamālayādadya punarnivṛttāḥ
vidrāvayantaḥ pramathāṃścaranti nāgānivājau śarabhāḥ sadarpāḥ
jayaḥ kuto vai bhavitā maheśa gaṇeśvarāṇāṃ kuta eva śāntiḥ
vakrasthitaścaiṣa na caiṣa vadhyo 'ayudhyamāno vṛṣavāha śukraḥ
naivābhināśo 'asti tava prasādāddhataṃ ca taṃ tvaṃ kuruṣe prasādam
ityevam uktaḥ pramatheśvareṇa nandīśvareṇeśvaradevadevaḥ
uvāca devaḥ prahasaṃstadānīṃ sa nandinaṃ sarvagaṇeśanāyakam
madhyāt samutpāṭya tam ānayasva yathopahāraṃ dhanavān namuṣyaḥ
sa evam ukto vṛṣabhadhvajena vṛṣadhvajo vai vṛṣasiṃhanādaḥ
jagāma tūrṇaṃ pravigāhya senāṃ yatrābhavadbhārgavavaṃśadīpaḥ
taṃ rakṣamāṇaṃ ditinandanaistaiḥ pāśāsivṛkṣopalaśūlahastaiḥ
vikṣobhya daityān vṛṣarāḍjahāra śukraṃ sa nandī śarabho yathebham
srastāmbaraṃ taṃ cyutabhūṣaṇaṃ ca vimuktakeśaṃ ripuṇā gṛhītam
vimokṣayiṣyanta ivābhyadhāvan surārayaḥ siṃharavān sṛjantaḥ
te vajraśūleṣuparaśvadhānāṃ sacakradaṇḍopalakampanānām
nandīśvarasyopari dānavendrā varṣaṃ vavarṣurjaladā ivogrāḥ
sa bhārgavaṃ prāpya gaṇādhipāgryo vaktrāgninā śastraśatāni dagdhvā
āyāt sa śukraṃ tu kare gṛhītvā nandīśvaro dānavayūthapālam
teṣāṃ ca teṣāṃ ca tato babhūva pramuktaśastrāstrasubhīmapātaḥ
jahīti gṛhṇeti ca vādināṃ vai mahāhavo devamanaḥpratoṣaḥ
tenāntareṇaitya bhavasya pārśvaṃ nandīśvaraḥ krodhavivarṇanetraḥ
ayaṃ sa śukro bhagavannitīśe nivedayāmāsa bhavāya śīghram
saptacatvāriṃśottaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
aṣṭacatvāriṃśaduttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
śukre 'atha śukrapatinā gīrṇe 'anneva bhujaṅginā
babhūvurdānavāḥ sarve daridrā iva niṣkriyāḥ
viśarīrā yathā jīvā garuḍā virayā iva
vihastā iva mātaṅgā viśṛṅgā iva govṛṣāḥ
nirviṣā iva nāgendrā nirvidyā iva ca dvijāḥ
sāgarā iva nistoyā vivegā iva mārutāḥ
payodā iva niḥśabdā viśikhā iva cāgnayaḥ
gatotsavā va divasā vipuṣpā iva pādapāḥ
hariṇā iva saṃtrastā vipakṣā iva pakṣiṇaḥ
grahā iva praśāntābhā grāhā iva jaloddhṛtāḥ
nandināpahṛte śukre gīrṇe cāpi kapardinā
dānavā jajñire śūrā dīnamānaparākramāḥ
vaimanasyaṃ paraṃ prāpto dānavānāṃ raṇe 'andhakaḥ
uvāca meghaninadaḥ saṃyugasthaḥ sa dānavaḥ
vikramya nandinā śukraṃ nayatā nayināṃ varam
hṛtāni no 'adya sarveṣāṃ jīvitāni na saṃśayaḥ
bhārgavaṃ tam ṛte śukraṃ ko 'anyo no dhārayiṣyati
dhairyaṃ ca vikramastejaḥ sattvaṃ vīryaṃ balaṃ dhṛtiḥ
śatrubhirno hṛtaṃ sarvaṃ deve śukre 'apavāhite
na tvahaṃ saṃyugaṃ jahyāṃ pramathaiḥ samabhidrutaḥ
sūdayiṣyāmyahaṃ sarvān pramathān saha nandinā
adyaitān vivaśān kṛtvā hatvā ca tridaśānapi
bhārgavaṃ mokṣayiṣyāmi pañjarasthaṃ yathā harim
śarīrānniṣkramet tasya asmākaṃ śeṣapālinaḥ
ityandhakavacaḥ śrutvā dānavā meghanardanāḥ
pramathānardayāmāsurmartavyakṛtaniścayāḥ
tatra ṣāṇāśivajraughaiḥ kaṭaṅkaṭaśilopalaiḥ
kārmukāṇāṃ vikṛṣṭānāṃ visṛṣṭānāṃ ca patriṇām
nipātyatām asīnāṃ ca śabdo 'abhūdbhṛśadāruṇaḥ
bhagnadhvajapatākāni kṣīṇapraharaṇāni ca
rudhirāsrāvacitrāṇi vraṇākusumitāni ca
pipāsitāni śrāntāni hatavājigajāni ca
satūṇīrapatākena aṅkuśāroṣitena ca
jambho dānavaśārdūlaḥ abhidudrāva nandinam
kṛṣṇāparvataśṛṅgasthaḥ sabalāka ivāmbudaḥ
stabdhalāṅgūladṛkkarṇaḥ prasāritamahākaraḥ
turaṅgā ye ca mātaṅgāḥ pramathā ye ca dānavāḥ
tasya mārgādapakrāntā mṛtyoriva yathā narāḥ
taṃ mattanāgaṃ dhāvantaṃ nadantam iva nīradam
vārayāmāsa balavān vikramya sa vināyakaḥ
athāśvasya ca viśramya saṃvartyātmakaraṃ karī
vināyakam urodeśe tāḍayāmāsa nardayan
sa vindhyakūṭakalpena tena nāgena tāḍitaḥ
nāsayā sa gṛhītvā taṃ nāsāyāṃ dānavadvipam
ākṣipya pātayāmāsa girivarṣmā vināyakaḥ
taṃ nāgaṃ pātayānaṃ tu nāgavaktram asṛksravam
bibheda tomareṇāśu kareṇārka ivāmbudam
mocayantaṃ tu caraṇau grīvāyāṃ dānavottamam
tenaiva tomareṇātha ājaghāna vināyakaḥ
punaścāsya vadhākāṅkṣī asiṃ jagrāha vīryavān
taṃ cāpi suvikṛṣṭena śareṇāsṛgbhujā tadā
sa dṛḍhābhihatastena ghūrṇitaḥ sālavṛkṣavat
airāvata ivābhāti balodvṛtto vināyakaḥ
vyaṃsastaṃ dhāvamānaṃ tu kujambhavadhakāṅkṣiṇam
vavāra sa gato 'aṃsena pātayāmāsa taṃ kṣitau
vyaṃsam aṃsena hatvā tu nāgavaktro mahābalaḥ
tribhiḥ prahāraiḥ sa babhau śoṇitākto vināyakaḥ
dharāyāṃ nāsayādāya kujambhaṃ tu vināyakaḥ
pracikṣepa mahāvīryo yathā bhūtabaliṃ naraḥ
so 'ardito dānavaśatairnānāyudhavitakṣitaḥ
cacāra devo daityeṣu pṛṣateṣu yathā hariḥ
sa dantaiścaraṇaiścāpi śuṇḍayātatayāpi ca
mamarda dānavān kruddhaḥ kuñjaro naḍvalāniva
tato gaṇeśā hyapi vīkṣya dānavairvināyakaṃ śastraśataiḥ parikṣatam
gṛhītaśastrā gajasiṃhavikramā vimuktarāvāḥ śataśo 'abhidudruvuḥ
tataḥ punaḥ śastrasahasravejitaṃ śarāsiśaktyṛṣṭinipātaduḥsaham
gaṇāsurāṇām asunāśanaṃ mahadbabhūva yuddhaṃ hatavājikuñjaram
aṣṭacatvāriṃśottaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
ūnapañcāśaduttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
nigīrṇo brāhmaṇaḥ so 'atha candrāvayavadhāriṇā
kathaṃ ca tapasāṃ śreṣṭho yogī yogena sa dvijaḥ
na niḥsṛto yogabalāddevadehānmahātapāḥ
andhakaścāsuraśreṣṭhaḥ sa tadā bhārgavaṃ vinā
cakāra katham āvāpaṃ gaṇeśaiḥ samabhidrutaḥ
kathayasva na me tṛptiḥ śṛṇvānasyeśaceṣṭitam
sūta uvāca
nigīrṇe bhārgave tena bhūtomādevabandhunā
dṛṣṭvā svasainyaṃ pramathairbhajyamānaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
dudrāva ratham āsthāya svayam evāndhako gaṇān
pramathāḥ petira vanyāṃ nistoyā iva toyadāḥ
kroḍeṣūrukapoleṣu pṛṣṭhabāhūdareṣu ca
ruruvurbāṇanirbhinnāḥ pramathāḥ kuñjarā yathā
yāntam āyāntam aprāptaṃ prāptaṃ dūrastham eva ca
apaśyadyaṃ yatastaṃ taṃ nirbibheda śarairbhṛśam
sahasraṃ ca sahasreṇa koṭiṃ koṭyā tathaiva ca
dhvajāḥ patākāśchitrāṇi vaijayantyo 'aṅkuśāḥ kuthāḥ
cāmarāṇi kirīṭāni kuṇḍalānyambarāṇi ca
tat sarvaṃ cicchide tūrṇaṃ śarairandhakadānavaḥ
visphuliṅgān yathaivāgnirdhārāsārān yathāmbudaḥ
sindhurājo yathodgārān karāniva divākaraḥ
nādān siṃhā ivāraṇye sīkarāniva kuñjarāḥ
mumoca bāṇāṃstīkṣṇāgrān parasainyavimardanān
nivātakavacā ye te anyonyasadṛśā bhṛśam
kāleyāḥ ṣaṣṭisāhasrāḥ kālakalpā mahāsurāḥ
bāhujaiḥ ṣaṣṭisāhasraiḥ pramathairyuyudhuḥ saha
prahrādaścānuhrādaśca saṃhrādaḥ śinibāṣkalau
virocano balirbāṇaḥ kujambho 'athāvaniṃjayaḥ
ekādaśaite prakhyātā ekādaśaraviprabhāḥ
ekādaśaiva pramathānardayan kalahaiṣiṇaḥ
prabhāmayaṃ vīrabhadraṃ viṭpatiṃ piṅgalaṃ tathā
vegapaṃ pavanādaṃ ca somārkāpyāyanāvapi
saṃvarttakānalaṃ caiva pāvakāpyāyanāvapi
yakṣo 'annadaśca balavān vidyutkeśaśca rākṣasaḥ
vihastaśastrakavacāvṛtāḥ śastraśatācitāḥ
dvārapālāśca rudrāṇāṃ rudrāṇāṃ ye ca sūnavaḥ
skandapāriṣadā ye ca ye ca śaktigaṇeśvarāḥ
te danostanayaiḥ sārdhaṃ danoḥ putrānvayāśca ye
cakruḥ kṛtāntasadṛśāḥ kalahaṃ kalahapraiyāḥ
tasmiṃstathā vartati samprahāre viśīrṇahārābharaṇasragastraiḥ
vyāviddhavastrā vikasatsunetrā neduḥ surāḥ siddhagaṇāśca khasthāḥ
ūnapañcāśaduttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
pañcāśaduttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
vyāsa uvāca
māyāvīryaṃ ca vīryaṃ ca andhakasyāmaradviṣaḥ
sṛṣṭaṃ bhagavatā samyagdevarūpanimittajam
nigīrṇo yasya devena śarīre bhārgavo muniḥ
kathaṃ tu kṛtavāṃstatra devadevaśarīragaḥ
kathaṃ ca tapaso vīryādyogavīryācca sa dvijaḥ
śvetābhrādiva vai candro niḥsṛto bhṛgunandanaḥ
kathayeśānacaritaṃ bhārgavasya ca dhīmataḥ
sūta uvāca
sa lokānagnivarṇābhān rudrakoṭiśatairvṛtān
kundenduśaṅkhavarṇānāṃ daṃṣṭriṇāṃ nakhinām api
dīrghalāṅgūlajuṣṭānāṃ sadarpāṇāṃ kṣamāvatām
jvalanaprabhakeśānāṃ nandyāvartakadhāriṇām
kiṃśukaprabhajihvānāṃ kailāsagirivarṣmaṇām
agnibandhanabaddhānāṃ siṃhānāṃ bhīmarūpiṇām
surāṃśca sendrān sādityān sāpsarogaṇamānavān
gaṇeśāsurayuddhaṃ ca so 'apaśyaddharadehagaḥ
varṣāṇāṃ tu śataṃ kakṣau bhramamāṇo bhavasya saḥ
na tasya dadṛśe chidraṃ śuceriva yathā kaliḥ
atha śabdo mahān āsīt pramathāsurasainyayoḥ
taṃ śrutvā śabdam āvigno bhārgavaḥ pratibodhitaḥ
tuṣṭāveṣṭaiḥ stavairdevaṃ somaṃ somavibhūṣaṇam
āpadbhāvaṃ prapannasya tasya devena śūlinā
liṅgena niṣkamasveti prasādābhyudayaḥ kṛtaḥ
sūkṣmarūpastato bhūtvā sa śukro munisattamaḥ
śukravan niḥsṛto liṅgāddevadevasya dhīmataḥ
śakravanniḥsṛto yasmācchiśnādbhārgavanandanaḥ
tasmācchukra iti khyātiṃ gato gatimatāṃ varaḥ
viveśa dānavānīkaṃ meghānīkaṃ śaśī yathā
taṃ dṛṣṭvā candrasaṃkāśaṃ candrodayanibhodayam
candrodaye yathā nRṇāṃ prītirāsīt suradviṣām
te dṛṣṭvā danudaiteyāḥ śukraṃ candrasamaprabham
sarve siṃharavāṃścakruḥ samprahṛṣṭā yuyutsavaḥ
nihatā dānavā ye tu pramathairjitakāśibhiḥ
tān āgatān mṛtyumukhān menire bhārgavāgamāt
vavandustaṃ nananduśca praseduśca mahāsurāḥ
śukrodayamudaṃ lebhe sa dānavamahārṇavaḥ
atha śākho viśākhaśca chāgavaktraścaturmukhaḥ
nandī ca somanandī ca nandiṣeṇaśca vīryavān
ghaṇṭākarṇaḥ śaṅkukarṇaḥ kuṇḍodaramahodarau
saṃvartakānalorvau ca yaśodīpto vibhākaraḥ
vegapaśca śikhaṇḍī ca tāmracūḍaśca kukkuṭaḥ
annadaḥ piṅgalo yakṣaḥ piṅgalaśca vaṭuḥ paṭuḥ
vidyutkeśaḥ sukeśaśca rākṣasau cāparājitau
ete cānye ca gaṇapā lokapālasamatviṣaḥ
viviśurdānavānīkaṃ śukrodayasamuddhatam
atha vāditraśabdāstu suṃhanādaravaiḥ saha
babhūvuḥ senayorugrāḥ sarvabhūtaprakampanāḥ
nandīśvaraṃ puraskṛtya kārttikeyaṃ ca ṣaṇmukham
mṛdranti pramathā daityān sarpāṃstārkṣya ivāhave
asipātāvalūnāgrā muśalāhatamastakāḥ
dānavāḥ śerate bhūmau vajrabhinnā ivācalāḥ
rirṅguḥ samare daityāḥ sarpāstārkṣyārditā iva
bhagnatrikorujaghanā ghanabāṇāvapīḍitāḥ
daityā viniṣṭananti ārttā yoyapūrṇā ivāmbudāḥ
tasmin gaṇapadaityānāṃ mathane bhṛśadāruṇe
babhūva pūrṇā daityānāṃ dharā dyauriva nīradaiḥ
kirīṭairmukuṭairhārairvalayābharaṇāṅgadaiḥ
pārihāryaiḥ sa keyūraiḥ śroṇīsūtraiḥ sakuṇḍalaiḥ
raktakuṅkumacitrāṅgī nānābharaṇabhūṣaṇā
dhanāḍhyā strīrivābhāti tatra tatra raṇāvaniḥ
siṃhānām iva dṛptānāṃ hastinām api vā yathā
utsāho 'abhūdgaṇeśānāṃ dānavān sampramardatām
te hanyamānāśaraṇā bhayārttāḥ śaraṇārthinaḥ
pramathairanubaddhāśca dānavāḥ sāgaraṃ śritāḥ
dṛṣṭvā tadrecitaṃ sainyaṃ dānavaiḥ pramathārditaiḥ
praviṣṭeṣu ca daityeṣu sāgaraṃ makarālayam
bhārgavaḥ sumahātejā yathāgniriva mūrchitaḥ
sa samudrālayān daityāñchaśāpa kupito bhṛśam
yasmāt sahāyānutsṛjya māṃ cāpi pitṛvaddhitam
prāṇatrāṇārtham abalāḥ praviṣṭāḥ stha payonidhim
tasmāt tatraiva nirhrīkā mama śāpaparikṣatāḥ
mīnabhāvam anuprāptā jātājātā bhaviṣyatha
yāvallokā bhaviṣyanti parvatāśca sasāgarāḥ
tāvadyūyaṃ jale matsyā bhaviṣyatha jalecarāḥ
naramāṃsāśanāḥ pāpā narabhakṣyā bhaviṣyatha
kṣapayiṣyatha macchāpaṃ varṣakoṭīśatānyuta
iti śāpahatāñcheṣān kṛtvārṇavajalaukasaḥ
virarāma mahātejāḥ śukraścandrasamadyutiḥ
tataste vārdhitoyeṣu guruśāpahatāsurāḥ
sāyudhāḥ satanutrāśca dṛśyante daṃśitāśca ha
uvāca pāṇinā spṛśya jīvayanniva taṃ girā
mā bhaistvaṃ dānavaśreṣṭha pratiyudhyasva śatruṣu
ahaṃ tvāṃ dhārayiṣyāmi āhāra iva jīvitam
ityevam uktaḥ śukreṇa so 'andhako dānaveśvaraḥ
tataḥ praviṣṭeṣvasureṣu sāgaraṃ nihanyamāneṣu ca śaṅkarānugaiḥ
dadhāra sarvān pramathāṃstadāndhako nadīnadān bhūrijalo yathārṇavaḥ
viśākaśākhau daśabhiḥ śatena ca sa naigameṣaṃ pratutoda dānavaḥ
sa vīrabhadraṃ ca tathā ca viṭpatiṃ prabhāmayaṃ yakṣavaraṃ ca piṅgalam
bibheda bāṇaistapanīyabhūṣaṇairyathāṅkuśāgrairiva hastipo gajam
śarān na yo dhārayate 'andhakeritān pradīptakālānalasūryasannibhān
vivṛścitāścandanavadgaṇeśvarā bhujodare vakṣasi mūrdhni cāsakṛt
tato 'asuraiḥ siṃharavāstadā kṛtāḥ saśaṅkhabherīśatadundubhotkaṭāḥ
punaśca yuddhaṃ prababhau bhayānakaṃ gaṇeśvarāṇāṃ saha dānaveśvaraiḥ
pañcāśaduttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
ekapañcāśaduttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
tridaśādhipatiṃ śakram ityuvāca pitāmahaḥ
asau vikṛṣṭacāpaśca sendrāyudhaghanopamaḥ
sṛjatīṣumayaṃ varṣam andhakaḥ kṣapayan ripūn
kṣamamāṇā hyatiṣṭhadhvaṃ kasmādetat parājayam
jitvā hyeṣa gaṇān sarvānandhako dānaveśvaraḥ
asmākam api mūlāni nirmūlāni kariṣyati
tadyāvadeṣa no bāṇaiḥ pramathān nayati kṣayam
tāvadeva vayaṃ pārṣṇiṃ gṛhṇāma kṛttivāsasaḥ
svayambhuvacanaṃ śrutvā balavṛtanibarhaṇaḥ
gṛhītavarmaśastrāstrāḥ śīghraṃ śighraparākramāḥ
sāhāyyaṃ karavāmādya gaṇānāṃ yudhyatāṃ raṇe
pūṣāryamā bhago mitro yamaśca ravinandanaḥ
aṃśastvaṣṭā jayaścaiva jayantaścaiva śakrajaḥ
maruto vasavaḥ sādhyāstathāśvigarudoragāḥ
tuṣitāścaiva lekhāśca viśvedevāśca guhyakāḥ
gandharvāścaiva yakṣāśca ye cānye devapakṣiṇaḥ
atha dundubhiśabdāśca siṃhanādāśca bhairavāḥ
babhūvurdevasainyeṣu pramathānāṃ priyaṃkarāḥ
devaiḥ patadbhistat sainyaṃ dānavānāṃ viloḍitam
prabhūtamīnaṃ kṣīṇāmbu rājahaṃsairyathā saraḥ
tato halahalāśabdaḥ saṃjajñe 'atīvabhairavaḥ
devatādhyuṣite sainye dānavānāṃ samākule
janyate dānavānīkam ajā vṛkaśatairiva
okāra iva vedānāṃ teṣām āsīt puraḥsaraḥ
duritāni tu sarvāṇi prāyaścittānalo yathā
uavāca krodharāgāndho dānavān dānavādhipaḥ
utpādya vairaṃ rudreṇa sarvalokābhirakṣaṇā
na śakyaṃ pramathāñjetum anirviṇṇaiḥ sahāmarān
maraṇācca na bhetavyaṃ yudhyadhvaṃ daityadānavāḥ
bhārgavastiṣṭhati hyeṣa yo naḥ saṃjīvayiṣyati
tat prāṇeṣvadayanto vai yūyaṃ devagaṇeśvarān
yathābalaṃ yathotsāhaṃ vārayadhvam aśaṅkitāḥ
māyābhiretān bahvībhirgūḍābhirgūḍharūpiṇaḥ
cakrurghorāṇi kalpānte nīradā iva
dhanuḥśabdān prakurvāṇāḥ siṃhanādaravāṃstathā
vikṛṣya tu mahācāpaṃ sāgarāmbudanardanaḥ
taṃ dānavednraṃ durvāraṃ dhāvamāna
vārayāmāsa śailādrirdharmacittam ivāśubham
gāḍhaṃ vidāritastena dānavena gaṇeśvaraḥ
saṃjughūrṇa tadā nandī vāyununno yathādrumaḥ
ghūrṇamāno babhau nandī mṛṣṭakuṇḍalabhūṣaṇaḥ
calatpallavapuṣpāḍhyo yathāśokatarustathā
tataścirāt samāśvasya suyaśāḥ suyaśāpatiḥ
hasatastasya netrābhyāṃ subhrūbhyām aśrubindavaḥ
nyasravanta yathārkasya kiraṇā dīptamaṇḍalāt
taṃ dhāvamānam ākāśe tarumārutavījitāḥ
tam apyasyāndhako bāṇaiścārukāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥ
cakarta dhartā lokānāṃ ditigarbhaṃ yathāhihā
vṛkṣe kṛtte tato nandī samṛgavyālapannagam
mandarāgraṃ samutpāṭya dudrāvāndhakam āhave
girikūṭaṃ tu taṃ nandī girikūṭavanālayaḥ
sa rathastena śṛṅgeṇa nandinā dṛḍham āhataḥ
sacakrakūbarahayaḥ pāṃsusāyujyam āgamat
tato 'andhakarathaṃ dṛṣṭvā sacakrākṣaṃ vicūrṇitam
nedurdevāḥ sagandharvāḥ pramathāśca saguhyakāḥ
nandinaṃ tāḍayāmāsa gajendra iva pādapam
triśūlidayitastena triśūlenābhitāḍitaḥ
nandīśvare ghūrṇamāne prahāreṇa bhṛśārdite
asurāṇāṃ bale jajñe simhanādaravo muhuḥ
siṃhanādena śatrūṇāṃ tena nandī prabodhitaḥ
paraśvadhahato raktaṃ cakṣarāndhakadānavaḥ
andhakaṃ virathaṃ dṛṣṭvā rarakṣuramaradviṣaḥ
āśāsvavasthitā devāsyathā lokam imaṃ tathā
atha bāṇo baleḥ putro bāṇapuṣpasamaprabhaḥ
sa taṃ rathaṃ dānavendra āruroha tadāndhakaḥ
yathodayaṃ tu bhagavān dinakṛt pūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ
dvipañcāśaduttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
viṣṇum ardayamānaṃ tu dānavān dānavārdanam
jambho 'ambuda ivārāvaṃ kṛtvā dudrāva dānavaḥ
na sa saṃvivije devaḥ siṃho dṛṣṭveva kuñjaram
kujambhaścaiva jambhaśca yavīyān dānavācalaḥ
anantam antaṃ śatrūṇām āvavāra rarāsa ca
vṛtro 'añjanagiriprakhyaḥ saṃvarttakanikāśadṛk
jighṛkṣurabhyagādidraṃ nadamānaḥ payodavat
taṃ dhāvantaṃ nadantaṃ ca dānavaṃ śatalocanaḥ
kuhare girīsaṃkāśam ājaghāna purandaraḥ
bhāvayatyo gadāyodhī śatāyuṃ vāyum āhave
tuhuṇḍahuṇḍāvaśvibhyām ayudhyetāṃ mahāsurau
prahlādena bhagaḥ sārdham aṃśena ca virocanaḥ
aryamāṇaṃ yamaṃ caivāyudhyetāṃ bilvakelvalau
vipracittimukhā ye ca baliṣvagrā mahāsurāḥ
gaṇeśvarāṃste devāṃśca ayudhyanta sahasraśaḥ
tatakṣe vatsaradanaiḥ śaraiḥ kārmukaniḥsṛtaiḥ
so 'andhakena dṛḍhaṃ viddhaḥ śarairmarmavidāraṇaiḥ
rarāsa nandī saṃrabdhaḥ payoda iva saṃkṣaye
vajreṇa śatadhāreṇa so 'andhakasya gaṇeśvaraḥ
cūrṇayāmāsa turagān niyantāraṃ rathaṃ tathā
tato 'andhakaṃ karṇamūle kuṇḍalālakaśobhite
ājaghāna ghanārāvo varadaścārukuṇḍalaḥ
pātito nandinaḥ kroḍe kuñjareṇeva saṃyuge
apāsarpat padānyaṣṭau tānyevāpatitaḥ punaḥ
sa tena suprahāreṇa dānavaṃ prati roṣitaḥ
vajreṇa śatadhāreṇa khaṇḍaśaḥ pracakāra ha
bāhupāśena caivainaṃ baddhvā bhūtapatiḥ svayam
iyeṣa bhūmau niṣpeṣṭum andhakaścāvamocayat
sa mocayitvā hi ātmānaṃ māyām āsthāya mohanīm
abhidudrāva śailādiṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cocivān
tam āpatantaṃ vegena gaṇeśvaramahattarāḥ
nandiṣeṇaḥ somanandī śaṅkukarṇo mahodaraḥ
ghaṇṭākarṇo vīrabhadraḥ sa ca devaḥ prabhāmayaḥ
bhartāram abhirakṣantasteṣāṃ pāriṣadāgragāḥ
andhakaṃ yodhayanti sma siṃhāḥ śakragajaṃ yathā
taṃ nandiṣeṇaḥ śūlena somanandī ca muṣṭinā
śareṇa vīrabhadraśca ghaṇṭākarṇo 'asināpi ca
śaṅkukarṇaścalāgreṇa pādapena prabhāmayaḥ
nandīśvarastu gaṇapo gaṇapairvimukhīkṛtam
ājaghānottamāṅge tu andhakaṃ dānavādhipam
dṛṣṭvāsurapatiṃ devairgaṇapaiḥ samabhidrutam
asurāṇāṃ bale jajñe dhāva gṛhṇeti nisvanaḥ
tān yuddhāyāgatāneko viṣṇuḥ sarvānadīdharat
cakrahastaṃ tu dṛṣṭvaivaṃ vikrāntaṃ raṇamūrdhani
vyāyacchamānaṃ niśceṣṭaṃ pradhāvantaṃ pragarjitam
yaṃ yataḥ paśyate 'asau vai taṃ taṃ vivyādha sāyakaiḥ
pṛthavaḥ pītaniśitā garuḍāṅgaruhandharāḥ
andhakasya śarā ghorāścyavante dhanuṣo 'akṣayāḥ
mukheṣu dantaveṣṭeṣu udareṣu kareṣu ca
devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ cānye nandinaṃ cāpare gaṇāḥ
anye śākhaṃ viśākhaṃ ca kumāram api cāpare
vyapāśritya sthitā devāḥ śakuntā iva pādapān
yathāśanibhayānmartyā yathā siṃhabhayānmṛgāḥ
yathā ca garuḍānnityaṃ bhujagā bhujagāśinaḥ
vitresuḥ surajālārttā mūḍhā iva ca babhramuḥ
tathā vraṇajasiktāṅgaṃ tadbabhau pārṣadaṃ balam
kampante pādapā yadvat kānaneṣvanileritāḥ
tathāndhakabhayāddevāḥ santrastā raṇamūrdhani
tato nārāyaṇo 'ananta ūrjitaḥ śakra eva ca
aśvinau vasavaścāṣṭau ādityā dvādaśaiva ca
nandī viśākhaḥ śākhaśca vīrabhadraḥ prabhāmayaḥ
viṭpatiḥ śaṅkukarṇaśca somanandī vināyakaḥ
dudruvuḥ sāyudhā devāstaṃ dānavagaṇādhipam
cakrāyudhaṃ sa cakreṇa śakraṃ vajreṇa dānavaḥ
muṣṭinā nandinaṃ caiva paṭṭiśena prabhāmayam
bhallena caiva pūṣāṇaṃ gadayā yamam eva ca
āhatya vairiṇastūrṇaṃ sarvāneva raṇe 'andhakaḥ
sa kūṭayodhī kūṭāni girīṇāṃ girisannibhaḥ
avirāmam aviśrāmaṃ nirucchvāsaṃ bhayākulam
chinnanāsākṣidantauṣṭhā bhagnapādakaṭīkarāḥ
uttrastodbhrāntacakitā dṛśyante pramathāmarāḥ
saudhāgraśṛṅgopalaśastravarṣī muhuḥ sṛjan bhātyasuro 'ambarasthaḥ
tā me
śabdam
abjaṃ mahaddhūmalatāvṛtaṃ ca khadyotatulyaṃ ca mahāgnicūrṇam
tripañcāśaduttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
tataḥ suparṇapuṅkhināṃ suparṇapatrapatriṇām
suparṇatulyapātināṃ suparṇatuṅgatuṇḍinām
śataṃ śarīrabhedināṃ śarīrasārabhojinām
dhanuḥ prapūriteritā raṇapracāritairvṛtāḥ
svamārgayānadeśikā jave manonilopamāḥ
yathā divākareritāḥ karā mahācaleṣviva
śarāhatāśca kuñjarāḥ śarāhatāśca vājinaḥ
śarāhatāśca devatā gaṇeśvarāśca sarvataḥ
vinirgatāntraśoṇitā vikīrṇahārabhūṣaṇāḥ
vimuktakeśabandhanāḥ patanti gāḍhavedanāḥ
hayaṃ gajaṃ suraṃ yathā prapaśyate hi yaṃ yataḥ
yathā madāndhakuñjarapraṇaṣṭapādapaṃ vanam
mukheṣu kecidāhatā nirīkṣaṇeṣu cāpare
urodareṣu cāpare tathā hatāśca pṛṣṭhataḥ
śataghnayo yathācitāḥ śaraistathā marudgaṇāḥ
gaṇāśca bhīmavikramā na bhūmim āpurāhatāḥ
surāsuraiḥ pravartitā tato vraṇāmbuvāhinī
gajendranakrasaṃkulā rathāṅgacārukacchapā
kirīṭakūṭadardurā dhanurguṇābhitantukā
vikīrṇahāraśarkarā sitāmbarātipheninī
surāsuraiḥ pravartitā surāsurātudistarā
tato 'añjanāmudatviṣastaḍitprahāsahāsinaḥ
piśācayakṣarākṣasāḥ pipāsayātikarṣitāḥ
surā yathā varāmṛtaṃ papustathaiva śoṇitam
tadāndhake śarāhate maheṣuṇātha nandine
yuddhabhūmivarṇana tripañcāśaduttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
catuṣpañcāśaduttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
cukrudhurdānavā ghorāścaturviṃśatidarpitāḥ
prahlādaścānuhlādaśca saṃhlādaḥ śitivāṣkulau
tathā tuhuṇḍo huṇḍaśca śambhuḥ kārtasvanaḥ kubhaḥ
mayastārastārakākṣo vidyunmālī pramohanaḥ
ete 'amarṣavaśaṃ prāptāścaturviṃśatidānavāḥ
te 'añjanācalasaṃkāśāḥ kāñcanācalasannibham
nandinaṃ tāḍayāmāsuḥ śūlaśaktyṛṣṭipaṭṭiśaiḥ
nākṣubhyata tadā nandī nārttim āpanna ca vyathām
tato vikṛṣya bhagavān ātataṃ kārmukaṃ mahat
te bāṇamārganisrāvairdānavāḥ śoṇitakṣarāḥ
kṣaranta iva śailendrāstapanīyarasān babhuḥ
tatastoṣoddhato nandī śukreṇojjīvitaṃ punaḥ
jīvitasraṃsanaṃ prāpya sa dānavamahācalaḥ
śīrṇopalaḥ papātāśu vajrāhata ivācalaḥ
balirutpāṭya śailāgraṃ cikṣepoddiśya nandinaṃ
tat sadhātumṛgavyālaṃ sarkṣavṛkṣaṃ girestaṭam
nirbhrāntopalavṛkṣālam abhyadhāvadgaṇeśvaram
śṛṅgasya balimuktasya tasya vyālādayo javāt
apakrāntānayārttasya puruṣasyeva bāndhavāḥ
tadāpatat tadgiryagraṃ nandī bāṇena vīryavān
tadvidārya gireḥ śṛṅgaṃ giriśṛṅganiketanaḥ
so 'abhyāhato gaṇeśena prāhlāditanayo vaśaḥ
papāta sahasā bhūmau vātāhata iva drumaḥ
jahuḥ sasamaramārāt taṃ dānavāḥ śarapīḍitāḥ
prasṛtāmbudasaṃkāśāṃstato 'ambudanibhākṛtiḥ
andhakaḥ khāt kṣitin prāpya dānavānidam abravīt
adya dākṣāyaṇīputrā nibodhadhvaṃ vaco mama
kuleṣu jātā vīrāśca sarvāstrakṛtaniścayāḥ
dravadhve vai kim uddiśya paṭunārācavejitāḥ
ekena nandinā bhagnāḥ śataśo 'atha sahasraśaḥ
hrīḥ kathaṃ vai na bhavati jalpatāṃ vo gṛhājire
prāśnikāḥ pārśvataḥ sthitvā nirvairā vītamatsarāḥ
ityandhakavacaḥ śrutvā sarve te dānavā raṇe
punarnivṛttā yuddhāya pragṛhītavarāyudhāḥ
andhakaḥ so 'abhyayānnandiṃ sārdhaṃ dānavapuṅgavaiḥ
śitāgrarukmavikṛtāḥ pṛthavaḥ priyadarśanāḥ
andhakasya dhanuḥsṛṣṭā niṣpatanti maheṣavaḥ
śalabhairiva kedārā bhramarairiva pādapāḥ
andhakena kṛtā devāḥ śataghnaya ivottamāḥ
yathā cāpratighāḥ sūktā niyataṃ brāhmaṇāśiṣaḥ
tathā te niśitā hyugrā brahmadaṇḍā ivodyatāḥ
anivāryā hyamoghāśca te 'andhakasya maheṣavaḥ
so 'api nityāyatadhanuḥ pariveṣīva bhāskaraḥ
asṛjadbāṇanikarān kiraṇān bhāskaro yathā
tasya bāṇarujaḥ prāpya nadītīra iva drumāḥ
sīdanti gaṇapāḥ sarve devāśca sahavāsavāḥ
sa viṣṇum ekena śareṇa viddhvā dvābhyām anantaṃ tribhireva śakram
yamaṃ ca somaṃ ca jalādhipaṃ ca vasūṃśca nirdārya rarāsa ghoram
aśvidvayaṃ cāpi śaradvayena viddhvā bhagāṃśāryamacandrapūṣṇaḥ
tato 'atha nandīśvaram ugrakarmā gaṇeśvarāṃścāpi śaraistatakṣa
tathā dahatyandhaka ātatāyī yathā pataṅgān bhagavān hutāśaḥ
nivāritāste śaradāritāśca tadāndhakenāmarayodhamukhyāḥ
na spandituṃ śekurudīkṣituṃ vā raṇe 'andhakaṃ khe manujā ivārkam
yaśāṃsi dīptāni tataḥ prahāya devāḥ sanārāyaṇadevapālāḥ
viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaścaiva ananto 'atha śatakratuḥ
ādityā vasavaḥ sādhyā aśvinau ca surottamau
tuṣitāścaiva viśvāśca devāścaiva svadhābhujaḥ
andhakena śarairbhagnā mārutena yathā drumāḥ
candramā bhagavān vahnirvittapālaśca rākṣasaḥ
andhakena raṇe bhagnāḥ śarairāśīviṣopamaiḥ
gandharvā guhyakāḥ sarpā garuḍāśca mahoragāḥ
viṭpatiḥ śaṅkukarṇaśca somanandī prabhāmayaḥ
piṅgalo nandiṣeṇaśca ghaṇṭākarṇo mahodaraḥ
vidyutkeśaḥ sukeśaśca sa ca devo vināyakaḥ
anye ca pramathāḥ śūrā vīrabhadrapurogamāḥ
andhakena raṇe bhagnāḥ śataśo 'atha sahasraśaḥ
catuṣpañcāśaduttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
pañcapañcāśaduttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
brahmaṇā sahitā jagmuḥ śaraṇyaṃ śūlapāṇinam
te praṇamya mahādevam idam ūcurbhayārditāḥ
mayā dattavaro yasmāt tasmādyūyaṃ vinirjitāḥ
krīḍārtham eva ca mayā saṃgare sa upekṣitaḥ
tato devaḥ smitaṃ kṛtvā pārśvasthaṃ śūlam aikṣata
devābhiprāyatattvajñaḥ śūlo jajvāla tatkṣaṇāt
tato 'andhakaṃ tadā bhittvā sa śūlastaṃ mahābalam
dānavendraṃ mahākāyam āninyeśaṅkarāntikam
patitāḥ puruṣā bhūtvā te 'apyayudhyanta duḥsahāḥ
nānāśastrapraharaṇāste 'apyayudhyan gaṇeśvaraiḥ
odyatapāṇayaḥ
jaghnuḥ kecidgaṇāneva dravataste mahābalāḥ
na teṣāṃ yudhyamānānāṃ kaścit tasthau gaṇeśvaraḥ
saṃgrāme dānavendrāṇāṃ bhayāt sarve pradudruvuḥ
tān dṛṣṭvā vidrutān sarvān gaṇān saha sureśvaraiḥ
vā vijñāpatyāmāsurājñāṃ no dātum arhasi
devadevastadā prāha sarvāsḥ praharaṇodyatāḥ
asṛgbindusamudbhūtān bhakṣayadhvaṃ mahāsurān
evam uktāstu tāḥ sarvā yogeśvaryo mahābalāḥ
hatvā hatvāsurān yuddhe cakhāduśca ma
devo 'api jvalitaṃ śūlam abravīdandhakāntakṛt
andhakaṃ paca sūryāgnau sahasraṃ śaradāṃ śatam
pūrṇe sahasre varṣāṇāṃ sāttvikaṃ bhāvam abhyagāt
lokānāṃ kāraṇaṃ devaṃ bubudhe govṛṣadhvajam
snāyvasthiśeṣastuṣṭāva devaṃ candrārdhamaulinam
saṃhāraheturapi yaḥ punarantakāle taṃ śaṃkaraṃ śaraṇadaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi
dhyāyanti niścitadhiyāmitadivyabhāvaṃ taṃ śaṃkaraṃ śaraṇadaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi
yaścandrakhaṇḍam amalaṃ vikasanmayūkhaṃ baddhvāsayaṃ priyatayā śirasā bibharti
yaścārdhadeham adadadgirirājaputryai taṃ śaṃkaraṃ śaraṇadaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi
yaḥ siddhacāraṇaniṣevitacārutoyāṃ gaṅgāṃ mahormirabhasāṃ gaganāt patantīm
mūrdhnā dadhe srajam ivāpratilolapuṣyāṃ taṃ śaṃkaraṃ śaraṇadaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi

yaḥ pādapadmaparipīḍanayā dadhāra taṃ śaṃkaraṃ śaraṇadaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi
yenāsakṛdditisutāśca danoḥ sutāśca vidyādharoragagaṇāśca varaiḥ samagrāḥ
saṃyojitā munivarāḥ phalamūlabhakṣāstaṃ śaṃkaraṃ śaraṇadaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi

kṛ trividhabandhavimokṣabhāvā jñānānvayaśrutagaṇairapi naiva yuktāḥ
taṃ saṃśritāḥ sukhabhujaḥ puruṣā bhavanti taṃ śaṃkaraṃ śaraṇadaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi
yaḥ kālakūṭam apibat samudīrṇavegaṃ taṃ śaṃkaraṃ śaraṇadaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi

nandiṃ ca mṛtyuvadanāt prabhurujjahāra taṃ śaṃkaraṃ śaraṇadaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi

ekeṣuṇā tripuram eva purā jaghāna taṃ śaṃkaraṃ śaraṇadaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi

ma vibhūṣaṇāṅgaṃ taṃ śaṃkaraṃ śaraṇadaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi
baddhvā taṃ śaṃkaraṃ śaraṇadaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi
paricintyamānaṃ taṃ śaṃkaraṃ śaraṇadaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi

prasādāddhi stadā
tasyaivaṃ stuvato devaḥ śūlapāṇirvṛṣadhvajaḥ
pūrṇe varṣasahasre tu prītaḥ provāca śaṃkaraḥ
divyaṃ dadāmi te cakṣuḥ paśya māṃ dānaveśvara
yat kiṃcit kāṅkṣitaṃ phalam uttamam

athavā sarvalokānāṃ bhava rājā yathā purā
brāhmaṃ vaiṣṇavam aindraṃ ca padam āvṛttilakṣaṇam
yadi tuṣṭo 'asi deveśa gāṇapatyaṃ vidhatsva me

vāṅmanobhiḥ
te vā stuvanti mūḍhā mṛgā iva vane mṛgatṛṣṇikābhiḥ
ṅkuśaṅkitataṭe smṛti
pyaṭena pūṣā karoti vimalaṃ kiraṇaughajālaiḥ
naktaṃ tu śūlahasitai rajamīmukhāni sampūrṇamaṇḍalavapurdhavalīkaroti
bhṛgvādayaśca ṛṣayastava deva siddhāḥ siddhiṃ gatāścaraṇapadmavaraprasādāt

vidyāvayoE sya sametya śaktāstejaḥsṛjāśugamita

iti skandapurāṇe pañcapañcāśaduttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
ṣaṭpañcāśaduttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
evaṃ stutaḥ sa bhagavān brahmaṇāyugmalocanaḥ
uvāca devāṃstān sarvān brahmaṇā sahitāṃstadā
prīto 'asmi vibudhā yāta nāśito devakaṇṭakaḥ
kim anyat karavāṇyadya priyaṃ vo varatānaghāḥ
stuvantaḥ prahvamūrdhāno deveśaṃ hṛṣṭamānasāḥ
tvam eva deva sarveṣām asmākaṃ śaraṇaṃ param
tvaṃ pitā sarvalokānāṃ tvayāyaṃ nāśito 'andhakaḥ
brahmaṇā sahitā jagmuryathāsthānaṃ mudā yutāḥ
tato gaṇānapīśāno yuddha kṛtaśramān
evaṃ tam andhakaṃ jitvā kṛtvā ca gaṇanāyakam
brāhmaṇo labhate yo rakṣāṃ na saṃśayaḥ
śarīra yogaṃ rūpaṃ dharmaṃ ca vindati
iti skandapurāṇe ṣaṭpañcāśaduttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
saptapañcāśaduttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
vyāsa uvāca
anugṛhyāndhakaṃ devo visṛjya sagaṇān surān
divaṃ deveṣu yāteṣu gaṇape cāndhake kṛte
praviśya rañjayāmāsa ṃ merugṛhāniva
somāṃ somānuvadanāṃ somārdhatilako haraḥ
sakhīnāṃ dṛśyate madhye tārāṇām iva rohiṇī
dṛṣṭvā devyapi deveśam upāyātaṃ vṛṣadhvajam
uttasthau āsanāt tūrṇaṃ sakhībhiḥ sahitā tadā
andhakaṃ ca jitaṃ yuddhe devyāḥ priyacikīrṣayā
śaṅkaraḥ kathayāmāsa punaśca pravarīkṛtam
āsuraṃ tyājito bhāvaṃ tvām avajñātavān hi naḥ
praṇataḥ prāñjalirbhūtvā vyajñāpayata pārvatīm
tava preṣyatvam āyātaḥ paśya māṃ saumyacakṣuṣā
devenānugṛhīto 'ahaṃ tava hāsaśca kiṃkaraḥ
kṣāntaṃ dāntaṃ ca bhaktaṃ ca tvadāśrayaparāyaṇam
ityevam uktvā girijāṃ girikūṭanibho 'andhakaḥ
vāgbhirāhavanīyābhirastuvat prāñjalirnataḥ
vibhāvarī vāricarī śarvarī śarvavallabhā
dhṛtirmatistathā kīrtirdīptiḥ prāptiḥ pramohinī
medhā sudhā tathā sādhvī svadhā svāhā mahādyutiḥ
puṣṭiriṣṭistathā tuṣṭirgṛṣṭirdṛṣṭistruṭistaḍit
smṛtiḥ prītiḥ spṛhā hānirvāṇī glānirdayā kriyā
lakṣmīḥ śrīḥ sannatiḥ śraddhā māyā māyādharārcitā
aditirditistathā kadrūḥ siṃhikā surasā danuḥ
rākā kuhūḥ sinīvālī carṣaṇī sukhadāyinī
dīkṣā dakṣāvarā rakṣā śikṣā kakṣaniketanā
dharaṇī dhāraṇī dhanyā vīraṇī vai guhāraṇī
lā golā tathā caiva maṅgalāvidhā tathā
rovṛtā satā śca sakṣatranandinī
nakṣatracitrā dyauḥ pṛthvi kriyā smṛtiralolupā
śuddhā śuddhiḥ sudhīḥ kīrtiḥ kṛttivāso 'adharapriyā
dhanurjyā jayinī pūjyā ījyā vrajyā jayapradā
varā vareṇyā varadā varanārī vacoraṇiḥ
bhūtirbhūtādhijananī sukṛtiḥ sumanā ratiḥ
bhāratī bhāsam āyuktā yuktaraktavacodharī
ājñā prajñā tathā saṃjñā ulkā nāsāsamudbhavā
vedamātātha gāyatrī durgā sāvitryathāpi ca
dharmiṇī dharmajananī tejanī tejasāṃ varā
rajanī rañjanī dhīrā yonirvanajalocanā
śradarthinī danunadī śrutārthā śrutavattarā
balayālātakadharā mekhalā mekhalādharā
prīyatāṃ me jagaddhartrī śyāmā śyāmāmbarā hyumā
andhakasya tutoṣāti tuṣṭā cedam uvāca tam
prītāsmi putra yat prāptaṃ gāṇapatyaṃ tvayā śubham
bhavānīṃ varadāṃ dṛṣṭvā so 'andhako gaṇapottamaḥ
praṇataḥ prāñjaliḥ prāha himavattanayām umām
yaṃ ca tvaṃ me varaṃ devi dadāsīśānavallabhe
uvācāndhakam āsādya prīyamāṇā punastadā
jñānenānena tuṣṭā asmi tava putra śubhena vai
macchandādeva cāpyetadgāṇapatyaṃ tavānagha
pāpavyayo mahān āsīt tenāsi pravarīkṛtaḥ
mama devasya cāpīṣṭaḥ kiṃkaro mama cāpyatha
bhava tvam anaghaḥ śrīmān gaṇeśvaragaṇeśvaraḥ
ye ca tvāṃ kīrtayiṣyanti divā rātrāvathāpi vā
teṣāṃ kīrtiryaśaḥ svargo dharmaścaiva bhaviṣyati
anujñātaśca pārvatyā mumude harapārśvagaḥ
ityevam andhakaṃ devastamorikṛtamūṣaṇaḥ
saptapañcāśaduttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
aṣṭapañcāśaduttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
vyāsa uvāca
anndhakaṃ gaṇapaṃ kṛtvā devyā saha maheśvaraḥ
kiṃ cakre 'ataḥ paraṃ brūhi nuda kautūhalaṃ mama
jitvāndhakaṃ tato vyāsa kṛtvā ca gaṇanāyakam
girīndrasutayā sārdhaṃ vijahāra surārttihā
atha bhūteśajananī ṣaḍānanatanūkarī
apṛcchat putrasambaddhaṃ praśnaṃ praśnavidāṃ varā
varaṃ bhūmiruhāḥ pañca na ca koṣṭharuhā daśa
ṣoḍaśehāṅgam aṅgāni bhittvā putro 'abhijāyate
tasmāt putrāt kathaṃ śreṣṭhaḥ koṣṭhajādbhuvijaḥ sutaḥ
ityevaṃ pṛcchatīṃ pṛcchāṃ śikṣāṃ dīṣāṃ kriyāṃ matim
sūkṣmārtha eṣa rambhoru yaṃ pṛcchasi varānane
koṣṭhajāt tanayādyasmādbhūmijastanayo varaḥ
śālmalau vaitaraṇyāṃ ca asipatravaneṣu
evamādyeṣu cānyeṣu kukṛtairanuveṣṭitān
śāsyato mṛtyuvacanādrākṣasaiḥ krūrakarmabhiḥ
pitRṃstathāśubhairghorairveṣṭitān rākṣasārditān
tatra ye duṣṭacāritrāḥ putrasaṃkhyāṃ na te gatāḥ
śaṭho yadvadbalīvardaḥ ṣaṇḍho vāpi narādhipaḥ
tatrāpi codyate duḥkhaṃ duḥkhaṃ ca narakaṃ viduḥ
yat pitRṃstrāyate tasmāt sutaḥ putrastataḥ smṛtaḥ
indriyāṇāṃ tu prābalyāt tat putreṣvapi pārvati
ime hi taravo devi dakṣaśāpāddhatendriyāḥ
pāpakāni na kurvanti saṃvṛtaiḥ karaṇaiśca ha
etasmāt kāraṇāddevi koṣṭhajānāṃ śatādapi
eko bhūmiruhaḥ putraḥ śasyate na tu koṣṭhajaḥ
chedaṃ bhedaṃ tathā trāsaṃ pāṭanācca niśācaraiḥ
kurvadbhistaravaḥ putrāḥ pitRṇāṃ
chedaṃ bhedaṃ trāsanaṃ ca rākṣasairnirayopagaiḥ
kathaṃ pitRṇāṃ taravo vārayanti yamakṣaye
śṛṇuṣva chedaṃ bhedaṃ ca pitRṇāṃ yamasādane
yajñe 'arthitāste devānāṃ taravo
dakṣaśāpena bhagavan vayaṃ hyupahatendriyāḥ
tamobāhulyatāṃ prāptā niṣkriyā niṣparikramāḥ
asukhāḥ karaṇairhīnā mahatā tamasāvṛtāḥ
etāṃ daśām anuprāptā dharmayuktān kuruṣva naḥ
ityeṣāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā devaḥ salilasambhavaḥ
yajñavṛkṣārtham āhedaṃ vṛkṣān vṛkṣapatirvacaḥ
sthāvarāḥ svāgataṃ vo 'astu tuṣyāmi śaraṇaiṣiṇām
nāśayāmyeṣa vo vatsā dakṣaśāpakṛtaṃ tamaḥ
śālā bilvāḥ palāśāśca varuṇāḥ kiṃśukāstathā
rohītakāśca ye cānye yajñāṅgaprabhavā drumāḥ
te sūpayuktā yajñeṣu tvakpatraphalaśākhinaḥ
mūrtīḥ subhāsvarāḥ prāpya mama loke nivatsyatha
eṣāṃ yajñiyavṛkṣāṇāṃ yūyam apyanugāminaḥ
yajñopayuktā gacchadhvaṃ teṣām eva salokatām
sthāṇuliṅgopayuktāśca janairbhaktipuraḥsaraiḥ
dharmeṇa śuddhadehāśca gatim iṣṭām avāpsyatha
taṃ bhayāt trāyatāṃ caiva dharmo vo bhavitā mahān
tarava ūcuḥ
kathaṃ vayaṃ putrakṛtāstān pitRn nirayopagān
ye ca prāṇivadhe yuktāḥ pṛṣṭhamāṃsāśinaśca ye
rājñām ākrośakā ye ca ye ca piṇḍāpahārakāḥ
aho bhṛśaṃ yātanābhiraśivābhirabhidrutāḥ
śāsyante mṛtyuvacanādrākṣasairbhīmavikramaiḥ
tānevaṃ tudyamānāṃśca kuṭyamānāṃśca rākṣasaiḥ
tāṃstathā tudyamānāṃśca kuṭyamānāṃśca rākṣasaiḥ
tanme sumanaso bhūtvā niśāmayata pādapāḥ
tasya tasya smṛtāḥ śīghraṃ taṃ deśaṃ yāsyathānaghāḥ
garbhādhānādibhiḥ kṛtvā putratve kalpayennaraḥ
ye cāpi pūrvajātān yo vidhinā niṣparigrahān
putraprakṛtakān kuryustāṃśca nistārayiṣyatha
sarvakāmāṃśca dāsyadhvaṃ sukhaṃ caiva tathottamam
karmakṣayaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ lokāṃścaiva tathākṣayān
tāṃ pṛcchatīṃ mahādeva idaṃ vacanam abravīt
śṛṇuṣva yena vidhinā gṛhyate 'avanijaḥ sutaḥ
śvo bhūte 'ahaṃ bhuviruhaṃ grahīṣyāmīti pārvati
sopavāsā bhavennārī śuciśīlā ścivratā
tataḥ śatasahasrāṃśāvastaśṛṅgaṃ gate ravau
viprān āmantrayedrātrau pāvanān vedavādinaḥ
śrutīnām ākarā hyete ratnānām iva sāgarāḥ
viprā viprādhipamukhi pūjanīyāḥ sahasraśaḥ
variṣṭham etaddānānāṃ yadbrāhmaṇamukhe hatam
brahmaṇatve mahāsattve aṇadhātustu bhakṣaṇe
jāyante ye punarjātā hyupanītā mahātmabhiḥ
viyadityucyate vyoma prakāraḥ prāpaṇe smṛtaḥ
divaṃ samprāpayantyete devi viprāstataḥ smṛtāḥ
satyasāramayā hyete viprāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ svayambhuvā
siddhirna teṣvatuṣṭeṣu śakyāḥ prāptuṃ surairapi
ahaṃ nārāyaṇo 'ananto brahmā śakro 'anilaḥ śikhī
taddānaṃ nābhinandāmo viprā yatra na pūjitāḥ
yeṣāṃ prasādāt sulabhā āyurdharmo balaṃ sukham
śrīryaśaḥ svargavāsaśca tān viprānarcayedbudhaḥ
viprān āmantrayitvātha śucivastrā śucismitā
śayīta sanamaskārā sadarbhā bhūmim āśritā
tatastaṃ sapatākaṃ ca sātapatraṃ sabhūṣaṇam
tarukaṃ pramadā kṛtvā tarucchāyānugāminī
puṇyāhaṃ kārayitvātha ṛtvijā hyathavātmanā
tṛptānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca tattvenākūtam ātmanaḥ
grahīṣye tadanujñāṃ vai kartum arhatha me 'anaghāḥ
tatastairabhyanujñātaṃ taṃ taruṃ taruṇaṃ priye
bhūmidevasamakṣaṃ vai gṛhṇīyāt tanayaṃ priye
pitRṇāṃ nirayasthānāṃ madhu so 'amuñca varṣati
gṛhīto vidhinānena subhru bhūmiruhātmajaḥ
satputrāṇāṃ śatāccāpi devi candranibhānane
eko bhūmiruhaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ putratve kalpitaḥ sutaḥ
ityetat te mayā śiṣṭaṃ śriṣṭamliṣṭavacoraṇi
yathā bhūmiruhaḥ putro viśiṣṭaḥ koṣṭhajāt sutāt
aśokataruko dṛṣṭaḥ komalaḥ sumanoramaḥ
asīcca me tadā bhāva eṣa me tarupotakaḥ
ābhyāṃ ca me mahādeva kucābhyāṃ dvijapāvana
kṣīram āgāt sudhāsāraṃ putrasnehāt sukhapradam
tam ahaṃ deva gṛhṇīyāṃ putraprakṛtakaṃ tarum
yadi me kuruṣe 'anujñāṃ tavāhaṃ vaśavartinī
tuṣṭiprado hyaputrāyāḥ putrako bhavitānagha
ityevaṃ bhāṣamāṇāṃ tu bhavānīṃ bhagavān bhavaḥ
sadbhāvānniḥsṛtaṃ vākyam avadat paratāpanaḥ
devi phullāravindākṣi kathaṃ nāma na te sutaḥ
ahaṃ ca te pradāsyāmi putrān paramaśobhanān
anujñātā mayā devi kurvaśokataruṃ sutam
anukūlaṃ patiṃ jñātvā taṃ tāmarasalocanā
praṇipatyāvyayā tuṣṭā idam āha maheśvaram
deva jānāmyahaṃ dharmaṃ yathā strīṇāṃ na vidyate
yā tu bhartāram āmantrya nārī dharmaṃ samācaret
avamanya tu yā nārī bhartāraṃ daivataṃ gurum
atītam api yā nārī bhartāraṃ paripṛcchati
anujñātā hi sā tena prīyamāṇena cetasā
patiśuśrūṣaṇasyaite kalāṃ nārghanti ṣoḍaśīm
śuśrūṣāṃ kurute bhartuḥ sā satyeva vibhāvyate
tenāgryā saha vicacāra cārurūpā bhānorbhā iva saha bhānunā bhavānī
aṣṭapañcāśaduttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
ūnaṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
pārvatyā niścayaṃ jñātvā bhagavāṃstryambakastadā
sumāliṃ piṅgalaṃ yakṣaṃ prāha vākyavidāṃ varaḥ
pārśvasthaṃ nandinaṃ tatra bhagavāñchaṃkaraḥ svayam
parvatendrasutāśokaṃ taruṃ putraṃ grahīṣyati
tvayi āyattaṃ ca tat sarvaṃ tasmāt kuru mamājñayā
ityuktaḥ parameśena piṅgalaḥ piṅgalekṣaṇaḥ
uvāca somayā sārdhaṃ tridaśānāṃ patiṃ patim
gaṇādhipa yathājñaptaṃ tat kariṣyāmi yajñahan
tasyāśokataroḥ pārśve vidadhāvannam uttamam
nandinaṃ tejasāṃ rāśirdiṇḍicaṇḍeśvaro 'abravīt
brahmaṇyān brahmaṇān nandin devī yajñena yakṣyati
audakāyāṃ virūpāsya brāhmaṇā brahmasambhavāḥ
upāsate ye varuṇaṃ pātālatalasaṃśrayāḥ
saṃyamanyāṃ tathā caiva ye yamaṃ paryupāsate
brāhmaṇā brahmaṇā tulyāstān nimantraya bhūtapa
tathodayagireḥ śṛṅge satyo nāma mahāhradaḥ
rājahaṃsānucaritaḥ kāntatāmarasāvṛtaḥ
vasanti yatra te satyāḥ satyānāma tapodhanāḥ
satyena yeṣām ādityo dinaṃ nayati nityaśaḥ
teṣāṃ niṣkalmaṣastasmin hrade snāto divākaraḥ
pratyahaṃ kurute devaḥ prayāṇaṃ śubhakarmakṛt
teṣāṃ praṇamya śirasā hi ātmānaṃ sannivedya ca
atharvāṅgirasastāṃśca nimantraya gaṇa dvijān
ye ca cakracarāḥ siddhā ye kapotoñchavṛttayaḥ
upāsate ye ca śakraṃ tān āmantraya vai dvijān
brahmāṇaṃ ca sapatnīkaṃ brāhmaṇāṃśca nimantraya
kṣīrodavelānilayāstapovananivāsinaḥ
ye māṃ sadārāḥ sasutāḥ sāgnihotraparicchadāḥ
bhaktā yeṣām ahaṃ nityaṃ prasādasumukho 'agraṇīḥ
tān bālakhilyān vāgīśa vyālāniva durāsadān
āmantraya yato bhūtvā suyaśāḥ suyaśāpate
saṃcaraṃśca tribhuvanaṃ vāyuravyāhato yathā
te ca sarve samāyāntu viprāṇāṃ pariveśakāḥ
sāgaraṃ so 'ambarākāraṃ sāmbaro 'ambagocaraḥ
āsasāda pravalgantaṃ raṅgastham iva vāraṇam
sa taṃ timiśatākīrṇam arṇavaṃ pramathāgraṇīḥ
apaśyat kṣaratīṃ kṣīraṃ divyaṃ tadamṛtākaram
surabhīm abhivādyaiva śaṃkarānucaro 'arihā
viveśa nandī varuṇo yatrāste sagaṇo 'arcitaḥ
varuṇaṃ dvārapālena pūrvam eva niveditaḥ
sa cāpyapāt tadā rājā dūrādeva prahṛṣṭavat
tasyārghaṃ gāṃ ca pādyaṃ ca nivedya varuṇaḥ svayam
āsīnaṃ tam apāṃ goptā papraccha vadatāṃ varaḥ
bhagavan kiṃ cirasyādya tvayā vayam apekṣitāḥ
vada sarvānabhiprāyān kartā te 'ahaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
tataḥ sa varuṇaṃ prāha dānavairaparājitam
aśokatarukaṃ putraṃ giriputrī grahīṣyati
krīḍārtham umayā sārdhaṃ nimantrayati te haraḥ
taddevaputrābhivṛtaḥ sadāraḥ saha phenapaiḥ
śvo yāhi mandaragiriṃ prītiṃ vardhaya śūlinaḥ
ityuktvā so 'abhyanujñāto varuṇena gaṇeśvaraḥ
niṣkrānto varuṇāvāsācchvetābhrādiva bhāskaraḥ
sa pūjyamānaḥ siddhaiśca cāraṇaiśca surairapi
prāpodayagiriṃ nandī hareṣustripuraṃ yathā
so 'atha tasya gireḥ śrṅge rañjite tāpanaiḥ karaiḥ
nililye garuḍaḥ pakṣī prabhañjanapathe yathā
hradaṃ tatrārṇavākāraṃ kāñcanāmbujaśobhitam
śīrṇotpalataraṅgāḍhyam apaśyat so 'apsarovṛtam
hradasya tasya rodhaḥsu sāśokeṣu sahasraśaḥ
apaśyata ṛṣīn satyān ādityāyutasannibhān
sa tāṃstapodhanān dṛṣṭvā tapanābhāṃstapodhanān
nandī prahvāñjalipuṭo hi āsādyāvandata dvijān
nandinaṃ samayujyanta vāsadrumam ivāṇḍajāḥ
taiḥ sūryakiraṇāpītaiḥ pītacīrāmbarairapi
saṃvṛtaḥ sa babhau nandī jambudvīpa ivācalaiḥ
atīva prababhau vyāsa tīrtheṣviva maheśvaraḥ
te nandinaṃ sukhāsīnaṃ satyaṃ satyāstapodhanāḥ
ūcurharṣākulairvākyairvismitānanalocanāḥ
samākrāntastvayā tāta dharmeṇa nirayo yathā

sahomaṃ yat tvayā sārdhaṃ drakṣyāma iha śaṃkaram
ahaṃ tu kāryavān āgāṃ yuṣmākam imam āśramam

tatra śarvam amarādhipaprabhuṃ tārakādhipavibhūṣaṇaṃ śivam
brāhmaṇāmantraṇe
ūnaṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
ṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
āmantrya tānṛṣīn sarvān satyavīryayaśaḥśrutān
harājñayā raviṃ devam upāsarpata bhūtapaḥ
sūryaraśmisahasreṣu tāpasān sa marīcipān
apaśyat sa sukhāsīnāṃśchāyāsviva vihaṅgamān
tataḥ sūryarathaṃ śīghram upetyārūṇasārathim
so 'aṃśumālinam atriṃ ca atharvāṅgirasāvapi
devānṛṣīn bhujaṅgāṃśca aśvāṃścāmantrayacchubhaḥ
ādityāśvādibhirnandī rudrapiprīṣubhistadā
devānṛṣīn bhujaṅgāṃśca tata āmantrya bhūtapaḥ
sa vāyuriva śīghrastu garuḍo vā yathāṇḍajaḥ
dhaneśabhavanaṃ nandī kailāsaṃ samupāgataḥ
parvataṃ dhanadāvāsaṃ paśyamānaḥ prahṛsyata
sa bhūteśo dhaneśasya girīśavacanaṃkaraḥ
asasāda nagasyāgre bhavanaṃ kāñcanaṃ śubham
kailāsāgre sanniviṣṭaṃ kailāsāgrasamatviṣam
pātākābhirdhvajaiścāpi kiṅkiṇījālamālibhiḥ
hāsaiśca puraghoṣāṇāṃ sannāditam aharniśam
bheryā paramaghorāṇāṃ vāditraśatanāditam
bhābhirjuṣṭāṃ sabhāṃ tasya tato rudrasabhāsadaḥ
tam ṛddhyā parayā yuktaṃ sevyamānaṃ śriyā tathā
śuktikarṇaṃ śuktikarṇairyakṣendrairabhisaṃvṛtam
upagīyamānaṃ gandharvairekapiṅgāyatekṣaṇam
mādyantaṃ svarṇayā naddhamālayāmalalolayā
dhanadaścāpi taṃ dṛṣṭvā śaṃkarānucaraṃ varam
pūjayañchaṃkaraṃ somam utpapātāsanāddrutam
sāśokādiva puṣpāḍhyādudagrāt parvatādraviḥ
grahā yathā dīpyamānā dinahānau grahādhipam
saputradāraḥ sāmātyaḥ praṇeme manasā haram
tataḥ kathā bahuvidhāḥ kṛtvoddiśya maheśvaram
aśokatarukaṃ putraṃ giriputrī grahīṣyati
nimantrayati tatra tvāṃ draviṇeśa maheśvaraḥ
śvaḥ saputraḥ sadāraśca sānugaḥ sāpsarogaṇaḥ
mandaraṃ yāhi vitteśa deveśaḥ prīyate tvayā
sa yamaṃ dharmavaktāraṃ hartāraṃ prāṇināṃ prabhum
sāgniṃ sadharmaṃ savyādhim apaśyadgaṇanāyakaḥ
āyāntaṃ nandinaṃ dṛṣṭvā yamo bhūtaśatāvṛtaḥ
pādābhyāṃ nandinaḥ so 'atha nipapāta tutoṣa ca
aśokatarukaṃ putraṃ giriputrī grahīṣyati
tatra tvāṃ sānugaṃ devo nimantrayati śaṃkaraḥ
tāṃścāmantrayate devaḥ sammānya bahumānataḥ
kalyaṃ sa bhagavān kalyaḥ kālaḥ kālapriyaṃ girim
sūryātmajagṛhānnandī śakralokaṃ tato gataḥ
sukṛtīnāṃ tam āvāsaṃ vāsavaṃ lokam adbhutam
viveśa tvaritaṃ nandī ditigarbhaṃ yathāhihā
gāndharvam upaśṛṇvāṇaṃ nandī śakram apaśyata
sa pūjāṃ rudrasadṛśīm avāpya tridaśeśvaram
upāviśadameyātmā śakrābhyāse varāsane
tam āsīnam upāsīnaḥ śatakraturarindamaḥ
paryapṛcchata harṣeṇa kiṃ cirādāgato bhavān
mandāravāsito 'avyagraḥ provāca kuliśādharaḥ
aśokatarukaṃ putraṃ giriputrī grahīṣyati
tatra tvāṃ sāmaraṃ devo nimantrayati bhūtapaḥ
dvijapūrvaṃ dvijā ye ca tavālayanivāsinaḥ
saputradārāṃstāṃścāpi nimantrayati śaṃkaraḥ
śvaḥ saputraḥ sadārastvaṃ devadevasya śāsanāt
prītiṃ yāsyati deveśaḥ parāṃ suranarārttihā
śitaśūladharaṃ pinākinaṃ girirājendrasutāpatiṃ prabhum
ṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
ekaṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
śakreṇa tu kṛtānujño nandī pramathanāyakaḥ
sa muhūrtānmahāvego mahāvega ivānilaḥ
vairājaṃ bhavanaṃ prāptaścaturvaktrasya pārṣadaḥ
hataklamāṃ sa tu sabhāṃ sabhāṃ merugireriva
tāṃ kathām iva citrārthāṃ citrārthairbahubhiryutām
dadarśa sa sabhāṃ nandī bahvāścaryasamākulām
tasyāṃ sabhāyām ālīnaṃ yatibhiḥ saha so 'adbhutam
apaśyadabjajaṃ nandī devaiḥ pañcabhirāvṛtam
vedārthaṃ bhāṣamāṇaṃ taṃ yatīnāṃ paripṛcchatām
tāṃśca bhāṣyavidaḥ sarvāñchrutvā sādhviti vādinaḥ
nandī pitāmahaṃ samyak pūjayāmāsa satvaram
tataḥ pitāmahaḥ prāha nandinaṃ gaṇanāyakam
kiṃ cirādāgato 'asīti sa ca taṃ pratyabhāṣata
aśokatarukaṃ putraṃ giriputrī grahīṣyati
imāṃśca tapasāgnyābhān savedān vedavādinaḥ
vraja mānada devānām ekam ājñāpayatyajaḥ
ityevaṃ vacasāṃ kartā vacaḥ śrutvā sa nandinaḥ
japyapriyam uvācedaṃ hṛṣṭarūpaḥ pitāmahaḥ
aham api āgamiṣyāmi ebhiḥ saha śivāntikam
mokṣyate cāpyaśoko 'asau dakṣaśāpakṛtaṃ tamaḥ
ityuktaḥ pratimānyeśam īśasya dayito 'agraṇīḥ
brahmaṇo bhavanāt tūrṇaṃ kṣīrodam udadhiṃ yayau
sa velānilayān viprān bālakhilyāṃstapodhanān
nānāniyamasaṃyuktānapaśyadgaṇanāyakaḥ
vandamānaṃ tam ālokya gaṇeśaṃ suyaśāpatim
āśīrbhiranukūlābhirnananduste tapodhanāḥ
tapodhanānāṃ hṛṣṭānāṃ nandī madhyagato babhau
grahāṇāṃ saumyarūpāṇāṃ yathā madhyagatoḍupaḥ
kacciddrakṣyāma deveśaṃ sāmbam ambāpatiṃ bhavam
tato nandī dvijaśreṣṭhāñchreṣṭho vai pramathādhipaḥ
sālāṅkāram idaṃ vākyam abravīddvijasaṃsadi
iha cāgamanaṃ yanme tacchṛṇudhvaṃ tapodhanāḥ
aśokatarukaṃ putraṃ giriputrī grahīṣyati
śvaḥ sarve dārasahitāḥ saśiṣyatanayāgnayaḥ
mandaraṃ yāta viprāgryā mām ambāṃ cānugṛhṇata
ityevaṃ nandinā prokto bālakhilyā maharṣayaḥ
bho nandin āgamiṣyāmaḥ śvaḥ prabhāte vayaṃ prabho
dhanadavaradam etya bhūtanāthaṃ gaṇapatinātha idaṃ tadāvabhāṣe
ekaṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
dviṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
āmantriteṣu vipreṣu nārāyaṇapadatraye
bhagavān kratukāmaghnaḥ pūṣṇo dantanipātanaḥ
mālī maulī balī kālaḥ kāle vacanam abravīt
ambike jagataḥ sarve brāhmaṇā brāhmaṇaḥ samāḥ
yāmo 'aśokataroḥ pārśvaṃ tathā kuru girīndraje
sākāśajālapātālaṃ jagajjanani tatra hi
piṇḍīkṛtaṃ tvaddhitārthe bhaviṣyati gireḥ sute
krāntaṃ trivikramākrāntaṃ nārāyaṇapadatrayam
atha devī divo nāthaṃ ḍiṇḍimuṇḍeśvaraṃ haram
avadadvaradaṃ kāntaṃ kāntaṃ candrārdhabhūṣaṇam
ayaṃ nandīśvaro deva āvayoḥ paramo hitaḥ
varakoṭīsahasrāṇi tvatto 'arhati na saṃśayaḥ
varado hyasi lokānāṃ lokānām api ceśvaraḥ
yadi tuṣṭo 'asi śailāderdiśasva pravaraṃ varam
uvāca pramatheśānaṃ vriyatām īpsito varaḥ
tataḥ kapīndravadanaḥ sureśasadṛśadyutiḥ
praṇamya śirasā prāha nandī śaṃkaravallabhaḥ
prabhāvāt tava deveśa varadāsmyajarāmaraḥ
śiṣṭānāṃ madviśiṣṭānāṃ gaṇānāṃ gaṇapādhipaḥ
ityevaṃ nandinaṃ devo bhāṣamāṇaṃ tadā natam
prītyāpaśyadvirūpākṣaḥ śaśāṅkakṛtaśekharaḥ
pramṛjya prāha harṣeṇa harṣayan nandinaṃ bhṛśam
bhaktimānasi me nandin sadāraṃ sagaṇāśrayam
tāṃ ca bhaktiṃ puraskṛtya pārśvastho 'asi mayā kṛtaḥ
yaśca tvāṃ dveṣṭi vidviṣṭaḥ sa me dharmarato 'api hi
sandhyākālaṃ tu kālajñaḥ kālaḥ kālanihā haraḥ
upoḍhaṃ vīkṣya nṛttasya devaḥ kālam amanyata
upaspṛśya tataḥ so 'adbhirapāṃ sraṣṭā trilokapaḥ
anvāsta bhagavān sandhyāṃ lokasaṃsthāṃ nu pālayan
bhartāraṃ vīkṣya nṛtyantaṃ viṣaktakarapallavam
sahadharmacarī devī bhartāraṃ sānvanṛtyata
dampatī vīkṣya nṛtyantau sāṭṭahāsaṃ gaṇāgraṇīḥ
prānṛtyata tato nandī devayoḥ prītim āvahan
pramathā nīlameghābhāḥ pranṛttāstūryanisvanaiḥ
tato bheryo jharjharāśca kikhirānakamaṇḍukāḥ
āḍambarā ḍiṇḍimāśca śaṅkhāścaiva prasasvanuḥ
nandī visṛjate hāsaṃ pramathā nedurulbaṇāḥ
tattūryavaraśabdāḍhyaṃ śivāśanirivākulam
jaguścānye 'atimadhuraṃ gandharvā iva pārṣadāḥ
mṛgāṅke hyudite candre candrāvayavabhūṣaṇaḥ
samāpya niyamaṃ devaḥ sāmbanandīśapārṣadaḥ
virarāmotsavāt tasmāt pārvatīṃ cedam abravīt
uṣitvā śarvarīm etāṃ śarvaryamitavikrame
aśokatarukaṃ putraṃ tataḥ śvastvaṃ grahīṣyati
dhāreyī sā sadarbhāyāṃ dhārāyāṃ dhāraṇīdharā
suṣvāpa devavacanādekāṃ rātriṃ yatavratā
tataḥ śatasahasrāṃśāvudite 'arke 'arkabhāvanaḥ
umām āha prayāmeti yatrāśokaḥ sutaḥ sa te
bhavam āha prayāmeti siñjamānavibhūṣaṇā
pādacāreṇa bhagavān pādapaṃ pādapālayaḥ
tam aśokataruṃ prāpa sanandī sāmbiko haraḥ
sādhayānaṃ dadarśānnam annadaṃ pramathaiḥ saha
so 'apaśyat parvataprakhyān rāśīn rāśividāṃ varaḥ
sa sādhitaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā yakṣeṇānnaṃ pinākadhṛk
tatrāgānmudito bhūtvā yatra sāmbo 'ambikāpatiḥ
te praṇamya mahādevaṃ devāstenābhipūjitāḥ
parivārya tadāśokam idam ūcurharāgrataḥ
adyaprabhṛti vṛkṣo 'ayaṃ sarvataḥ sukhasaṃyutaḥ
sarvābharaṇapuṣpāḍhyaḥ sarvagandharasānvitaḥ
bhaviṣyati na saṃdeho devyāśca sudṛḍhaṃ priyaḥ
tato girīndratanayāṃ girīśaḥ praṇatārtihā
paśyānnaparvatānetāniti provāca kāmadaḥ
dṛḍhaṃ tutoṣa deveśā piṅgalasya guhāraṇiḥ
sumālinaṃ yakṣavaraṃ piṅgalaṃ parvatātmajā
yat te manīṣitaṃ kāryaṃ tat kuruṣva kim āsyate
tataḥ sātipramuditā divyāmbaranivāsinī
manojavam anujñāpya śaṃkaraṃ bhuvaneśvaram
daityaśokapradā devī tam aśokaṃ vibhāvarī
alaṃcakāra sasnehā alaṃkāraiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ
ātapatraṃ ca tasyāgre muktādāmāvabhāsitam
ucchrāyamāsa girijā mayūrāṅgaruhaiḥ saha
ā mūlādakaroddevī varapaṅkāṅkitāṃ tanum
jāmbūnadamayaiścāpi paṭṭairmaṇivirājitaiḥ
sarvato bhūṣayāmāsa aśokatarukaṃ priyam
tasya śākhāpraśākhāsu muktādāmāni pārvatī
atha vāsoyugaiḥ śvetaistam aśokaṃ guhāraṇiḥ
vāsayāmāsa lokānāṃ jananī putralālasā
śrīveṣṭakaṃ nameruṃ ca guggulaṃ ghṛtam eva ca
tataḥ śaṅkhaninādena devatūryaraveṇa ca
baliṃ balavato bhāryā cakāra caratī tapaḥ
tathārcayantyāstaṃ vṛkṣaṃ candrahārāmṛtaprabham
stanābhyām asravat kṣīraṃ putrasnehābhisaṃgamāt
umayā so 'arcito vṛkṣaḥ aśoko vanadīpakaḥ
nandinātha samānītān brāhmaṇān brahmaṇaḥ samān
vācayāmāsa puṇyāhaṃ dattvā teṣāṃ yathepsitam
tataḥ puṇyāhaghoṣānte āśīrvādasya cobhayoḥ
anumānya patiṃ devī ṛṣīṃstānabravīt tu sā
ityevaṃ bruvatīṃ devīṃ pārvatīṃ putralālasām
samam ūcurdvijāḥ sarve iṣṭato gṛhyatām iti
tataḥ śaṅkharavo divyaḥ sarvatūryaravānvitaḥ
vedānuccārayan viprā nṛtyantyapsarasāṃ gaṇaḥ
ṛtavaḥ ṣaṭ ca saṃhṛṣṭāḥ svaiḥ svaiḥ kusumasaṃcayaiḥ
tat pravāditagāndharvaṃ pranṛttāpsarasāṃ gaṇam
paśyanti hṛṣitā devā aśokatarukotsavam
vādayan kacchapīṃ vīṇāṃ vīṇavādayatāṃ varaḥ
nārado nṛtyate harṣādvātanunna ivānalaḥ
samāpya niyamaṃ sātha gṛhītvāśokaputrakam
girīndratanayā bhāti dharā iva jalokṣitā
atha nandīśvarādiṣṭāḥ pramathāste sahasraśaḥ
adadan svāsanāni āśu viprāṇāṃ vipravatsalāḥ
svarṇānāṃ rajatānāṃ ca sphaṭikānāṃ prabhāvatām
pramathaiḥ kīryamāṇānām āsanānām abhūt svanaḥ
meroḥ śikharavarṣāṇāṃ mahatī kuśajairiva
tathāsanānyudvahatāṃ pramathānāṃ babhau ravaḥ
varṣānnamṛṣṭākāmānāṃ meghānāṃ stanatām iva
āsanaiḥ pramathā rejuḥ sārkāgnaya ivācalāḥ
pramathāste hṛṣṭarūpā hi āsanāni mahāsanāḥ
asaṃsaktāsanā paṅktirnirmitā viśvakarmaṇā
mandarasya śubhe pṛṣṭhe viprapaṅktyo viniḥsṛtāḥ
snāte patha iva dṛṣṭvā rejaturāsanabhūṣaṇāḥ
dvijātīnanuliptāṃstu yakṣajambālamiśrakān
saśekharān sasragdāmānanuhūya samodyatān
anilaiḥ sāṅganādāśca rejurdevā iva dvijāḥ
suślakṣṇaiśca sugandhaiśca gandhacūrṇaiḥ sapiñjaraiḥ
avakīrṇāstato devairbhūmidevāḥ samantataḥ
divyacandanapaṅkāṅkā divyacūrṇāvacūrṇitāḥ
brāhmaṇā rejurekasthā ekasthā iva pāvakāḥ
divyaṃ dhūpaṃ cārayitvā māmājñā sarvaśaśca ha
tataḥ sphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ padmareṇurivārjitāḥ
hastaśaucaṃ muhūrtena dattaṃ śaṃkarakiṃkaraiḥ
baddhakakṣāstataḥ śūrā baddhakakṣā iva dvipāḥ
pariveṣṭum upakrāntāḥ pramathā brāhmaṇarṣabhān
bhājanānyatha svarṇāni rājatasphāṭikāni ca
muhūrtena dvijātīnāṃ dadurdevā vinītavat
hṛtvā hṛtvā babhuu rekhaṃ daṇḍe vāri samaṇḍalam
brāhmaṇānāṃ viduścaiva daduśca pramathādhipāḥ
bhṛṅgāraiḥ kāñcanaiḥ kecit pānīyaṃ guṇavardhanam
āvījurbrāhmaṇān hṛṣṭāḥ pramathāstapasonilas
ekaikaṃ brāhmaṇāṃstatra sevante vāsavaṃ yathā
apsarovārasaṅghāśca sarvālaṃkārabhūṣitāḥ
nanṛturdevacetāṃsi muṣṇantyaḥ sarvatodiśam
viśvāvasūrnāradaśca tumburuḥ parvatastathā
kustumburuḥ śāliśirāḥ parjanyo gaṇḍamaṇḍakaḥ
namerurguggulūn miśro ghṛtadhārāvasecitaḥ
dhūpaḥ saṃcāryate tatra pratīhārībhiruttamaḥ
pūjyamānaḥ suraiḥ sendraiḥ śloko dhūpatrayāṅkanaḥ
tṛptiṃ na devā gacchanti priyāṇām iva darśanāt
trayāṇām eva dhūpānāṃ jahurna pavanā gatim
taṃ dṛṣṭvā candramaulistu tarukotsavam īśvaraḥ
pārvatīharṣado harṣaṃ pupoṣānuttamaṃ muhuḥ
carācaraṃ paśupatau trailokyaṃ harṣaṇāyate
pranṛttāpsaraso vāraṃ divyadhūpādhivāsitam
ṛtubhiḥ kusumaiḥ kīrṇaṃ tat sado gaganāyate
tataḥ śālyodanaṃ tūrṇaṃ
bhakṣyabhojyānnapānena tatṛpurlokapūjitāḥ
tataḥ śrutimukhaḥ puṇyo rākṣasāsuravejanaḥ
puṇyāhaśabdaḥ prakṛto vipraistrailokyapūraṇaḥ
tataḥ sāmbam aśokaṃ taṃ saharaṃ saha nandinā
kusumākṣatasaṃyuktam āśīrbhirabhinandya ca
mahāntaḥ susvanāḥ sarve brahmasūtrajaṭādharāḥ
praṇamanto virūpākṣaṃ yayurviprā yathāgatam
surāśca pūjitā dānairvākpradānaiśca śūlinā
yathāgataṃ gatāḥ sarve parivārya śatakratum
gaṇāśca gaṇapālena pūjitāḥ sagaṇādhipāḥ
yathāvāsaṃ yayuḥ sarve harṣāduddhūtavāsasaḥ
yā naivaṃ dayitā bharturyatheśasya gireḥ sutā
kathaṃ sā subhagā nāma strītvaṃ cāpi bibharti kim
aho strīṇāṃ balaṃ sūkṣmaṃ devairapi sudurjayam
yena rudrasamā īśāḥ strīṇāṃ vaśyatvam āgatāḥ
anye tānabruvaṃstatra mahātmāno gaṇādhipāḥ
deva evaiṣa rūpeṇa bhāryā bhūtvāvatiṣṭhate
māvamanyata devīṃ tāṃ yogāt kiṃ nāvabudhyatha
ityevaṃ jalpamānāste anyonyena gaṇottamāḥ
jagmuḥ svabhavanānyeva dīpyamānā yathāgnayaḥ
devo 'api nandinā sārdhaṃ so 'ambayā cābhirūpayā
aśokatarukasyādha upaviṣṭo 'ambikārcitaḥ
tataḥ praṇamya varadaṃ somā somavibhūṣaṇam
uvāca vacasāṃ yonirbhūtasaṃghapatiṃ patim
sunirvṛttāsmi saṃvṛttā tripurāndhakasūdana
yanmayāśokatarukaḥ putraḥ prakṛtakaḥ kṛtaḥ
nūnaṃ me sukṛtaṃ deva tapaḥ paramabhāsvaram
devairyaccāpi muṣitam iṣṭaputraphalaṃ purā
bhavaṃ bhavānī prītyaivam uktvā muktāvalīdharā
papāta padbhyāṃ devasya netrāsrāpūritekṣaṇā
tām utthāpya girīśastu pariṣvajya ca pīḍitam
brahmaṇyā ca śaraṇyā ca tvaṃ me nityaṃ priyā priye
kiṃ punaryadyaśonmiśram īdṛśaṃ dharmasaṃyutam
tarpitā brāhmaṇā devi devāśca sagaṇāstvayā
gṛhītaḥ putrakaścāyaṃ tvayāśokataruḥ priye
ehi devi gṛhān yāma sampūrṇaste manorathaḥ
bhūyaḥ sutaṃ taṃ drakṣyāmaḥ stabakaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam
ityuktā patinā sādhvī harṣapūrṇamukhekṣaṇā
prāhedaṃ vacanaṃ tatra haritaṃ hariṇekṣaṇā
gopāyasva hare yatnādgajāśvāccāṇḍajāṇḍapāt
yadi vāpi bhavedeṣa stabakaiḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ
aśokaputrako mahyaṃ tadā māṃ draṣṭum arhasi
iti saṃdiśya haritam udbhrāntahariṇekṣaṇā
sāpāṅgacakṣurvikṣepaṃ kṛtvomā patinā saha
viveśa sadanaṃ devī prabhevādityamaṇḍalam
dvisaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
triṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
vyāsa uvāca
śārvaṃ tejaḥ samādāya vahniḥ kiṃ kṛtavāṃstadā
senāpatye kathaṃ cāsāvabhiṣiktaḥ surottamaiḥ
iti vijñāpito dhīmān vyāsenākliṣṭakarmaṇā
provāca vadatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pitāmahasutastadā
dāhātmako 'api bhūtānāṃ dahyamānaḥ sa tejasā
gaṅgām abhyarthayāmāsa dhāraṇe tasya tejasaḥ
sā tenābhyarthitā devī hutāśena trilokagā
tadā saṃkrāmayāṃcakre gaṅgāyāṃ yogamāyayā
jñātvāpi durdharaṃ tat sā pratipede varānanā
arthipraṇayanirbhaṅgadoṣabhītā saridvarā
bhinnāñjanarucā tanvyā romarājyā rarāja sā
ghanarājyā ghanāpāye lekhevānuṣṇadīdhiteḥ
jagāma ca tadā glāniṃ kiṃcidāviplutekṣaṇā
nopalebhe tadā devī ratiṃ śayyāsaneṣu ca
amṛtasyandibhiḥ śītaiḥ spṛṣṭāpi śaśinaḥ karaiḥ
mamlau sā tejasā tena dahyamānā tadānaghā
śaramadhyāt samabhavadbālo bālaparākramaḥ
ṣaḍvaktro dvādaśabhujaḥ sūryakoṭisamadyutiḥ
samidhya vidhinā tatra pāvakaṃ pāvakatviṣaḥ
kṛttikāstaṃ tadā dṛṣṭvā prasnutorupayodharāḥ
upatasthuśca taṃ vedāḥ sopavedāḥ sasaṃgrahāḥ
kalā vidyāśca nikhilā lakṣmīrmedhā sarasvatī
kāntirdharmo dayā kṣāntirdhṛtirdhairyaṃ parākramaḥ
yogastejo balaṃ prajñā sthitigāmbhīryasatkriyāḥ
sandhāya līlayā bāṇaṃ sa mumoca girau
taddṛṣṭvā mahadāścaryaṃ sattvānāṃ tannivāsinām
atha prekṣya bhayaṃ tasmādātmano balasūdanaḥ
mātRḥ sampreṣayāmāsa vināśāyāmitadyuteḥ
āgatya mātarastatra dṛṣṭvā taṃ tejasāṃ nidhim
airāvatagajaskandham ārūḍhaḥ pākaśāsanaḥ
āgacchataḥ surān dṛṣṭvā nanādoccairmahādyutiḥ
babhūvustena nādena muhurmūḍhā divaukasaḥ
abhūdairāvaṇasyāpi madadhvaṃsaḥ kapolayoḥ
arcīṃṣi ca pradīptāni visasarja sahasraśaḥ
trilocanasutasteṣāṃ surāṇāṃ suradarpahā
roṣādātāmranetrānto visasarja śatakratuḥ
atha darpaṃ vihāyāśu praṇeme pākaśāsanaḥ
gṛhāṇa rājyam apyetat prārthanīyaṃ manasvinām
tvam eva yukto lokānāṃ pālane pāvakātmaja
agnāveva haviḥ puṇyaṃ hūyate
prāha prabhavatāṃ śreṣṭho vihasya vibudhādhipam
śādhi śakra tvam evedaṃ rājyaṃ ciram abhīpsitam
niśāmya tadvacaḥ śrīmān skandasyākliṣṭacetasaḥ
arthavadvacanaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ punarāha śacīpatiḥ
darśaya no vicitrāṇi kāryajātānyanekadhā
saṃgatāni vibhinnāni
na vicālayituṃ cetaḥ śakra śaktā haṭhānmama
rājyaṃ rājīvapatrākṣa na jātu manasāpyaham
doṣāṇāṃ nityam āvāsaṃ kāmaye pākaśāsana
vapuḥ saṃmānayāmīha nāham ājñāpaye vibho
atha tadvacanaṃ śrutvā puruhūtaṃ mahābhujaḥ
dvādaśākṣaḥ sahasrākṣam idam āhoruvikramaḥ
mama prabhavati śrīmān lokānāṃ prabhuravyayaḥ
ananyabhūrameyātmā vṛṣaketuḥ purandara
tam ārādhya prabhuṃ bhaktyā gṛhāṇājñāṃ śatakrato
tasyābhiprāyam ājñāya devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ
ājagāma sapatnīko didṛkṣustanayaṃ tadā
svāhayā sahito vahnirgaṅgā ca saritāṃ varā
kṛttikāśca susaṃhṛṣṭāḥ śvetaṃ śikhariṇāṃ varam
cintayāmāsurāyāntaḥ kaṃ nu skando 'abhiyāsyati
atha teṣām abhiprāyaṃ jñātvā matimatāṃ varaḥ
ṣoḍhā samabhavat skando yogīśo balavat tadā
naigameṣo yayau gaṅgāṃ vahniṃ śākho mahādyutiḥ
svāhāṃ jagāma saṃhṛṣṭaḥ kākapakṣadharo guhaḥ
kṛttikāḥ ṣaṇmukhasśrīmān vegādabhisasāra ca
manorathān sa sarveṣāṃ devadevātmajaḥ prabhuḥ
yugapadyoginām īśaḥ pūrayāmāsa mūrtibhiḥ
sudhākaṇaparisrāvi cūḍāratnaṃ ca pārvatī
svamanonirmalāṃ gaṅgā viśuddhām amṛtodbhavām
dviṣatprāṇaharāṃ gurvīm amoghāṃ havyavāhanaḥ
arciṣmatīṃ dadau cāsmai śaktiṃ śaktāya sūnave
patākāṃ mahatīṃ raktāṃ jvalatpāvakasaprabhām
kiṅkiṇīnāditāṃ divyāṃ prādāt svāhā mahātmane
supuṇyagandhām utphullāṃ svarajaḥparipiñjarām
kṛttikāśca dadustasmai mālām añcitakesarām
athājagmuḥ surāḥ sarve pitāmahapuraḥsarāḥ
śvetādreḥ śikharaṃ ramyaṃ vṛṣaketuṃ didṛkṣavaḥ
tān āgatān samaṃ sarvāṃstadā tatra divaukasaḥ
dṛṣṭyā sambhāvayāmāsa mahādevaḥ prasannayā
praṇamya devadeveśaṃ labdhvānujñāṃ divaukasaḥ
śilāsu śaśigaurīṣu niṣeduramitaujasaḥ
prottuṅgaśikharaḥ śveto dyutimānapi bhūdharaḥ
vyajñāpayanmahādevaṃ praṇamya vadatāṃ varaḥ
tārakākhyena no lakṣmīrāmṛṣṭā prasabhaṃ prabho
vajraṃ vakṣaḥsthale tasya kaṭhine kuṇṭhatāṃ yayau
āsādya mṛdutāṃ bheje kaṇṭhaṃ tasyāmaradviṣaḥ
daṇḍo vaivasvatasyāpi pradīptānalabhāsvaraḥ
samare ripusurvāro mahāpāśaḥ pracetasaḥ
tasya kaṇṭhe samabhavanmantreṇeva vaśīkṛtaḥ
utpāṭya prasabhaṃ tena nandane kalpapādapāḥ
niveśitā yathākāmaṃ svagṛhodyānabhūmiṣu
samīpe tasya sāśaṅkastālavṛntāyate 'anilaḥ
miṣatāṃ sarvadevānāṃ devadeva diteḥ sutaḥ
abhiṣicya surāḥ skandaṃ senāpatye mahādyutim
evaṃ vijñāpitastatra vajriṇā vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
dadāvanujñāṃ skandāya senāpatyābhiṣecane
iti skandapurāṇe skandābhiṣekānujñāne
trisaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
catuḥṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
atha te skandam ādāya surā brahmapuraḥsarāḥ
vistīrṇe śvabhrapāṣāṇakaṇṭakoṣaravarjite
skandasya paritaḥ sarve tadā saṃhṛṣṭacetasaḥ
niṣeduste suraśreṣṭhā jvalitānalavarcasaḥ
tat puṇyam amaraiḥ pṛktaṃ sthānaṃ puṇyataraṃ punaḥ
abhūdgāṅgairivāmbhobhiḥ sametaṃ yāmunaṃ payaḥ
ājagāmātha taṃ deśaṃ kṣitirmūrtimatī tadā
skandābhiṣeke saṃjāte harṣasamphullalocanā
athāsau kṣipram abhavaddeśaḥ kanakabālukaḥ
adhyāsata mahātmāno yaṃ deśam apamatsarāḥ
nirastaduritaḥ so 'abhūt tatra teṣāṃ vibhūtibhiḥ
atha siṃhāsanaṃ divyaṃ śātakumbhaṃ susaṃskṛtam
gṛhītvā giribhiḥ sārdham ājagāma himālayaḥ
ratnairoṣadhibhirgandhaiḥ pūrṇān puṇyaiśca vāribhiḥ
ādāya kalaśān haimān phullāmburuhamālinaḥ
udanvantaḥ susambhrāntāḥ pracalanmaṇikuṇḍalāḥ
gaṅgā ratnamayāṃścārūn kalaśān sphuritatviṣaḥ
haimāmbujakṛttottsaṃsān pūrṇān paramavāriṇā
gṛhītvā saha sarvābhiḥ saridbhiḥ saritāṃ varā
ājagāma tadā harṣāt praskhalantī sameṣvapi
abhiṣecanikān kumbhān grāhayitvā susaṃskṛtān
devībhiḥ saha bahvībhirājagāma divaukasām
ākrāmantīva tejāṃsi tejasā svena pārvatī
adbhiḥ paramapuṇyābhiḥ pūrṇān ratnāṃśumālinaḥ
kalaśān sphāṭikāñchubhrān grāhayitvā susaṃskṛtān
nānāratnavicitrāṃśusamūhasphuritodaram
hāraṃ ca nirmalaṃ śuddhaṃ śaśāṅkakiraṇatviṣam
kāntaṃ muktāvitānaṃ ca cetohāri sunirmalam
abhyāgamat tadā tatra prahṛṣṭo yādasāṃ patiḥ
dānavādhipamātaṅgaviṣāṇollikhitāṅgadaḥ
ratnāṅgadāni cārūṇi dyutimanti dhaneśvaraḥ
samādāyābhyagāt sāraṃ sarvāsām iva sampadām
niśākarāṃśugaurāṇi dīrghāṇi rucimanti ca
ādāya ratnadaṇḍāni cāmarāṇi mahādyutiḥ
ṛtavastaṃ tadā deśam ājagmustuṣṭacetasaḥ
arundhatī śacī svāhā sinīvālī girīndrajā
aditirdevamātā ca niśā sānumatiḥ kuhūḥ
hrīḥ śrīḥ puṣṭirdiśo dyauśca sutāḥ sarvāḥ prajāpateḥ
rākā ca dhiṣaṇā caiva surabhirdevayoṣitaḥ
oṣadhyo mūrtimatyaśca kauśikī vanadevatā
ahaḥ kāṣṭhā muhurtāśca māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ kalāḥ
airāvaṇaḥ supratīko vāmanaḥ kumudo 'añjanaḥ
puṣpadanto mahāpadmaḥ sārvabhaumaśca diggajāḥ
ṛṣigaṇāstvaritābhiyayurguhaṃ niyamitorjitanityatapaḥkriyāḥ
upayayurgaruḍāśca vimatsarā bhujagarājasurūḍhabalodayāḥ
nanṛturāyatalolavilocanā vividhabhāvavilāsarasānvitāḥ
paramayauvanarūpaguṇānvitāḥ pramuditāḥ parito 'apsaraso 'alasāḥ
virajaso 'atitarāṃ mṛduvṛttayo vibudhacittasukhāśca samīraṇāḥ
ābhiṣecanikaṃ kṛtvā vidhiṃ tasya bṛhaspatiḥ
āśīrbhirāśiṣāṃ dhāma samāśliṣya śivātmajam
maṅgalāni jagustasya gandharvā nāradaśca yaḥ
pratisārya tadā vīṇāṃ tāraṃ raktam anākulam
atha taṃ dakṣiṇe pāṇau gṛhītvā kṛtamaṅgalam
guruḥ siṃhāsane tasmin prāṅmukhaṃ saṃnyaveśayat
bhṛśaṃ dundubhayaścitrāḥ samyak cetopahāriṇaḥ
mattadvirephasaṃgītāḥ svakiñjalkāruṇatviṣaḥ
puṇyagandhā vicitrāśca nipetuḥ puṣpavṛṣṭayaḥ
ādade kalaśaṃ pūrvaṃ pūrṇaṃ puṇyena vāriṇā
samādhāyāmbaraṃ pītaṃ tato viṣṇuḥ samādade
kalaśaṃ kaustubhamaṇeḥ parāmṛṣṭaṃ gabhastibhiḥ
tataḥ keyūraratnāṃśukhacitaṃ pākaśāsanaḥ
uttarīyaṃ niyamyāśu jagrāha kalaśaṃ tadā
nibadhya śaśilekhāṅkā jaṭā jvalanapiṅgalāḥ
jagṛhuḥ kalaśān rudrā bhujaṅgakṛtakaṅkaṇāḥ
bibhrato 'api parāṃ dīptiṃ sukhasaṃsparśamūrtayaḥ
ādityā jagṛhuḥ pūrṇān kalaśān puṇyavāribhiḥ
ādaduḥ kalaśāṃstatra pūrṇān puṇyena vāriṇā
aśvināvapi puṇyābhiḥ pūrṇāvadbhiḥ susaṃskṛtau
ādadāte tadā kumbhau haimau ratnāṃśumālinau
haimāmburuhasaṃchannāṃścitrān ratnagabhastibhiḥ
nāgagandharvarājāno lokapālā marudgaṇāḥ
ṛṣayo bālakhilyāśca pitaraḥ patageśvarāḥ
dharmo dhātā vidhātā ca kālo mṛtyurvasundharā
sandhyā kāntirdhṛtirmedhā kīrtirlakṣmīḥ sarasvatī
samudrāḥ sarito vedāstīrthāni girayo grahāḥ
kumbhān ādadire tatra pūrṇān paramavāriṇā
atha te hṛṣṭamanasaḥ prahṛṣṭaṃ pāvakātmajam
jayinaḥ śarvaputrasya ṛṣayaśca samāgatāḥ
jagrāha maghavā tasya śvetam ātapavāraṇam
dudhuvuścāmarairdīrghaiḥ śaraccandrāṃśunirmalaiḥ
parito ratnadaṇḍaiśca lokapālā mahādyutim
amṛtādutthitaṃ divyam upanītaṃ pracetasā
hemāvadāte vistīrṇe śaśāṅkakiraṇadyutim
tasya vakṣaḥsthale hāraṃ babandha saritāṃ varā
hāreṇālaṃkṛtaṃ vakṣaḥ kiṃ tu hāro guhorasā
ābabandha mahābāhoraṅgadāni svalaṃkṛtā
bhujeṣu pāraṇālānastambhapīneṣvarundhatī
dīptimān pāvakasutastadābhūddīptimattaraḥ
mahāpāriṣadāñchūrān balinaḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
ghaṇṭākarṇaṃ suraktākṣaṃ nandiṣeṇaṃ ca durjayam
caturthaṃ balināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ khyātaṃ kumudamālinam
dadau sthāṇurmahāvīryaṃ mahāpāriṣadaṃ kratum
sampravṛtte tadā ghore saṃgrāme tārakāmaye
kruddho jaghāna daityānāṃ yo yutāni caturdaśa
vibudhāśca dadustasmai senāṃ nairṛtasaṃkulām
daityayakṣakṣayakarīm ajeyāṃ viśvarūpiṇīm
unmāthaṃ ca pramāthaṃ ca mahāvīryaparākramau
kārttikeyāya saṃhṛṣṭo raṇe paramadurjayau
jvālājihvaṃ tathā jyotim ātmajāya vibhāvasuḥ
parighaṃ paṭahaṃ bhīmaṃ dahātidahanau tathā
aṃśo 'apyanucarān pañca dadau skandāya dhīmate
dadau jvalanaputrāya viṣṇuḥ prīto mahāyaśāḥ
skandāya dadatuḥ prītāvaśvinau ca mahābalau
ḍambarāḍambarau cobhau dadau dhātāgnisūnave
dadau tvaṣṭā mahāmāyau skandāyānucarāvubhau
suprabhaṃ ca mahāmāyaṃ śubhakarmāṇam eva ca
prādādvidhātā skandāya śatrupakṣaniṣūdanau
pālintakaṃ mahāvīryaṃ kālakaṃ ca mahābalam
dadau pāriṣadau pūṣā skandāyāmitatejase
balaṃ cātibalaṃ caiva mahākāyau mahābalau
pradadau kārttikeyāya vāyuḥ prīto mahātmane
dadau jvalanaputrāya varuṇaḥ pāśadhāriṇau
suvarcasaṃ mahāvīryaṃ tathā cāpyativarcasam
kāñcanaṃ ca mahāmāyaṃ tathā jīmūtamālinam
ucchṛṅgaṃ ca viśṛṅgaṃ ca śilāpāṣāṇayodhinau
pradadau kārttikeyāya mahāpāriṣadau tadā
unmādaṃ puṣpadantaṃ ca śaṅkukarṇaṃ ca durjayam
mahāvīryān mahāsattvān prādāt putrāya pārvatī
jayaṃ mahājayaṃ caiva dadurnāgā mahātmane
dadau ca paramaprītaḥ skandāya vṛṣavāhanaḥ
bahūn pāriṣadāñchūrān samare durjayān paraiḥ
sanandaṃ dvādaśabhujaṃ tathā kṛṣṇopakṛṣṇakau
kṛtagrīvaṃ kapiskandhaṃ kāñcanākṣaṃ jalandhamam
akṣisantardanaṃ kuṇṭhaṃ pārśvagrīvaṃ mahodaram
ekākṣaṃ dvādaśabhujam ekapādaṃ mahājaṭam
sahasrabāhuṃ vikacaṃ vyāghrāsyaṃ kṣitikampanam
pṛṣṭhavaktraṃ sunāmānaṃ pārśvānanamahānanau
jvālājihvaṃ karālaṃ ca śitakeśaṃ tatodaram
aṣṭajihvaṃ caturdaṃṣṭraṃ meghanādaṃ pṛthūdaram
vidyudakṣaṃ dhanurvaktraṃ jaraṭhaṃ mārutāśanam
udarākṣaṃ jhaṣākṣaṃ ca vajranābhaṃ ca suprabham
dhūmraṃ śvetaṃ kaliṅgaṃ ca siddhārthaṃ varadaṃ tathā
kṣepavāhaṃ sujātaṃ ca siddhayātraṃ mahāvaram
govrajaṃ kanakāpīḍaṃ mahāpārśvaṃ mahodaram
gāyanaṃ hasanaṃ caiva bāṇakhaḍgadharaṃ prabhum
vaitāliṃ cātitāliṃ ca tathā śaṭhikavātikau
raṇotkaṭaṃ prabhāsaṃ ca śvetamūrdhānam acyutam
kālakaṇṭhaśarīraṃ ca kuṣmāṇḍaṃ śatrutāpanam
gomāyuvaktraṃ śyenāsyaṃ bhūtalonmāthanaṃ tathā
yajñavāhaṃ pravāhaṃ ca kākāsyaṃ kākalocanam
mañjulaṃ vakranāsaṃ ca mahānāsaṃ gajodaram
madhuraṃ suprasādaṃ ca kirīṭaṃ makuṭotkaṭam
vasanaṃ madhuvarṇaṃ ca kalaśaṃ kalaśodaram
śvetavaktraṃ suvaktraṃ ca cāruvaktraṃ ca pāṇḍaram
kaṇṭhabāhuṃ subāhuṃ ca bakaṃ kokilakaṃ tathā
acalaṃ kanakākṣaṃ ca balānām agranāyakam
saṃcāraṃ ca kokamukhaṃ gṛdhrāsyaṃ jambukaṃ tathā
lomaśaṃ ca jarāsyaṃ ca uṣṭragrīvaṃ kamaṇḍalum
daṇḍakaṃ dīrghavaktraṃ ca haṃsavaktraṃ mahābalam
ṭuṇḍukaṃ śatapādaṃ ca śatākṣaṃ cāpapṛṣṭhakam
śikṣakaṃ cāpavaktraṃ ca śākhavaktraṃ ca kuṇḍakam
mahāyogān mahāsattvān satataṃ brahmacāriṇaḥ
apradhṛṣyān mahāvīryān samare ripusūdanān
nānāśastrapraharaṇān nānārūpān mahaujasaḥ
nānāvaktraiḥ parivṛtān gaṇaiśca gaṇanāyakān
gajendracarmavasanān vyāghrakṛṣṇājināmbarān
raktakeśān hariśmaśrūn muṇḍān digvāsaso 'aparān
jaṭinaḥ piṅganetrāṃśca bhujaṅgakṛtamekhalān
pannagāṅgadinaḥ śūrāñchavasadbhogīndrakuṇḍān
pāvanaiḥ paridigdhāṅgān bhasmabhiścandrapāṇḍuraiḥ
nṛtyato valgamānāṃśca hāsotphullavilocanān
gaṇaiḥ parivṛtānanyairbahubhirgaṇanāyakān
kūrmakukkuṭavaktraiśca śaśagodhāvṛkānanaiḥ
kharoṣṭrāśvamukhairbhīmairvarāhamahiṣānanaiḥ
manuṣyameḍhravaktraiśca śvaśṛgālamṛgānanaiḥ
bhīmairmakaravaktraiśca śiśumārajhaṣānanaiḥ
ākhubabhruviḍālānāṃ tulyāsyai ripudurjayaiḥ
chāgameṣamukhaiścānyaiḥ śukakāraṇḍavānanaiḥ
ṛkṣaśārdūlavaktraiśca dvipisiṃhānanaistathā
garuḍakroṣṭukāsyaiśca kākakokilavaktrakaiḥ
govānaramukhaiścānyaiḥ śyenagṛdhramukhaistathā
mahājaṭharapādāṅgaistārakākṣairmahābalaiḥ
pārāvatamukhaiścānyaiḥ kṛkavākumukhaistathā
pītakauśeyavāsobhiścīravalkaladhāribhiḥ
phaṇīndrānaddhagātraiśca citragonasakaṅkaṇaiḥ
sthūlodaraiḥ kṛśāṅgaiśca sthūlāṅgaiśca kṛśodaraiḥ
hrasvagrīvairmahākarṇairnānāvyālavibhūṣaṇaiḥ
nānākṛlibhujairvīrairnānābhujagabhīṣaṇaiḥ
nānāveṣairmahāyogairnānāsthānanivāsibhiḥ
nānāvastradharaiścānyairnānāmālyānulepanaiḥ
nānācarmābarairanyairnānābharaṇadhāribhiḥ
uṣṇīṣibhirmukuṭibhiḥ kambugrīvaiḥ susaṃsthitaiḥ
kirīṭibhiḥ pañcaśikhairjaṭāmukuṭadhāribhiḥ
śikhaṇḍibhirdīrghajaṭairmuṇḍaiḥ kapilamūrdhajaiḥ
kṛṣṇanirmāṃsavaktraiśca dīrghapṛṣṭhaiḥ kṛśodaraiḥ
sthūlapṛṣṭhairmahāgrīvairlambodaramahodaraiḥ
mahābhujairmahāvaktrairhrasvagrīvaiḥ kṛśānanaiḥ
kubjaiśca dīrghajaṅghaiśca hastikarṇaśirodharaiḥ
dīrghoṣṭhairdīrghajihvaiśca dīrghākṣairdīrghanāsikaiḥ
mahādaṃṣṭraiḥ sudaṃṣṭraiśca citradaṃṣṭrairmahābalaiḥ
suvibhaktaśarīraiśca dīptimadbhiḥ svalaṃkṛtaiḥ
piṅgalākṣairmahākarṇaiḥ śaṅkukarṇairakarṇakaiḥ
dīrghadaṃṣṭraiḥ pṛthūraskaiḥ sthūloṣṭhairharimūrdhajaiḥ
nānāpādoṣṭhadaṃṣṭraiśca nānāhastaśirodharaiḥ
nānācarmabhirācchannairnānāvāsobhirāvṛtaiḥ
hṛṣṭaiḥ paripatadbhiśca nṛtyadbhiśca mahāravaiḥ
śvetāṅgairlohitagrīvaiḥ piṅgākṣairbhīmadarśanaiḥ
kalmāṣapāṇipādaiśca jātīhiṅgulakaprabhaiḥ
cāmīkarāpīḍanibhaiḥ śvetairlohitarājibhiḥ
rājāvarttasavarṇaiśca mayūrasadṛśaprabhaiḥ
pāśodyatakaraiḥ kaiścidvyāttavaktrairmahāravaiḥ
piṅgākṣairnīlakaṇṭhaiśca mahāparighabāhubhiḥ
śataghnīśaktihastaiśca gadāmuśalapāṇibhiḥ
śūlāsipāṇibhiḥ kaiścinmahākāyairmahābalaiḥ
bhuśuṇḍīprāsahastaiśca vīraiḥ paraśupāṇibhiḥ
pāśamudgarahastaiśca cakratomarapāṇibhiḥ
citrāyudhadharairvīrairāvṛṇvadbhirdiśo diśam
ghaṇṭājālavinaddhāṅgaiḥ kiṃkiṇījāladhāribhiḥ
vṛtā gaṇairgaṇādhyakṣā mahāsattvairmahābalaiḥ
mahābalā mahāsattvāḥ samareṣvaparājitāḥ
prabhāvatīṃ viśālākṣīṃ palitāṃ vṛṣanāsikām
śrīmatīṃ bahulāṃ siṃhīṃ vijayāṃ bahuputrikām
gopālīṃ suprabhāṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ bṛhadambālikāṃ kṛśām
jayāvatīṃ mālatikāṃ dhruvaratnāṃ prabhākarīm
suprabhāṃ vasudāṃ caiva viśokāṃ nandinīṃ tathā
vajracūḍāṃ mahācūḍāṃ vajranemiṃ mahāprabhām
añjanīṃ ca bharatsenāṃ kamalākṣīṃ śaśiprabhām
śatruñjayāṃ mahānāsāṃ krodhanāṃ śalabhīṃ khaṣīm
mādhavīṃ śukavaktrāṃ ca kīrtinemim aninditām
gītapriyāṃ mahāmāyāṃ vāyasīm amṛtāṃ satīm
sarasvatīṃ bhogavatīṃ subhrūṃ ca kanakāvatīm
sutāṃ lakṣmīṃ vīryavatīṃ vidyujjihvāṃ mahābalām
padmāvatīṃ sunakṣatrāṃ kandarāṃ bahuyojanām
santānikāṃ śivāṃ caiva kamalāṃ maladām api
sudāmāṃ bahudāmāṃ ca suprabhāṃ ca yaśasvinīm
nṛttapriyāṃ varārohāṃ sitolūkhalamekhalām
śataghaṇṭāṃ śatānandāṃ śatanetrāṃ yaśasvinīm
vapuṣmatīṃ ca śīlāṃ ca bhadrakālīṃ ca bhairavām
saṃhārikāṃ niṣkuṭikāṃ bhūtāṃ catvaravāsinīm
sumaṅgalāṃ svastimatīṃ vṛddhikāmāṃ janapriyām
dhanadāmsupradāṃ caiva bhavadāṃ sukhadām api
ailīṃ bhelīṃ samelīṃ ca vetālīṃ jananīṃ niśām
kaṇḍūṃ piṅgalikāṃ caiva devamitrāṃ yaśasvinīm
lambuṣīṃ sanakāṃ caiva citrasenām athācalām
kukūnikāṃ śaṅkhinikāṃ tathā jharjharikām api
kuṇḍālikāṃ lokavilāṃ kaṇḍarāṃ ca śatodarīm
utkvāthinīṃ jurelāṃ ca mahāvelāṃ ca kaṅkaṇām
manojavāṃ kaṇṭakinīṃ vighasāṃ pūtanāṃ tathā
vaiśayāṃ carcikāṃ vāmāṃ krodhanāṃ mukhamaṇḍikām
maṇḍodarīṃ ca ṭuṇḍāṃ ca koṭarāṃ meghavāsinīm
subhagāṃ lambinīṃ lambāṃ vāmadhūlīṃ vikatthanām
ūrdhvaveṇīdharāṃ caiva lalāṭanayanāṃ tathā
pṛthubarhāṃ mahākāyāṃ madhukumbhāṃ taḍitprabhām
manthānikām unmanikāṃ jarāyuṃ jarjarānanām
khyātāṃ dahadahāṃ caiva tathā dhamadhamām api
khaṭaṃkhaṭāṃ mahāvīryāṃ vṛṣaṇāṃ maṇituṇḍikām
baddhaveṇīṃ dharādhārāṃ piṅgākṣīṃ lambakarṇikām
āmodāṃ ca pramodāṃ ca tathā lambapayodharām
śaśolūkamukhīṃ kṛṣṇāṃ kharajaṅghāṃ mahāravām
śiśumāramukhīṃ śvetāṃ lohitākṣīṃ vibhīṣaṇām
jaṭālikāṃ kāmacarīṃ dīrghajihvāṃ ca lolupām
kanelikāṃ vāsanikāṃ mukuṭāṃ ca mahābalām
lohitākṣīṃ mahākāyāṃ haripiṇḍīṃ ca durjayām
paśudāṃ vittadāṃ vīrām aṅgadāṃ ca mahābalām
payodāṃ gopradāṃ śaṅkhāṃ suniṣaṇṇāṃ tarasvinīm
pratiṣṭhāṃ supratiṣṭhāṃ ca rocamānāṃ surocanām
gokarṇīm aśvakarṇīṃ ca aśirāṃ kharikāṃ tathā
kacakracāṃ megharavāṃ meghamālāṃ virocanām
etāścānyāśca bahulā mātaro mārutasyadāḥ
ekākṣarāṃ sugandhāṃ ca kṛṣṇakarṇīṃ ca dāruṇām
kṣurakarṇīṃ catuṣkarṇīṃ karṇaprāvaraṇāṃ tathā
catuṣpathaniketāṃ ca gokarṇīṃ mahiṣānanām
kharakarṇīṃ mahākarṇīṃ bherīsvanamahāsvane
śaṅkhakumbhaśravāṃ caiva saṃgrāmeṣvaparājitām
gaṇāṃ ca sugaṇāṃ caiva tathā vātīṃ ca kāmagām
catuṣpatharavāṃ caiva bhūtinīṃ vanyagocarām
kārttikeyānuyāyinyo nānārūpāḥ sahasraśaḥ
dīrghadantyo 'atinakhyaśca dīrghavaktrātibhīṣaṇāḥ
caturā madhurāścaiva yauvanasthāḥ svalaṃkṛtāḥ
māhātmyena ca saṃyuktāḥ kāmarūpā mahābalāḥ
nirmāṃsagātryaḥ śvetāśca jāmbūnadasamaprabhāḥ
kṛṣṇā jīmūtavarṇāśca dhūmrakeśyo mahābhayāḥ
asurāṇāṃ mahādaṃṣṭrā dīrghadaṃṣṭrāḥ sitāmbarāḥ
ūrdhvakarṇīdharāścaiva piṅgākṣyo lambamekhalāḥ
tāmrākṣyastāmravaktrāśca haryakṣyo harimūrdhajāḥ
vṛkṣacatvaravāsinyaścatuṣpathaniketanāḥ
guhāśmaśānavāsinyaḥ śailaprasravaṇālayāḥ
nānābharaṇadhāriṇyo nānāsraganulepanāḥ
nānāvastrāṇi bibhratyo nānāyudhadharāstathā
etāścānyāśca saṃhṛṣṭā dadau skandāya kauśikī
vaijayantīṃ dadau tasmai mālām añcitakesarām
viṣṇurvividhagaṇḍāḍhyām utphullāṃ cārudarśanām
samprītā prītamanase dadau skandāya pārvatī
kamaṇḍaluṃ sudhāvārisampūrṇam amṛtodbhavam
dadau prītā kumārāya gaṅgā gambhīracetase
garutmān dayitaṃ putraṃ citrabarhaṃ śikhaṇḍinam
dadau skandāya samprīto balinaṃ kāmarūpiṇam
tāmracūḍam adādvīram aruṇaścaraṇāyudham
mahābhārasahaṃ chāgaṃ kāmagaṃ kāmarūpiṇam
brahmaṇyāya dadau brahmā medhyaṃ kṛṣṇājināmbaram
tejasāṃ nidhaye tasmai dadau daṇḍaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ
skandāya paramaprītaścārucāmīkarasrajam
senāpatiṃ tam abhiṣicya hutāśaputraṃ samyak prahṛṣṭamanaso vibudhāḥ sametāḥ
daityeśvarasya nidhanāya mahāprabhāvā yātrāṃ surārijayinīsahitāḥ pracakruḥ
iti skandapurāṇe senāpatyābhiṣeke
catuḥṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
pañcaṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
skandaṃ purodhāya surāḥ samastāḥ sannāhayāmāsuranīkam āśu
āhatya bherīḥ śataśo mahadbhirdaṇḍairdṛḍhaṃ hāṭakaratnacitraiḥ
digvāraṇān bhūdharakūṭakalpān mandākinīvāribhirāplutāṅgān
teṣāṃ suyatnādgajavājimukhyān haimāni yantrāṇi tathāyudhānām
citrāḥ samucchiśriyire patākā dhvajāśca cāmīkaracārudaṇḍāḥ
kṣurapramālā vividhā babandhuḥ pakṣeṣu ghaṇṭāśca samāsasarjuḥ
rathaṃ ca kārtasvaracārucakraṃ sāṃgrāmikaṃ ratnamarīcicitram
saṃyojayāmāsurudāraveṣaiḥ prahṛṣṭacittaiḥ khagamaisturaṅgaiḥ
babandhuruccairviniyamya piṅgā jaṭā bhujaṅgairbṛhatīḥ śvasadbhiḥ
citrāṇi hṛṣṭāḥ kavacāni rudrā vakṣaḥsu daityadvipavikṣateṣu
citraṃ dadhānaḥ kavacaṃ mahādyutirnibaddhanistriṃśatalāṅgulitravān
bibhraddhanuḥ sajjam apīddhapauruṣo jahau śaśāṅkaḥ sahajāṃ na saumyatām
yatnādbabandhuḥ kavacāni sūryāḥ kiṃcitpradīptāni tadā svadīptyā
lauhānyabhedyāni śaraiḥ parāstaiścārūṇi cāmīkaracitritāni
nibaddhabhāsvatkavacaḥ sudhanvā supīnanistriṃśanibaddhapārśvaḥ
rucā parītaḥ parayātimātraṃ sphuran muhuḥ pronnatapūrvakāyaḥ
parābhavaṃ vidviṣatāṃ samāje pracetasaḥ khyāpayatīva pāśaḥ
dṛṣṭiṃ dhaneśo 'api hutāśapiṅgāṃ dadhadgadāyāṃ parighorubāhuḥ
īśaprasādena nijena veti suradviṣām āhanane vināśam
sainye 'atha devadviṣatāṃ nipeturulkāḥ sphuradvahnikaṇā bṛhatyaḥ
vinā ghanairvyoma rarāsa bhīmaṃ savṛkṣaśailā vicacāla corvī
rajo nabhastaḥ paritaḥ papāta vāteritaṃ rāsabhapṛṣṭhadhūsram
dhvajā nipeturdṛḍhahemadaṇḍā raktāmbuvṛṣṭiṃ sasṛjuḥ payodāḥ
kapolabhittīḥ prajahau gajānāṃ madaśca pārāvatakaṇṭhanīlaḥ
sthāneṣu dīpteṣu vineduruccairdīptasvarāḥ pakṣimṛgāśvasaṃghāḥ
senā prahṛṣṭā mahatī surāṇām abhyāyayau daityapatiṃ rarāṇā
sainyāni tāni tridaśāsurāṇām anyonyam āsedurudāyudhāni
kṣubdhānyatīva pralaye mahābdheḥ pūrvāparāṇīva tadā jalāni
niśāmya daityā raṇatūryanisvanaṃ prarūḍhagarvā balino jayotsukāḥ
atipraharṣādasamāptamaṅgalā gṛhītaśastrāḥ samarāya niryayuḥ
rathāśvapādātasamuddhataṃ rajo raṇājire vānarakaṇṭhadhūsaram
svanaśca teṣām atidāruṇo mahān nabhastadā vyāpa diśaśca sarvataḥ
śastrāṇi gātreṣu tantutravatsu nipātyamānāni parasparasya
dṛṣṭvāsurān sattvabalopapannān surāḥ sahāyānanapekṣya kecit
sannehire mattagajānivebhā madāmbubhiḥ śyāmakapoladeśāḥ
balāni vegādabhisṛtya dūram agresarāṇi tridaśāsurāṇām
svajīvitāśām apahāya jaghnuranyonyam āviṣkṛtapauruṣāṇi
nikāmavairāśayamānasānāṃ jighāṃsatāṃ tatra paraspareṇa
sa samprahārastumulastadāsīt surāsurāṇām anavo mahājau
sedurgajāstomaraśaktibhinnāsturaṅgamā bāṇahatā nipetuḥ
saphenam āsyai rudhiraṃ vamanto dṛḍhaprahārānmumuhuśca yodhāḥ
chināni peturniśitaiḥ kṣurapraiḥ sakuṇḍalāni ānanapaṅkajāni
muṣṭiprahāraistalapārṣṇighātairvikarṣaṇāveṣṭanapīḍanaiśca
mātaṅgamukhyān dviradaiḥ prabhinnaisturaṅgamān vājibhiruttamāṃśca
rathān rathaiḥ pattigaṇān padātairgaṇā nijaghnuryudhi dānavānām
utpatya vegādiṣubhirgaṇendrā gajādhirūḍhān ditijendrayodhān
muṣṭiprahāraiḥ kuliśograpātairvibhinnamastiṣkavinirgatākṣān
paraśvadhaiścicchidurāttaroṣāḥ khaḍgaiścakarturbibhiduśca śūlaiḥ
mahādvipālānanitāntapīnaiḥ prapothayāṃcakrurarīn bhujaiśca
utpatya vājipravarādhirūḍhān rathasthitān vāraṇadhūrgatāṃśca
pracukṣubhe tadbalam āsuraṃ tadā gaṇendraniṣpiṣṭabalāgranāyakam
garutmataḥ pakṣasamīraṇāhataṃ mahāhradaṃ yadvadagādham ambudheḥ
athābhivīkṣya prasabhaṃ gaṇādhipairnihanyamānāni balāni tārakaḥ
ruṣā tadā tāmratarāyatekṣaṇaḥ samabhyagānmaulibalābhipālitaḥ
saṃchādayan bāṇatalairnabhastalaṃ marmātigaiḥ kaṅkamayūrapatribhiḥ
tasyāgamaṃ daityapaterviditvā tadā nanādānalasūnuruccaiḥ
svapāṇisaṃsthām abhivīkṣya śaktiṃ vicitracāmīkaracārughaṇṭām
nabho vigāhya pradiśo diśaśca sa kārttikeyasya tadā ninādaḥ
manāṃsi devadviṣatāṃ prasahya vimohayāmāsa mahāsamāje
athāpatantaṃ samabhīkṣya tārakaṃ balena guptaṃ mahatā mahāhave
mumoca śaktiṃ jvalitānalaprabhāṃ vināśanāyāmaravidviṣāṃ guhaḥ
sā tena muktā jvalanātmajena jvālābhirāvṛtya nabho diśaśca
papāta vakṣaḥsu ca saṃhateṣu suradviṣāṃ citratanutrabhṛtsu
samaṃ samastaistvanivāryavegā vidārya corāṃsi viveśa tūrṇam
devadviṣaste 'abhihatāḥ samastāḥ paryastapṛthvāyataraktanetrāḥ
saṃdaṣṭajihvādharavihvalāṅgāḥ prāṇāñjahuḥ śoṇitam udvamantaḥ
bibheda tadvaddviṣatāṃ balāni raṇājire śaktibhiragnisūnuḥ
dititanayasamūhaiḥ sārdham āvipratāpaiḥ
tridaśasamitimukhyaiḥ stūyamānaḥ prahṛṣṭaiḥ
pratigamadamitaujāḥ śūlapāṇeḥ samīpam
pañcasaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
ṣaṭṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
vyāsa uvāca
tataḥ paraṃ sa deveśastripurārirvṛṣadhvajaḥ
kva jagāma ca deveśaḥ kim uvācācalātmajā
kāni cainam umā prāha śaṃsaitat pṛcchato mama
sūta uvāca
vyāsenaivaṃ tadā pṛṣṭa ākhyātum upacakrame
sarvāgamaparārthajño brahmasūnurmahātapāḥ
nānāratnasamākīrṇe hemaśṛṅga ivocchrite
tasya pārśve sthitā devī rarāja himavatsutā
vyabhre viyati pūrṇendo rohiṇīva samīpagā
sovāca parameśānaṃ praṇamya girijā tadā
pūrvapraṇayalabdhā ca tena pṛcchāmyaśaṅkitā
pāvanāni pavitrāṇi nāmāni tava kāmada
sārthāni śrotum icchāmi kathitāni tvayā vibho
evaṃ pṛṣṭastadā gauryā prāha sarvaṃ surādhipaḥ
mṛtyuhartā yataścāpi harastena prakīrtitaḥ
puraṃ śarīram ākhyātaṃ sarveṣāṃ prāṇinām iha
sarvaprāṇigataṃ yasmāt tat puraṃ śayanaṃ mama
pālayāmi paśūn yasmāt sṛjāmi ca yadṛcchayā
teṣāṃ ca patirevāhaṃ tasmāt paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ
īśa evāham anyeṣāṃ na ca mām īśate pare
nayāmi ceśatāṃ bhaktān īśānastena kīrtitaḥ
diśo hi mama vāsāṃsi sarvadikṣu vasāmyaham
vāsaścāhaṃ diśāṃ yasmāddigvāsāstena saṃsmṛtaḥ
bhūtānāṃ śaṃkaro yasmāt tenāhaṃ śaṃkaraḥ smṛtaḥ
lokānāṃ śivakṛdyasmācchivastasmādahaṃ smṛtaḥ
nīlaṃ yena mamāṅgasya saṃraktaṃ lohitatviṣam
śūlī śūlena samprokto lakulena ca lākulī
īśāneti mahaiśvaryaṃ mahādeveti cākṣayam
digvāseti paraṃ mokṣaṃ śaṃkareti sukhaṃ mahat
śiveti śivam atyarthaṃ śūlīti paramaṃ balam
lākulīti parāllokān kīrtayallabhata naraḥ
śūlinā devadevena devyāḥ priyahitecchayā
vyāsa uvāca
śṛṇu vatsa yathā dattaṃ punarjanma pinākinā
yamena hriyamāṇāya śvetāya vigatāyuṣe
sarvavidyāvinītātmā yasya putraḥ kuśadhvajaḥ
babhūva sumahātejā viśvāmitra ivāparaḥ
chāyevānapagā bhaktirbabhūva vṛṣabhadhvaje
sarvabhāvena deveśaṃ dhyāyaṃstasthau mahāmuniḥ
na ca tasmai sutāṃ prādāt tām asau suravidviṣe
jāmātā kāṅkṣitaścāsīt tena cakragadādharaḥ
viṣṇuḥ paramadharmātmā duhitrā cāsya suvrata
tasya taṃ duhitā jñātvā hataṃ pitaram ātmanaḥ
śveto 'api tat tato jñātvā vairāgyaṃ param āsthitaḥ
rudram evārpitāvasthastanniṣṭhastatparāyaṇaḥ
athāgāt sumahān kālastapyatastasya dhīmataḥ
kṣīṇāyuṣam atho jñātvā śvetaṃ mṛtyuviceṣṭitam
suto vivasvato hṛṣṭaḥ kālamṛtyupurogamān
kiṃkarān preṣayāmāsa tam ānetuṃ dvijottamam
tam athābhyetya te dūtāḥ sthitāḥ śvetajighaṃsayā
tān dṛṣṭvā sa tadā śveto yamadūtānavasthitān
hā heti maraṇādbhītastrāsātduḥkhapariplutaḥ
anvacintayadavyagraḥ paritrāṇāya śaṃkaram
taṃ tathā duḥkhitaṃ jñātvā bhaktaṃ mṛtyuvaśaṃ gatam
śaṃkaraḥ prahasan devīm idam āha sureśvaraḥ
kṣīṇāyurabhavanmūḍho mṛtyupāśavimohitaḥ
vyavasthaiṣā purā sṛṣṭā brahmaṇā lokakartṛṇā
prāṇinām āyuṣo hāniḥ kālasaṃsthānasaṃkṣaye
brahmāpi hi sṛjallokān mūḍho bhavati śailaje
mṛtyuduḥkhānvitāllokān yasmāt sṛjati mohitaḥ
anujñātā mayāpyeṣā sṛṣṭirmṛtusamanvitā
ekabhaktitayā tasya dṛḍhaṃ prīto 'asmi pārvati
trātā tasya bhaviṣyāmi jīvayiṣyāmi taṃ munim
evam uktaḥ sa pārvatyā devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ
nandīśvarapurogāṃstān gaṇeśān gaṇapādhipaḥ
śaṅkukarṇaṃ ca gaṇapaṃ tathānyāṃśca sahasraśaḥ
muneḥ śvetasya rakṣārthaṃ preṣayāmāsa śūladhṛk
mahābalāste gaṇanāyakendrā ājñāṃ gṛhītvā parameśavaktrāt
tūrṇaṃ yayuḥ śvetamunerupāntaṃ dūtān didhakṣanta ivāntakasya
mṛgam ekam ivāraṇye vyādhairbahubhirāvṛtam
grīvāyāṃ kālapāśena hastapāde ca yantritam
mṛtyunā svayam ākṛṣṭaṃ sravadrudhiracakṣuṣā
vikṛtāsyairmahādaṃṣṭraiḥ saṃraktaśmaśrumūrdhajaiḥ
vidyutsadṛśanetraiśca lohadaṇḍograpāṇibhiḥ
yamadūtairmahāghoraiḥ kṣipyamāṇaṃ samantataḥ
dṛṣṭvā tathā taṃ munim ārttam uccaiḥ krośantam īśetyasakṛdgaṇendraḥ
mumoca pāśānmunim āśu tasmāt pāśāt paśūnām iva bandham īśaḥ
gacchadhvaṃ yamakiṃkarā munim itastyaktvā śarīrairdṛḍhairbhakto hyeṣa surāsureśvaram ajaṃ śambhuṃ jagatkāraṇam
yaḥ sraṣṭā pavanāgniśakramarutāṃ brahmādibhirvanditastrātā so 'asya vṛṣendraketurajito nainaṃ yamo drakṣyati
te dṛṣṭvā gaṇapān dūtāḥ kālamṛtyupuraḥsarāḥ
bhayānmuktvā muniṃ śvetam abruvan dūrataḥ sthitāḥ
pūrṇaḥ kālo munerasya kṣīṇam āyurgaṇeśvarāḥ
akṣatā gacchata kṣipraṃ kṛpaṇā yamakiṃkarāḥ
yāvaccaite na kupyanti pramathendrāḥ suroṣaṇāḥ
mā vaḥ siṃhā ivāraṇye vāraṇān madamohitān
sakṛdeva samāhatya kariṣyanti gatāyuṣaḥ
athaivam uktā gaṇanāyakena nandīśvareṇāmitavikrameṇa
bhītā yayuste pitṛrājadūtā gatvā ca cakruḥ kathayāṃ yamasya
teṣām upaśrutya tadā vacāṃsi tīvrāṇi nandīśvarabhāṣitāni
ādityasūnuḥ pracukopa mohāt svayaṃ prayātuṃ ca matiṃ cakāra
dṛṣṭvā muniṃ śvetam apetamohaṃ vṛtaṃ gaṇendrairharatulyarūpaiḥ
muñcadhvam enaṃ tarasetyavocannandīśvarādyān graharājasūnuḥ
saṃrakṣyamāṇaṃ svayam eva mūḍhaṃ gacchākṛtātmanniti nandyuvāca
gaṇendrā gatajīvo 'ayaṃ viprastiṣṭhati mūḍhavat
kālena paripūrṇena kṣīṇāyuriha kaścana
saṃtyajya tadimaṃ dehaṃ prāpnotu gaṇapādhipāḥ
mamāyattam idaṃ sarvaṃ bhūtagrāmaparīkṣaṇam
puṇyapāpīyasornityaṃ karmaṇoḥ pravicāraṇam
tenārpayata me kṣipraṃ śvetam enaṃ gatāyuṣam
athavainaṃ gṛhītveha sarva eva gaṇeśvarāḥ
prayāma śūlino 'abhyāsaṃ niyataṃ sa vimokṣyati
pitṛrājavacaḥ śrutvā nandīśvarapurogamāḥ
nyavedayadyathāvṛttaṃ nandī sarvagaṇādhipaḥ
śrutvā tu bhagavān vākyaṃ nandinā samprabhāṣitam
prāha vaivasvataṃ sākṣāt snigdhagambhīrayā girā
ataḥ kṣīṇāyuṣo 'apyasya mṛtyurna prabhaviṣyati
matprasādājjito mṛtyuḥ śvetenānena tāpana
mamādeśāt tvayāpyasya naiva kāryaḥ parābhavaḥ
asya bhaktiviśeṣeṇa pareṇa paritoṣitaḥ
iti devavacaḥ śrutvā praṇamya tapanātmajaḥ
paramārtham avijñāya provācedaṃ pinākinam
tvayaiva bhagavanneṣā sthitiḥ sṛṣṭā purātanī
adhikāranivṛttau hi śakrasyāpi vṛṣadhvaja
tvayaiva pavanaḥ sṛṣṭo hyahaṃ caiva sureśvara
na kenacidayaṃ panthāḥ kālamṛtyukṣayātmakaḥ
vyabhicīrṇo mahādeva kālātikramadhāraṇāt
evam etāṃ parāṃ sṛṣṭiṃ vicintya vibudheśvara
moktum arhasi viprāgryaṃ kāle pūrṇe gatāyuṣam
evaṃ sthitirabhinnā syādahaṃ ca na vimānitaḥ
mṛtyuścāntaḥśarīrasthaḥ śvetastadvaram āpsyati
ityuktaṃ pretarājena śrutvā vākyaṃ vṛṣadhvajaḥ
dīptāṅgāra ivaikasmāt saṃhāra iva pāvakaḥ
nandīśasya tataḥ skandham upāśritya pinākadhṛk
idaṃ prāha vaco vyāsa taṃ dṛṣṭvā yamam āsthitam
aho dinakṛtaḥ sūnorasya śāṭhyaprabhāṣitam
paritrāto mayā śveto yama gaccheti bhāṣitaḥ
kiṃ nvayaṃ mūḍha eva syāduta pauruṣagarvitaḥ
tiryagdṛṣṭiṃ samādhāya saroṣaṃ yamam aikṣata
mahāvṛkṣa ivāraṇye mahāvāyusamīritaḥ
bhasmasāttvaṃ yayau tūrṇaṃ prajahāsa tato bhavaḥ
śvetaṃ tatastaṃ praṇataṃ muniṃ tu sagadgadaṃ mṛtyubhayādviṣaṇṇam
prādādvaraṃ śūladharaśca tasmai mṛtyurna te vipra bhaviṣyatīti
dadau ca nityaṃ gaṇapatvam eva provāca cainaṃ parituṣṭa īśaḥ
tyakṣyanti ye deham apetamohāsteṣāṃ gatiḥ śvetasamā smṛtā me
tavaiva nāmnā ca nadī supuṇyā śvetasya gaṅgeti bhaviṣyatīyam
santarpaṇānnaikavidhaṃ pitRṇāṃ svarlokadaṃ sthānam atīva yasyām
nandīśacaṇḍeśasamānadharmāḥ praṇamya devaṃ purataḥ sthito 'abhūt
dṛṣṭvātha sūnuṃ vigatāsum arkaḥ śokābhitaptastvarito javena
brahmādibhiḥ śakrapuraḥsaraistaiḥ sārdhaṃ jagatkāraṇam ājagāma
vijñāpayāmāsurathāmarāste ādityasūnupratijīvahetoḥ
mūḍho yato 'ayaṃ jagadīśvareṇa kṛcchraṃ tatastīvram idaṃ prayātaḥ
prasīda deveśa kuru prasādaṃ jīvatvayaṃ pretagaṇādhirājaḥ
yathāpurā caiṣa bhavatvidānīm ārttiṃ hi naśchindhi surāsureśa
