vijñaptim evaṃ tridivālayānāṃ brahmādiśakrārkapuraḥsarāṇām
śrutvā yamaṃ taṃ karuṇāyamāna uttiṣṭha putreti vibhurbabhāṣe
protthāya tūrṇaṃ bhagavantam āśu nanāma padbhyāṃ sahasā gṛhītvā
brahmādayaste ca surendrasaṃghā dṛṣṭvā tatastān praṇatānavocat
brahmārkaviṣṇujvalanādināthaḥ kartā surāṇāṃ suranātha ekaḥ
sureśvaraḥ somajaṭārdhamaulirdevāḥ prayāta svaniketanāni
vijñaptireṣā saphalā kṛtā vo maivaṃ kṛthāstvaṃ punarātmamoham
pragṛhya sauriṃ pitṛrājam āśu śveto 'api tasthau maraṇādvihīnaḥ
iti kathitam idaṃ te śvetamṛtyupraṇāśaṃ himagiritanayāyā bharturīśasya śambhoḥ
ṣaṭṣaṣtyuttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
saptaṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
vyāsa uvāca
puṇyāni āyatanānīha devadevasya śūlinaḥ
yāni dṛṣṭvā na śocanti janmamṛtyū mahāmune
evaṃ kṛtārtham ātmānaṃ mucye yanmunisattama
sādhu vyāsa mahābuddhe bhaktimānasi śaṃkare
sthānāni śūlino yastvaṃ puṇyāni śrotum icchasi
kṛtārthastvaṃ mahāyoga muktaḥ saṃsārabandhanaiḥ
śṛṇu vakṣyāmi te vatsa guhyam etat paraṃ hi me
sthānānuvarṇanaṃ śambhormṛtyujanmabhayāpaham
ādityabandhanaṃ nāma kūṭaṃ vindhyagireḥ śubham
taddṛṣṭvā manujo vyāsa janma prati na śocati
hemasomodbhavaṃ nāma kūṭaṃ himagireḥ śubham
ye tadāyatanaṃ śambhorabhigacchanti mānavāḥ
satyo nāma hradaḥ puṇyo hemapadmasamāvṛtaḥ
yatra te munayaḥ satyāḥ satyānalaraviprabhāḥ
dhārayanti mahātmāna āśīrbhiḥ sarathaṃ ravim
puṇyam āyatanaṃ tatra sthāpitaṃ taiḥ pinākinaḥ
yaistadāyatanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ bhavabhaktairviyadgamaiḥ
uśīravījaḥ śailendrastatrāśramapadaṃ mahat
āgastyasya tṛṅāṅgasya devadānavapūjitam
tasmin āyatane rudraṃ tṛṇāṅgaḥ sa mahānṛṣiḥ
dakṣiṇāmūrtim āsthāya stauti nityaṃ kapardinam
meruśṛṅge mahotsedhe sauvarṇaṃ sthāpitaṃ mahat
liṅgaṃ bhagavato vyāsa yatrāste śūladhṛk svayam
sthāpitaṃ sumahalliṅgaṃ devadevasya śūlinaḥ
taddṛṣṭvā mānavo vyāsa rudralokam avāpnuyāt
mokṣavidyāsvabhijñāśca sāṃkhyayogaviśāradāḥ
bhavanti manujā dṛṣṭvā talliṅgaṃ paramādbhutam
tapanīyamayaṃ śubhraṃ devatā yadupāsate
taddṛṣṭvā devatā liṅgaṃ prāpnuvanti paraṃ padam
kṣīrode sāgare divyaṃ bālakhilyaiḥ svayaṃ kṛtam
tasmiṃścandraprabhaṃ liṅgaṃ sphāṭikaṃ maṇirañjitam
sauvarṇaṃ yakṣarājena sthāpitaṃ gandhamādane
yaistadāyatanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ kuberasya surāsuraiḥ
ebhyaḥ puṇyatamānīha yāni gamyāni mānuṣaiḥ
śṛṇu tāni mahābuddhe sthānāni śaśimaulinaḥ
sarvaparvatarājasya śṛṅge himavataḥ śubhe
mahālayam iti khyātaṃ sthānam ādyaṃ svayambhuvaḥ
yatra sarvāmarā vyāsa caturvaktrapuraḥsarāḥ
saṃsiddhā munayaścaiva ye ca yogīśvarā bhuvi
yatra sākṣānmahādevo nyastavān padam ātmanaḥ
abhigamya tam īśānaṃ mahālayanivāsinam
na taṃ paśyantyadharmajñā ye 'api pāpakṛto narāḥ
mahāgaṇapatistatra dvārasaṃstho mahābalaḥ
sa teṣāṃ gamanaṃ hanti ye narāḥ pāpakāriṇaḥ
yogino yate devāśca siddhāśca paramarṣayaḥ
taṃ praṇamya yayuḥ siddhiṃ puṇyaṃ paśupateḥ padam
tasya saṃkalpanādeva drakṣyāmīti mahālayam
mahālayaṃ mahat kṣetraṃ mokṣasiddhipradaṃ śubham
kulānyubhayataḥ sapta dṛṣṭvā trāyati mānavaḥ
tataḥ puṇyatamaṃ vyāsa kedāraṃ nāma nāmataḥ
paraṃ dhāma vṛṣāṅkasya tasyaivottarataḥ śubham
jaṭābhārājjalaṃ puṇyaṃ mumoca
te bhavanti gaṇā vyāsa kuṣmāṇā rudravallabhāḥ
mahārūpā mahātmāno nandino 'apyadhikapriyāḥ
kedāravāsinaṃ dṛṣṭvā devadevaṃ jagatpatim
brahmā śakrastathā viṣṇuḥ somo yakṣagaṇādhipaḥ
kedārasalilaṃ pītaṃ yairnaraiḥ sumahātmabhiḥ
kathaṃ śocanti te vyāsa prāptaṃ kiṃ nu na taiḥ sukham
mūrdhnaḥ somamahendraviṣṇumarutāṃ sraṣṭurvibhoḥ śūlinaḥ
gatvā tam api deveśaṃ gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt
abhigamya tam īśānaṃ na śocenmaraṇaṃ prati
trayāṇām api lokānāṃ pradeśe himavadgireḥ
eṣa śreṣṭhatamo vyāsa sarvasiddhipradaḥ śubhaḥ
vipannasya pramādādvā gāṇapatyā gatirvarā
nātaḥ puṇyatamaṃ kiṃcit sarvalokeṣu vidyate
yāti sāyujyatāṃ śambhoḥ paramaiśvaryasaṃyutaḥ
girāviha mṛto jantuḥ kiṃ tataḥ paramaṃ padam
kucakuṇḍa iti khyāte tīrthe yatromayā kṛte
tadgaurīśikharaṃ puṇyaṃ ye 'abhigacchanti mānavāḥ
aśvamedhaphalaṃ prāpya te yānti paramāṃ gatim
ṛṣabhaṃ śṛṅgam aparaṃ vajrasphaṭikasannibham
yatra nandī tapastepe varaṃ cāvāpa śaṃkarāt
ṛṣabhaṃ prāpya tat kūṭaṃ sthānaṃ puṇyam umāpateḥ
dṛṣṭvā pāpavinirmukto rudralokam avāpnute
anyaddhimagireḥ kūṭaṃ hemakūṭasamaprabham
taṃ namasya mahādevaṃ kinnaroragacāraṇāḥ
mṛtyubhītāśca puruṣā janmaduḥkhaistathārditāḥ
tadāyatanam āsādya krāmān āpuryathepsitān
taṃ dṛṣṭvā manujo vyāsa rājasūyaphalaṃ labhet
gaṅgādvāre śubhadvāre mahāpuṇye mahātmanā
dakṣeṇa sthāpitaṃ liṅgaṃ bhaktihetoḥ kapardinaḥ
vṛkṣāḥ kanakhalā nāma yatrāsan kanakātmakāḥ
mānuṣāṇām aśīlatvāt saṃvṛkṇā dāravo babhuḥ
viśvātmā yatra viśveśaḥ śambhurambikayā saha
bahurūpeśvaro nāmnā naikaprāṇivarapradaḥ
mānavā yanna paśyanti janma ceṣa mumukṣavaḥ
vājimedhaṃ daśaguṇaṃ yaṃ dṛṣṭvā prāpnute naraḥ
dṛṣṭveśvaraṃ nīlapayodakuṇḍaṃ saṃsārapaṅke na punaḥ patanti
yatra japyaṃ purā kṛtvā liṅgaṃ sthāpitavān dvijaḥ
japyeśvaraṃ tam āsādya prāṇāṃstyakṣyanti ye narāḥ
anyadāyatanaṃ vyāsa śaśibimbārdhamaulinaḥ
yatra śūladharo devaḥ svayam eva vṛṣadhvajaḥ
cakāra bhairavaṃ rūpaṃ nandyumāgaṇabhīṣaṇam
yaddṛṣṭvā himavatputrī babhūva bhayavihvalā
krīḍāhetorbhavo yatra trāsayitvā girīndrajām
saumyarūpo 'abhavadbhūyaḥ sāntvayāmāsa śailajām
maraṇaṃ janma ca vyāsa nāsau punaravāpnuyāt
yadevāśramiṇāṃ puṇyaṃ tatheśavratacāriṇām
tatphalaṃ bhairavaṃ dṛṣṭvā prāpnoti narapuṅgavaḥ
avāpa śaṃkarādvyāsa gaṇeśatvaṃ tathottamam
yaistadāyatanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ te yānti paramāṃ gatim
yatra vaikhānasā viprāḥ śivabhaktiparāyaṇāḥ
bhāskarānalasaṃkāśā nivasanti tapodhanāḥ
bhikṣāhetorvanaṃ tat tu prāviśat kila śūladhṛk
vimūḍhaiḥ pātitaṃ vyāsa devadāruvanāśrame
jñātvā śaṃkarajaṃ sarvaṃ tadapāyaṃ sudāruṇam
saṃstutya vividhaiḥ stotraiḥ śaṃkaraṃ paryatoṣayan
tatastadabhavalliṅgaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ pinākinaḥ
jagataśca tataḥ puṃstvaṃ tatkṣaṇāt samapadyata
tatra taiḥ sthāpitaṃ liṅgaṃ parameśasya bhaktitaḥ
taddṛṣṭvā vājimedhānāṃ daśānāṃ prāpnute phalam
evaṃ dāruvanaṃ puṇyam īśasyāste mahāmune
dadhīcena mahaddivyaṃ puṇyam āyatanaṃ kṛtam
sthāneśvaram iti khyātaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam
takṣakena bhujaṅgena dṛḍhabhaktena śaṃkare
takṣakeśvaram ityevaṃ sthāpitaṃ jāhnavītaṭe
taṃ dṛṣṭvā puruṣo devam aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet
agastyena kṛtaṃ cānyat puṇyam āyatanaṃ mahat
dṛṣṭvā paramayā bhaktyā puruṣastaṃ śucivrataḥ
girau kālañjare liṅgaṃ dṛṣṭvā sthānam umāpateḥ
yat tadrāvaṇaputreṇa meghanādena rakṣasā
sthāpitaṃ toṣayānena sarvabhūtapatiṃ bhavam
yatra mandodarīputraḥ sthāṇunā śaśimaulinā
māyārathapradānena kṛtaḥ prāptamanorathaḥ
puruṣāḥ svargam āyānti divyayogasamanvitāḥ
tatra śrīparvato nāma parvataḥ śrīniketanaḥ
siddhāmaraśatākīrṇaṃ siddhikṣetraṃ taduttamam
śūlino yatra liṅgānāṃ puṇyānāṃ varadāyinām
sahasraṃ sthāpitaṃ vyāsa śilādena mahātmanā
ye paśyanti tam īśānaṃ śrīparvatanivāsinam
janmamṛtyubhayamteṣāṃ nāsti puṃsāṃ kadācana
yogābhyāsaparā viprāḥ siddhiṃ yānti yathepsitām
manasāpyabhigacchanti ye narāḥ śrīgiriṃ mune
na te yānti yamāvāsaṃ mṛtyāvapi samāgate
tataścottaragokarṇaṃ haraliṅgāṅkitāśramam
taptaṃ yatra tapastīvraṃ rākṣasaiḥ piśitāśanaiḥ
rāvaṇādyairmahābhāgairlabdhaśca vara īpsitaḥ
purā yatra tapaḥ kṛtvā prasādya ca pinākinaṃ
aśvamedhaṃ daśaguṇaṃ taddṛṣṭvā labhate naraḥ
mṛtaśca rudrasāyujyaṃ gacchatyatra na saṃśayaḥ
tato dakṣiṇagokarṇaṃ sthānaṃ puṇyaṃ pinākinaḥ
spṛkkayā jātayā yatra laṅkāmalayasānuṣu
eko rākṣasaśārdūlo yatrādyāpi vibhīṣaṇaḥ
samabhyarcyāmareśānaṃ bhuṅkte rājyam aśaṅkitaḥ
mānavā ye 'abhigacchanti gokarṇāyatanāśramam
daśānām aśvamedhānāṃ prāpnuvanti phalaṃ śubham
jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa yasmin āyatanaṃ kṛtam
yatra devāśca siddhāśca yakṣaguhyakakinnarāḥ
hariścandragireḥ śṛṅgam ākūṭaṃ yairnirīkṣitam
kārohaṇam iti sthānaṃ trinetrāyatanaṃ mahat
yatra kākāṃ tapasyantīm āruroha prajāpatiḥ
āruroha yataḥ kākāṃ tasmin deśe prajāpatiḥ
tasmāt kārohaṇo nāmnā sa deśaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
tasmin deśe 'avatīrṇaśca bhagavān vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
kṣīṇe kṛtayuge vyāsa tretāyugamukhodaye
dvitīyaṃ dvāpare prāpta tṛtīyaṃ ca kalau yuge
evaṃ sa dharmasaṃvāsāddeśaḥ puṇyatamaḥ smṛtaḥ
bhārabhūtistvasau bhūtvā tasmin deśe pinākadhṛk
bhārān baddhvā dvijātīnāṃ narmadāyāṃ vicikṣipe
tretāyāṃ diṇḍimuṇḍaśca śirāṃsi vinikṛttavan
dvāpare cāṣaḍhirbhūtvā nṛttenānugṛhītavān
evaṃ pratiyugaṃ vyāsa tasmin deśe śivaḥ svayam
avatīrṇaścānugṛhya brāhmaṇāñchuddhamānasān
teṣām āyatanāni sma sarveṣām eva suvrata
yena dṛṣṭāni devasya īśānalokam āpnuyāt
vartamāne kalau cāpi jñātvā duḥkhārditaṃ jagat
caturaḥ puruṣān sṛṣṭvā svasmānmukhacatuṣṭayāt
yūyaṃ yāta mahīṃ sarve dvijā bhūtvā tapasvinaḥ
mām evaiṣyatha yogīśā nītvā viprān paraṃ padam
mānuṣeṣu tadā viprā mokṣadharmaparāyaṇāḥ
ujjayinyāṃ gurujyeṣṭhaḥ kauśiko nāma nāmataḥ
dvitīyo gārgya ityeva jambūmārge satāpanaḥ
tṛtīyaścābhavanmitro mathurāyāṃ mahāmanāḥ
atrivaṃśaprasūtasya nāmnā vai somaśarmaṇaḥ
rūpaṃ kṛtvā sitāṅgaṃ tu jagāmātrergṛhaṃ śubham
jagāmojjayinīṃ devaḥ śmaśānaṃ ca viveśa ha
sa tatra bhasmanātmānam avaguṇṭhya vṛṣadhvajaḥ
ulmukaṃ vāmahastena gṛhītvā samupāviśat
tatra prathamam ādāya śiṣyaṃ kauśikam īśvaraḥ
jambūmārge dvitīyaṃ ca mathurāyāṃ tato 'aparam
svasiddhāntaṃ dadau yogam uvācedaṃ ca lākulī
rahasyaṃ paramaṃ hīdaṃ pañcārtha iti saṃjñitam
anayā dīkṣayā viprān prāpayadhvaṃ paraṃ padam
nadītīreṣu medhyeṣu puṇyeṣu āyataneṣu ca
śūnyāgāreṣvaraṇyeṣu vāso vaḥ saṅgavarjitaḥ
vaco bhagavataḥ śrutvā śiṣyāḥ paśupateḥ svayam
dharmapādāṅkite deśe avatīrṇo yato bhavaḥ
sa deśaḥ paramastasmānmahāpuṇyatamaḥ smṛtaḥ
āśramo yogināṃ yatra pravṛttaḥ pāpanāśanaḥ
aṣṭāyatanam ityevaṃ sthānam atra mahātmanaḥ
yaddṛṣṭvā manujā vyāsa prāpnuvanti paraṃ padam
kārohaṇaṃ śivasthānaṃ ye 'abhigacchanti mānavāḥ
etat paśupateḥ kṣetraṃ purāṇam ṛṣibhiḥ stutam
sarvapāpavinirmukto yatheṣṭāṃ prāpnuyādgatim
kārohaṇaṃ sthānam atīva puṇyaṃ śaivāni yatrāyatanāni dhīmat
gatvā narāstāni mahāphalāni saṃsāragehaṃ na punarviśanti
vārāṇasyā muniśreṣṭha yatra sannihito haraḥ
tatra bhāgīrathī puṇyā uttarāṃ bhajate diśam
siddhikṣetraṃ bṛhatkṣetraṃ lokeṣu triṣu viśrutam
avimuktaṃ smṛtaṃ nāmnā na vimuktaṃ hareṇa tu
avimukteśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā devaṃ tatra hyumāpatim
gāṇapatyā gatiḥ proktā mṛtyukāle mahāmune
yatrāste gaṇapo dvāri vidyutkeśo mahābalaḥ
daṇḍapāṇirmahātejāḥ samādeśāt svayambhuvaḥ
tam adṛṣṭvā na paśyanti devadeveśvaraṃ haram
yogino 'api mahātmānaḥ puṇyaṃ tasyāpi darśanam
daṇḍapāṇiṃ śucirdṛṣṭvā haradattavaraṃ gaṇam
yatra siddhā mahātmāno yogaiśvaryabalānvitāḥ
channāḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā praṇamanti svayambhuvam
śakraḥ pitāmaho viṣṇurdhaneśo varuṇo yamaḥ
tathā saptarṣayaḥ siddhā gandharvāḥ pannagāstathā
tataḥ puṇyatamaṃ nāsti siddhikṣetram iti śrutiḥ
gaṅgā dakṣiṇatastasminnuttareṇa varāṇasī
sthāpayedvidhinā yoṣā pumān vā vidhipūrvakam
sahasraṃ sthāpitaṃ tena liṅgānāṃ bhavati prabhoḥ
tryakṣaḥ sa gaṇapo bhūtvā rudrasāyujyatāṃ vrajet
ataḥ kṛtvā muniśreṣṭha brahmādityapurassaraiḥ
tasmin bhagavataḥ kṣetre kāśipuryām anekaśaḥ
dṛśyante 'adyāpi liṅgāni sthāpitāni mahātmabhiḥ
siddhāḥ pāśupatā ye ca bhavabandhamumukṣavaḥ
prāpya vārāṇasīṃ puṇyāṃ siddhikṣetram anuttamam
vedeṣu gīyate vyāsa tat kṣetraṃ śaśimaulinaḥ
nāvimuktāt paraṃ kṣetraṃ nāvimuktāt paraṃ padam
nāvimuktāt paraṃ puṇyaṃ nāvimuktāt parā gatiḥ
yā gatirdhyāyato nityaṃ pare brahmaṇi līyataḥ
saiva saṃtyajataḥ prāṇānavimukte smṛtā gatiḥ
kṣetraṃ puṇyam umāpateḥ suravṛṣairjuṣṭaṃ sadā siddhaye
ye sevanti tadīśabhaktiparamā martyāḥ śamaprāptaye
taddṛṣṭvā manujaḥ samyagiṣṭāṃ gatim avāpnuyāt
dṛṣṭvā pāpavinirmuktaḥ svargalokam avāpnuyāt
tena dṛṣṭena viprendra gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt
rudralokaṃ mṛtaścāsau prāpnuyāt sarvakāmikam
gāyāyām anyadīśasya sthānaṃ bhagavataḥ śubham
gṛdhrakūṭeśvaraṃ nāmnā sarvapāpavimocanam
na taṃ dṛṣṭvā vimuhyanti mṛtyukāle narottamāḥ
dvādaśābdavratastāpi dvijaḥ phalam avāpnuyāt
ayandāyatanaṃ puṇyaṃ magadhāsu pinākinaḥ
nagare pāṭalīputre nāmnā prahasiteśvaram
magadhāsu smṛtānyaṣṭau sthānāni śaśimaulinaḥ
śiṣyaiḥ parivṛto yāni babhrāma nakulīśvaraḥ
yāni dṛṣṭvā bhavet sadyaḥ pumān pāpavivarjitaḥ
yavaneṣu smṛtaṃ sthānaṃ puṇyam anyadumāpateḥ
tripiṣṭapam avāpnoti taṃ dṛṣṭvā mānavaḥ prabhum
aṅgadeśe paraṃ puṇyaṃ sthānaṃ proktaṃ pinākinaḥ
hemacūḍeśvaraṃ nāmnā taṃ dṛṣṭvā na vimuhyati
bhāgīrathyāstato vyāsa sāgarasya ca saṃgame
brahmaṇā sthāpitaṃ liṅgaṃ puṇyaṃ tatra pinākinaḥ
daśānām aśvamedhānāṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā prāpnute phalam
prabhāse śūlinaṃ dṛṣṭvā dehabhede gaṇo bhavet
puṣkare śaṃkaraṃ dṛṣṭvā na śocenmṛtyujanmanī
mahākāleśvaraṃ devam ujjayinyāṃ mahāvrataḥ
abhigamyāpnuyādvidvān gaṇatvaṃ tripuradviṣaḥ
drimacaṇḍeśvaraṃ devaṃ dṛṣṭvā trāyati mānavaḥ
śaṅkukarṇeśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā na śocenmaraṇaṃ naraḥ
ḍiṅgeśvaram iti khyātaṃ rudrasyāyatanaṃ mahat
abhigamya ca dṛṣṭvā ca taṃ devaṃ jagataḥ prabhum
śivabhaktiparo vyāsa sarvakāmānavāpnuyāt
mṛtasya ca gatiḥ proktā gāṇapatyaṃ mahātmanaḥ
suvarṇākṣe paraṃ sthānaṃ devadevasya saṃsmṛtaṃ
taddṛṣṭvā manujo vyāsa rājasūyaphalaṃ labhet
saptagodāvare sthānaṃ dṛṣṭvā puṇyaṃ kapardinaḥ
sthānaṃ puṇyatamaṃ cānyacchreṣṭhaṃ jagati kīrtitam
taṃ vīkṣya mānavo vyāsa sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhet
janmaprabhṛti yat kiṃcit kṛtaṃ karmāśubhaṃ mahat
tatkṣanānnaśyate sarvaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhadreśvaraṃ haram
yatra tatra mṛtaścāpi gāṇapatyaṃ labhennaraḥ
ekāmre ca vibhoḥ sthānaṃ dṛṣṭvā svargam avāpnuyāt
virajāyāṃ haraṃ dṛṣṭvā vājimedham avāpnuyāt
nepāleṣu ca deveśaṃ dṛṣṭvā paśupatiṃ prabhum
daśāśvamedhān āpnoti rudralokaṃ ca gacchati
bhaktānāṃ praṇatānāṃ ca sarvakāmapradaṃ smṛtam
kathitāni mayā vyāsa yairgatiḥ prāpyate śubhā
tasya sāyujyatāṃ devo dadāti vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
maṅgalyaṃ paramaṃ puṇyaṃ medhyaṃ sarvabhayāpaham
sthānānāṃ kīrtanaṃ śambhornityaṃ kuryācchucirnaraḥ
munivarasutaśiṣṭā pāpasaṃśuddhakartrī
iti skandapurāṇe śivāyatanavarṇane
saptaṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
aṣṭaṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
śrutvā kathām āyatanānubaddhāṃ candrārdhabimbāsthitamaulinastu
vyāso munistaṃ vacanaṃ babhāṣe brahmātmajaṃ brahmavidaṃ munīndram
dharmyā supuṇyā bhagavaṃstvayaiṣā guhyā kathā me vidhivat pradiṣṭā
sthānāni śambhordayitāni ko 'anya evaṃ parijñātum ṛṣiḥ samarthaḥ
pṛṣṭastathaivaṃ muninā munīndraḥ praśnaṃ yathāvat kathayāṃcakāra
dagdhaṃ yathā tat tripuraṃ tathā tvaṃ śṛṇuṣva putreti vaco bruvāṇaḥ
bhagneṣu daityeṣu sadānaveṣu mayo babhūvādhṛtiduḥkhataptaḥ
ādāya daityaṃ sa hi tārakākṣaṃ vidyutprabhaṃ cendrasamaprabhāvam
te śītakāle himaparvatasthā grīṣme ca pañcajvalanābhitaptāḥ
vyabhre payaḥplāvitabhūmibhāge cerustapaḥ prāvṛṣi ca prayattāḥ
teṣām agāddivyasamāsahasraṃ tathā sutīvre tapasi sthitānām
carmāsthiśeṣā jvalanaprabhāvāstapoviśeṣādditiputrasiṃhāḥ
ādityatejaḥpratimānavīrā babhūvurādityavapuḥprakāśāḥ
pitāmahastānabhigamya sarvān priyaṃ bahūktvā vacanaṃ babhāṣe
taptaṃ tapo vo vigatapramohā varaṃ tvidānīṃ vṛṇuteti hṛṣṭāḥ
taṃ prāñjalirbhūminiviṣṭajānurmayaḥ sureśaṃ praṇato 'abhyuvāca
avadhyatām apratimaṃ balaṃ ca jñānaṃ ca divyaṃ paramaṃ sukhaṃ ca
dātuṃ na śakyo vara eṣa tubhyaṃ tasmāt paraṃ sāntaram eva cānyam
tvaṃ putra yācasva tataḥ pradāsye cintā ca te mā danujānyathā bhūt
pūrṇe sahasre tripuraṃ samānāṃ sameṣyate hyardhanimeṣamātram
tasmin kṣaṇe yastriṣu saṃgateṣu pureṣu divyeṣu surapravīra
ekeṣuṇā tat tripuraṃ daheta sa no vināśī tripurasya bhūyāt
śrutvā tatastadvacanaṃ mayasya brahmā varaṃ taṃ hṛṣitāntarātmā
prādādabhīṣṭaṃ danujādhipāya dattvā ca tūrṇaṃ svapuraṃ jagāma
candrāṃśusaṃsṛṣṭatalaiśca harmyaiḥ śītānilāhlādasukhapraveśaiḥ
muktāpravālairmaṇikhaṇḍacitrairālambitaiścitrataḍitprakāśaiḥ
prāsādapaṅktisthitaratnakhaṇḍairmahāmaṇīndudyutisannikāśaiḥ
satoraṇābhyucchritaharmyapṛṣṭhairalaṃkṛtaṃ tat tripuraṃ rarāja
ramyaistathodyānaśatairupetaṃ prabhrāntaṣaṭpādamayūrahaṃsaiḥ
vāpībhirākrāntavihaṅgamābhiḥ praphullanīlotpalasaṃvṛtābhiḥ
savrīḍam īṣaccapalekṣitābhiryoṣidbhirākīrṇam atīva reje
lauhaṃ puraṃ yat tadadhaścakāra tat tārakākṣāya mayaḥ pradattvā
haimaṃ tṛtīyaṃ svayam eva divyaṃ jagrāha rājā maya ātmano 'arthe
adhiṣṭhitaṃ tat tripuraṃ tadābhūt samaṃ tribhistairdanurājasiṃhaiḥ
te sarvataḥ svaḥ prabhavān vijitya priyāsahāyāḥ saha mitrabhṛtyaiḥ
matvā ca teṣāṃ prasabhaṃ nipatya nānāvidhāścakruratīva pīḍāḥ
vanāni vaibhrājapuraḥsarāṇi saṃchinnavīrutkusumāni cakruḥ
vāpīḥ pracakruḥ kamalairvihīnā jahruśca rambhādipuraḥsarāstāḥ
saṃtrastagātrīḥ surayoṣitastairanyāśca cakrurmahatīḥ prapīḍāḥ
teṣām atītaḥ sumahānathaivaṃ prakurvatāṃ devavināśanāni
vṛttaṃ yathā sarvam aśeṣatastannyavedayan āśu pitāmahāya
tān āha devaḥ kamalāsanasthaḥ sarvān sureśān parisāntvayitvā
mahābalāste tripurāsurendrā hantuṃ na śakyā hi balādbhavadbhiḥ
tasmādayaṃ viṣṇurahaṃ ca yuṣmān pragṛhya śambhuṃ śaraṇaṃ prayāma
gatiḥ sadā naḥ śaśibhṛt sureśāḥ sa tān balāddhaṃsyati śūlapāṇiḥ
tatheti te 'api praṇipatya devā brahmārkaśakrānilapāvakādyāḥ
kailāsam āgamya sureśvareśaṃ dṛṣṭvā haraṃ tuṣṭuvurādṛtārthāḥ
haryarkaśakrāgnipitāmahānāṃ sraṣṭre namo deva rāya
sūkṣmāya nityaṃ parameśvarāya nityaṃ namaḥ sarvagatāya dhātre
namaḥ parāyātipare pumāṃse purāya ṣaḍviṃśakasaṃjñitāya
somānilārkajvalanāmbubhūmivyomātmakāyādisṛje namo 'astu
pūṣṇo namo dantavināśanāya kamāṅganāśāya namo 'astu nityam
namaḥ pradhānāya parāya puṃse yogādhigamyāya sadā namo 'astu
vidyāsṛje dharmasṛje namo 'astu sraṣṭre namo yajñasurasurāṇām
namastṛtīyekṣaṇadhāriṇe ca namo namo nīlaśikhaṇḍine ca
namo 'astu nityaṃ puruṣottamāya śmaśānavāsāya namaḥ sadaiva
namo 'astu daityāndhakanāśanāya namaḥ sadā mohavināśanāya
tamovināśāya namo 'astu nityam ajñānanāśāya namo 'astu nityam
namaḥ sadā mokṣavarapradāya namaḥ sadāyāmṛtasaṃsthitāya
yogeśvarāyāmarasaṃstutāya namo 'astu rudrāya parāya dhāmne
harāya śarvāya śivāya goptre namo 'astu bhīmāya ca śambhave ca
guṇairvihīnāya guṇotkaṭāya guṇeṣvatītāya guṇāsthitāya
gītāya sāṃkhye puruṣāya nityaṃ namo 'astu yogopaniṣatsthitāya
mahāpurāṇāya parāt parāya sthūlāya sūkṣmāya namaḥ sadaiva
prasādyamānaḥ kuru naḥ prasādaṃ tuṣṭaḥ pareśāna varaṃ prayaccha
śambhustathaivaṃ stuvatāṃ surāṇāṃ brahmendraviṣṇvarkapuraḥsarāṇām
prītastayā stotraviśeṣabhaktyā jagāda vākyaṃ paramādbhutārtham
tuṣṭo 'asmi devā vṛṇutādya śīghraṃ samīhitaṃ vo yadi kiṃcidasti
aṣṭaṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
devā ūcuḥ
durgaṃ tat tripuraṃ kṛtvā bādhyamāno baladarpitaiḥ
hṛtā apsarasaḥ sarvā dhvaṃsitāni vanāni ca
na teṣāṃ nigrahe śakto brahmāpyeṣa pitāmahaḥ
tathā kuru suraśreṣṭha varo 'ayaṃ naḥ pradīyatām
idam āha mahātejāḥ surān āśvāsayanniva
śatam aṃśaṃ sureśā vai gṛhītvā mama tejasaḥ
rudratejomayā bhūtvā dānavān vinihaṃsyatha
tataste punareveśaṃ prāhurvākyam idaṃ surāḥ
śaktāḥ sahasram apyaṃśam udvoḍhuṃ na vayaṃ tava
kā naḥ śaktiḥ sureśāna tejo māheśvaraṃ param
draṣṭuṃ dhārayituṃ vāpi prasādaṃ kuru naḥ prabho
na kathaṃcidvayaṃ śaktāstān hantuṃ dānavān balāt
tebhyaḥ kila varo datto brahmaṇānena śūladhṛk
nimeṣārdhaṃ kṣaṇe tasminnetadvastripuraṃ balī
sakṛdekam iṣuṃ kṣiptvā yaḥ pradhakṣyati dānavān
bhaviṣyati sa vo mṛtyurnānyathā maraṇaṃ hi vaḥ
tacca kartuṃ na śaktāḥ smaḥ prasādaṃ tena naḥ kuru
tataḥ sa bhagavān devaḥ praṇatān vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
punarāśvāsayan prāha samudvignān divaukasaḥ
yadyevaṃ suraśārdūlāstripuraṃ durgamaṃ mahat
iṣum ekaṃ sakṛt kṣiptvā pradhakṣye nimiṣe kṣaṇe
brahmaviṣṇupriyārthaṃ hi śakrasyānugrahāya ca
dhakṣyāmi tripuraṃ durgam ākrāntaṃ dānavaistribhiḥ
yādṛśaśca hi māṃ voḍhuṃ śaktaḥ syāt surapuṅgavāḥ
tato devāḥ praṇamyeśaṃ prahṛṣṭamanaso 'abhavan
tataḥ sa bhagavān brahmā tathā viṣṇuhutāśanau
dhātāraṃ bhāskaraṃ śakraṃ pavanaṃ dhanadaṃ yamam
vasūn rudrāṃstathādityān gandharvānaśvināvapi
garuḍān parvatān nāgān guhyakān samahodadhīn
ṛṣīn siddhāṃstathā yakṣān grahāṃ
sitaṃ kālaṃ tathā caiva vanaspatīn
divasāni muhūrtāni kṣaṇān kāṣṭhālavāṃstathā
ayane ca ṛtūn māsān pakṣān saṃvatsarāṃstathā
sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ yacca nakṣatrāṇi tathaiva ca
kāṃściccakradvaye cakruḥ pratāpa
ścii ratha cānyān yuyujuḥ surapuṅgavān
kṛtvāśvāṃścaturo devān rathe tasmin nyayojayan
viṣṇuḥ pitāmaho 'agniśca praṇamya parameśvaram
rathaḥ sajja iti prāhurvināśāya suradviṣām
tataḥ sa bhagavāñchambhuḥ stūyamānaḥ suraistribhiḥ
pitāmahaṃ tato vīkṣya provāca vacasāṃ patiḥ
dagdhavyaṃ tripuraṃ yena tam iṣuṃ śīghram ānaya
tataḥ provāca taṃ brahmā praṇamya vṛṣabhadhvajam
tataḥ pārśvasthitau dṛṣṭvā śambhurviṣṇuhutāśanau
dṛṣṭipātena tau devau samāhvayadarindamaḥ
tau dvāvañjalim ādhāya sureśānam upasthitau
oṣadhīnāṃ patiṃ somaṃ puṅkhe tasya nyayojayat
śalyaṃ ca pāvakaṃ cakre brahmāṇaṃ sa tato 'abravīt
mahyaṃ dadāsi yadi ājñām aham eva hi sārathiḥ
rudrapāriṣadā ye ca nandīśvarapurogamāḥ
śaṅkukarṇapurogāśca ye ca caṇḍeśvarādayaḥ
gaṇeśvarā mahāyogāstryakṣāḥ paṭṭiśapāṇayaḥ
nanāśastrapraharaṇā nānāyuddhaviśāradāḥ
nānābharaṇavastrāśca nānāvidyāviśāradāḥ
vādayantaḥ samaṃ vādyān bherīśaṅkhasvanān bahūn
ājagmurgaṇamukhyāste sahasrāṇi caturdaśa
nānāvidhānāṃ puṣpāṇām upariṣṭāt sahasraśaḥ
aśaktā bhāram udvoḍhuṃ mumuhurdevatā bhṛśam
tatastān devedeveśo jñātvā mūḍhān divaukasaḥ
jagāma tripuraṃ śīghraṃ viśvakarmadidṛkṣayā
athāgatam ṛṣiṃ dṛṣṭvā viśvakarmā mayastadā
sa dattvā hi āśiṣastasmai vetrāsana upāviśat
brahmāṇaṃ sārathiṃ kṛtvā svayam āyāti śaṃkaraḥ
nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā sa tadā dānavādhipaḥ
tārakākṣaṃ samāhūya vidyunmālinam eva ca
tathānyānasurān bhrātRn bāṇanemipuraḥsarān
nāradena yadākhyātaṃ sarvam aśrāvayat tadā
yodhayennirbhayo yastvāṃ cintāṃ tvaṃ maya mā kṛthāḥ
saṃgatya daivatāḥ sarve yadi yoddhum ihāgatāḥ
durbalaḥ kurute bhedaṃ dānaṃ sāntvam athāpi vā
praṇāmaṃ jyāyasaḥ śatrorvayaṃ tu balinaḥ sadā
durbalasya ripordaṇḍo balinā vijigīṣatā
tadvayaṃ balino daityā hīnāśca tridivaukasaḥ
hatvā daṇḍena tān sarvān sthāsyāmo nirvṛtāḥ sukham
tārakākṣavacaḥ śrutvā vidyunmālī vaco 'abravīt
mamāpyetadatīveṣṭaṃ rājño 'asya vacanaṃ śubham
na śaktā yoddhum asmābhirdevatā balavarjitāḥ
te cedyotsyanti saṃmūḍhāḥ prayāsyanti tataḥ kṣayam
anyonyaṃ tu vayaṃ yuddhādupāyaṃ teṣu yuñjamahe
adya hatvā surān sarvān kuru rājyaṃ triviṣṭape
hiraṇyakaśipuṃ smṛtvā hiraṇyākṣaṃ ca daityapa
tataḥ śrutvā mayo vyāsa vidyunmālivibhāṣitam
yastulyaḥ svabale śatrurhīno vā daityapuṅgavāḥ
samā divaukaso 'asmākaṃ balenāsurapuṅgavāḥ
tairdevaiḥ sārdham asmākaṃ yuktaṃ sāmādiyojanam
ya eṣa bhagavān īśaḥ sarvabhūteśvareśvaraḥ
asmākaṃ devatānāṃ ca sraṣṭā hartā ca sa prabhuḥ
sa hantuṃ svayam āyāti upāyastasya kīdṛśaḥ
praṇāmaḥ saṃśrayaścaiva guṇopāyau kapardinaḥ
yadi kārkaśyam āsthāya yodhayāmaḥ pinākinam
brahmādyāḥ śaraṇaṃ śambhum arditā yānti śāntaye
abhidhyānāt kṣaṇenaiva praṇaśyeta bhavedapi
kīdṛśaṃ tena yuddhaṃ no devadevena śambhunā
kiṃ na vettha śiśuprajñā loṣṭugiryoryadantaram
īpsadhve mohitā yuddhe kālapāśena yantritāḥ
yadi yūyam api prājñā mama śuśrūṣavo yadi
mā kṛḍhvaṃ śambhunā yuddhaṃ gacchadhvaṃ śaraṇaṃ śivam
tam evaṃvādinaṃ śrutvā viśvakarmāṇam ūrjitam
nārado bhagavān prāha dānavāntakaraṃ vacaḥ
bhavatāṃ tat tapaḥ kṣīṇam aiśvaryaṃ bhuktam eva ca
klībatām api kurvanto yūyaṃ naṃkṣyatha dānavāḥ
vṛtaḥ sarvāmaraiḥ śambhurvadhārthaṃ bhavatām iha
praṇatānapyasau yuṣmāṃstatpriyārthaṃ nihaṃsyati
kathaṃ danusutā bhūtvā rājāno baladarpitāḥ
bhītā mṛtyuṃ jigīṣadhvaṃ kṛpaṇā iva dānavāḥ
prāpsyathādhikam aiśvaryaṃ tyakṣyathāsūn raṇe yadi
vinā yuddhaṃ vipannānām aśubhā vo gatirbhavet
pramathendrāstato yūyaṃ bhaviṣyatha na saṃśayaḥ
guṇaṃ sandhigataṃ nāsti yuṣmākaṃ devataiḥ saha
śauryeṇa bhavatāṃ prītaḥ kadācidvṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
kariṣyāmi ca vo rakṣāṃ śastrāghātaniṣedhanīm
uttiṣṭhata danoḥ putrā vijayāya yuyutsayā
nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā tārakākṣo mahābalaḥ
vidyunmālī ca daityendrā bāṇādyāśca mahāsurāḥ
kālapāśārditā mūḍhāḥ kṣīṇapuṇyā gatāyuṣaḥ
nārado 'api tato hṛṣṭo rakṣāṃ baddhvā tu māyayā
yuyutsūnasurān kṛtvā yayau śarvarathaṃ prati
tataste dānavāḥ sarve yuddhāya kṛtaniścayāḥ
nānāpraharaṇopetā babhūvuryuddhalipsavaḥ
tarakākṣo balo bāṇo vidyunmālī ca dānavaḥ
avādyanta tataḥ śaṅkhāstūryāṇi ca sahasraśaḥ
dānavānāṃ bale ghore kātarāṇāṃ bhayaprade
saratho 'ayam ihāyāti asāvanyaḥ pradṛśyate
katham āhata ityevaṃ vacāṃsi ūcuḥ parasparam
vigatabhayaviṣādāstraipurā daityasaṃghāḥ
te vīkṣya durgaṃ tripuraṃ gaṇeśā nandīśacaṇḍīśamukhāḥ suyattāḥ
nādaṃ pracakruḥ sahitāḥ pravīrā yuyutsavo dānavarājasiṃhaiḥ
caṇḍeśvaraścaṇḍavapurmahātmā jvalatpradīptograkuṭhārapāṇiḥ
dīptaṃ triśūlaṃ parigṛhya nandī tryakṣaḥ pratasthe haratulyavarṣmā
pārśve sthito 'abhūt sa ca śaṅkukarṇaḥ pragṛhya dīptaṃ muśalaṃ gaṇendraḥ
bhṛṅgirharātmā sa ca vīrabhadrastathā gaṇendrāḥ śataśaḥ pravīrāḥ
vajtratriśūlāsibhuśuṇḍihastā yuyutsavastasthurupetaharṣāḥ
samāgataṃ taṃ ratham īkṣya daityā yuddhāya nirjagmurupetamohāḥ
te tārakākṣapramukhāḥ suvīrāḥ sannahya nānāyudhadīptahastāḥ
sārdhaṃ gaṇendraiḥ samaraṃ pracakrurdanoḥ sutāḥ kopavaśaṃ prayātāḥ
tasthau tathaivāsakṛdātmanā ca paśyan raṇaṃ tadgaṇadaityapānām
vivyādha bhṛṅgiṃ daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkairvidyutprabhuḥ kopaviraktanetraḥ
bhṛṅgiṃ samāsādya śilīmukhāste nāśaknuvaṃstasya rujaṃ prakartum
vidyutprabhaṃ bhṛṅgiriṭistato 'asau śūlena dīptena jaghāna pṛṣṭhe
sa tena śūlena hato jaghūrṇa tyaktvā ca bhṛṅgiṃ prayayau bhayārtaḥ
vivyādha tīkṣṇairniśitaiḥ pṛṣatkairvināyakaṃ saptabhiraṃsadeśe
punastriṣaṣṭyā daśabhiśca bhūyo vidyutprabhastaṃ gajarājavaktram
sa puṣkarāgreṇa gajendrasiṃho grīvāṃ tadā daityapaterviveṣṭya
utpāṭayāmāsa śiraḥ śarīrāt padmaṃ hradānnāga iva pramattaḥ
kruddhāvupāgamya hi śaṅkukarṇaṃ śilīmukhairvivyadhaturgaṇendram
taṃ jaghnaturnaikavidhaiḥ pṛṣatkairvajrābhighātapratimaiḥ sutīkṣṇaiḥ
dīptena hatvā muśalena vīrau sampreṣayāmāsa puraṃ yamasya
anye ca daityāstripurādhivāsāḥ kruddhā viniṣkramya gaṇendrasiṃhaiḥ
nārācacakrāsikuṭhārahastā ghoraṃ mahadyuddham atīva cakruḥ
daityādhipāste haratulyakalpairgaṇeśvaraiḥ prāptaśivaprasādaiḥ
prabhraṣṭanānāyudhavastrahārāśchinnairbhujaiḥ śoṇitam udvahantaḥ
vajrāhatā petuḥ samudre giriśṛṅgakalpāḥ
taṃ śaṅkukarṇo ditijādhipeśaṃ muñcantam ugraṃ śaravarṣam āśu
bhallena daityaṃ girisannikāśaṃ jaghāna mūrdhni prasabhaṃ gaṇeśaḥ
protthāya tūrṇaṃ sa hi tārakākṣaścikṣepa tasmai gaṇapāya cakram
kruddhastato 'asāvabhavadgaṇendrastaṃ tārakākṣaṃ sa hi saṅkukarṇaḥ
nipātya muṣṭyā prajaghāna mūrdhni samāhataḥ so 'api jagāma kṛcchram
mumoca roṣaṃ virarāva tīvraṃ mamāra paścādasuvipramuktaḥ
dṛṣṭvā vipannaṃ ditijādhipendraṃ pragṛhya daityā bhavanaṃ mayasya
tato mayastān rudataḥ sureśān āśvāsayan prāha vacaḥ suresaḥ
sṛṣṭaṃ mayā vo 'amṛtam etadāste tenainam utthāpayāśu daityāḥ
tato gṛhītvāmṛtam uttamaṃ taddaityādhipaṃ daityavṛṣāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ
cakruḥ sajīvaṃ hi yathā purāṇaṃ mayaṃ praṇemuśca muhuḥ śirobhiḥ
sa tārakākṣastata āśu bhūyo yuyutsayā yuddhapathaṃ jagāma
āyāntam ālakṣya pitāmahastaṃ pūrvaṃ mṛtaṃ jīvitam āśu bhūyaḥ
provāca vākyaṃ sa surāsureśaṃ nivedayan vāmakāreṇa daityam
hato 'apyayaṃ śaṃkara tārakākṣaḥ kṛto mayenāśu sajīva eva
tasyāsti devāmṛtam uttamaṃ hi tenāsurāñjīvayate 'asurendraḥ
doṣo mahāneṣa surendrahetormṛtān mṛtāñjīvayate yadājau
tato 'amṛtaṃ tanmayasaṃstham āśu pradhyānamātreṇa jahāra śambhuḥ
pitāmahastaṃ punareva hṛṣṭaḥ pinākinaṃ prāha vacaḥ praṇamya
dṛṣṭaṃ mayā yuddham idaṃ gaṇānāṃ daityādhipaiḥ sārdham ahīnasattvaiḥ
divyaṃ sahasraṃ vigataṃ samānāṃ kṣayaṃ na caitat tripuraṃ jagāma
kṣipasva dīptaṃ tam iṣuṃ sureśa prayāntu nāśaṃ suravidviṣaste
saṃkalpamātrādidam eti nāśaṃ daityādhivāsaṃ tripuraṃ taveśa
yadi tvahaṃ mānayitavya īśa vimunca śīghraṃ tripure śaraṃ tam
vijñapta evaṃ caturānanena pratīpam ālīḍham anaṅgahantā
kṛtvā dhanustadbalavadvikṛṣya yuyoja dīptaṃ tam iṣuṃ pināke
saṃkalpamātreṇa tadā sa tāni purāṇi devaḥ sahitāni trīṇi
cakre jagatsṛṣṭivināśakartā jagacca niṣpandam abhūt tadāśu
viṣṇvātmakaṃ pāvakasomapuṅkhaṃ trailokyasaṃhāra iva pradīptam
cikṣepa devastam iṣuṃ tadograṃ kṣiptvā ca kaṣṭaṃ dhigitīti cāha
nandī samāgamya tato maheśaṃ provāca vākyaṃ kim iti praṇamya
nandīśvaraṃ taṃ bhagavānuvāca mayasya bhaktasya śubhaṃ cikīrṣuḥ
nandī pragṛhyātha sureśvarājñāṃ tūrṇaṃ yayau viśvakṛtaḥ puraṃ tat
dṛṣṭvā mayaṃ tatra sa dānaveśaṃ mūrdhnā natāṅgaṃ vṛṣabhadhvajasya
mṛtyorbhayārtaṃ śaraṇārthinaṃ ca nandī samāśvāsayadīśabhaktam
nandīśvaraṃ dānavarāṭ sa dṛṣṭvā śrutvā priyaṃ tacchivasamprasādam
athāgnirāgāt tripuraṃ didhakṣan pradīpayitvā sakalaṃ samantāt
tam āgataṃ viśvakṛto nivāsaṃ viṣṇvinduyuktaṃ jvalanaṃ sa nandī
nandī hutāśaṃ sa tato 'abhyuvāca mayo 'atra tiṣṭhatyamareśabhaktaḥ
taṃ vahnirāhāsurarājam āśu tūrṇaṃ vinirgaccha mayeti vākyam
haimaṃ gṛhītvā sa maheśaliṅgaṃ purādviniṣkramya mayo 'asurendraḥ
pātālam āśu praviveśa hṛṣṭaḥ kurvan namaskāram umāpriyasya
nandīśvaraḥ so 'api sureśapārśvam āgamya cākhyāya ca saṃsthito 'abhūt
tataḥ pradīptaṃ tripuraṃ babhūva viśkiṣṭayantrārgalanaṣṭaveśma
vātāyane harmyavimānasaṃsthāścandrānanāḥ pīnapayodharāḍhyāḥ
paryaṅkasuptā madavihvalākṣyo mārgaṃ priyāṇāṃ muhurīhṣamāṇāḥ
vilocanaistāmranibhāṅgarāgaiḥ śyāmāvadātā jaghanairviśālaiḥ
daityāṅganāḥ svaṃ dadṛśuḥ pradīptam āliṅgyamānāḥ śarapāvakena
prāsādasaṃsthāḥ prayayurbhayārttāstrāsena kinnarya ivācalasthāḥ
priyānathodvīkṣya samāgatāṃstān mohaṃ samāliṅgya bhṛśaṃ vijagmuḥ
priyā gṛhītvā ditijāstataste pranaṣṭakāmāstarasābhijagmuḥ
niṣkrāntamātrāḥ śivaśaktimūḍhāḥ petuḥ samudre balaviprayuktāḥ
daityān samudre patitāṃstatastān matsyā mahānto girisannikāśāḥ
tīvrāśca nakrā makarāśca ghorāḥ saṃjagrasurnaṣṭabalān vimūḍhān
jalecarendrāstvapare mahāntaḥ saṃchinnahārāḥ patitāḥ striyastāḥ
hīnāḥ priyairbhakṣayituṃ pravṛttāḥ karāladaṃṣṭrā vivṛtānanāśca
tā bhakṣyamāṇāḥ patitāstaruṇyaḥ priyān saroṣaṃ bahuśo nirīkṣya
rujā mahatyā parikhidyamānāḥ saṃcukruśurdīnataraṃ yuvatyaḥ
tāsāṃ tadā daityavilāsinīnāṃ reje bhṛśaṃ krodhanirīkṣitaṃ tat
ratāvasāne parikheditānāṃ priyairivānyām abhigantukāmaiḥ
sarve tato daityavṛṣāḥ sabhāryāḥ pradahyamānāstripurānalena
śaraśca so 'agnīndujanārdanātmā pradahya kṛtsnaṃ tripuraṃ puraṃ tat
kṣiptvā samudre sma śamaṃ prayātaṃ śaśāma śambhośca karaṃ jagāma
pūrvaṃ yathā divyaśarīrayuktāṃścakāra sṛṣṭipralayādihetuḥ
daityā hatāstat tripuraṃ pradagdhaṃ śāntiḥ kṛtā naḥ sma surāsureśa
namo 'astu sarvatra sadā sthitāya sraṣṭre surāṇāṃ parameśa tubhyam
tān āha devaḥ sa tadā surendrān brahmārkaviṣṇvindradhaneśvarādyān
sadaiva yūyaṃ pratipālanīyā rakṣyāśca devāḥ sutavanmayaiva
pūrṇābhilāṣā hatavidviṣaśca prayāta hṛṣṭāḥ svaniveśanāni
devāstato devavaraṃ praṇamya jagmuḥ svakīyāni niveśanāni
devo 'api siddhairabhivandyamānaḥ kailāsaśṛṅgaṃ sahito gaṇendraiḥ
caṇḍeśanandīśvaravīrabhadrairjagāma kartā jagatastrinetraḥ
vyāsa uvāca
kasmāt kruddho nagendraṃ taṃ krauñcaṃ dāritavān guhaḥ
pakṣān sarvagirīndrāṇāṃ kasmācciccheda vāsavaḥ
śṛṇu vyāsa mahābuddhe yanmāṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
kumāreṇa yathā bhinno mainākiḥ krauñcaparvataḥ
apaśyadvāsavaḥ skandaṃ saṃghātaṃ tejasām iva
śarastambavane dṛṣṭvā kumāram analaprabham
surarājyamadāviṣṭaḥ śakraḥ papraccha ṣaṇmukham
na māṃ pūjayase dṛṣṭvā devarājam ihāgatam
tam evaṃvādinaṃ śakraṃ prāha śūladharātmajaḥ
brahmādyā māṃ vijānanti siddhā vedavidaśca ye
kiṃ tvayā jānatā śakra kāryaṃ kiṃ pūjitena vā
ehyehi tvaṃ mayā sārdhaṃ kuru śīghraṃ pradakṣiṇam
bāḍham ityevam uktvātha kumāraḥ ṣaṇmukhastadā
śakreṇa saha saṃgatya mayūravaram āsthitaḥ
kṛtvā sunirvṛtastasthau upaviṣṭaḥ śilātale
javenātha kumārastaṃ krauñcaṃ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam
provācendraṃ tadā dṛṣṭvā jetāham iti satvaraḥ
asakṛdbruvata evaṃ tayoḥ śakrakumārayoḥ
tataḥ śakra uvācedaṃ kumāraṃ vacanaṃ tadā
eṣa evāvayoḥ krañco jayasākṣī mahābalaḥ
nānṛtaṃ vakṣyati hyeṣa pautro himagirervaraḥ
pṛcchyatāṃ śakra ko doṣa iti āha jvalanātmajaḥ
taṃ śakraṃ sādaraṃ prāha kena tvam acalāgrataḥ
kṛtapradakṣiṇo brūhi pramāṇaṃ hi tvam āvayoḥ
tataḥ krauñco vimūḍhātmā saṃcintya suciraṃ nagaḥ
ayaṃ śacīpatiścakre mām ihāgre pradakṣiṇam
papāta śikharaṃ tūrṇaṃ kuliśena yathā hatam
tatrāsan yāni bhūtāni surādyāni girīśvare
tāni saṃtyajya śīghraṃ taṃ prayayuḥ sarvato diśam
jahṛṣe vāsavaścāpi manasā pūjayan girim
tataścukrodha rudrātmā gireḥ krauñcasya ṣaṇmukhaḥ
guhaṃ draṣṭuṃ saṃkruddhaṃ vāsavastadā
kṣīṇāyuṣo yathā puṃso mṛtyupāśa
mūrtimānapatadbhūmau saṃjñāprāṇavivarjitaḥ
patiṃ vinihataṃ dṛṣṭvā patnyastasya suduḥkhitāḥ
vilapantyastadā dīnaṃ petuḥ krauñcācalopari
pāriyātraśca sahyaśca niṣadhodayavāmanāḥ
sarve parvatarājāna ājagmuḥ śokapīḍitāḥ
parivārya giriṃ krauñcaṃ rurudurduḥkhitā bhṛśam
bhrātṛputraṃ hataṃ jñātvā devadevī girīndrajā
śarveṇa sahitā krauñcam ājagāma mahāvratā
kumāreṇa hataṃ dṛṣṭvā krauñcaṃ bāndhavam ātmanaḥ
pīḍitābhūt tadā devī dṛṣṭvā pitaram arditam
śuśoca girijā dṛṣṭvā muhurvīkṣya sureśvaram
śokenāpi susantaptā namaścakrurmahābalāḥ
vyajñāpayata dīnātmā duḥkhaśokapariplutaḥ
śakreṇānena bhagavan ātmānaṃ bahumanyatā
nidhanaṃ nāyitaḥ pautro mamāyaṃ krauñcaparvataḥ
nāntaraṃ veda yo darpāt kumārasyātmanaśca ha
spardhāṃ kṛtvā kumāreṇa hate pautre mamādhunā
nirvṛto gatadarpo 'ayaṃ sukhaṃ tiṣṭhatu vāsavaḥ
vinedurduḥkhasaṃtaptā bāndhavābhāvapīḍitāḥ
pitaraṃ duḥkhitaṃ dṛṣṭvā tathānyān bāndhavān girīn
atha tān duḥkhitān dṛṣṭvā sarvān govṛṣavāhanaḥ
mā kārṣṭa śokam ityuktvā tanayaṃ prāha ṣaṇmukham
nāśubhaṃ kurvate kasmāt krauñcaṃ nihatavānasi
bhrātṛsūnurbhavanmātureṣa krauñco mahāgiriḥ
kathaṃ bhrātaram enaṃ svaṃ hatavānasi ṣaṇmukha
tam evaṃvādinaṃ devaṃ ṣaṇmukhaḥ pitaraṃ tadā
idaṃ provāca savrīḍaṃ vacanaṃ paramādbhutam
śakrasyāpanayāddeva krauñca eṣa hato mayā
asanmantritavān yasmādvijñaptim aparāṃ śṛṇu
tvatprasādādahaṃ krauñcaṃ jīvayāmi nagottamam
uttiṣṭheti tataḥ krauñcaṃ bhrātaraṃ prāha ṣaṇmukhaḥ
sa bibhrat pūrvavaddehaṃ krauñco nagapatiḥ kṣaṇāt
uttasthau nīrujo vyāsa āścaryaṃ tadabhūt tadā
jīvitenācalenaivaṃ ṣaṇmukho vahnisaprabhaḥ
samakṣaṃ sarvadevānāṃ śakrasya ca mahābalaḥ
vāyuviṣṇuyamānāṃ ca brahmaṇaśca mahātmanaḥ
devadevaṃ praṇamyeśaṃ pitaraṃ hyumayā saha
babhāṣe vacanaṃ devaḥ kumāravararūpadhṛk
śakreṇānena devendrā matsamakṣaṃ prabhāṣitam
tanmayaiṣā mahāśaktirnikhātā vasudhātale
utpāṭayatu sa hyetāṃ mahāṃ mattastato hi saḥ
evam uktvā tato devo bālārkasadṛśaprabhaḥ
tūṣṇīṃ babhūva hṛṣṭātmā tasthau ca pitṛpārśvataḥ
utpāṭayitum utsehe tāṃ śaktiṃ vasudhāṃ gatām
na ca cālayituṃ śakto yatnādapi surādhipaḥ
tato 'anye daivataśreṣṭhā yamānilapuraḥsarāḥ
matiṃ cakruḥ samuddhartuṃ yatnaṃ śaktyāśca daṃśitāḥ
na ca cālayituṃ śekustāṃ śaktim amarottamāḥ
tato viṣṇurameyātmā devān dṛṣṭvā hataujasaḥ
tenāsau cālyamānāpi yasmācchaktirdharātale
na cacāla mahāvīryā skandatejobalānvitā
tato viṣṇurameyātmā jñātvā tattvārtham ādṛtaḥ
kumāraṃ pūjayan bhaktyā śaktyutkṣepānnyavartata
atha sarve 'amarā vyāsa viṣṇuśca surasattamaḥ
devānāṃ mahādevasutaḥ prabhuḥ
nāthaḥ pālayitā sraṣṭā ārtighnaḥ pravaro mahān
tvayā nāthena deveśa vayaṃ sarve sunirvṛtāḥ
tiṣṭhāmaḥ sahitāḥ sarve tvam asmān pāhi sarvataḥ
śakravyatikramaṃ caiva bāliśyānmohakāritam
praṇayādyācito 'asmābhiḥ kṣantum arhasi sarvadā
evaṃ sa bhagavān sarvaiḥ kumāraḥ saṃstuto 'amaraiḥ
devarājastathā śakro hṛṣṭā guham apūjayan
bhagavānapi saṃtuṣṭastanayāya varān dadau
yayau cāpi gireḥ śṛṅgaṃ divyaṃ himavataḥ śubham
sārdhaṃ guhena devyā ca mātRṇāṃ gaṇanāyakaḥ
krauñcena sahitāścāpi meruvindhyādayo 'acalāḥ
śakraśca surarāḍdevaḥ svāni sadmāni bhejire
evam etadyathā krauñcaḥ krauñcasārasavāsinaḥ
guhena dāritaḥ śaktyā paścāccaiva kṛto 'amaraḥ
dṛśyate cāpi tat krauñce kṣataṃ śaktyācalottame
ya imaṃ śṛṇuyānmartyaḥ sarvapāpaiḥ sa mucyate
vyāsa uvāca
bhagavan parameśāno mātRṇāṃ nāyakaḥ katham
kā etā mātaraścāpi śaṃsaitat pṛcchato mama
kathaṃ mātṛgaṇā jātāḥ kiṃnimittam athāpi ca
kiṃvīryāḥ kimprabhāvāśca sambhutāste gaṇāḥ prabho
kaścāsām āśrayastena vartante tadgaṇāḥ śubhāḥ
kena sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃ vāpi etadicchāmi veditum
atra te vartayiṣyāmi mātRṇām udbhavaṃ śubham
purā hi bhagavān brahmā sṛṣṭvemā vividhāḥ prajāḥ
avekṣamāṇaḥ kāleya cacāra vibudheśvaraḥ
sa kadācit prajādhyakṣaḥ saṃdhyākāla upāgate
deśaṃ ramyaṃ samāsādya tīre pūrvamahodadheḥ
ramye cakāra saṃdhyāṃ hi varṣakoṭim atandritaḥ
cintayāmāsa ramyo 'ayaṃ deśo dṛṣṭimanoharaḥ
aṭṭāṭṭahāsakaiścaiva khātakaiśca samanvitam
śṛṅgāṭakacatuṣkeṇa catuṣpādam iva sthitam
vaprakhātakasaṃyuktairgṛhaiścāpi mahādhanaiḥ
madhye mandākinī vāpī sariddivyā manoharā
nalinīvanasaṃchannā prahṛṣṭakhaganāditā
tat sṛṣṭvā tu puraṃ brahmā sauvarṇaṃ maṇibhūṣitam
avadhyāste jarāhīnāstejobalasamanvitāḥ
bhaviṣyanti mahābhāgā matprasādānna saṃśayaḥ
asmin sadaiva kāmānām iṣṭānāṃ surasattamaḥ
devo varṣati koṭiṃ vai tenāsmin sukhino janāḥ
evaṃ sa bhagavānuktvā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
adhiṣṭhitaṃ puraṃ tadvai sarvairbrāhmaṇakaṇṭakaiḥ
yeṣāṃ patirasukrodhaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
brahmahā yajñahā vipra devāntakasurāntakaḥ
siṃhanādo bhīmanādo mada ityevamādayaḥ
atha daityāḥ samāgamya haimakuṇḍapuraḥsarāḥ
tasmin puravare sthitvā pīḍāṃ cakruranekaśaḥ
yajñahomādikāśchinnāḥ kriyāstairasurādhamaiḥ
tānevaṃkāriṇo jñātvā sarva eva divaukasaḥ
vaco divaukasāṃ śrutvā jñātvā daityaviceṣṭitam
ājagāma bhavaṃ draṣṭuṃ ramyaṃ hīmagirervanam
yatra gaurī tapastepe bhartṛdehārdhadhāriṇī
praviṣṭāstatra te devā brahmādyāḥ sarva eva hi
striya evābhavaṃstūrṇaṃ pārvatyāstapaso balāt
tatastān devadeveśaḥ strībhūtān hi surottamān
kimartham āgatā yūyam iti papraccha śūladhṛk
nivedya śambhave paścāt kṛcchraṃ strībhāvam ātmanaḥ
yathaivaṃ puruṣāḥ pūrvaṃ bhavāma iti te 'abruvan
tānuvācātha deveśaḥ surān strībhāvam āgatān
yāta yūyaṃ surāḥ sarve striyo bhūtvāsurāntikam
strīṇām eva hi te vadhyā dānavā baladarpitāḥ
tanūrmūrtimatīḥ kṛtvā parato mātaraḥ śubhāḥ
ye ya eva yathā pūrvaṃ bhaviṣyatha surottamāḥ
atha bhūyaḥ praṇamyeśaṃ devatā idam abruvan
yayā sārdhaṃ balāddaityān haṃsyāmaḥ parameśvara
tato devo 'asṛjaddevīṃ rudrāṇīṃ mātaraṃ śubhām
vikṛtaṃ rūpam āsthāya dvitīyām api mātaram
nāmnā tu bahumāṃsāṃ tāṃ jagatsaṃhārarūpiṇīm
mātarāvasṛjaddve tu vārāhīṃ vaiṣṇavīm api
abhūt pitāmahādbrāhmī śarvāṇī śaṃkarādapi
kaumārī ṣaṇmukhāccāpi viṣṇorapi ca vaiṣṇavī
vārāhi mādhavāddevī māhendrī ca purandarāt
sarvatejomayī devī mātRṇāṃ pravarā śubhā
bahumāṃsā mahāvidyā babhūva vṛṣabhadhvajāt
sarvāsāṃ devatānāṃ ca dehebhyo mātaraḥ śubhāḥ
svarūpabaladhāriṇyo nirjagmurdaityanāśanāḥ
vāyavyā vāruṇī yāmyā kauberī ca mahābalāḥ
mahākālī tathāgneyī anyāścaiva sahasraśaḥ
tā gatvā tat puraṃ ramyaṃ daityān bhīmaparākramān
daityahīnaṃ ca taccakruḥ purāgryaṃ hemabhūṣitam
ājagāma pradeśaṃ taṃ mātRṇāṃ varaditsayā
tān dṛṣṭvā nihatān sarvān daityānamaravidviṣaḥ
parituṣṭastadā tāsāṃ varān prādādvṛṣadhvajaḥ
jagato mātaro yūyaṃ mātṛbhūtā bhaviṣyathaḥ
yuṣmākaṃ ye bhaviṣyanti bhaktāḥ puruṣapuṅgavāḥ
striyo vāpi mahābhāgā na tān hiṃsanti hiṃsakāḥ
mṛtā mama gaṇāścāpi bhaviṣyantyajarāmarāḥ
bhavatīnām idaṃ sthānaṃ koṭīvarṣam iti śrutam
ahaṃ heturhi yuṣmākaṃ yasmāt sṛṣṭā mayaiva ca
hetukeśvaranāmnāhaṃ sthāsyāmyatra varapradaḥ
yastu yuṣmān mayā sārdhaṃ vidhivat pūjayiṣyati
sarvapāpavimuktātmā sa parāṃ gatim āpsyati
dānavā nihatā yasmācchūlena bahumāṃsayā
śūlakuṇḍam idaṃ nāmnā khyātaṃ tīrthaṃ bhaviṣyati
iha śūlodakaṃ pītvā bahumāṃsāṃ praṇamya ca
adhṛṣyaḥ sarvahiṃsrāṇāṃ bhaviṣyati narottamaḥ
pratikūleti vikhyātā ramyā mandākinī nadī
ahaṃ brahmā ca viṣṇuśca ṛṣayaśca tapodhanāḥ
mātṛtantrāṇi divyāni mātṛyajñavidhiṃ param
puṇyāni prakariṣyāmo yajanaṃ yairavāpsyatha
brāhmaṃ svāyambhuvaṃ caiva kaumāraṃ yāmalaṃ tathā
sārasvataṃ sa gāndhāram aiśānaṃ nandiyāmalam
tantrāṇyetāni yuṣmākaṃ tathānyāni sahasraśaḥ
narāṇāṃ yajamānānāṃ varān yūyaṃ pradāsyatha
yāśca nāryaḥ sadā yuṣmān yakṣyante sarahasyataḥ
yogeśvaryo bhaviṣyanti rāmā divyaparākramāḥ
chagalaḥ kumbhakarṇaśca madīyau gaṇanāyakau
yuṣmākaṃ dvārapālatve sthāsyatastau mamājñayā
koṭīvarṣam idaṃ sthānaṃ mātRṇāṃ priyam uttamam
śmaśānaṃ pravaraṃ divyaṃ bhaviṣyati sukhapradam
varānevaṃ hi tāllabdhvā mātaro lokamātaraḥ
bhaktyā praṇamya deveśaṃ mumudurbhṛśam arditāḥ
tataḥ prabhṛti tāḥ sarvāḥ sahitāḥ śaśimaulinā
koṭīvarṣe vasanti sma sarvalokābhayapradāḥ
evaṃ sa bhagavān devo mātRṇāṃ gaṇanāyakaḥ
abhavacchaṃkaro vyāsa yanmāṃ tvaṃ pṛṣṭavānasi
utpattim etāṃ jagatīśvarīṇāṃ brahmendraśakrānilavanditānām
paṭhenmanuṣyaḥ śṛṇuyācca nityaṃ yaḥ svargalokaṃ sa mṛto labheta
śakreṇa girayaḥ pūrvaṃ chinnapakṣā yathā kṛtāḥ
tat pravakṣyāmi te vyāsa śṛṇu sarvam aśeṣataḥ
purā siṃhavapuḥ kṛtvā viṣṇunā paramaujasā
hate pitari sa śrīmān mahādaityapatīśvaraḥ
bahūnyabdasahasrāṇi cakārograṃ mahātapaḥ
praṇamyovāca varadam idaṃ brahmāṇam āgatam
rājānaṃ hatavān viṣṇuḥ pitaraṃ mama māyayā
saṃgrāme tam ahaṃ viṣṇuṃ yathā hanyāṃ tathā kuru
ajayyaḥ samare viṣṇuravadhyaśca surāsuraiḥ
prasādāddevadevasya jagatsraṣṭurumāpateḥ
naiṣa śakyo mayā dātuṃ varastubhyaṃ mahāsura
anyaṃ vṛṇu yatheṣṭaṃ tvaṃ varaṃ yāvaddadāmi te
tasya viṣṇostato deva śakrasyānyasya vā ripoḥ
kathaṃ hanyām ahaṃ viṣṇuṃ śakraṃ caiva śatakratum
sarvaśailādhipaḥ śrīmāṃścakramaddhimavān giriḥ
dvābhyām utpatya pakṣābhyām ājagāma viyaccaraḥ
purā hi girayo vyāsa āsan pakṣasamanvitāḥ
tam āgatam atho dṛṣṭvā prahrādo himavadgirim
prāhedaṃ vacanaṃ prītaḥ kṛtvā svāgatam āditaḥ
devatā bhrātaro bhūtvā asmākaṃ devatāśca hi
avamanyāsurānasmān rājyaṃ kurvanti darpitāḥ
vayaṃ yūyaṃ ca saṃgatya jitvā devānaśeṣataḥ
devānāṃ yajanaṃ yeṣu hūyante yeṣu cāgnayaḥ
prīyante devatā yeṣu deśāṃstānacaleśvara
ijyāhīnāṃstato devān sukhaṃ haṃsyāma nirvṛtāḥ
naitadyuktam iti prāha sāśaṅko dānavādhipam
eṣa tvāṃ sahitaḥ śailairneṣyāmi nidhanaṃ samam
daityarājaṃ tataḥ kruddhaṃ dṛṣṭvā parvatasattamaḥ
atha śailaistadā sārdhaṃ himavānacalottamaḥ
pitṛdevātmikāḥ sarvā yajñahomādikāḥ kriyāḥ
śakrāyāśrāvayat sarvaṃ parvatānāṃ vyatikramam
imaṃ vyatikramaṃ prāptā na doṣo naḥ kathaṃcana
tenedaṃ kāritaṃ sarvaṃ yajñadeśopamardanam
tānevaṃ bruvataḥ śakraḥ sutarāṃ manyumān girīn
pakṣahīnāṃstadā cakre kṣiptvā vajraṃ punaḥ punaḥ
hīnapakṣāstataste tu sarva evācaleśvarāḥ
peturmahītale vyāsa chinnapakṣāḥ khagā iva
pakṣacchedaṃ nagendrāṇāṃ bhṛśaṃ cukrodha pīḍitaḥ
kiṃ karomīti saṃcintya ciraṃ daityagaṇādhipaḥ
badaryāśramam āgatya dadarśa viṣṇum āsthitam
tasyāsīt sumahadyuddhaṃ viṣṇunā sārdham adbhutam
na śaśāka ca taṃ viṣṇurjetuṃ prahlādam ojasā
ātmānaṃ veda hīnaṃ ca viṣṇuḥ prahlādadānavāt
aśakto dānavaṃ jetuṃ manyumānabhavat prabhuḥ
atha dhyātvā mahādevaṃ praṇamya ca punaḥ punaḥ
prasādaṃ tam anusmṛtya śaivaṃ viṣṇuḥ surottamaḥ
hīyamānam athātmānaṃ hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sutaḥ
jñātvā ca balinaṃ viṣṇuṃ yuddhadeśādapākramat
ajitaṃ viṣṇunātmānaṃ śivatejovimohitaḥ
prahrādo jitam ātmānaṃ bubudhe dānaveśvaraḥ
prahrādāsurasaṃgrāmaṃ ghoraṃ devabhayaṃkaram
abhūdabdaśataṃ divyaṃ viṣṇunā sārdham adbhutam
na śrutena na vīryeṇa na śauryeṇa na tejasā
hiraṇyakaśipurnāsīdrājā tatsadṛśo mahān
nāndhako na hiraṇyākṣaḥ prahlādasadṛśo bale
bhṛguśāpāt kilāyāto daityatvaṃ viṣṇureva saḥ
nābhavaṃstasya rājye tu duḥkhaśokānvitāḥ prajāḥ
evaṃ sa dānavaśreṣṭhaḥ kṛtvā yuddhaṃ tu viṣṇunā
paścāttāpopataptāṅgo viṣayebhyo gataspṛhaḥ
varadānam anityaṃ tajjñātvā ca tapasaḥ phalam
niḥspṛhaḥ sarvakāryeṣu viṣayepsāvivarjitaḥ
sarvasannyastakarmā tu dhyānābhyāsaparāyaṇaḥ
punarāvartakaṃ janma buddhvā cānityatāṃ parām
kaṣṭaṃ rājyam iti jñātvā prahrādaḥ paramārthavit
abhiṣicya sutaṃ rājye ditijānāṃ virocanam
daityadānavarājānaṃ kṛtvā tam asureśvaram
mokṣasiddhiṃ parām icchan pravrajyākṛtaniścayaḥ
paraṃ tattvam athānveṣṭuṃ guṇātītam ajaṃ śivam
sākṣādbhagavataḥ śiṣyaṃ kapilasyāsuriṃ munim
śiṣyatvenopasaṃgamya mokṣavidyām avāptavān
prakṛtīnāṃ paraṃ tattvaṃ vikārāṇāṃ paraṃ tathā
kṣetrajñaṃ puruṣaṃ jñātvā bhoktāraṃ bhoktṛvarjitam
mokṣavidyāparārthajñaḥ sāṃkhyasiddhāntapāragaḥ
sa yogaṃ paramaṃ labdhvā sāṃkhyācāryo mahāmuniḥ
śrīmānevaṃ tribhuvanaripurdaityarājo mahātmā
kṛtvā vairaṃ vibudhaguruṇā viṣṇunā dīrghakālam
siddhaḥ paścājjagadabhayadaḥ prāptayogaśca bhūtvā
muktaḥ paścāt sa padam amṛtaṃ brahma cādyaṃ hyavāpa
kṣetrajñaboddhā guṇaviprayukto duḥkhairvihīno bhavapāśabandhaiḥ
evaṃ tāṃśchinnapakṣāṃstu girīn sarvān purandaraḥ
pracakāra muniśreṣṭha prāk pṛṣṭo yadahaṃ tvayā
vyāsa uvāca
yāto himavataḥ śṛṅgaṃ pārvatyā sahito haraḥ
kim anyadakaroddevaḥ kiṃ cainaṃ prāha pārvatī
sūta uvāca
ṛṣiḥ paramayogīśaḥ kathayāmāsa tattvataḥ
babhāṣe girijā devaṃ praṇamya parameśvaram
uñchavṛtterhiraṇyasya naimiśāraṇyavāsinaḥ
svayam eva prayātāhaṃ dvijaṃ pūjāṃ pratīcchitum
māhātmyaṃ tasya taddṛṣṭvā brāhmaṇasya tapasvinaḥ
gatāhaṃ vismayaṃ deva dvijāḥ śreṣṭhatamā iti
devebhyo 'api garīyāṃso brāhmaṇā iti me matiḥ
śreṣṭhāstapasvino viprā devebhyo 'api garīyasaḥ
madīyā yāḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ prathamāḥ prabhavo hyaham
rudrā dvijātayaḥ pūrvaṃ mayā sṛṣṭā mahaujasaḥ
madīyāṃ sṛṣṭim ālokya brahmaṇāpi sisṛkṣuṇā
brāhmaṇā mūrdhataḥ sṛṣṭāḥ pūrvam eva mahāprabhāḥ
agrabhūto hyahaṃ teṣāṃ dvijaśreṣṭhastadābhavam
uttamaiṣāparā sṛṣṭirbrāhmaṇāḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
dharmādikaṃ caturvargaṃ sarvaṃ teṣu pratiṣṭhitam
jagat pratiṣṭhitaṃ sarvaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ hi tejasā
mṛtyujanmāpahaṃ yat tanmama pāśupataṃ vratam
na varṇāḥ sādhayantyanye muktvā brāhmaṇasattamān
lakṣaṇaṃ sampravakṣyāmi dvijātīnām idaṃ śṛṇu
brāhmaṇastu bhavejjātyā saṃskārāddvija ucyate
vidyayā vipratāṃ yāti brāhmaṇyaṃ trividhaṃ smṛtam
yaśca jātyā bhavedvipro yaśca syādvedapāragaḥ
tayostrāṇe vadhe cāpi puṇyapāpe same smṛte
jātyā ca yo bhavedvipraḥ sarvāgamaviśāradaḥ
tādṛśaṃ bhojayecchrāddhe daive karmaṇi vāpi yaḥ
so 'api śreṣṭhaḥ smṛto devi pūjitastārayet kulam
sarvathā jātimātreṇa yo 'api syādbrāhmaṇaḥ kvacit
nānṛtaṃ brāhmaṇo brūte na hanti prāṇinaṃ dvijaḥ
vidvadbrāhmaṇatāṃ labdhvā kiṃ na labdhaṃ hi dehinā
mūrtayo yāḥ smṛtā hyaṣṭāvarkasomādayo mama
prabhavanti sadā devi viprāḥ śreṣṭhatamāstataḥ
nāsādhyaṃ vidyate teṣāṃ dvijānāṃ paramaujasām
ruṣitāste prasannā vā prayacchanti śubhāśubham
dvijāstapasvino ye tu vedavidyāviśāradāḥ
ahaṃ pitāmahaścaiva teṣāṃ yonidvayaṃ smṛtam
mattaḥ pūrvaṃ prasūtāste tato devi pitāmahāt
āvāṃ hetū dvijātīnāṃ prakṛtitvāt tvam eva ca
prakṛtistvaṃ samākhyātā puruṣaḥ paramo hyaham
brahmaviṣṇū smṛtau yau tau rajaḥsattvaguṇātmakau
āvābhyāṃ tau prajāyete sṛṣṭikāle prajāpatī
ahaṃ hyagnistamo viṣṇuḥ sattvaṃ brahmaṇi saṃsthitam
sattvaṃ nāśayate tau hi sa cāgneḥ samprajāyate
vahnitejāḥ smṛtā hyete mahātmāno dvijātayaḥ
sarvataḥ prabhavantyete nāsti teṣāṃ nivāraṇam
ārjavaṃ samatāṃ caiva viddhi tejo dvijātiṣu
tapovidyāsamāyuktādārjavastu viśiṣyate
aśāṭhyaṃ hanti pāpāni samatā mohabandhanam
purā bhāgīrathītīre dvijaḥ paramadharmavit
nāmnā dānarucirnāma uñchavṛttirbabhūva ha
sarvavidyāvinītātmā sarvabhūtābhayapradaḥ
ṣaṣṭhe kāle tato 'aśnāti tasyedaṃ vratam uttamam
athaivaṃ vartamānasya bhūyān kālo jagāma ha
babhūvātyartham arciṣmānarkāgnī iva tejasā
tasyaivaṃ tapaso vahniḥ prītastuṣṭim agāt parām
kadācidatha kālena ṣaṣṭhe kāle samāgate
nāpaśyadatithiṃ kaṃcidbubhukṣāklamakheditaḥ
aprāśyaiva tadā kiṃcidupavāsaparāyaṇaḥ
yathaivāsyāḥ patiścakre tathā sāpyakarot tadā
śītakṣudupataptāṅgo naikadvandvasamāvṛtaḥ
dvitīye 'atha samāyāte ṣaṣṭhe kāle sa ha dvijaḥ
śītadurdinajāddoṣānnaivātithim avaikṣata
athāgnistasya tajjñātvā niścayaṃ paramaṃ mahat
śvapākasadṛśaṃ rūpaṃ vikṛtaṃ kutsitaṃ ca hi
apaśyadvṛkṣamūlasthaṃ ghoraṃ vikṛtarūpiṇam
śvapākaṃ śītasaṃkhinnaṃ naikavraṇaśatāṅkitam
durdṛśaṃ vṛddham ārtaṃ ca prasravatkṛmiśoṇitam
kṛpaṇaṃ tam atho dṛṣṭvā śvapākaṃ dvijasattamaḥ
śītāpanayanārthaṃ ca vahnim asyānayaddvijaḥ
atha taṃ vahnisaṃsargāt samāśvastam uvāca saḥ
tam uvāca tato dīnaṃ śvapākastapasāṃ nidhim
nāhaṃ saṃskṛtam āhartuṃ yogyo 'annam iti cābravīt
tam evaṃvādinaṃ dhyānājjñātvā vahnim upasthitam
provāca dvijaśārdūla idaṃ vacanakovidaḥ
nāhaṃ jātiṃ garhayāmi pūjayāmi na cānagha
ātmā sarvagato hyeṣa sarvaprāṇiṣu saṃsthitaḥ
ātmānaṃ tam ahaṃ bhaktyā pūjayāmi paraṃ śivam
tiryakṣu na hi me kutsā tvadvidheṣu viśeṣataḥ
kṛmikīṭākhusarpeṣu śvapāgdevadvijātiṣu
yadā sarvagato hi ātmā tadā kutsā kathaṃ ca naḥ
bhuṅkṣva saṃskṛtam annaṃ tu prāpayāsmānanugraham
evam ukto dvijendreṇa śvapākaḥ prītimāṃstadā
vimuktaḥ saha patnyā tu prāptavānamṛtaṃ padam
evam ārjavasampanno brāhmaṇaḥ kṛtalakṣaṇaḥ
śṛṇvan nityam idaṃ paṭhaṃśca vidhivadvidvāñchucirmānavaḥ
sṛṣṭeḥ prabhavānmama te dvijendrā māhātmyam itthaṃ paramaṃ hyavāpuḥ
dvijamāhātmyam ullikhya pārvatīparameśayoḥ
babhūvetthaṃ susaṃvādaḥ puṇyaḥ pāpavināśanaḥ
pārāśarya tapodhana
iti skandapurāṇe dvijamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmā
vyāsa uvāca
prāpya pāśupataṃ yogaṃ brahmādyāstridivaukasaḥ
kīdṛśaṃ tat paraṃ yogaṃ jñānaṃ pāśupataṃ śubham
yajjñātvā brāhmaṇāḥ siddhāḥ prāpnuyurmokṣam uttamam
iti pṛṣṭastu śiṣyeṇa provāca munisattamaḥ
yanmāṃ pṛcchasi tajjñānaṃ yogaṃ māheśvaraṃ param
sarvāsāṃ yogavidyānāṃ yat tattvaṃ parikīrtyate
sāṃkhyayogāgamopetāḥ sarvādhyātmaviśāradāḥ
yad abuddhvā mahābhāga jñānaṃ śaṃkarabhāṣitam
tadyathā kathitaṃ teṣāṃ tryambakeṇa divaukasām
tat te 'ahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi saṃkṣepāt tattvaviniścayam
tasyāhaṃ sthitapakṣaṃ tu saṃsārotpattināśanam
namaskṛtya maheśānaṃ puruṣaṃ bhūtabhāvanam
prakṛteḥ paramaṃ guhyaṃ pudgalaṃ parameṣṭhinam
yaṃ sāṃkhyāḥ puruṣaṃ prāhuḥ pañcaviṃśam ajaṃ vibhum
yogāścāpi hi ṣaḍviṃśaṃ vyāpinaṃ triguṇātmakam
yo 'asṛjat sṛṣṭikāle tu devau sarvajagatsṛjau
prajāpatī mahātmānau dhyātvā viṣṇupitāmahau
taṃ praṇamya mahādevaṃ tryakṣaṃ varadam īśvaram
lakṣaṇaṃ viddhi yogasya procyamānam idaṃ mayā
chidyante paśupāśāni yasyābhyāsānmahāmune
eṣa bhoga iti vyāsa kīrtitaḥ śambhunā purā
bhavajanmāpahaḥ sūkṣmaḥ prapannānāṃ divaukasām
śarīre tiṣṭhataḥ puṃso yadātmani manaḥ sthitam
kṛtānāṃ pratyayaiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ sukhaduḥkhādisaṃjñinām
aśeṣalopa ityuktaṃ sādhakasya tu yuñjataḥ
abhisandhistadā yasmādīśvarasyātmanaśca ha
sukhādānam athaikena bhāvanā yojanāt
pra tiṣṭhataḥ sataḥ
athādhikaraṇaṃ tatra kramaśaḥ parikīrtyate
pratyāhāram ato vidyā prāṇāyamastathaiva ca
dhyānaṃ ca dhāraṇā caiva yogābhyāsa udāhṛtaḥ
vaśyā hi dhātavastasmādbhavantyasya na saṃśayaḥ
antarikṣe ca sarvāstu kīrtitā hi na saṃśayaḥ
sthānatrayanibaddhāstu caturlakṣaṇasaṃsthitāḥ
kriyāḥ pramādinā naitāḥ śakyāḥ sādhayituṃ kvacit
tisra etāḥ sadā mṛtyuṃ pravṛttā mohalakṣaṇāḥ
ajñānaṃ kampate tāsu bahirantaścarāsvapi
bhūtendriyamanaḥkāladiṅnivṛttiḥ prabhāvataḥ
daśaivāśāstrayaḥ kālā bhūtānīndriyavistaraḥ
manaḥpracārasaṃyukto viṣayābhāvalakṣaṇaḥ
trikālaviṣayaṃ jñānam aiśvaryodayam eva ca
cale manasi nābhūtāṃ bhavetāṃ saṃsthite samam
manaḥ sarvam idaṃ yasmāt sādhanaṃ yogakarmaṇaḥ
prāṇanigrahaṇe dhyānaṃ prāṇāyāmam iti smṛtam
prāṇa eva hi vāyūnāṃ sārathye vartate sadā
prāṇanigrahaṇe yogī nityam abhyāsam ācaret
dvirapāne sakṛt prāṇe samāne ca
ebhirdhyānagatiḥ sūkṣmā vāyusaṃrodhakāritā
sakṛdeva samāhārādasakṛt parimokṣaṇāt
kumbhakaṃ caitaduddiṣṭaṃ prāṇāyāmādidhāraṇāt
prāṇo vāyurasau ātmā śarīre jīva
vidyādrūpadvayaṃ tasya sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ ca sarvataḥ
avyaktaṃ sūkṣmarūpaṃ tu sthūlam ākāralakṣaṇam
sthūlādārabhya sūkṣmaṃ tu dhyānābhyāsānnirūpayet
sūkṣmasaṃropaṇājjyotiḥ prakāśo jāyate mune
dhyāyataḥ sthūlalakṣyaṃ tu sarvadikṣu sṛtaṃ manaḥ
yadā dīptimadutpadyet tadāśu sthāpayet punaḥ
girau vṛkṣe marutpṛṣṭhe śvabhre prāsādapaṅktiṣu
samudre vasudhāyāṃ vā manaḥsaṃyogam ācaret
acaitanyaṃ diśenmohādvāyurdṛṣṭam ato 'anyathā
saṃhṛtya ca tato vyāpi bhūyo dhyānagatiṃ caret
pravṛttajñānayogasya viṣayāsaṃgasaṃkṣaye
prātibhāni hi vighnāni sattvādiguṇajāni tu
ākāśagamanaṃ divyam apsarogaṇasaṃgajam
sattvādetāni vighnāni prātibhāni tu lakṣayet
rajovighnāni saṃvidyāt prātibhāni na saṃśayaḥ
kṣayaśūlajvaronmādakuṣṭhasarpagrahāṇi tu
yātanodgamapūrvāṇi tāmasāni vinirdiśet
guṇatrayasamutthāni prātibhāni sadā muniḥ
yuñjan saṃlakṣayecchīghraṃ cikitsedāśu caiva hi
prāṇādyānabhisaṃdhāya manaḥ saṃhṛtya caiva hi
prāṇāyāmena kumbhena hanyādvighnāni sarvataḥ
rajaḥ sattvaṃ tamaścaiva pradhānasya guṇāstrayaḥ
nirīho nirvṛto yogī sacetā ghaṭate yadā
prātibhāni tadā yānti vighnāni hi samaṃ kṣayam
prādurbhāvastatasteṣāṃ guṇānāṃ mohakāraṇam
tamo raudraṃ vijānīyāt sattvaṃ brahmaṇi saṃsthitam
rajastu vaiṣṇavaṃ vidyāt teṣāṃ hantā maheśvaraḥ
mahādevaṃ paraṃ jñātvā yogābhyāsarato dvijaḥ
guṇatrayavinirmuktaḥ śaṃkare layam āpnuyāt
tataḥ śāstrapraṇītena dharmādharmavivarjitaḥ
krameṇa sopadeśena dhyānābhyāsaṃ samācaret
śabdādīn viṣayān jitvā śrotrādīndriyagocarān
sābhimānaṃ saniyamaṃ tyaktvā sāṃkhyaviniścayam
aṣṭau prakṛtayo nityā vikārāścaiva ṣoḍaśa
puruṣaḥ pañcaviṃśaśca sāṃkhyasiddhāntagocaraḥ
etadeva paraṃ guhyaṃ sāṃkhyānāṃ tattvaviniścaye
prakṛterantaraṃ jñātvā puruṣasya ca mucyate
iti skandapurāṇe pāśupatasyogavarṇanaṃ nāma dhyānavidhau
yogaṃ sāṃkhyaṃ ca sarvatra dvividhaṃ jñānam ucyate
tatra sāṃkhyaratāḥ kecit kecidyogapathāśritāḥ
avyaktaṃ prakṛtiścaiva tathāhaṃkāra eva ca
aṣṭau prakṛtayo hyetāstanmātraiḥ pañcabhiḥ saha
pañca buddhīndriyāṇi āhuḥ pañca karmendriyāṇi ca
manaḥ pañca ca bhūtāni vikārāḥ ṣoḍaśa smṛtāḥ
puruṣaḥ pañcaviṃśaśca sarvārambhavivarjitaḥ
nityaḥ sarvagataḥ sūkṣmaścetāvāṃstriguṇojjhitaḥ
saṃśuddho vimalo bhoktā akartā sākṣivat sthitaḥ
viditvā na viśantyenaṃ bhūyaḥ saṃsārapañjaram
pañcaviṃśati tattvāni sāṃkhyairetāni yogibhiḥ
sūkṣmā prakṛtiravyaktā bhojyā sarvaratā calā
nityā cācetanā caiva vijñeyā sarvakāmikī
bhinnakāryapracārāṇām eteṣāṃ guṇasaṃjñinām
hetunā puruṣārthena sādhikā vṛttirucyate
avikalpyaṃ ca mānuṣyaṃ sarvam etadguṇātmakam
mūḍhaṃ niścetanaṃ bhūtaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmam athāpi vā
amūrtaṃ mūrtimadvāpi triguṇaṃ sarvam ucyate
mokṣavighnakarā hyete kīrtitā yogino guṇāḥ
vibhāgena vikārasthā yathādharmaṃ samāśritāḥ
bhūtasargastridhābhūtaḥ sāṃkhyajñaiḥ paripaṭhyate
saṃsiddhaḥ prākṛtaścaiva tathā vaikṛta ucyate
tatra dharmeṇa saṃsiddhā yoge māheśvare sthitāḥ
necchanti saṃbhavaṃ vyāsa dharmo pañcātmataḥ smṛtaḥ
te puno dravyasaṃbandhāt sāṃkhyadṛṣṭāntapaṇḍitāḥ
icchanti kāryam āśritya kāraṇāśrayiṇo na hi
pradhānāt puruṣādbuddhirabhūt sattvādhikāsakṛt
guṇānāṃ pariṇāmena prākṛtānāṃ jalādivat
vyavasāyastathā rūpaṃ niścayaśceti bhāṣyate
aham eva hi karteti ahaṃkāra udāhṛtaḥ
buddhibhūtādahaṃkārāt sattvotpannāt prakāśinaḥ
buddhīndriyāṇi jātāni pañca sattvodayāni tu
ataḥ karmendriyāṇi āhurguṇājjātāni rājasāt
tāmasādapyahaṃkārāt tanmātrāṇyabhavan punaḥ
śaktaṃ sarvāśrayaṃ sūkṣmam anivāritadikpatham
liṅgaṃ tacca samākhyātaṃ dehināṃ yacca kāraṇam
prākṛtasya vikārasya dehabhedāḥ sahasraśaḥ
tattvasargaḥ smṛtaḥ pūrvaḥ piṇḍasargastato 'aparaḥ
pratyayānāṃ tataḥ sargastṛtīyaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ
bhedāḥ pratyayasarge tu vaiṣamyādapare smṛtāḥ
pañcāśat parito bhedā ye ca teṣāṃ guṇā daśa
ṣaṣṭirete padārthā hi gīyante kapilādibhiḥ
sā tuṣṭirnavadhā bhinnā siddhiścaivāṣṭadhā punaḥ
smṛtaḥ pañcavidhaścāpi teṣām eva viparyayaḥ
aṣṭabhedāstribhinnā syāddaśabhiḥ kāryabandhanaiḥ
ete ṣaṣṭipadārthāstu saṃkhyājñānam iti śrutiḥ
nyūnām ekādhikām eke ṣaṣṭim anye tu jānate
antaraṃ tattvam anveṣṭuṃ prakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca
sāṃkhyatantraṃ mahadbuddhvā jñātvā tat prakṛteḥ param
pañcaviṃśam ajaṃ tattvaṃ bhoktāram abhimāninam
saṃdehāpagamo nābhūdabuddhvā parameśvaram
svayogaṃ śambhunā vatsa grāhito gatasaṃśayaḥ
tadā ṣaḍviṃśakaṃ tattvaṃ jñātvā sarvagam īśvaram
yastayoḥ parato nityaḥ ṣaḍviṃśastu īśvaro vibhuḥ
taṃ jñātvā paramaṃ tattvaṃ mucyate janmabandhanāt
sāṃkhyaṃ kṛtsnam api jñātvā guṇāntaravicāraṇāt
pañcaviṃśakasaṃbodhānnaiva muktiḥ prajāyate
sa baddho bhoktṛpāśaistu guṇaiḥ prakṛtisaṃbhavaiḥ
abhimānātmako bhoktā puruṣatvādamocakaḥ
eṣa uktaḥ samāsena sāṃkhyasiddhāntavistaraḥ
yogābhyāsaṃ parāsaṃgaṃ sūkṣmajñānam aninditam
mataṃ paśupateḥ kṛtsnam amṛtāspadalambhanam
ṣaṭsaptatyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
ākāśaḥ pavanastejo bhūmirāpastathaiva ca
eṣām ekatra saṃghātāccharīraṃ nāma jāyate
rasāḥ somātmakāḥ sarve tathāhāraścaturvidhaḥ
dehināṃ tu rasotpattirāhārasya niṣevaṇāt
rasādraktasamutpattiḥ śoṇitāt piśitaṃ smṛtam
meda utpadyate māṃsāt tasmādasthīni cābhavan
majjā cāsthibhavā jñeyā tataḥ śukrasamudbhavaḥ
raktaśukrasamāyogādgarbhaḥ saṃbhavati striyāḥ
ṛtuyogasamādhānāddaivakarmavaśādapi
kalalaṃ tvekarātreṇa pañcarātreṇa cārbudam
piśitaṃ saptarātreṇa māsāccāṅkurasaṃbhavaḥ
śiraḥpāṇimukhaskandhagrīvāpṛṣṭhādisaṃyutaḥ
pañcānām atha māsānām akṣikarṇādisaṃbhavaḥ
pañcabhūtātmakaṃ tat tu cetovadavatiṣṭhati
mṛtaḥ puno 'ahaṃ jāto jātaścaiva puno mṛtaḥ
idānīṃ jātamātrastu yogam evābhyāsāmyaham
na puno yena saṃsāraṃ pravekṣyāmyaśubhodayam
deham āviśate vāyuḥ smṛtim ākṣipya tāmasaḥ
agnīṣomātmakaṃ sarvaṃ bhūtagrāmaṃ caturvidham
āgamānveṣaṇe saktāḥ pāpānuṣṭhānavarjitāḥ
matvā saṃsārajaṃ kleśaṃ janmamṛtyubhayārditam
vairāgyaṃ janmataḥ kṛtvā sarvārambhaparikṣayāt
sarveṣāṃ yogināṃ guhyaṃ sarvayoganidarśanam
tato māheśvaraṃ yogam ākhyāsye tat paraṃ tava
tejāgniḥ kāmajo vahniḥ krodhāgnirvīkṣaṇānalaḥ
jaṭharāgniśca bhūtātmā pañcaite dehavahnayaḥ
prāṇo 'apānaḥ samānaśca udāno vyāna eva ca
pañcaite vāyavo nityā dehino dehasaṃbhavāḥ
ākāśaprabhavā hyete śarīraṃ caiṣu tiṣṭhati
māṃsaraktasamākīrṇaṃ snāyumedosthisaṃcayam
tvacāvanaddhaṃ durgandhaṃ śakṛnmūtrasamāvṛtam
taḍidabhrāgamānityaṃ mṛtpātrāpātasaṃnibham
sarvānarthasamāyuktaṃ na cirānnāśagāmi ca
ekarūpaṃ navadvāraṃ tristhūṇaṃ pañcadevatam
viṣayendriyasaṃkīrṇaṃ naikavyādhisamārditam
prāṇādibhiravaṣṭabdhaṃ śarīraṃ yantravat sthitam
āmapātram ivāpātācchīryate kālaparyayāt
pañcabhūtāni bhūtāni dehānniṣkramya sarvaśaḥ
āviśanti tathātmānam ātmā ca viśate drutam
bhūteṣu pavanaḥ śreṣṭho jīvastadvinibandhanaḥ
vāyvagnī sahitau jīvo na jīvaḥ prāṇināṃ pṛthak
mūrtiranyā na jīvasya mṛtyau dṛśyati dehinaḥ
pañcarūpāt paro devaḥ sūkṣmāt sūkṣmataro mataḥ
nāsau paśyati na ghrāti na śṛṇoti na jalpati
na jānāti na ca sparśejjīvaḥ prāṇasamāvṛtaḥ
prāṇo nāma mahāvāyurjīvaṃ dhārayate dvija
sa prāṇo dhārayatyagniṃ sa ca jīva iti smṛtaḥ
vāyusaṃdhāraṇo hyagniḥ kriyāsu parivartate
evam etaccharīraṃ tu pañcabhūtaguṇātmakam
hṛdaye karṇikāyāṃ tu madhyasthastejasāṃ nidhiḥ
ātmā sarvagato nityaṃ varjito viṣayādibhiḥ
nāḍīkarmasamādhānāt satatābhyāsayogataḥ
bhābhiḥ prakāśito dṛṣṭo vikārairvipramocitaḥ
dṛṣṭo bhavati viprendra muktiścaiva tataḥ smṛtā
ṣaḍviṃśakaparijñānāllayam ādhāya tatra hi
sarvaprāṇigataṃ sūkṣmam ātmadehe ca saṃsthitam
yo 'abhyupāyaḥ parastasya vijñānād īśvarasya tu
yogābhyāsaṃ paraṃ taṃ te pravakṣyāmi dvijottama
tṛtīyaḥ ṣaṭsaptatyuttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
antarātmā ca cetovān manaḥ saṃkalpajaṃ smṛtam
mahābhūtapracārācca kṣobhāgnirjīva ucyate
na śarīraṃ vinā cetastaccennāsti kutaśca tat
ceto 'api na vinā jīvaṃ sa cāpi na vinā manaḥ
yasya ceto 'adhikaṃ teṣāṃ sa cetovān prakīrtitaḥ
cetasā tu vijānāti śubhāśubhanibandhanam
śabdādiviṣayātīta indriyāṇi nigṛhya tu
jīvo bandhātmako jñeyaḥ śubhāśubhanibandhanāt
udrekājjāyate duḥkhaṃ saukhyaṃ sattvāt prajāyate
saukhyasya pariṇāmāddhi duḥkhotpattiḥ śarīriṇām
sukhaduḥkhātmakaṃ mohaṃ bhūtāni āviśya tiṣṭhati
manaścetaḥsamādhānādviṣayodvijanādapi
tasya nāśaḥ samākhyātaḥ saṃgasya ca vivarjanāt
icchānigrahaṇe saktāḥ krodhādiparivarjitāḥ
ātmā sarvagato hyeṣaḥ sūkṣmaḥ saṃbhogavarjitaḥ
athaiśvaryaṃ paraṃ dhyānādyogajaṃ prāpnute muniḥ
asukhānyapi karmāṇi mahāpāpakṛtānyapi
prāpya karmakṣayaṃ kṛtsnaṃ dhyānayuktyā mahāmune
kāmaroṣau tathā saṃgo dveṣo rāgaviniścayaḥ
pāruṣyaṃ krūratā caiva bhāvāḥ kṣatranibandhanāḥ
mohabhāvāntarātītaḥ samaduḥkhasukhaḥ sadā
dhyānena kṣīyate karma pāpaṃ vā yadi vā śubham
kṣīṇakarmā tato yogī tat paraṃ brahma vindati
yoginaṃ puruṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāpairmucyanti tatkṣaṇāt
yogam eva paraṃ jñātvā sarvāśubhavimocanam
dhyānaṃ dhyeyaṃ paraṃ caiva dhātāraṃ caiva ye viduḥ
tāpanāt tapanāt tāpyānmuktāste duḥkhabandhanāt
nirguṇaḥ sāṃkhyamukhyānāṃ puruṣaḥ paripaṭhyate
dīpanirvāṇavat teṣāṃ dehabhede gatiḥ smṛtā
īśvaraḥ sarvanirmuktaḥ kṣetrajño yogināṃ mataḥ
dhāraṇābhiḥ samaṃ tābhiḥ prāṇāyāmaistathaiva ca
bhikṣopāttarasāhāro mumukṣuriti śabdyate
karmamārgādatikrānto dhyānīti parikīrtyate
na hṛṣyati sukhe caiva dhyānīti sa viśabditaḥ
pūrvaḥ saṃketanaḥ proktaḥ paścāt saṃkathanaḥ smṛtaḥ
saṃsaktaśca tṛtīyastu teṣāṃ bhedam imaṃ śṛṇu
pratirūpaṃ vibhoḥ kṛtvā daśabhirniyamairyutaḥ
vedādṛtasukhāsaṃgaḥ sattvakarmā tvabāndhavān
sarvārambhaparityāgāt kapilādiniṣevitaḥ
smṛtaḥ saṃkathanaḥ panthā yogāgniparidīpakaḥ
samyagetān munirjñātvā nirmamo 'anyatamaṃ śritaḥ
sarvān dhyānavidhāṃstvetānucyamānānimān mayā
śṛṇu vyāsa mahābuddhe yogaiśvaryaphalapradān
pañcaviṃśatimaṃ tattvaṃ kṣaraṃ tat prakṛteḥ param
akṣaraṃ ca paraṃ brahma ṣaḍviṃśakam iti smṛtam
mana ekagataṃ kṛtvā dhāraṇābhiḥ punaḥ punaḥ
vāyunigrahaṇaṃ kuryāt pratyāhārapuraḥsaram
muhūrtārdhaṃ kṣaṇaṃ vāpi pratyāhāraṃ samācaret
talāt triṃśacchataṃ cordhvaṃ prāṇāyāmanibandhanam
tadbaddhvā vijane deśe dhyānābhyāsaṃ samācaret
kṣudhārto vātibhukto vā rujā duḥkhānvito 'api vā
yogahastaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā vāmasyopari dakṣiṇam
aspṛśan daśanairdantānoṃkāraṃ brahma saṃsmaran
dhyāyīta nirmamo vidvān prāṇāyāmapuraḥsaram
ātmānam ātmanā yojya sarvāṅgāni tu saṃharet
nirīhaḥ pihitākṣaśca nikṣipya hṛdi dhāraṇām
pāṣāṇa iva niṣpando munirdhyānaṃ samācaret
ekatrāspandasaṃdhānaṃ manaso dhāraṇā smṛtā
vikārā guṇajāḥ sarve naśyante vighnahetavaḥ
anveṣṭi ca paraṃ brahma svaśarīraṃ samāsthitam
kṛtvaikyaṃ prāṇamanasām indriyāṇāṃ vinigrahāt
sarvabhāvaparityāgānmokṣam āpnotyasaṃśayam
athaiśvaryagatāṃ siddhiṃ dhyāyannaṣṭavidhāṃ yadā
paśyate yogasaṃsiddhyā tadā yogī prakīrtyate
brahmasomādikān devān yadā yuktaḥ prapaśyati
manasā yogināṃ siddhiḥ sāṃkhyāstattvaviniścayāt
na viśeṣo 'asti yogānāṃ muktvā māheśvaraṃ vidhim
yogino dhyānasaṃsiddhiṃ sāṃkhyāstattvaviniścayam
śabdādīn viṣayān yukto na dhyāyan vetti vai yadā
araṇye maunam ādhāya dhyāyedoṃkāram akṣaram
vedādau yaḥ svaraḥ prokto vedānte ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ
tasya prakṛtilīnasya yaḥ paraḥ sa mahān smṛtaḥ
trisaṃsthānaṃ trimātraṃ ca tribrahma tryakṣaraṃ tathā
mātrāhīnaṃ samātraṃ ca yo vidyāt sa vimucyate
oṃkāraḥ paramaṃ tattvam ātmā brahma ca kīrtyate
kṣetrajñairātmasaṃbodhādyogibhiḥ sūkṣmadarśanāt
īśvaraṃ prāpnute yogī yam avāpya vimucyate
indriyāṇi tu sarvāṇi śabdarūpādinigrahāt
viditvā karmajān hanti yogī doṣānaśeṣataḥ
dhyānaśaktyā tataḥ śuddhaḥ sarvajinmokṣam āpnute
yuñjan pratidinaṃ vyāsa ṣaṅmāsādyogam āpnute
tam ātmānaṃ paraṃ jñātvā yogaśaktyā mahāmuniḥ
paramaiśvaryasaṃyukta amṛtaṃ padam āpnuyāt
pañcamaḥ aṣṭasaptatyuttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
ūnāśītyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
pañca karmendriyāṇyatra pañca buddhīndriyāṇi ca
pañcabhūtaṃ manaścātra vikārāḥ ṣoḍaśa smṛtāḥ
mahān buddhirahaṃkārastanmātrāṇi ca pañca hi
imāḥ prakṛtayo vyāsa deham aṣṭau samāśritāḥ
nābhimadhye tu nāḍīnāṃ śatam ekaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
sarvāṅgeṣu tu yāstvanyā jalānnarasavāhikāḥ
tāsāṃ triṃśat sahasrāṇi vyānasrotasi saṃsthitāḥ
udānasyāparā nāḍyo brahmamūrdhni pratiṣṭhitāḥ
cakranābhī samāśritya bhūtasaṃghātam āsthitam
tanmadhye tu guṇaspṛṣṭaḥ karmātmā bhūtamohanaḥ
nakṣatroddyotasaṃkāśo jyotsnāpuñjanibhaḥ prabhaḥ
vighātajanano 'anyeṣāṃ sūryāyutanibhaḥ sthitaḥ
saṃbhūto 'agnirivotpātī girinīhārasaṃnibhaḥ
guṇastho bhūtayonistu puruṣaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ
nirdhūmāṅgārasaṃkāśo navijñātāgamakriyaḥ
ṣaḍviṃśaḥ puruṣaḥ sūkṣma īśvaraḥ paramo vibhuḥ
sa eṣa kathito vyāsa pareṣāṃ parataḥ sthitaḥ
mahādevam imaṃ jñātvā mucyate tatkṣaṇānmuniḥ
guṇatrayavikārasthaḥ kathitaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ
bhūyaḥ saṃsarate tasmādajñānenaiva mohitaḥ
devamānuṣatiryakṣu bhrāmyate rāgamohitaḥ
ṣaḍviṃśakasamādhānāt siddhistasya vikārataḥ
kriyākāryavinirmuktaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvasṛk prabhuḥ
paramaiśvaryasaṃpūrṇaḥ kṛtakṛtyo maheśvaraḥ
ajaḥ svayambhūḥ ṣaḍviṃśaḥ kūṭastho hyacalo dhruvaḥ
tatastattvāni jāyante puruṣaśca guṇaiḥ saha
tasminneva ca līyante ṣaḍviṃśe tu maheśvare
yathāgnirnirdahedante bhūtagrāmam aśeṣataḥ
ṣaḍviṃśakapadārthajñastathā karmāṇi nirdahet
sarvavyāpi yathākāśaṃ sūkṣmaṃ naiva tu lipyate
ṣaḍviṃśakarato yogī tathā pāpairna lipyate
ṣaḍviṃśāt parato nāsti tasmāt tatparamo bhavet
brahmaviṣṇvādikaṃ sarvaṃ bhūtagrāmam aśeṣataḥ
īśvarājjāyate vyāsa tasminneva pralīyate
sa eṣa sarvago devaḥ ṣaḍviṃśaḥ parameśvaraḥ
prāṇo 'apānaḥ samānaśca udāno vyāna eva ca
ye pañca vāyavo dehe teṣāṃ nigrahaṇe yatet
apānaṃ ca samāṇaṃ ca kṛtvaikagatam ādṛtaḥ
vyānena sahitaṃ prāṇam udāne saṃniveśayet
nāsāgre tu sakṛt prāṇaṃ prāpayedyogaśaktitaḥ
bhadrāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ samāsthāya ṣaḍviṃśaṃ cintayet tataḥ
mātrāḥ pañcadaśa proktāḥ prathamaṃ sandhibandhanam
mātrā viṃśati vijñeyāḥ pañcamaḥ sandhivigrahaḥ
ekam āsanam āsthāya ṣaḍviṃśaṃ samanusmaran
sarvāṅgāni samāhṛtya niṣpando dhyānam ācaret
śanaiḥ saṃcārayedvāyuṃ nāḍibhiḥ srotasi sthitam
tāvat tiṣṭheta yuktātmā dhyānayogādgataspṛhaḥ
somamaṇḍalasaṃkāśaṃ yāvat paśyeddhṛdi sthitam
jyotirdehāśritaṃ dṛṣṭvā yogaiśvaryaṃ pravartate
trikālaviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ pratyakṣaṃ yogino bhavet
sarvavidyāvidāṃ vyāsa yatīnāṃ vratacāriṇām
tapasvināṃ ca viprāṇāṃ yogī śreṣṭha udāhṛtaḥ
nānyathā mucyate jantuḥ saṃsārāt tamasaḥ parāt
ṣaḍviṃśakaparijñānaṃ muktvā yoganibandhanam
jitvā hyaṣṭaprakāraṃ tu āsanānāṃ nibandhanam
mātrotkarṣeṇa jitvā ca prāṇāyāmaṃ caturvidham
tanmātrāṇīndriyairjitvā viṣayairindriyāṇi ca
yogāspadaṃ samādhāya pūrvoktaṃ guṇavarjitam
dhyāyīta hṛdi taṃ devaṃ viśvaṃ viśveśvaraṃ vibhum
anādinidhanaṃ śāntaṃ traiguṇyaparivarjitam
tālau jihvāṃ samādhāya dantairdantān na ca spṛśan
kṛtvā manasi tat sarvaṃ prāṇāpānau niruddhya ca
oṃkāraṃ tvasakṛddhyāyan saṃhṛtyāṅgāni kūrmavat
śarīraṃ sarvam āpūrya vikṣipet sarvam ātmani
tat saṃhṛtya munirbhūyo vyāpi bhūtaṃ pravistṛtam
nāḍīvāyupracāreṇa bhūyo bhūyastathārabhet
madhyāṅge cāparāhaṇe ca kṛṣṇaṃ dhyāyīta tāmasam
taijasaṃ sarvataścāpi dhyānadevaṃ jayedguṇān
yena ṣaḍviṃśakaṃ buddhvā hṛdayasthaṃ maheśvaram
paramātmā paraṃ brahma kāraṇaṃ puruṣo mahān
īśvaro nirguṇo bhoktā ṣaḍviṃśaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ
jāgarti svapate bhuṅkte saṃtiṣṭhati dadāti ca
sa sraṣṭā sa ca saṃhartā guṇātīto maheśvaraḥ
yogaṃ pāśupataṃ tubhyam ādyaṃ mokṣagatipradam
sūkṣmaṃ tat paramaṃ jñānaṃ pravakṣyāmi tavānagha
yasya samyakparijñānādvijñeyaṃ nāparaṃ bhavet
ṣaṣṭha ūnāśītyuttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
aśītyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
brahmādyā devatā vyāsa dakṣayajñavadhe purā
śaṃkaraṃ śaraṇaṃ jagmurvīrabhadrabhayārditāḥ
gaṇendreṇābhiyuktāstu bhasmakūṭāni bhejire
yadā bhasma praviṣṭāste tejaḥ śāṃkaram uttamam
abhavaṃste tadā raudrāḥ paśavo dīkṣitā iva
bhasmābhasitagātrāṇāṃ śaṃkaravratacāriṇām
svaṃ yogaṃ pradadau teṣāṃ tadā deva umāpatiḥ
sarvāsāṃ mokṣavidyānāṃ yat tattvam atiricyate
yo yogaḥ sakalo vyāsa kṛcchropāyaprasādhanaḥ
yo 'ayaṃ bhagavatā sākṣādyogo māheśvaraḥ paraḥ
tattvataḥ kalpitasteṣāṃ prapannānāṃ divaukasām
vrataṃ pāśupataṃ prāpya ṣaḍmāsājjñānam āpnute
sarvadharmaṃ bahiḥkṛtvā niṣakalasya prabhāvataḥ
dīkṣāṃ pāśupatīṃ prāpya taṃ viśanti maheśvaram
sarvajñānasamāyuktaṃ tapodharmabahiṣkṛtam
pāpiṣṭhā dharmavanto vā bhaktāḥ kevalam īśvaram
dahet somakṛtaṃ vahnirīśvaraṃ cānalaṃ viduḥ
kṛtākṛtaṃ dahatyagnirbhūyaḥ somasamāgataḥ
bhasmanā mocitāḥ sarve brahmādyā abhimāninaḥ
ātmānam uddharedvyāsa yaḥ snānaṃ bhasmanā caret
tejasā tasya saṃspṛṣṭo mucyate janmanā dvijaḥ
sāṃkhyaṃ visyāstapaścaiva tyaktvā dharmāṃśca vaidikān
ātmānaṃ yaḥ paśuṃ kṛtvā mahādevaṃ hutāśanam
dīkṣito brahmabhasmabhyāṃ śivayājī munirbhavet
evaṃ vratam anuprāpya bhūtvā pāśupato muniḥ
idaṃ māheśvaraṃ jñānaṃ guhyaṃ paramam abhyaset
jñeyaṃ jñānaṃ tathā jñātā trayaṃ dehe yathā sthitam
ātmā yaśca yathā cāsau sthānatrayasamāsthitaḥ
nāḍīṣu ca yathā hi ātmā ātmanyevānutiṣṭhati
sarvataḥ sarvabhūteṣu nigūḍhastiṣṭhate yathā
payasīva ghṛtaṃ vyāsa yaṃ viditvā vimucyate
na sa vettuṃ vinā jñānaṃ śakya ātmā kathaṃcana
rūpaśabdarasātītaṃ kastvaṃ vetti maheśvaram
tathā hyahaṃ mahābhāga prāsādāt tryambakasya tu
ātmajñānaṣaropāyaṃ kathayāmi tavānagha
śuddhaṃ vimalam ābhāti akṣaraṃ paramaiśvaram
sarvabhāvaguṇātītaṃ nirvikalpaṃ nirañjanam
bahirantaścaraṃ dīptam avināśi varaṃ dhruvam
yathā tadakṣaraṃ brahma procyamānaṃ tathā śṛṇu
om ityeksākṣaraṃ pūrvaṃ kṣaraṃ tasmādvinirgatam
tryakṣaraśca trimātraśca oṃkāro brahma śabdyate
akāre tatra viṣṇustu ukāre tu pitāmahaḥ
makāre bhagavān īśo mātrāyāṃ prakṛtiḥ smṛtā
prakṛtistrītvam āsthāya nityaṃ tau īśapārśvagau
patnīrūpeṇa sā śambhuṃ bhajate prakṛtiḥ sadā
kṣaranṃ tu prakṛtiḥ khyātākṣarastu svayam īśvaraḥ
īśvarānnirgatā sā hi prakṛtirguṇabandhanā
tasyāḥ sraṣṭā mahādevo yato viṣṇupitāmahau
yenaiva dhyāninā vyāsa īśvaro 'asau vikalpitaḥ
sa tam āviśya muktātmā kṛtārtho jāyate muniḥ
nainaṃ jānantyamārgasthāstarkahetuparāyaṇāḥ
bhoktāraṃ prakṛterīśaṃ paraṃ ṣaḍviṃśasaṃjñitam
oṃkāraḥ prakṛtirnityaṃ tanmadhye ceśvaraḥ sthitaḥ
oṃkāraṃ dhyāyatā yena atītya prakṛtiṃ mune
īśvaro 'asau mahān vinnaḥ sa muktaḥ paśubandhanaiḥ
īśvarī prakṛtiḥ khyātā guṇabandhādvimohanī
brahmatvādbṛṃhaṇī hyeṣā viṣṇutvādvibhavāśritā
prasādādīśvarasyaiṣā prakṛtistriguṇātmikā
sābhimānā bhavasraṣṭrī bhoktā tasyā maheśvaraḥ
aṣṭabāhustripādā ca pañcadehamukhī tathā
jaganmātā smṛtā hyeṣā guṇatrayavikārajā
ubhe śubhāśubhe tasyā vidyāvidye tathā hyubhe
udbhavo 'atha praṇāśaśca kriyānuṣṭhānam eva ca
nimittaṃ cābhavadyonirbhāvāḥ saṃkṣepatastvamī
īśvarājjāta oṃkāraḥ sa ca tasmin pratiṣṭhitaḥ
ataḥ kṛtvā mahābhāga yoginaḥ kapilādayaḥ
īśabhojyau guṇātmānau jñātvā viṣṇupitāmahau
mahāmohau tamoniṣṭhau viṣayāsaṅgasaṃyutau
saṃsārabhramaṇau mūḍhau sarvānityasamāyutau
īśvarepsurbhavedvidvān dhyānayogaparāyaṇaḥ
yenāsau īśvaro vinno yogenātmani saṃsthitaḥ
ekāśītyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
ātmā sūkṣmo mano buddhirahaṃkāro guṇāstathā
bhūtānīndriyasaṃghātastanmātrāṇi daśānilāḥ
vibhaktāḥ kramaśo dehe vibhāgena yathāśrayam
hṛdaye karṇikāyāṃ tu yat padmaṃ sarvatomukham
veṣṭitaṃ tantubhiḥ sūkṣmaistadūrdhvaṃ sarvadehinām
ātmā tatra sajīvastu samanaskaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ
tat suṣuptam iti prāhuḥ saṃsiddhāḥ śivayoginaḥ
jvālinī stimitā dhūmrā vidyunmeghā viśālinī
mālinī śaṃkarī caiva sumaitrī bodhanī tathā
etā daśa mahānāḍyo jīve tasmin pratiṣṭhitāḥ
śayānaṃ pratibuddhaṃ vā yāstā bibhrati dehinam
śabdādiviṣayebhyastu ātmā sarvagataśca yaḥ
ahaṃkāro mato buddhirbhāvāścetaśca dehajāḥ
saha jīvena tiṣṭhanti dhārayantaḥ śarīriṇam
ta eva sahitāḥ sarve jīvaścaiva tu pañcamaḥ
sthito manasi sūkṣmastu śītāṃśurnāma tantukaḥ
cetaḥ sa eva samproktaḥ sa eva puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ
manaḥ somaḥ sukhaṃ brahmā jñānaṃ dharmo ratistathā
ahaṃkāro hutāśaśca mṛtyurduḥkham athāmayam
kāmaroṣau jarā tṛṣṇā adharmaśceti tāmasāḥ
viṣṇurbuddhistathā kāryaṃ kāraṇaṃ bhūmireva ca
jñānaṃ vairāgyam ākāśaṃ rājaso bhāvavistaraḥ
jīvamadhye sthitā sūkṣmā vidhūmā pāvakī śikhā
amṛtaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ gatiścaiva hi sā parā
madhye tasyāḥ sthitaṃ saumyam amṛtaṃ śaśimaṇḍalam
madhye tasyāgnisaṃkāśo jīva īśaḥ pradṛśyate
sarasā lohitā mukhyā prītā rasavatī tathā
vidhūmā cāmṛtā caiva nikuṇṭhā bahuvistarā
etāḥ sūkṣmatarā nāḍyaḥ sambhidya daśapāvakam
tarpayanti sadā somaṃ bhūtādhāraṃ payo 'amṛtam
saṃchādayati vṛddhastāṃ jīvamadhyagatāṃ śikhām
tadevāmṛtam ākhyātam īśvarāspadam uttamam
yāmṛtetyaparā nāḍī sā tu svapne pratiṣṭhitā
ubhāvetau munirjitvā svapnajāgaraṇāśrayau
mamatvādyāśca ye bhāvā manasaścaiva yā ghṛṇā
yadvā kuryādahaṃkārastajjñānāt sarvam utsṛjet
bhoktā vahniḥ smṛtasteṣāṃ tajjñātā kena baddhyate
iti jñātvā tyajeccintāṃ bhavedyogaparaḥ sadā
vahneryadauṣṇyaṃ tat pāpaṃ tejo dharma udāhṛtaḥ
prakṛtiryā sa jīvastu yā śikhā sa maheśvaraḥ
nirmamā yogaviduṣaḥ śaṃkaravratam āsthitāḥ
gacchanti svatanuṃ tyaktvā hitvā māyāṃ paraṃ padam
idam anyat paraṃ jñānam asmāt sūkṣmataraṃ punaḥ
muktvā pāśupatān siddhān yanna bhūteṣu vidyate
na spṛśanti tadātmānaṃ vikārāstasya te bahiḥ
sa evaṃ dṛśyate dhyānānnānyopāyāt kathaṃcana
sarvabhāvaguṇātītaṃ sucintyaṃ parameśvaram
jñānena ye prapaśyanti yoginaste pare smṛtāḥ
chāyaiṣā dṛśyate yā tu cakṣurviṣayam āśritā
sa jīvaḥ kīrtito vyāsa sthitihetuḥ śarīriṇām
mahānāgaḥ smṛto nāmnā vāyurākāśagocaraḥ
ākāśe karṇikāyāṃ ca nāḍyāṃ jīve ca saṃsthitaḥ
gāndhārī vijayā caiva saṃjayā talavartinī
nāga etāsu nāḍīṣu vāyuḥ samparivartate
sā jayā vijayā yā ca dve te prāṇavahe smṛte
apāne talagāndhāryau nāḍyau nāgena saṃyute
yogādapānamanasornāgena samudīritāḥ
vṛddhaṃ saṃdhārayeddeham āyuṣā ca balena ca
nāḍī tvanyā suṣumṇeti somavahnimanaḥsthitā
sāsmin sadhātuke dehe kūrmāre cānile sthitā
gulphe karatale saktā nikuñcā saprasāriṇī
samānavyānasaṃyuktā raktamāṃse hi tarpayet
nāḍyāṃ nābhinibaddhāyāṃ tulāyāṃ tasu pratiṣṭhitau
adha ekaścarennāḍyā vāyuranyastadūrdhvagaḥ
adhaḥsthaḥ pādasambaddha ūrdhvagaḥ śirasi sthitaḥ
devadattamahānāgakṛtakūrmadhanaṃjayāḥ
prāṇāste pañca vikhyātā vahnayo yājinaḥ
hutam eṣu yadiṣṭaṃ vā somaṃ tadupatiṣṭhati
somaṃ viśanti yajvāno na teṣāṃ muktilakṣaṇam
dīptiragneḥ smṛtā yā tu oṣadhibhyaśca yadrasam
tarpaṇaṃ yacca somasya karṇikāyāṃ tadāsthitam
netreṣu dṛśyate yo 'ayaṃ jyotiśchāyāprakāśakaḥ
sa jīvaḥ sarvasattvānām ātmā tatra samāsthitaḥ
taccāmṛtaṃ samākhyātaṃ jñānalabhyaṃ taducyate
tasmāt paratarā nāsti jñānavijñānayorgatiḥ
jñātvaivaṃ saṃtyajenmohaṃ guṇatrayavikārajam
vimohāstyaktasaṃsargāḥ kriyākāryavivarjitāḥ
taṃ viśanti maheśānam īśvaravratacāriṇaḥ
itīdaṃ yogam ākhyātaṃ vyāsa māheśvaraṃ tava
yogavidhāvaṣṭama ekāśītyuttaraśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
dvyaśītyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
vyāsa uvāca
aho jñānaṃ tvayākhyātam ajñānavinivartanam
adyāhaṃ gatasaṃdeho mahādevaṃ paraṃ prati
śaṃkarāt prakṛtirjātā brahmaviṣṇū tadātmakau
jñātvā ṣaḍviṃśam īśānaṃ mucyate bandhanāditi
niṣkalaṃ sakalaṃ jñānaṃ ko 'anya evaṃ prabhāṣate
tvatprasādādahaṃ tāta prāptajñāno mahāśubhaḥ
visaṃdeho bhavaṃ śāntaḥ praṣṭavyaṃ kiṃcidasti me
tat tvāṃ vijñāpayāmīdaṃ niṣṭhām ākhyātum arhasi
vinā kleśaṃ tanuṃ tyaktvā yogī yogabalānvitaḥ
īśvarādhārasamprāpterupāyaṃ mokṣalambhanam
kathayasva muniśreṣṭha praṣṭavyaṃ nānyadasti me
evam uktaḥ sa śiṣyeṇa vyāsena sumahātmanā
śṛṇu vyāsa paraṃ jñānam īśvarādhānakāraṇam
svadehaṃ ripuvat tyaktvā ṣaḍviṃśe layam āpnuyāt
yā nāḍyo vāyvavaṣṭabdhāḥ saṃvaranti śarīriṇam
śataṃ tāsāṃ śatānāṃ tu karṇikāmadhyam āśritam
tam āśrityāsthitā nāḍyo nābhyāṃ pādeṣvadhogatāḥ
śirobaddhāḥ smṛtā bhūyastā eva karam āsthitāḥ
karam āśritya tā bhūyaḥ karṇikāṃ punarāśritāḥ
dvisaptatisahasrāṇi nāḍīnām aparā mune
tāsām ekaikaśo bhedāḥ sūkṣmasūkṣmatarāḥ smṛtāḥ
tāsu saṃcarate prāṇaḥ karṇikāvyomasambhavaḥ
tatrātmā sūkṣmasaṃlakṣyaḥ prāguktastiṣṭhati dvija
yā prabhā durdṛśā tasya tāṃ bhajedyogavinmuniḥ
tattejaḥ sarvanāḍīṣu vibhaktaṃ sarvadehinām
tena nāḍyo bahiḥsparśānmanaḥ kurvanti vistṛtam
tattejaścakṣuṣā hṛtvā sarvanāḍīsamāśritam
vāyurdhanaṃjayo nāmnā yo hṛdi sphurate sadā
trīṇi tasya mukhāni āhuḥ śiro nābhi hṛdeva ca
ye 'anye prāṇā navākhyātā vāyavaḥ kīrtitā mayā
tadvaśādutkramantyete tasmiṃstiṣṭhanti saṃsthitāḥ
nābhībandhanam āsādya nāḍīnāṃ vaktram āsthitam
dvitīyaṃ karṇikāyāṃ tu tṛtīyaṃ tālusaṃsthitam
kṣurikā paraśuḥ śūlaṃ trividhotkrāntirucyate
śūlaṃ hṛdi kṣuraṃ nābhyāṃ tālau paraśurāsthitaḥ
tāluke hṛdi vā baddhaṃ trayaṃ nābhyāṃ pratiṣṭhitam
tālau viyojitaṃ sarvaṃ prāṇam eva vimuñcati
ākṣiptaṃ tritayaṃ nābhyāṃ karṇikāyāṃ viyojitam
yathā jīvo na baddhyeta yoginastadidaṃ śṛṇu
bāhyaḥ śarīrajaścaiva mṛtyurdvividha ucyate
viṣaśastrāgniyogaistu sarpadaṃṣṭrimarujjalaiḥ
bāhyo mṛtyuriti khyātaḥ śarīraṃ tu nibodha me
yogopāyakṛto yaśca yaśca kālakṣayāgataḥ
tayorbhedavikāre tu śṛṇu vyāsa samāsataḥ
yo 'ayam āghoṣajaḥ śabdaḥ śrūyate śrotrasandhitaḥ
śabdasparśaguṇātīto rūpayogaṃ vimuñcati
evam agnau praṇaṣṭe tu sarva evānilāstataḥ
udānenāśu saṃyujya karṇikāyāṃ viśanti hi
indriyāṇi mano yānti manaḥ prāṇavinirgamam
teṣu sarveṣu līneṣu prāṇān vāyurnipīḍayet
pīḍyamānāstataḥ sarve te bhavantyekato 'anilāḥ
śeṣastatra hi mūrmāro jīvaṃ tyaktvā sa tiṣṭhati
niṣkramanti tato dehāt tvaritaṃ vāyuneritāḥ
prāgupāttastato 'asyānyo dehaḥ sūkṣmo vijāyate
sa tatra sandhito jīvo bhūyo mūḍhaśca tiṣṭhati
evaṃ kālakṛtā hyeṣā sarvabhūtagaṇasthitiḥ
vinā yogaṃ na jīyeta sūkṣmaṃ māheśvaraṃ padam
upaviṣṭaḥ prasupto vā utkrāntyabhyastasaṃyamaḥ
svecchayā mucyate vyāsa jñātvā taṃ tu maheśvaram
kṣurikāṃ paraśuṃ vātha śūlaṃ vā dhārayenmuniḥ
tataḥ sarve 'asya līyante vikārāḥ karaṇaiḥ saha
vīkṣate ceśvaraṃ brahma ṣaḍviṃśaṃ svatanusthitam
sukham ārohati brahma harmyapṛṣṭhaṃ talādiva
padārthaṃ pañca vijñāya duḥkhāntapariniṣṭhitaḥ
pañcabhirbrahmabhiḥ pūto bhasmanā dīkṣito dvijaḥ
śaṃkaraikamanā yogī jñānam etadavāpnute
māheśvaram imaṃ yogaṃ niṣkalaṃ muktikāraṇam
mahādevaparo bhūtvā jñānam etadavāpnuhi
mahādevaṃ prapannā ye tān muktvā śivayoginaḥ
evaṃ pāśupatā viprā niṣkalaṃ taṃ maheśvaram
tryaśītyuttaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
bhavyabhūtabhavānāṃ ca saptānām ūrdhvataḥ sthitaḥ
nāsau tarkavinirdeśyo lokāstasmin pratiṣṭhitāḥ
brahmāṇḍaṃ sakalaṃ tasmiñchivaloke pratiṣṭhitam
nāsau naśyati saṃhāre dhruvaḥ sthāṇuḥ surālayaḥ
yatrāhaṃ sanakādyāśca brahmā caiva pitāmahaḥ
bālakhilyapurogāśca siddhāśca kapilādayaḥ
śivayogapariprāptyā sattvādiguṇavarjitāḥ
tiṣṭhāmo nirvṛtā vyāsa sevamānāstam īśvaram
paramāṇurasau īśo bhāvagamyo manīṣiṇām
kṣamā satyaṃ dhṛtiścaiva tapo vairāgyam eva ca
sraṣṭṛtvaṃ jñānavairāgyādātmabodho maheśatā
aṣṭamaṃ dhruvam adhyeyam akṣaraṃ muktikāraṇam
māyādhāma tadīśasya jagatsaṃhārahetumat
ūrdhvato brahmalokasya yojanānāṃ mahātmanaḥ
viṃśatīnāṃ tu koṭīnāṃ puraṃ sthāṇoḥ samāsthitam
etāvān ūrdhvasaṃcāro gatyantaśca tataḥ smṛtaḥ
asaṃkhyātāḥ pure tasmin nityāḥ sūkṣmāstathāvyayāḥ
jñānādhikāradharmiṇyaḥ śaivīprakṛtayaḥ sthitāḥ
yābhyo jajñe maheśānau brahmaviṣṇū prajāpatī
tābhyāṃ prakṛtibhūtābhyāṃ sraṣṭṛtvaṃ paramaṃ dadau
akṣayo vimalaḥ sūkṣmo niṣkalaḥ sakalo 'api ca
yadāsīddhaimam aṇḍaṃ tu laukikaṃ tu āpavargikam
tasmādbījasya nirbhedaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ sa vibhuḥ smṛtaḥ
prakṛtirvaiṣṇavī proktā sā ca tasmādvinirgatā
surāsurādisṛṣṭyarthaṃ brahmatvaṃ punarāsthitā
aṇḍasya bhedataḥ padmabrahmaṇaḥ śaṃkarātmanaḥ
yat sthānaṃ vigraheśasya īśvarasya parātmanaḥ
nāmnā śivapuraṃ vyāsa gatirīśvarayoginām
śataṃ śatasahasrāṇāṃ yojanānāṃ taducyate
mahīmaṇḍalasaṃsthānaṃ tanmadhye vistṛtaṃ smṛtam
mahatā haimajātena prākāreṇa suveṣṭitam
jarāmṛtyuśramavyādhikopamohamadādayaḥ
śataṃ śatasahasrāṇāṃ yojanānāṃ yathādiśam
tat puraṃ vṛṣabhāṅkasya sarvavyāpi samṛddhimat
divyā mārakatī bhūmiḥ sparśamātrasukhāvahā
vaidūryamaṇikalpāni bālārkasadṛśāni ca
mahāhradapramāṇāni nālairvaidūryasannibhaiḥ
indranīlanikāśāni mahāmaṇinibhāni ca
pure bhagavataḥ śambhoḥ pārāśarya nibodha tāḥ
varadā ca vareṇyā ca vareśā varavarṇinī
vārāhī vāribhadrā ca varā caiva mahāpagāḥ
nānākusumasaṃmiśraṃ tā vahanti jalāmṛtam
na devā na munīndrāśca nāsurāḥ pitaro na ca
meruśṛṅgapratīkāśo digbhadrastapanaprabhaḥ
prāsādo lakṣapādastu kāmagaḥ kanakāmayaḥ
vaidūryairvyomasaṃkāśaiḥ sphāṭikaiścandrasaprabhaiḥ
prabālairarkasaṃkāśairindranīlamayaiḥ paraiḥ
śaśiraśmiprakāśābhiḥ kvacidarkāṃśurūpibhiḥ
śobhitaṃ tat patākābhirvirarāja sukhānilam
śuśubhe tat puraṃ kīrṇaṃ pādapairgirisannibhaiḥ
mahīdhrāṇāṃ yathā meruḥ sarveṣāṃ pravaro mahān
tatra viśveśvaraḥ sākṣānmahābhūtapatirharaḥ
sadāste sahitaḥ patnyā ṣaḍviṃśaḥ parameśvaraḥ
lakṣmīrmeghā dhṛtiścaiva hrīḥ śrīḥ kīrtiḥ sarasvatī
śivabhāvārpitātmāno ye narā rudratatparāḥ
yatra tatra mṛtā vatsa teṣāṃ tatrāspadaṃ smṛtam
ye ca māheśvarā vyāsa tiṣṭhante śaṃkarālaye
munayaḥ śaṃkaraṃ bhaktāstāñchṛṇuṣva samāhitaḥ
ṛbhurbrahmā surajyeṣṭho naranārāyaṇāvapi
śiṣyaḥ siddhaḥ pañcaśikhastathā
munirhayaśirā yaśca yajñavalkādayastathā
tryakṣāḥ śaṃkaravarṣmāṇaḥ paramaiśvaryasaṃyutāḥ
tiṣṭhantīśvaramūlasthā guṇātītā mumukṣavaḥ
īśvaraṃ te samāviśya prāpnuvantyapavargikam
yaiśca dṛṣṭāni viprendra śivaliṅgāni tāni tu
kedāro madhyamaścaiva girīśaśca mahālaye
catuḥśṛṅgeśvaro devaḥ śrīgirau ca maheśvaraḥ
kārohaṇaśca deveśo gaṅgādvāre ca śaṃkaraḥ
bhadreśaśca mahādevaḥ śaṅkukarṇeśvarastathā
mahākāleśvaraścaiva gokarṇe ca tathā hyubhau
avimukteśvaraścaiva yāni cānyāni bhūtale
te 'api yānti mṛtā vyāsa tat puraṃ girijāpateḥ
yogaḥ pāśupato yaśca mayā te parikīrtitaḥ
bhaktiryeṣāṃ bhave nityaṃ kṛtārthāste narottamāḥ
mṛtāḥ śivapure vyāsa tryakṣāḥ paṭṭiśapāṇayaḥ
nandīśaskandasaṃkāśā yogaiśvaryabalānvitāḥ
rudrā bhavanti te vyāsa sadā śaṃkarapārśvagāḥ
eṣa te kathitaḥ sarvo yogo māheśvaraḥ paraḥ
sakalaṃ niṣkalaṃ caiva jñātvaivaṃ param īśvaram
bhaviṣyasi ca yogātmā jñānasyāsya prabhāvataḥ
jñānaśaktyā smṛ brahmāṇḍodbhavakāraṇe
yajñadharmapracārārthaṃ vedaṃ svāyambhuvasmṛtam
vijñānāt tvam anusmṛtya caturdhā vikariṣyasi
tvatkṛtāḥ pracariṣyanti tīrthakṛt tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi
śāṃkarajñānasampanna īśvare layam āpsyasi
evam uktaḥ sa viprendro hṛṣṭasarvatanūruhaḥ
upasadya munīndraṃ taṃ bhasmasaṃskāram āptavān
tatkṣaṇāccāsya yogo 'asau prādurbhūto mahāmuneḥ
śarvāyatanavīkṣārthaṃ vicacāra mahītale
vāyuruvāca
evaṃ sanatkumārastu pṛṣṭo vyāsena dhīmatā
munīndraḥ kathayāmāsa purāṇaṃ skandasambhavam
śivayogodbhavaṃ dhyānaṃ sarvajñānārṇvamvaṃ mahat
tasmādyūyam api jñātvā vrataṃ pāśupataṃ dvijāḥ
abhyasya śāṃkaraṃ yogam īśvare layam āpnuta
vedārthasmṛtisambaddhā vidyāścakre mahāmuniḥ
purāṇaṃ prathamaṃ prāhurādyaṃ nandīśvaro dvijāḥ
kṛtsnasya jagato viprā ādikartā yathā haraḥ
tathā sarvapurāṇānāṃ purāṇo 'ayaṃ paraḥ smṛtaḥ
ṣya sāyujyaṃ śṛṇuyādvibhoḥ
ādyaṃ puṇyam umāpaterdvijavṛṣāḥ stotrānuvādaṃ paraṃ
sarve te jvaladarkavahnivapuṣastryakṣāḥ śaśāṅkatviṣaḥ
iti skandapurāṇe tryaśītyadhikaśatatamo 'adhyāyaḥ
ārṣaṃ skandapurāṇaṃ sayogavidhi samāptam
ālaṣka saṃ caitraśukladvādaśyāṃ samāptam
śubham
mārgaḥ
aṣṭāśītitamo adhyāyaḥ
aryamā bahubhirbāṇaiḥ prahlādaṃ daityapuṅgavam
ājaghāna rathaṃ ghoraṃ dhvajaṃ cāsya vyaśātayat
jaghāna bahubhirbāṇairvṛṣṭyā megho yathācalam
śarānagaṇayanneva hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sutaḥ
gṛhītvā kūbare tasya rathaṃ hemapariṣkṛtam
nirjitāstarjitāścaiva yuddhāya ca punaḥ sthitāḥ
tataḥ saṃkulam evābhūddevānāṃ dānavaiḥ saha
parasparajigīṣūṇāṃ yuddhaṃ bhīrubhayāvaham
tato bheryaśca śaṅkhāśca paṭahāsekyapuṣkalāḥ
jharjharyaḥ pepukāścaiva ḍiḍṇimā goviṣāṇakāḥ
avādyanta bale vyāsa ubhayeṣāṃ sahasraśaḥ
keśaśaivālabahulā dhanurjyākṛtatantukā
niṣṭanacchastramaṇḍūkā dukūlacchatraphenilā
uṣṇīṣavarahaṃsā ca karapādaśiropalā
hārakeyūrasikatā mukuṭotphullapaṅkajā
medosrakaphapaṅkā ca prāṇajīvitanāśinī
prāvartata nadī ghorā hastyaśvarathavāhinī
tasyāṃ snāyanti rakṣāṃsi pibanti ca ramanti ca
nṛtyanti cāpi vividhāsbhīrūṇāṃ bhayadāstathā
gṛdhrā gomāyavaścaiva śvāno mārjāravāyasāḥ
cakṣūṃṣi karapādāntraṃ bhakṣayanto 'abhiremire
mamāyaṃ hastinaḥ pādo mamāyaṃ medapaṭṭakaḥ
mamāyaṃ ca karaḥ śukro bāhuśca rudhirasyadaḥ
mamāyaṃ tava nāyaṃ ca gṛhṇa paśyeti caiva hi
kalahaṃ cakrire tatra krūrāḥ piśitabhojanāḥ
tyaktvānye ca hatāṃstatra svadehān sumahārathāḥ
vimānaiḥ strījanākīrṇaiḥ prayayurbrahmaṇaḥ sadaḥ
apare pāpakarmāṇo hanyamānā ruṣāndhitaiḥ
kecidārttasvaraṃ kṛtvā ṣārditāḥ
mriyante puruṣā yuddhe śataśo 'atha sahasraśaḥ
daśantaśca tṛṇānyanye bhrātaḥ putreti cāpare
krandamānā janā bhītāḥ prāṇān kṛcchreṇa tatyajuḥ
saṃdaṣṭauṣṭhapuṭāḥ keciddevāsuramahārathāḥ
śarasannatamarmāṇaḥ patantyurvyāṃ drumā iva
aśivāni śivā neduraṭṭahāsāṃśca rākṣasāḥ
ārttanādāṃśca puruṣāstathaiva gajavājinaḥ
siṃhanādāśca śūrāṇāṃ bāhuśabdāśca puṣkalāḥ
dhanuṣāṃ kṛṣyamāṇānāṃ śabdā vādyaravāstathā
athendraśca dhaneśaśca yamaḥ kālaśca vīryavān
varuṇo marutaścaiva viśvedevāśca sarvaśaḥ
mitraścaiva jayantaśca bhagaḥ pūṣāryamā tathā
kāpālī cāpi yo rudro vasavaśca mahābalāḥ
nāsatyaścaiva dasraśca pṛśnayaśca surottamāḥ
ete cānye ca devānāṃ pravarā bāhuśālinaḥ
prabhañjanā ivākāle mahānta iva cācalāḥ
vṛṣabhā iva nardanto bṛṃhanta iva kuñjarāḥ
grasantaśca yathā grāhāśchindanto makarā iva
varṣamāṇā iva ghanāḥ siṃḥā iva ca nardinaḥ
dānavānāṃ balaṃ sarve vegenaivābhyavārayan
yuddhe aṣṭāśītitamo 'adhyāyaḥ
